Ayssi comensan las paraulas de Albucasim .	The words of Albuca's doctrine begin here.
O, filhs, pus yeu he a vos complit aquest libre, le qual es le derier de la sciencia de medicina, per le compliment de lu so consequit la fi en lu, e per las exposicios de lu, e per las declaracios de lu, es a mi vist que yeu complesca aquel a vos am aquest tractat, le qual es partida de la operacio am ma, so es cyrurgia.	Oh, children, since I have completed this book for you, which is the last of the science of medicine, according to its conclusion and through my explanations and declarations, it appears to me that you will be able to grasp what I wish to convey to you in this treatise, which is a part of surgical operation.
Quar la operacio am ma es prostrada en nostre regio e en nostre temps de tot privada, entro que fort leu peric la sciencia de lu, e le vistigi de lu es ostat; e no romasero de lu sino alcunas petitas descripcios en les libres dels Antics, les quals mudero las mas e endevenc ad aquels error e heyssitacio entro que son clausas las entencios de lu e es elonguada la forsa de lu e l’art.	Now the surgical operation is almost lost in our region and in our time, so that the science of it has perished, and its knowledge remains hidden; and there remain only a few brief descriptions in the books of the Ancients, which have been corrupted by many errors and obscurities, so that the intentions of it are closed off and its power and art are stretched out.
E es vist a mi que yeu vivifique aquela am ordenacio de aquest tractat en aquela segon la via de exposicio e de declaracio e de abreviacio; e per que vengua am las formas dels ferramentz de cautheri e dels autres instrumentz de la obra cum sia per addicio de la declaracio, e per preparacio de lu, la qual causa es necessaria.	And it appears to me that you will revitalize the ancient order of this treatise through the way of exposition and declaration and abbreviation; and for that, you should come with the forms of the instruments of cauterization and other tools of the work, as is necessary for addition to the declaration and preparation of what is to be done.
Mays la causa per la qual no es atrobat bo artifex am la sieua ma en aquest nostre temps, es quar la art de medicina es longua, e que cove le sieu actor denant aquo esser excercitat en la sciencia de anotomia la qual recontec Gualia entro que sapia les juvament dels membres e las formas de aquels, e la conjunctio e la separacio de lor; e haia la conoyssensa dels osses, dels nervis e dels lacertz, e·l nombre de aquels, e la egrecio de lor; e de las venas pulsatils e de las quietas, e dels locs del eyssiment de lor.	However, the reason why a good craftsman is not found with his own hand in this our time, is because the art of medicine is long and requires its actor to be exercised in the science of anatomy, which Galen knew well, so that he could know the joints of the members and their forms, and their conjunction and separation; and have knowledge of the bones, nerves, and ligaments, and their number, and the arrangement of them; and of the pulsating and quiet veins, and the places of their efflux.
E per aquo ditz Ypocras que am u nom es mot, mays en l’obra petit, e majorment en la art de la ma.	And therefore says Hippocrates that with a small name one can accomplish much, but most of all in the work of the hand.
Mays nos ja avem dit de aquel en l’introit de aquest libre; quar qui no es scient aquo que li avem dit de anotomia, no es evacuat que no caia en error per la qual siran mortz les homes, ayssi cum yeu he vist trops de aquels, quar alscus son formatz en esta sciencia e gettan se de aquela ses sciencia e ses experiment.	But we have already said this about him in the introduction to this book; for whoever is not knowledgeable about anatomy as we have described it, will certainly fall into error by which men are killed, just as I have seen many of them, because some are formed in this science and then stray from that true science and experience.
Quar yeu vi un metge folh e enperit aver incidit un apostema escrophilos en le colh de una femna, e incidic alcunas arterias del colh per que fluic gran sanc entro que la femna cazec morta entre las mas de lu.	For I saw a foolish and experienced doctor who had inserted an abscess into the throat of a woman, and had cut through some arteries in the throat, so that a great deal of blood flowed out and the woman died among others.
E vi un autre metge que pres que el traguera una peyra d’un home le qual avia procesit en sa etat, e la peyra era gran, e venguet a lu e trayssec aquela peyra am un tros de la vesiqua, per que aquel home al tertz dia es mort.	And I saw another doctor who told him to pull out a stone from a man's bladder, which he had processed in his state, and the stone was large, and it came to him and he extracted that stone with a piece of the intestines, so that that man died on the third day.
E yeu ja apelat fuy a estrayre aquela, e vi que per la grandesa de la peyra e per la disposicio del malaute conogui subre lu que morira.	And I have already cried out against it, and saw that because of the largeness of the stone and the condition of the patient, he knew in advance that he would die.
E vi un autre metge le qual prenia stipendic de un duc de nostra terra per cyrurgia, e endeven a un crastrat negre le qual era deves lu fractura en la coyssa de lu; e perparec le metge am la sua ignorancia, estrayssec la fractura, sobre la plagua, am pulvinas e astelas am forta strectura, e no layssec a la plagua espiracio.	And I saw another doctor who took a stipend from a duke of our land for surgery, and then operated on a blacksmith's leg which was broken in the joint; and the doctor prepared himself with his ignorance, extracted the fracture, over the wound, with pulleys and astels with strong tension, and did not give the wound any breath.
E aprop le desliet segons los sieus desiriers, e aprop le relieg, e aprop le leyssec per alcus jorns e comandec que nos deslies le liament; e estec ayssi entro que la coyssa e·l pe foro apostematz, e pervenguet a perdicio.	And then he loosened the bandage according to his desires, and then released the ligature, and then left it untied for some days, and commanded that we loosen the tie; and thus it happened that the joint and leg became inflamed, and ultimately led to perdition.
E yeu fuy apelat a lu, e aparelhegui a desliar le liament, e conseguida es tranquilitat e enayssi amermet de sas dolors.	And I was called to him, and I prepared to loosen the tie, and he gained tranquility and eventually became free from his pains.
Mays empero ja corrupcio era confermada en le membre, per que no pogui refrenar aquela, e no cessec perambular la corrupcio en le membre entro que·l malaute peric.	But however, corruption had already been confirmed in the member, so that it could not be restrained and did not cease to corrupt the member until the patient was endangered.
E vi un autre metge le qual perforec un apostema cancros, e fo ulcerat aprop alscus dias, entro que foc magnificada la malicia de lu am lo senhor de lu.	And I saw another doctor who perforated a cancerous abscess and it became ulcerated within a few days, until the wickedness of it increased with its lord.
La qual causa es quar le cranc caut es pur de humor melencolic, lahoras no cove que pervengua a lu am ferr de tot, sino que sia an membre le qual suffertes que de tot fos hostat.	Which is because the cancerous tumor is pure of melancholic humor, so that it does not need to be treated with iron throughout, but rather should be considered as a member which suffers from being totally attacked.
E per aquo, filhs, necessari es a vos que la operacio am ma sia devisada en dos devesios: so es en operacio a lu qual es associada salut, e en obra am la qual es perilh en las majors disposicios.	And therefore, children, it is necessary for you to divide the surgical operation into two parts: one is in the operation which is associated with health, and the other is in the work where danger lies in the greater dispositions.
E yeu ja he exsitat aquo en tot loc de aquest libre en le qual venc opperacio en la qual es error e temor; per que necessari es a vos que guardetz aquo e layssetz aquel, per que les folhs no atrobo via a parlar e a vos desonestar.	And I have already existed in every place of this book where the operation is one in which there is error and fear; therefore it is necessary for you to keep this and avoid that, so that foolishness does not obstruct the way to speak and to deceive.
E donc prenetz las vostras armas am sollicitut e am proteccio de Dieu , e les vostres malautes am falicitat e am fermetat.	And therefore take your own arms with solicitude and protection of God, and your own patients with felicity and firmness.
E usatz de la milhor via per la gracia de Dieu perdusent a salut e a lausabla successio, e laysatz las malautias terriblas de difficil sanacio, e ostatz las vostras armas de aquo que vos fa temer, per so que ysitatio en vostra fe e en le vostre nom no vos evasisca: quar mays es remanent a la vostra gloria, e pus aut en le mon e en derier a las vostras sanctitatz.	And use the best means by the grace of God to avoid losing health and the noble succession, and abandon the terrible diseases of difficult healing, and hold your own arms from this which makes you fear, so that your situation remains in your faith and in your name does not deceive you: because it is more remaining to your glory, and all the more in this world and forever in your sanctity.
Gualia ja diyssec en alcunas sieuas monicios:	Galen already said in some of his own writings:
“No mediquetz malautia mala, per so que mals metges no siatz nompnatz”.	"Do not heal bad illnesses, because bad doctors are not named."
E yeu ja he devesit aquest libre segontz tres capitols.	And I have divided this book into three chapters.
Comensa la divisio del libre, e primier de la primieyra partida.	The division of the book begins, and the first part of the first chapter.
Le primier capitol ordenat del cap entro·s pes, en las formas dels instrumentz e en les ferrementz dels cauteris, e de aquo que necessari es en la opperacio.	The first chapter, arranged from head to foot, in the forms of instruments and ironwork of cauterization, and of what is necessary in the operation.
La divisio de la segonda partida.	The division of the second part.
Le segon capitol, de siccio e perforacio, e de ventosas, e de plaguas, e de extractio de sagetas e de semblantz ad aquelas, tot capitolat e ordenat de las formas dels instrumentz.	The second chapter, on drying and piercing, and on cupping, wounds, and extraction of splinters and similar things, entirely chaptered and ordered in the forms of instruments.
Divisio de la tersa partida.	Division of the third part.
Le tertz capitol, de restauracio e de dislocacio, e de curacio de torcio e de semblantz ad aquels; capitol ordenat del cap entro·s pes, e de las formas dels instrumentz.	The third chapter, on restoration and dislocation, and on curing of torsion and similar things; chapter ordered from head to foot, and in the forms of instruments.
De cauteri am foc e am medicina aguda e rememoracio de la opperacio.	On cauterization with fire and acute medicine, and recollection of the operation.
Am aquel comensa le tractat de tot le libre.	Here begins the treatise of the whole book.
Cove que yeu digua la qualitat dels juvamentz de aquel cauteri e dels noccumentz de lu, e en qual compleccio sia prohibit cauteri.	You should know the quality of the joints of that cauterization and the nonuments of it, and in what composition it is prohibited to cauterize.
Donc dic que·l sermo de la qualitat del juvament de cauteri e del noccument de lu es sermo lonc e prolixs, e subtil per sciensa, e secret amaguat; e ja de lu a parlat gran multitut de savis, e de lu se son desacordatz, et a mi abasta un petit dels sermons de lor, temen perlonguacio.	Therefore I say that the sermon on the quality of the joint of cauterization and its nonument is a long and prolix discourse, subtle by science, and secret and hidden; and already many wise men have spoken about it, and among them there has been disagreement, and for my part, I will not venture to recount all their sermons, fearing prolongation.
E donc dic que cauteri comfereys a tota compleccio universalment la qual es am materia o ses materia, exceptat dos compleccios, las quals son compleccios caudas ses materia .	And therefore I say that cauterization agrees with all universal composition universally, which is in matter or its matter, except for two compositions, which are compositions without material.
En la compleccio cauda e secca am materia se desecordero; quar alcus dyssero que cauteri es juvatiu ad aquela, e les autres dyssero le contrari de aquel, que cauteri no es convenient en malautia la qual es per qualiditat e per siccitat, quar natura del foc es qualiditat e siccitat, e enconvenient es que malautia cauda e secca am aquo que es caut e sec sia sanada.	In the dry and withered composition with material it will desiccate; because some say that cauterization is beneficial to that, and others say the opposite of that, that cauterization is not suitable in a disease which is due to quality and dryness, for nature of fire is quality and dryness, and it is inconvenient that the diseased part, which is hot and dry, should be healed with heat and dryness.
E diysec aquel que ditz le contrari de aquel, que per cauteri es fayt juvament en tota malautia cauda e secca que ve en les cors dels homes, quar quan tu comparas le cors de home e las humiditatz de lu a la compleccio del foc, atrobas le cors de home freg.	And you will find that the one who says the opposite of that is wrong, for through cauterization it is made to heal in all hot and dry diseases that are found in the bodies of men; because when you compare the human body and its humors with the composition of fire, you find the human body cold.
E yeu dic per le sermo de aquel, que esperiment aquo ja a mi alscunas vetz a descubert.	And I say by the sermon of that, that experience has already shown me several times to uncover.
Mays empero no cove que vengua sobre aquo aquel que ja es exproat e excersitat en le capitol de cauteri per derier exercici, e a conogut la diversitat de la compleccio dels homes e la disposicio de las malautias en lor meteyssas, e las causas de aquelas, e·ls accidentz de lor, e l’espasi del temps de aquelas.	But however it is not necessary that what has already been explained and exercised in the chapter on cauterization should come again over this, for I have already known the diversity of the composition of men and the disposition of diseases in their members, and the causes of those, and the accidents of theirs, and the space of time of those.
Mays en las autras compleccios, no es sobre vos temor, e majorment en las malautias fregas e humidas, quar ja totz les metges se son acordatz sobre aquels, e no so desecordatz en le juvament am cauteri en aquelas.	But in other compositions, there is no fear for you, and most of all in cold and humid diseases, because already all doctors have agreed on those, and are not discordant in the treatment with cauterization in those.
E sapiatz, filhs, que del secret de curacio per cauteri am foc e de la bontat de lu, so sobre cauteri am medicina comburent, es quar le foc es simple, la accio del qual no perven sino al membre le qual es cauterizat e no notz al autre membre am lu ajustat sino am petit nocument.	And know, children, that from the secret of healing by cauterization with fire and the goodness of it, there is something more about cauterization with medicine combined, because the fire is simple, the action of which does not affect except the member that is being cauterized, and does not harm another member adjusted to it but with a small injury.
Mays la accio de medicina comburent perven ad aquel en les membres le qual de lu alunhat, e fort leu fa venir en le membre malautia de dificil sanacio e fort leu ausit.	But the action of combined medicine reaches that member which is distant from it, and very easily brings disease to a difficult-to-heal member and very easily causes harm.
Mays le foc, per la sua sublimitat e de la sua substancia bontat, no fa aquo sino que superfluisca E ja es a nos conogut per experiment e per longitut de servitut de studi am l’art sobre le veritat de las causas; e per aquo yeu so excusat de la longitut del sermo E si no fos que no es legut al mieu libre en aquest pausero a vos secret amaguat am le foc, e la qualitat de la operacio de lu en les cors e de la sieua expulcio per la qual expellis las malautias, am sermo philosophic demostratiu, le qual siria acuit en las vostras pessas.	But the fire, due to its sublimity and good substance, does not do this except in a superfluous way. And it is already known to us by experiment and the length of service in studying the art above the truth of causes; and therefore I am excused for the length of the sermon. But if it were not that it is not read in your free book in this pause, I would reveal to you a secret hidden with the fire, and the quality of its operation in bodies and its expulsion by which diseases are expelled, with a philosophical and demonstrative sermon, which would be sharpened in your minds.
E sapiatz, filhs, que els se desacordan del temps en le qual es convenient far cauteri e pausan le milhor temps de primaveyra.	And know, children, that they disagree about the time when it is convenient to perform cauterization and pause for the best time of spring.
E yeu dic que cauteri es convenient en tot temps, per so que le nocument per le temps accident es submergit en le juvament de aquo que am le cauteri es atirat, e majorment si le cauteri es per dolors o de dolors necessaries, fortz e fistinas, las quals no suffertan tarditat per so que es temut de aquelas que vengua malicia, que es major que petit nocument entrant per lo temps.	And I say that cauterization is convenient at any time, because the harm caused by the accidental timing is submerged in the joint of what is attracted to the cauterization, and most of all if the cauterization is for pains or necessary pains, strong and fierce, which do not suffer tardiness because it is feared that those who bring evil may come, which is greater than a small harm entering through time.
E aysso no catz en vostras pessas, o, filhs, aquo no estiman sino le poble vulguar e les fols metges, so es que ad aquela malautia que es sanada per cauteri no es redicio tot temps, e pausan aquel consequen.	And thus it does not occur in your minds, or, children, that this is not esteemed except by the common people and foolish doctors, for it is that to that disease which is healed by cauterization there is no reduction at all times, and they pause on the consequence.
E la causa no es ges ayssi quo els cuydan per aquo, quar cauteri no es sino en loc de medicina la qual altera la compleccio e esicca las humiditatz las quals son causa per que veno las dolors.	And the cause is not thus as they say, for cauterization is nothing but a place of medicine that alters the composition and dries up the humors which are the cause why pains come.
Mays empero cauteri superflueys sobre la medicina per volicitat de la sua valitut e vertut de la sua operacio e grandesa del sieu senhor.	But however, cauterization exceeds medicine by the will of its virtue and the grandeur of its lord.
E es possible que la sua malautia retorne en alcuna hora del temps, segon la compleccio del malaute e la locacio de la sua malautia, e la vertut de lu, e aquo que es preparat en le cors de lu de la agreguacio de las superfluitatz en lu, e aquo que es pervengut a lu en la sua acquisicio en viandas e semblantz de aquelas causas; sino que la malautia en la qual sia aministrat cauteri sia malautia subtil en membre de paucas superfluitatz e humiditatz, ayssi cum cauteri de dent per dolor e semblantz ad aquel, possible es que en lu no retorne aquela dolor, mays aquo se fa en petitz.	And it is possible that its disease may return at some hour of time, according to the composition of the patient and the location of its disease, and the virtue of it, and what is prepared in the body of it from the accumulation of superfluities there, and what has been gained through its acquisition in foods and similar causes; but if the disease in which cauterization is administered is a subtle disease in a member with few superfluities and humors, as with cauterization for toothache and similar pains, it is possible that this pain will not return in full, but rather becomes small.
E mays sermo vulgar es que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina, e es sermo dreyturier, no ad aquo que els entendo en lu, quar els crezo que no es curacio que aprofieyta am medicina ni am autra causa aprop cauteri.	And it is also common saying that cauterization is the ultimate remedy of medicine, and it is a saying that is most true, not to what they understand in it, because they believe that there is no healing that is beneficial through medicine or any other cause approaching cauterization.
E la causa es en contrari de aquo; e la entencio que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina no es sino quan administram las manieyras de curacio en alcunas malautias, e aquelas medicinas no conferieysso, e aprop en la fi de la causa aministra hom cauteri, e aprofieyta ad aquela.	And the cause is contrary to that; and I understand that cauterization is the ultimate remedy of medicine not only when we administer the healing methods in some diseases, and those medicines do not concur, and approaching the end of the cause, one administers cauterization, and it proves to be beneficial.
E lahoras de aqui cat16 que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina, no segon la entencio la qual entendo les vulgars e trops dels fols metges.	And from now on, know that cauterization is the ultimate remedy of medicine, not according to the understanding which I understand as common and foolish among doctors.
E diyssero les antics que cauteri am aur es milhor que cauteri am ferr, e no diyssero aquo sino per la equalitat del aur e sublimitat de la sua sustancia.	And the ancients said that cauterization with gold is better than cauterization with iron, and they did not say this except for the equality of gold and its sublime substance.
E diyssero que le loc de cauteri no fa brac, cum aquo no sia absolutament vertat, quar yeu ja he aquo proat e he atrobat que aquel no fa aquo sino en alcus cors ses les autres, e cauteri am aquel es bo e milhor que am ferr ayssi quo els diyssero; mays empero quan tu fas cauteri am foc am de aur, no es a tu declarat, quar es egnit segon la quantitat que tu vols per la rugor de l’aur, e quar prepara a recebre freg; e si ajustas sobre lu ignicio se fon l’aur per le foc, e caso en le foc alcunas laminas per que le artifex catz per la occupacio de aquel.	And they said that the place of cauterization does not make a difference, as it is not absolutely true, because you have already proven and proved that it does not make a difference in some bodies except for others, and cauterization with gold is good and better than with iron as they said; but however when you do cauterization with fire using gold, it is not declared to you, because it is hidden according to the quantity that you want by the roughness of the gold, and since you prepare to receive heat; and if you adjust above it ignition so that the gold melts in the fire, and the craftsman sees through the occupation of that.
E per aquo es fayt cauteri am ferr deves nos pus leugerament e pus propdanament a rectitut de operacio.	And therefore it is necessary to perform cauterization with iron more lightly and more precisely in order to achieve the rightness of operation.
E yeu ja he ordenat aquest capitol en le cauteri segon capitols, et he ordenat aquels del cap entro les pes, per so que aleugo le demandant aquo que vol de lu.	And I have already organized this chapter on cauterization according to chapters, and I have organized those from head to foot, in order that the demanding one may be satisfied with it.
De cauteri de dolor de cap per frigiditat e humiditat.	On Cauterization for Headache due to Coldness and Humidity.
Le capitol primier.	The First Chapter.
Aquesta cauterizacio confereys a la humiditat e frigiditat sobre le servel accident de la qual so doas causas, so es causa de soda e multitut de flux raumatic, apelat corissa, del cap a las partidas dels huelhs e de las aurelhas fluent, e multitut de dormir, e de dolor de dentz e del guolayro, e universalment de tota malautia que ve per fregiditat, ayssi cum paraliticament, sodo e apoplexio, e semblantz en aquelas malautias.	This cauterization is applied to the humidification and coldness on the upper part of the head, which has two causes: one cause being soda and another being a great flow of rheumatic fluid, called corissa, from the head to the parts of the eyes and ears that are fluent, and a great deal of sleepiness, and toothaches, and pain in the jaw, and universally all diseases that come through coldness, such as paralysis, sodomy, apoplexy, and similar things in those diseases.
La forma de aquesta cauterizacio es aquesta, que primieyrament comandes al malaute que sia evacuat am medicina lacsativa le cap mondificant, per tres o per quatre nueytz, segon que exhigeys la vertut del malaute e la edat de lu e la sua costuma.	The form of this cauterization is as follows: first, I command the patient to be evacuated with laxative medicine in the morning, for three or four nights, according to what the disease demands and the age and habit of the patient.
E aprop comanda li que raza le sieu cap am razor, e aprop fay aquel sezer entre las tuas mas sobre una banca cayrada e que pause las suas mas sobre le pietz sieu.	And then I command him to shave his head with a razor, and after that make a section between the hairs on top of his head, and place it on a well-crafted bench, so that he may rest his head on his own feet.
E aprop pausa la razit de la tua palma aprop le pous sobre la razit del nas entre les huels sieus.	And then pause the razor's edge against the tip of your nose, right between the eyes.
Mays empero, cum le tieu dit del mieg loc es pervengut, signa aquel loc am tenta, e aprop igneys le cauteri olivar del qual aquesta es la forma:	But when the fire is reached, mark that place with a tent, and then ignite the cauterization oil of which this is the form:
E aprop pausa aquel sobre le loc senhat am tenta, a manieyra que descent, am la qual la tieua ma sia constrengida petit a petit, e tu revolveys aquel.	And then pause that oil on the marked place with a tent, in such a way that it descends, by which your own hand is gradually constrained, and you turn it.
E aprop leva la tua ma leugerament e reguarda le loc, e si veses ja del os esser descubert alcuna quantitat del cap, ayssi cum la quantitat de gra de errs, lahoras eleva la tua ma, e si no torno la tua ma am aquel ferr, am autre de aquel, si es enfrigidat, entro que sia vist del os aquo que yeu he dit a tu.	And then lift your hand lightly and look at the place, and if you see that some quantity of bone is already uncovered from the head, such as the amount of grain in errors, then raise your hand and if it is not returned to the iron, use another one that is not chilled, until what I have said to you is seen.
E aprop pren un petit de sal e disolveys aquel sobre le loc e leyssa aquel per tres jorns.	And then take a small amount of salt and dissolve it on the place and let it sit for three days.
E aprop pausa sobre lu coto enbegut en boder e leyssa aquel sobre lu entro que sia destrusida la scara del foc.	And then apply to it a poultice of beggar's ticks and let it sit on the wound until the scar of the fire is destroyed.
E aprop cura le loc am anguent tetrafarmacon entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the place with four-fold medicine, so that it may be healed.
E ja diyssero que quant la plagua roman uberta, tant mielhs geta le brac, per que es milhor e mays juvatiu.	And they said that as long as the wound remains open, so much the better it is for the cauterization to be applied, because it is more effective and beneficial.
E diyssero alcus de lor que sia cauterizada la codena entro al os, e sia tengut le cauteri entro que sia adhurida alcuna partida de la specitut del os.	And they said that some of them were cauterized in the cord into the bone, and kept the cauterization until it was absorbed by some part of the specificity of the bone.
E aprop sia ras aquo que es adhust del os, e aprop sia curat.	And then be rubbed with that which is adapted to the bone, and then be cured.
E diyssero autres que am lo cauteri pervengua al derier, entro que enprema en le os forta enprecio entro que le os caga, e aquesta es la forma de alphecati petit:	And others said that with the cauterization, it will reach the end, until it presses strongly on the bone, until the bone cracks, and this is the form of little alfalfa.
E estiman de aquel loc expiran la vapors del cap.	And they say that from that place, the fumes of the head will evaporate.
E sia tenguda la plagua uberta per lonc temps, e aprop sia curada entro que sia consolidada.	And then the open wound should be kept for a long time, and after that it should be cured until it is consolidated.
Mays a mi no so vistas aquestas doas specias de cauteri de tot, sino en alcus homes segon via de temor; e layssa aquel, deves mi, milhor es am salut, quan es; quar le cap es develitat per solucio de continuitat de lu ayssi cum havem testificat en les autres membres, e majorment quan le cap del malaute es de freul natura.	But to me, these two species of cauterization do not seem right at all, except in certain men according to the way of fear; and leave that, I say, is better for health when it is, because the head is revealed by solution of continuity, as we have testified in other members, and even more so when the patient's head is of a free nature.
E la specia de cauteri primieyra es mays salva e milhor deves mi; e de aquela husi e am aquela obra am salut.	And the first species of cauterization is more saved and better, as I say; and from that house and with that work, health ensues.
Capitol segon.	Second Chapter.
Del cauteri del cap.	On the Cauterization of the Head.
Quan en tot le cap accideys dolor cronica e longua e aquo es en le malaute prolonguat, e usa de gerras e de cochias e de capipurges e de emplaustres e de guatz e de cadels e de gualinas e de semblantz, e majorment si ja es cauterizat am un cautere le qual recontam e no aprofieyta a lu deguna de aquelas causas, lahoras considera quar si le cap del malaute es de fort creacio en la sua natura; e no es freul et atroba mot gran freg, lahoras aquel cauterisa am autra cauteri dejos aquel un pauc.	When in the entire head chronic and long-lasting pain occurs, and this is prolonged in the patient, and uses of warps, cochias, capipurges, emplausters, guats, cadels, and gualinas, and similar things, and most especially if it has already been cauterized with one cautery which does not benefit him at all, then consider that whether the head of the patient is of strong creation in his nature; and if it is not free and finds a great deal of coldness, then he cauterizes another cautery, leaving just a little bit.
E aprop cauterisa aquel sobre le corn del sieu cap am cauteri entro que la codena es partida.	And then cauterize that on the horn of his head with another cautery until the cord is parted.
Incisa la codena e sia descuberta del os la quantitat la qual havem recontat e cauteriza aquel am un cauteri en la partida deriera del cap en le loc le qual es apelat vas, — e es aquel loc en le qual es pausada ventosa.	Cut the cord and have it revealed on the bone the quantity which we have recounted, and cauterize that with one cautery in the back part of the head, in the place called "vas", where the wind is paused.
Et alleuja la tua ma en aysso, e no descobras le os, quar le malaute per aquo atroba mot gran dolor diversa de la dolor de totz les autres cauteris del cap.	And let your hand be in that way, and do not uncover the bone, for the patient by this will feel a great deal of diverse pain different from all other head cauteries.
E yeu diyre aquest cauteri en son loc, quar cove que·l cauteri am le qual so cauterisatz les corns del cap e le occiput es pus subtil cauteri que aquel am le qual es cauterisat le mieg loc del cap; e aquesta es la forma de lu.	And you will say that this cautery is in its place, for it is necessary to cauterize the horns of the head and the occiput with a more subtle cautery than that which is used on the middle part of the head; and this is its form.
Capitol ters.	Third Chapter.
De cauterisacio de emigranea no-antiqua.	On Cauterization for Headaches not Caused by Ancient Causes.
Quan endeve en la partida del cap dolor sodo, o es stenduda dolor entro al uelh, sia evacuat am medicinas le cap mondificantz, e sia aministrada l’autra curacio, la qual yeu he dita en las devesios de las malautias; e tot no aprofieyta, lahoras cauterisacio en lu es en dos manieyras: o cauterisacio am medicina acuta comburent, o am ferr.	When headache occurs in the back part of the head, or it is spread into the eye, be evacuated with medicines in the morning, and administer another treatment, which I have said in the divisions of diseases; and if nothing benefits, then cauterization in that place is done in two ways: either by medicine acute and combined, or by iron.
Mays cauteri am medicina comburent es que tu prenguas una dolsa de alh, e escorgas aquela e abcindas las extremitatz de lu de amdos les caps.	But the cauterization by medicine combined is that you take a sweet of aloes, and soak it in water, and abscind the extremities of it from both ends.
E aprop incideys le loc de la dolor en la templa am una lanceta lada entro que sia en lu feyt loc dejos la codena, entro que sia occultada.	And then cut the location of pain in the temple with a blunt lancet until a small pit is made, and it is hidden.
E aprop strenh sobre lu am stopada per descent constreccio, e layssa aquel per le spazi de tres horas; e aprop deslia le e tratz le alh, e laysa la plagua per dos o per tres jorn, e aprop pausa sobre lu coto submergit en boder entro que le loc fassa brac.	And then apply it to the place with a stopper made of descending constriction, and leave it for three hours; and then remove it and treat the aloes, and leave the wound open for two or three days, and then apply a poultice on top submerged in mud until the place becomes firm.
E aprop cura aquel am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with four-fold medicine, so that it may be healed.
E si tu voys, fe aquo am alcunas medicinas comburentz las quals yeu he scriutas en le douse tractat de medicinas comburentz.	And if you wish, do this with some combined medicines that I have written in the two treatises on combined medicines.
Mays la cauterisacio am ferr segon aquesta manieyra: igneys per cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma:	But the cauterization by iron, according to this manner: ignite by the cautery of which this is the form:
e es apelat claus clavilhs, quar le cap de lu es ayssi cum forma de clavel en le qual es alcuna curvitat, e·n le mieg loc de lu es eminensia petita.	and it is called "claw's claw", because the head of it is like a shape of a clove in which there is some curvature, and in the middle part of it is a small elevation.
E aprop pausa sobre loc de la dolor, e rete la tua ma — per que no sia adhurida la arceria la qual es dejos — e revol le ferr petit a petit am velocitat.	And then place the iron on the location of the pain, and hold your hand - so that it is not absorbed by the cord that is left - and turn the small iron gradually with speed.
E si la quantitat de lu que es adhurida per la specitut de la codena ayssi quo la maytat de lu, e elava la tua ma per so que la arteria no sia adhurida la qual es dejos, per so que no vengua flux de sanc.	And if the quantity of it that is absorbed by the specificity of the cord is as great as the majority of it, and lift your hand so that the artery which is left is not absorbed, lest there come a flow of blood.
E aprop enbibeys coto en aygua de sal e pausa aquel sobre le loc, e layssa aquel per tres dias; e aprop pausa coto mulhat am boder, e aprop cura am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then soak the poultice in saltwater and place it on the location, and leave it for three days; and then apply a mullet poultice wrapped in mud, and then cure with four-fold medicine until it is healed.
E si voys, cauterisa am la extremitat del cutellari segon cauteri, e guarda te de incisio de arteria en aquesta emigranea propriament no-antiqua.	And if you wish, cauterize the extremity of the cutlery according to the cautery, and beware of cutting off an artery in this not ancient headache properly.
Capitol quart.	Fourth Chapter.
De cauterizacio d’emigranea antiqua.	On Cauterization for Ancient Headaches.
Quan tu curas emigranea am aquo que havem dit de la curacio precedent, e aquo que havem dit en las divisios de las malautias, e no aprofieyta la curacio, e vezes per la malautia que no abasta a lu aquo que havem dit del primier cauteri am medicina o del cauteri am foc, lahoras cove que tu igniscas le cauteri cutellar entro que sia albificat, pus que significas sobre le loc de la dolor am linha de longuesa de la qual sia la maytat del dit, o quays aquel; e depausa la tua ma per una veguada e strenh aquela entro incidiscas la arceria e pervengua entro al os.	When you treat headaches with what we have said in the previous treatment and in the divisions of diseases, and if the treatment does not benefit, and sometimes the disease is so severe that it does not reach the point where we have described the first cautery by medicine or by fire, then it is necessary to ignite the cutlery cautery until it is white, because you signify on the location of pain with a line of length which is most of the digit or what it may be; and place your hand for one moment and strengthen that until you cut off the artery and reach the bone.
Empero necessari es a tu que guardes de la continuacio de la mandibula, la qual es mauguda deves la masticacio, e que le lacert no sia adhurit e le nervi le qual mau aquela, e que no s’endevengua espasme.	However, it is necessary for you to beware of the continuity of the jawbone, which is modified by mastication, and that the lacrimal duct not be absorbed and the nerves that accompany that, and that no spasm ensues.
E si es sobre la custodia e cautela de flux de sanc de l’arteria que es abciza, quar en la abcizio de lu es temor, e majorment ad aquel le qual ignora aquo que fa e no es studios e esproat; e layssa la operacio en lu al comensament.	And if it is about the custody and caution of the flow of blood from the artery that is cut off, for in the cutting off of it there is fear, and especially to him who ignores this process and does not study or practice; and leave the operation at the beginning.
E yeu vindre am rememoracio del regiment de flux de sanc accident de la arceria segon la sieua manieyra, en le sieu loc de aquest libre.	And you will come to remember the regimen of accidental bleeding from the artery according to your own manner in this very book.
E si veses de aquesta malautia que no abaste aquest cauteri e veses le cors del malaute tollerable, cauteriza aquel en le mieg loc del cap ayssi cum havem recontat, e cura la plagua entro que sia sanada.	And if you see that this disease does not yield to this cautery and you see the patient's body is tolerable, then cauterize it in the middle part of the head as we have recounted, and cure the wound until it is healed.
E si voys, aministra le cauteri le qual havem dit en le capitol de streccio de arceria am cauteri havent dos cotels, e es milhor cauterizacio aquesta e mays conferent.	And if you wish, administer the cautery which we have said in the chapter on stretching of artery with two handles, and this is the better cautery and most concurrent.
Capitol .v.	Fifth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de las dolors de aurelhas.	On Cauterization for Earaches.
Quan en la aurelha ve dolor per freg e es curat am causas lacsativas e am l’autra curacio la qual he dita en la divisio, e no es remauguda la dolor, lahoras igneys le cauteri, e es aquest le qual ha nom puncta, del qual aquesta es la forma:	When in the ear there is pain caused by cold and it is treated with laxative causes and with other treatment which I have said in the division, and the pain is not relieved, then ignite the cautery, and this is the one called "puncta", of which this is the form:
E aprop puncta aprop la ignicio, e sia menat al enviro de tota la aurelha ayssi cum roda es revolguda, o en le circuit de quascuna essemps si la dolor es en quascuna.	And then apply the puncta to the ignition, and be brought around the entire ear as a wheel is revolved, or in the circuit of each example if the pain is in each.
Alonga te am le cauteri de la razit de la aurelha pauc a pauc pus que aias senhat le loc am tenta.	And then stretch yourself with the cautery of the root of the ear little by little until you have marked the location with a tent.
E si le cauteri de detz puntz en tota aurelha, e quays aquela, e aprop cura les locz entro que sian sanatz.	And if the cautery of these dots is applied to the entire ear, and in each place, and then cure the locations until they are healed.
Capitol .vi.	Sixth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de turtura.	On Cauterization for Torture.
Turtura la qual es curada e am cauterizacio no es sino de las specias las quals veno per flecma, segon que havem dit en las divisios de las malautias.	Torture which is cured and by cauterization it is not but of the species which come from flux, according to what we have said in the divisions of diseases.
Esquiva cauterizacio de la specia que endeve per siccacio o per spasme del nervi.	Avoid cauterization of the species that comes from dryness or spasm of the nerve.
Quan tu curas aquela specia de turtura am jerras e capipurgi e guarguarismes, e no comfereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que tu cauterizas le malaute am tres cauteris: la i deves la razit de la aurelha, e·l segon un petit dejos le sieu templar, e le ters deves la conjunccio de doas labias.	When you cure that species of torture with jarrings and capipurgisms and guarguarisms, and your treatment does not confirm, then it is necessary to cauterize the patient with three cauteries: the first on the root of the ear, the second a little below the temple, and the third at the conjunction of two lips.
E pausa lo tieu cauteri per le contrari de la partida malauta, quar mollificacio no ve sino en la partida que apar sana.	And then pause your cautery on the contrary side of the ailing part, for softening does not come but on the opposite side that appears to be healing.
E la forma de cauterisacio es que cauterizas aquel am le cauteri en le dreyt de la extremitat de la aurelha pus sobirana un petit sobre le corn del cap, e en le templar autre, la longuesa del qual sia segon la longitut del dit pous, e depausa la tua ma am cauteri entro que sia comburida la quantitat de la maytat de la specitut de la codena.	And the form of cauterization is that you cauterize it with the cautery on the right side of the extremity of the ear, slightly above the horn of the head, and in the temple another one, the length of which is according to the length of the thumb's joint, and then place your hand with the cautery until the quantity of the majority of the cord's specific part is consumed.
E aquesta es la forma del cauteri, e es specia del cutellari, la forma del qual es denant mesa.	And this is the form of the cautery, and it is a species of the cutlery, the form of which is placed before us.
Mays empero pus subtil es que aquel un pauc ayssi co vesas; e cove que cotel en lu de superflua groceza un pauc.	But however subtle it may be, that a little bit is as you see it; and it is necessary to cut off the superfluous thickening a little.
E aprop cura le loc am aquo que es denant procezit entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the location with what is before us, until it is healed.
Capitol .vii.	Seventh Chapter.
De cauterizacio de apoplextia antiqua.	On Cauterization for Ancient Apoplexy.
Quan apoplextia es antiquada e curas aquela am aquo que havem dit e no confereys la tua medicacio e le malaute no ha febre, lahoras cauteriza aquel am quatre cauteris: sobre totz les corn del sieu cap; e am cauteri e le mieg loc del cap, ayssi cum havem dit; e am cauteri en le coguot.	When apoplexy is ancient and you cure it with what we have said, and your treatment does not confirm, and the patient has no fever, then cauterize that with four cauteries: on all the horns of his head; and with a cautery in the middle part of the head, as we have said; and with another one in the occiput.
E la manieyra del cauteri es fayta segon que es desus dit.	And the manner of the cautery is made according to what was previously said.
E ja es cauterizat sobre la boca del estomac; e es mays derier; e aprop sia curat am aquo que procezeys.	And it is cauterized on the mouth of the stomach; and this is the last one; and then it should be cured with what proceeds.
Capitol .viii.	Eighth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de obblivio fayta per flacma.	On Cauterization for Oblivion caused by Flux.
Cove que sian donatz al malaute en le comensament jerras grans e pilulas le servel mondificantz.	It is necessary to give the patient in the beginning large jarrings and pills of purging medicines.
E aprop ras le cap tot del malaute e pausa sus le coguot de lu emplaustre de cetre descrit en le tractat dels emplastres.	And then shave the head of the patient and apply an ointment to the occiput, as described in the treatise on ointments.
E pausa aquel alcunas veguadas, quar aquel es manieyra de cauteri.	And pause it for a few days, because this is the manner of the cautery.
E fay aquo segon aquel meteys orde le qual ja he dit.	And do so according to that order which I have already said.
E donc si per aqueles sanat bo es; e sino, lahoras fay a lu tres cauteris en la deriera partida de sieu cap, les quals sian deysendentz de la partida pus sobirana del cap entro a la partida pus dejos del col.	And thus, if it is well healed by those means; and otherwise, then do so to the three cauteries in the back part of his head, which are descendants from the upper part of the head down to the lower part of the neck.
E pausa entre quascun cauteri la grossetut del dit, e aprop cura lo cauteri am aquo que es procedit.	And pause between each cautery the thickness of the finger, and then cure the cautery with what has proceeded.
Mays si tu vos addicio e le malaute es aquo tollerant, lahoras fay a lu cauteri en le mieg loc; e si voys major addicio, lahora cauteriza aquel sobre les dos corns.	But if you wish to add more and the patient is tolerating it well, then do so to the middle part; and if you wish for even greater addition, then immediately cauterize that on both horns.
Aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat; e sia le cauteri olivar segon la forma denant donat.	And then cure that until it is healed; and be the cautery olive-colored according to the form previously given.
Capitol .ix.	Ninth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de parazili e de mollificacio de tot le cors.	On Cauterization for Paralysis and Softening of the Entire Body.
Cove que tu procesiscas en mondificacio del cap am jerras e am aquo que havem dit; e aprop ras le cap del malaute, e aprop cauteriza aquel am cauteri en le mieg loc del cap, e am cauteri sobre totz les corns del cap, e am cauteri sobre la deriera partida de lu, e am tres cauteris sobre les spondils del col.	Take care to process the head with jarrings and with what we have said; and then shave the head of the patient, and then cauterize that with a cautery in the middle part of the head, and with another one on all the horns of the head, and with another one on the back part of it, and with three cauteries on the vertebrae of the neck.
E si es necessari en la malautia de mollificacio del cors de trops aquel e les malautes tollerantz e la malautia es fort, lahoras cauteriza aquel am quatre cauteris sobre les spondils del dos, e dererament am cauteri entro que sia comborit de la codena mot de lu, e aleva la tieua ma.	And if it is necessary in the disease of softening of the body of many and the patients are tolerating well, but the disease is strong, then cauterize that with four cauteries on the vertebrae of the back, and gradually with one cautery until the cord's movement of life is consumed, and lift up your hand.
E aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat, e aquest sia cauteri olivar.	And then cure that until it is healed, and this be olive-colored cauterization.
Capitol .x.	Tenth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de epilemcia.	On Cauterization for Epilepsy.
No es cauterizat le epilemtic sino aquella epilemcia es per flecma.	No is cauterized the epileptic, but that epilepsy is caused by flux.
E donc cove que mondifiques le cervel de lu al comensament de lu am yeras e am l’autra curacio la qual havem dicta en la divisio quan le malaute es gran e es tollerant la exceperacio de las medicinas.	And thus, it is necessary to purge the brain of him at the beginning with jarrings and with other treatment which we have said in the division when the patient is great and is tolerant except for the exemption of medicines.
E si es enfant le qual no sufferte las medicinas, lahoras aministra guarguarissmes e mastiguatoris le servel mondifican, denant aquo per motz dias, am bonifficacio de las viandas.	And if the child who cannot tolerate medicines, then administer guarguarisms and mastiguoars as purgatives, before this for several days, with good food.
E aprop ras le cap del malaute, e aprop cauteriza aquel am un cauteri en le mieg loc del cap segon la manieyra precedent, e am autre cauteri en le occiput de lu, e sobre quascun corn del cap sieu cauterisa.	And then shave the head of the patient, and then cauterize that with one cautery in the middle part of the head according to the previous manner, and another one on the occiput, and each horn of the head is cauterized.
E si le malaute es fort e es tollerant, lahoras cauteriza aquel am cauteris les quals he ditz, en havent paraliticament e mollificacio del cors sobre les spondils del col e les spondils del dos.	And if the patient is strong and tolerant, then cauterize that with the cauteries which I say, having paralysis and softening of the body on the vertebrae of the neck and the back.
E sia cauteri olivar segon qu’es precedit.	And be olive-colored according to what has been previously said.
Mays si le malaute es enfant, lahoras pausa cauteri subtil segon aquesta manieyra.	But if the patient is a child, then pause on a subtle cautery according to this manner.
Capitol .xi.	Eleventh Chapter.
De cauterizacio de melencolia.	On Cauterization for Melancholy.
Quan las causas de melencolia so humiditatz corrompudas e flacma gros, lahoras cauteriza aquel am les cauteris les quals havem ditz en le havent paralisi.	When the causes of melancholy are corrupted and flux is gross, then cauterize that with the cauteries which we have said in having paralysis.
E si la causa de melencolia es superfluitat declinant a melencolia, e le cors del malaute es humit, lahoras da ha beure aquo que mundifica le cervel de lu segon aquo que ha precedut en la divisio.	And if the cause of melancholy is superfluity that declines into melancholy, and the body of the patient is humid, then give him to drink water that purifies the brain of it according to what has preceded in the division.
E aprop ras le cap del malaute, e aprop fay tortora decentment fayta de li sobre le cercle, e aprop depausa aquela en le mieg loc del cap.	And then shave the head of the patient, and then make a tortoise shell decently made of it over the circle, and then place that in the middle part of the head.
E le malaute sia sesent cayrat, e sia tengut de tota partida.	And the patient should be seated comfortably, and held by all parties.
E aprop pausa liniment; et es pus digne de boder antic de ovelhas.	And then apply a poultice; and it is more worthy of an ancient border of sheep's wool.
E escalfa aquel sobre le foc per calefaccio temprada per mesura, le qual le dit sufferta quan es mes en lu.	And warm that over the fire with a tempered heat by measure, which said enough when it is more in it.
E aprop vuo’ aquel en le mieg loc del cap de lu en le cercle, e leysa lu entro que sia enfregidat.	And then put that in the middle part of the head of him in the circle, and let it be there until it is cooled.
E fay aquo am le malaute en tota semmana una veguada, am le autre regiment de lu bo entro que sia sanat; o si vols, cauteriza aquel fazen petitz puntz segon lo mays de lu, sino que tenguas la ma am un cauteri ayssi ordenat: aquesta es specia de cauteri la qual humecta le cervel am equalitat.	And do this with the patient for a whole week once, with another regimen of it good until it is healed; or if you wish, cauterize that by making small points according to what is most of it, so that you hold your hand with a cautery thus ordered: this is a species of cauterization which moistens the brain with equality.
E aprop pausa aquel coto enbegut en boder o en grays de gualina.	And then put that in a cloth or in gray gauze, wrapped around it.
Capitol .xii.	Twelfth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de aygua descendent en le huel.	On Cauterization for Water that Descends into the Headache.
Quan a tu es declarat le comensament de aygua en le huel per les senhals les quals yeu he ditz en la divisio, lahoras comensa e dona en beure al malaute aquo que mondifique le cap de lu, e guarda aquel de totas humiditatz.	When you are declared the beginning of water in the head for the signs which I have said in the division, then begin and give to drink to the patient water that purifies the head of it, and guard against all humidity.
E fay aquel suzar en banh en degu per alcus jorns.	And make that sweat in a bath for several days.
E aprop comanda a lu que raza le sieu cap, e cauteriza aquel am cauteri en le mieg loc del cap; e aprop cauteriza aquel am dos cauteris sobre dos templas si es le comensament de ysement de aygua en dos huels, o de la un latz si es comensamen de l’aygua en un huel.	And then command him to shave his head, and cauterize that with a cautery in the middle part of the head; and then cauterize that with two cauteries on both temples if it is the beginning of water in two heads, or of one side if it is the beginning of water in one head.
Incideys am cauteri totas las venas e arcerias las quals so dejos la codena; e sian les cauteris en aquela lonh en la latitut de las templas.	And then cut all the veins and arteries that are left by the cord; and let the cauteries be in that length in the latitude of the temples.
E guarda te de fluxs de sanc quan es cauterizat; e si veses de lu fluxs de sanc, osta le am alcuna medicina, la qual es a tu possible.	And guard yourself from fluxes of blood when it is being cauterized; and if you see any bleeding from him, stop it with some medicine which is at your disposal.
E yeu vindre am savieza la qual es en extraccio de arcerias e am abscizio de aquelas e cautela de fluxs de sanc.	And you will find wisdom in the extraction of arteries and in the absorption of those and caution against bleeding.
E alcunas vetz es cauterizat en le cervitz dejos dos osses am dos cauteris dererament produzitz.	And some times it is cauterized on the cervical vertebrae left between two bones with two cauteries gradually produced.
Capitol .xiii.	Thirteenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de lacrimas antiquas.	On Cauterization for Old Tears.
Quan lacrimas dels huels so antiquas assuduament e per las venas e arterias las quals so en le loc manifest del cap defora e es verificat que aquo es superfluitatz frejas flecmatiquas, lahoras cauteriza aquel am cauteri le qual havem recontat en le capitol de comensament de aygua cazent en les huels, e am cauteri en le mieg loc del cap e am dos cauteris en la cervitz dejos dos templas, e am dos cauteris en la cervitz dejos dos osses.	When tears of the head are ancient and hardened through the veins and arteries which are in the manifest place on the outside of the head, and it is verified that this is superfluous watery flux, then cauterize that with the cautery which we have recounted in the chapter of the beginning of water descending into the head, and with a cautery in the middle part of the head and two cauteries in the cervical vertebrae left between two temples, and with two cauteries in the cervical vertebrae left between two bones.
E si indigeyses de addicio, lahoras cauteriza aquel en tot latz de la coa del huel sobre la extremitat del sobrecilh am petit cauteri.	And if you need addition, then cauterize that on the entire back of the head above the forehead with a small cautery.
Capitol .xiiii.	Fourteenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de fetor de nas.	On Cauterization for Stench of Nose.
Quan tu medicas aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no aprofieyta la tua medicacio, lahoras tu aparelha e dona en beure al malaute las cochias per tres noytz; e aprop ras le cap de lu, e cauteriza le am cauteri migier am cauteri olivar.	When you treat that with water which we have said in the division and it does not improve your treatment, then prepare and give to drink to the patient the cohies for three nights; and then shave the head of him, and cauterize it with a white cautery and an olive-colored cautery.
E aprop cauteriza aquel am cauteri clavelh am dos cauteris sobre les dos sobrecilhs dejos les cabels un petit.	And then cauterize that with a clove-shaped cautery and two cauteries on both forehead areas, just above the hairline.
E guarda te de la arceria que no incindas aquela.	And guard yourself from cutting into the artery, lest you hurt it.
E del cauteri clavilh aquesta es la forma.	And of the clove-shaped cautery, this is the form.
Capitol .xv.	Fifteenth Chapter.
De cauteri de mollificacio de palpebras dels huels.	On Cauterization for Softening of Eyelids of the Head.
Quan la palpebra del huel es mollificada per malautia o per humiditat, lahoras cauteriza aquela palpebre1 am un cauteri am aquest cauteri lunar; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	When the eyelid of the head is softened by disease or humidity, then cauterize that eyelid with a cautery having this lunary shape; and this is the form of it:
E si vos, cauteriza aquel sobre les dos sobrecils un petit am dos cauteris en tota partida, e sian elonguatz de las timporas.	And if you wish, cauterize that on both forehead areas a little with two cauteries in all parts, and let them be extended from the temples.
E sia la longitut de quascun cauteri segon la quantitat del sobrecil.	And let the length of each cautery be according to the quantity of the forehead.
E no premas trop la tua ma am le cauteri, mays segon la quantitat que la tersa partida de la palpebre sia adhurida.	And do not press too hard with your hand and the cautery, but according to the quantity that the third part of the eyelid is habituated.
Capitol .xvi.	Sixteenth Chapter.
De cauteri de la palpebre del huel quan les pels so convertitz a las partidas dedintz e punho le huel.	On Cauterization of the Eyelid of the Head when the skin is transformed into inner parts and pushes the head.
Quan les pels del huel son convertitz a las partidas dedintz ayssi que pungo le huel, cauteri en aquels es segon dos manieyras, quar cauteri o es am fer o es am medicina comburent.	When the skin of the head is transformed into inner parts just as it pushes the head, then cauterize those in two manners, either by fire or by a medicine that combines.
Si am cauteri de lu am foc, comanda al malaute denant aquo que leyse les sieus pels ayssi cum aquels les quals les mundan, entro que sian prolonguatz e engualhatz; e si punho aquel deves le lor naysement, lahoras tu strenh les huels de lu am una benda per so que no sia maugut entro que·ls pels sian nascutz.	If by a cautery of fire, command the patient beforehand to wash his skin thus as those who cleanse it, until they are prolonged and equalized; and if you push that which makes them swell, then take away their swelling, you strengthen the head of him with a bandage so that it is not hurt until the skin is born.
Donc cum siran nascutz e engualhatz, lahoras pausa le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop senha sobre la palpebre dels huels de lu am tenta, am senhal le qual sia segon la figura de fulha de merta, e sia le comensament del senhal prop dels pels.	Then when they are born and equalized, then pause the patient's head in your sight, and then sign on the eyelid of his head with a tenta, with a signal which is according to the figure of a mertal leaf, and let it be the beginning of the signal just above the skin.
E aprop pausa coto enbegut en album de huou o en mucillatge de ptilli sobre le huel.	And then put a cloth wrapped in alum or in mucilage of pellitory on the head.
E aprop igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma de lu.	And then ignite the cautery which is this shape of it.
E aprop cauteriza sobre la figura la qual as senhada, petit a petit, em motas veguadas, entro que sia comburida la superficia de la codena la qual es ayssi cum fuelha de mirta, tota aparent propriament.	And then cauterize on the figure which you have signaled, little by little, in many times, until the surface of the cord is burned just like a leaf of myrtle, all appearing properly.
E senhal de sanetat de la tieua obra es que tu vegus la palpebre de l’huel ja esser contrayta e·ls pels de lu esser elevatz deves la punctura del huel.	And the sign of health from this work is that you see the eyelid of the head already contracted and the skin of it elevated above the point of the head.
E donc eleva la tua ma e laysa aquel per tres jorns, e aprop pausa sobre lu coto am boder entro que sia eredicada la scara.	And then elevate your hand and let it be for three days, and then pause on the cloth with a border until the scar is eradicated.
E aprop cura aquela am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with an ointment until it is healed.
Mays si retorna per les pels alcuna causa aprop lor naysement e la palpebra es mollificada, lahoras fay autra vetz le cauteri sobre aquel tot ayssi cum avias fayt primieyrament.	But if some cause returns to the skin and causes swelling again, and the eyelid is softened, then do it again as you did first time.
Mays si les pels so en la palpebra dejos, lahoras cauterisa aquela entro que sia elevada al sieu loc natural e sia engualhat e que les pels no punhan le huelh.	But if the skin is in the eyelid left behind, then cauterize that until it is elevated to its natural place and equalized, so that the skin does not push against the head.
Mays le cauteri am medicina comburent aquest es que comandes al malaute que leyse les pels entro que sian prolonguatz e engualhatz, e aprop sia fayta de carta de drap la forma de fuelha de mirtra.	But the cautery with a medicine that combines is what you command the patient to wash his skin until it is prolonged and equalized, and then make a cloth of paper in the shape of a leaf of myrtle.
E aprop pren de sabo conogut e de caus viva ana unc. .i., o quays aquo, e aprop mescle3 aquelas causas be, e fay aquo am festinacio per so que no sia enfregidat; e aprop expandeys de aquo sobre la carta la qual es fayta ayssi cum forma de fulha de mirtra, e pausa aquel sobre la un huel od amdos; e pausa dejos le huel coto enbegut en album de huou, e el cap del malaute sia en le tieu se.	And then take one ounce of known salt and one ounce of living cause. The end! And thus it is, and then mix those causes well, and make this with a feast in order that it may not be cooled; and then spread water on the paper which is made in the shape of a leaf of myrtle, and pause that over one head or both heads; and pause behind the head cloth wrapped in alum, and the patient's head be in your sight.
E pausa le dit sobre le medicina e prem aquela un petit e no la mauguas entro que lo malaute senta la mordicacio de la medicina, quar mordicacio es en lu ayssi cum de foc.	And then pause the said thing on the medicine and press it a little bit, but do not hurt it until the patient feels the stinging of the medicine, because stinging is in it just like from fire.
E donc cum percevera aquo que el atrobo mordicacio, lahoras leyssa la medicina e mau aquela am le tieu dit; donc cum cessa la mordicacio, lahoras remau la medicina he lava le huel am aygua; e lahoras considera si vezes la palpebra ja es levada ayssi cum es lavada deves la costriccio am foc o am incisio, quar lahoras esta be; e si no torna sobre aquela de la medicina sobre le loc en le qual no ha empremut la medicina e no se denigra entro que sia engualhada la tua operacio e sia contrayt le huel.	And thus when the patient perceives that it is getting stinging, then pause the medicine and stop hurting it with your said thing; therefore when the stinging ceases, then wash away the medicine and rinse the head with water; and then consider if the eyelid has already been lifted as washed by fire or incision, because you are satisfied; and if not, then go back to applying the medicine on the location where it has not yet taken effect and do not neglect until your operation is equalized and the head is contracted.
E aprop pausa sobre lu coto am boder entro que sia eradicada la codena de la adhustio, e aprop cura aquel am enguent deafinicon o am autre entro que sia sanat.	And then pause on the cloth with a border until the scar of adjustment is eradicated, and then cure that with an ointment or another substance until it is healed.
E es necessari a tu, deves la tua operacio que guardes am pervigil diligencia que en le huel no caia re de la medicina, e si la palpebre aprop alscus dias es mollificada e alcuna causa dels pels punh en le huel, lahoras itera la tua medicina sobre aquel loc le qual de la palpebre es mollificat, e propriamen ayssi quo as fayt al comensament, e aprop enaviro lu entro que sia sanat.	And it is necessary for you to keep with diligent vigilance that the medicine does not fall on the head, and if the eyelid some days later becomes softened and some cause of skin pushes into the head, then iterate your medicine on that location where the eyelid has become softened, and just as you did at the beginning, and then apply it again until it is healed.
E aquesta es la forma de fuelha de mirtra.	And this is the shape of a leaf of myrtle.
E sapias que les huels dels homes son diversificatz segon la magnitut e la parvitat, e donc segon aquo es fayta la tua contraccio.	And know that the heads of men are diversified according to magnitude and smallness, and therefore according to this is made your contraction.
E no sira amaguada la via de rectetut ad aquel al qual es studi en aquesta art.	And may not be hidden the way of rectitude from him who studies in this art.
Capitol .xvii.	Seventeenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de fistula que es en le lacrimal de l’huel.	On Cauterization of Fistula that is in the Lachrymal of the Head.
Quan tu curas fistula am aquo que havem dit en las divisios de las malautias e no confereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que tu cauterizas aquela segon aquesta manieyra: comanda al malaute que pause le cap sieu en le tieu se, e tengua le cap de lu alcun ministre entre las tieuas mas en tal manieyra que no sia maugut ni agitat am le sieu cap.	When you cure a fistula with the water that we have said in the divisions of diseases and do not confirm your cure, then be it so that you cauterize that according to this manner: command the patient to pause his head in your sight, and hold his head by some minister between your hands in such a way that it is not hurt nor agitated with his own head.
E aprop pausa coto enfus en album de huou o en mucellage de ptilli sobre le huel de lu.	And then put a cloth wrapped in alum or in mucilage of pellitory on the head of him.
E aprop igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma:	And then ignite the cautery which is this shape:
le qual sia conquau, ayssi cum es forma de cana o de pena de voltor, de la una extremitat am la qual es fayta lo cauteri.	the one that is curved, like the form of a reed or a pen nib of a writer, from one extremity to which the cautery is made.
E si voys, sia penetrant entro a la autra extremitat.	And if you wish, be penetrating into the other extremity.
E si vols sia sort ayssi cum tenta.	And if you want, let it be like a test.
Mays empero aquel que es concau es milhor a la tieua obra.	But in any case, the one that is curved is better for your work.
E aprop prem la fistula si es uberta, e tra de lu sania et exsicca aquela.	And then press the fistula if it is open, and draw out the pus and dry it out.
E si no es uberta, lahoras obre aquela e extratz la poyredura de lu.	And if it is not open, then work on it and extract the congealed matter from it.
E aprop pausa sobre lu le cauteri le qual sia be ignit, e te am aquel la tieua ma un petit deves le cauteri del huel a la partida del nas, per so que no erre la tua ma o le malaute sia enquietat, e lahoras pausa le cauteri en le grays del huel e corrompas aquel.	And then pause on it the cautery which is well ignited, and apply that to your hand a little bit at the point of the head where the nose begins, so that you do not err with your hand or disturb the patient, and then pause the cautery on the gray hairs of the head and corrupt that.
E donc si al comensament del tieu cauteri perve entro al os, bo es; e sino, lahoras itera le cauteri una veguada o dos, si mestiers era; e layssa aquel ayssi per tres jorns, e aprop pausa sobre aquel coto am boder e enviro lu am enguent exsiccatiu entro que sia sanat.	And thus if at the beginning of your cautery it penetrates into the bone, it is well; and otherwise, then iterate the cautery one or two times, as needed; and leave that as is for three days, and then pause on that cloth with a border and surround it with a drying ointment until it is healed.
Mays si eran passatz xi dias e no es sanat, lahoras pausa sobre lu medicina aguda corrosiva entro que l’os sia descubert e sia ras segon que conveneys en le sieu capitol.	But if it is passed 11 days and it is not healed, then pause on the sharp corrosive medicine until the bone is uncovered and is scraped according to what is necessary in your own capital.
E es autra manieyra de cauteri de fistula la qual alscus primiers diysero: enten al loc de la fistula e fen aquela e aprop pausa en aquela fissura camaen subtil del qual es la forma de lu: E fon en aquela la quantitat de i unc de plom fundut; e te la tua ma am camaem am bona retencio, e no sia maugut le malaute per so que le plom fundut no pervengua al huel de aquel; e cove que pausas sobre le huel del malaute coto enfus en album de huou o en aygua, quar plom adhureys le loc de la fistula e sana aquela per sanacio meravilhora.	And there is another method of cauterization for a fistula which some of the first ones said: take the location of the fistula and fill it with that and pause in that fissure, just as subtle as its shape is. Pour into that the quantity of one ounce of melted lead; and apply your hand with care with good retention, so that the patient is not hurt by the melted lead not reaching the head of him; and take care to pause on the head of the patient with a cloth wrapped in alum or water, because the lead adheres to the location of the fistula and heals it through marvelous healing.
E si la fistula es sanada am aquo que havem dit del cauteri e de la curacio, bo es; e sino, lahoras es necessari aministrar trauc del nas e reduzir la fistula al cors del nas segon que vindra en son loc propri.	And if the fistula is healed with what we have said about cauterization and healing, it is well; and otherwise, then it is necessary to administer a thrust of the nose and reduce the fistula to the body of the nose according to its proper location.
Capitol .xviii.	Eighteenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la fendedura des potz.	On Cauterization of the Wound of the Lips.
Motas veguadas accideysso fissuras en las labias, e majorment en las labias dels enfantz.	Many times these fissures occur on the lips, and mostly on the lips of children.
Donc cum tu curas aquelas fissuras am aquo que nos havem dit en las divisios e no aprofieyta la tua cura, lahoras igneys le cauteri petit cutellar segon aquesta forma que s’ensiec:	Therefore, when you cure these fissures with the water that we have said in the divisions and it does not improve your cure, then ignite the small cutting cautery according to this shape which is seen:
E sia la conquavitat de lu segon la subtilitat de cotella.	And be the curvature of it according to the subtlety of a knife.
Aprop pausa aquel init cuytadament en aquelas fissuras entro que·l cauteri pervengua al preon de las fissuras.	And then pause that initial cut cautiously in those fissures until the cautery reaches the bottom of the fissures.
E aprop cura aquel am cerotz entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with cerotes until it is healed.
Capitol .xix.	Nineteenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de fistula en la boca.	On Cauterization of Fistula in the Mouth.
Quan en la razit de uvula o en le paladar o en las razitz de las dentz endeve apostema e aprop fa brac, e aprop es rompuda, e aprop es antiquada, e corr brac e es fayta fistula, e aprop tu curas aquela e no aprofieyta a curacio, lahoras cove que tu igniscas cauteri segon la quantitat que sia receubuda en la fistula, e aprop met aquel ignit en le trauc de la fistola, e te la tua ma entro que pervengua le ferr ignit al preon de lu, e al derier de lu fazen aysso una veguada o dos; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que nos havem dit de la curacio entro que sia sanat.	When an abscess develops in the uvula or palate or in the roots of the teeth and bursts, and then becomes old and forms a fistula, and you cure that but it doesn't improve, then it is necessary to ignite the cautery according to the quantity received by the fistula, and apply that ignited thing into the track of the fistula, and take your hand so that the hot iron reaches the bottom of it, and at the end do it once or twice; and then cure that with the water that we have said about healing until it is healed.
E donc si la sania es abscindita e es sanat, bo es; e sino, lahoras es necessari de descubrir le loc e hostar le os corrumput segon que vindra en son capitol.	And thus if the pus is discharged and is healed, it is well; and otherwise, then it is necessary to uncover the location and expose the corrupted bone according to what is written in its capital.
Capitol .xx.	Twentieth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de las dentz e de mollificacio de las angivas.	On Cauterization of Teeth and Softening of Gums.
Quan las angivas son mollificadas per humiditat e las dentz son maugudas, e curas aquelas am medicinas e no confereys, lahoras pausa le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop igneys le cauteri la forma del qual vindra aprop aysso, enayssi que tu pauses la quanula sobre la dent e entromet en aquela le cauteri ignit festinantment, e te la tieua ma un petit entro que·l malaute cente la calor del foc a la razit de la dent esser pervenguda.	When the gums are softened by moisture and the teeth are decayed, and you cure those with medicines but do not confirm it, then pause the patient's head in your sight, and then ignite the cautery in the shape which will be shown to you, so that you pause the quill on the tooth and insert the hot cautery into it hastefully, and take your hand a little bit until the patient feels the heat of the fire at the root of the tooth being reached.
E aprop leva la tua ma, e aprop itera le cauteri alcunas veguadas segon que vols.	And then lift your hand, and then iterate the cautery several times as you wish.
E aprop le malaute huompla la sua boca de aygua de sal e tengua aquela per una hora, e pueys stupa aquela, quar la dent mauguda es fermada e la gengiva mollificada es strenguda e la humiditat corrompuda es exsiccada.	And then have the patient open his mouth with salt water and keep it for an hour, and then stop it, because the decayed tooth is sealed and the softened gum is strengthened and the corrupted moisture is dried out.
Capitol .xxi.	Twenty-First Chapter.
De cauterisacio de dolor de dent.	On Cauterization of Toothache.
Quan dolor de dent es per fregiditat, o en lu es freg o verm, o no comfereys la curacio am medicina, lahoras cauteri en aquela es segon dos manieyras: o cauteri am boder de vacas, o cauteri am foc.	When toothache is caused by coldness, or if there is a worm or frost in it, or if the cure with medicine does not confirm, then use two methods of cauterization: either with the border of cows, or with fire.
Cauteri am boder es que tu prenguas boder de vacas e bulhas aquel en culhe de ferr , e aprop pren coto e envolopa le sobre la extremitat de la tenta, e aprop enmergeys aquel am boder bulhit, e pausa aquel sobre la dent dolorosa festinantment entro que sia enfregidat.	Cauteri am boder is when you take the border of cows and boil it in copper, and then take a cloth and wrap it around the extremity of the tent, and then immerse that in boiling border, and pause that on the painful tooth hastefully until it is cooled down.
E aprop itera aquela alcunas veguadas entro que la vertut del foc pervengua a la razit de la dentz.	And then iterate that several times until the virtue of fire reaches the root of the teeth.
E si voys, submergeys lana o coto en le boder desus dit, e pausa aquel sobre la dent dolent, e pausa sobre aquel ferr ignit entro que·l ferr pervengua al preon de la conquavitat de la dent.	And if you wish, submerge cloth or cotton in the boiling border as said above, and pause that on the painful tooth, and pause over that hot iron until the iron reaches the bottom of the cavity of the tooth.
Mays empero la cauterizacio am foc es que tu atendas a la quannula de eram o de ferr, e sia en le cor de lu alcuna grocesa e la acuitat del foc no pervengua a la boca del malaute.	But in any case, the cauterization with fire is that you attend to the quill of iron or copper, and it be in the heart of it some roughness, and the sharpness of the fire does not reach the mouth of the patient.
E aprop igneys le cauteri la forma del qual vindra, e pausa aquel sobre la dent e te la tua ma entro que·l cauteri sia enfregidat; e fay aquo alcunas veguadas quar la dolor sira remauguda o en aquel dia o en l’autre dia.	And then ignite the cautery in the shape which will be shown, and pause that on the tooth and take your hand until the cautery is cooled down; and do this several times until the pain is relented or the next day.
E cove que per empressio de aquel cauteri que·l malaute umpla la sieua boca de bon boder e tengua aquel per una hora e aprop scupa le; e aquesta es la forma del cauteri.	And it is necessary that through the impression of that cautery, the patient fills his mouth with good border and keeps it for an hour and then spits it out; and this is the form of the cautery.
E cauteriza am qual que tu voys extremittat segon que a tu es possible.	And cauterize as you wish, at the extremity, according to what is possible for you.
E aquesta es la forma de la cannula:	And this is the form of the quill:
Capitol .xxii.	Twenty-Second Chapter.
De cauterizacio de extrophulos.	On Cauterization of Extrophuli.
