Quan extrophulos so de flecma e de humors fregas e no so hobedientz a digistio per medicinas e tu voys la digistio de aquelas leugerament, lahoras tu igneys le cauteri conquau la forma del qual es aquesta seguen, havent dos extremitatz hubertas per que yesca le fum deves le cauteri per l’autra extremitat, e pausa aquel ignit sobre aquel apostema una veguada, e autre si indigeyses de aquel, entro que pervengua al preon del apostema.	When extrophuli are full of flesh and cold humors and do not respond to digestion by medicines, and you wish to facilitate their digestion lightly, then you ignite the cautery in a curved shape as follows, having two extremities with humps so that the smoke from the cautery rises from one extremity, and pause that hot thing on the abscess once or twice, or if needed more times, until it reaches the bottom of the abscess.
E si l’apostema es pauca, lahoras pausa le cauteri segon la quantitat del apostema, e aprop leyssa le per tres jorns e pausa sobre lu coto enfus en boder entro que sia remaugut aquo que·l foc ha comburit.	And if the abscess is small, then pause the cautery according to the quantity of the abscess, and leave it for three days and pause over that cloth wrapped in border until what the fire has burned away is renewed.
E aprop cura aquel am enguent e tentas e draps entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with ointment and tents and cloths until it is healed.
E la forma de la cannula o deu cauteri a tal es comveyter.	And the form of the quill or cautery is as follows:
Capitol .xxiii.	Twenty-Third Chapter.
De cauterizacio de rauquiera de votz e de constriccio de ale.	On Cauterization of Hoarseness and Constriction of the Throat.
Quan las humiditatz veno sobre le quanal del pulmo, e majorment quan aquo es am fregiditat de compleccio, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia evacuat al comensament am medicinas laxativas, e aprop cauteriza aquel deves la razit del golayro en le loc depremegut.	When the humors come out on the throat of the lung, and mostly when this is due to coldness of congestion, then it is necessary that the patient be evacuated at first with laxative medicines, and then cauterize that at the root of the goiter in the depremented location.
E guarda te que no pervenguas am le cauteri al golayro ni no comburas de la codena de lu sino un pauc.	And beware that you do not reach the goiter with the cautery nor burn away its code, but only a little.
E cauteriza aquel am autra cauteri deves la junctura del col en le derier espondil de lu.	And then cauterize that with another cautery at the junction of the neck in the last vertebra of it.
E·l cauteri de lu sia clavilh sego la maniera precedent.	And the cautery of it be claw-like, following the previous manner.
E aprop cura aquel am aquo que es precedit entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with water which is preceded by it until it is healed.
Capitol .xxiiii.	Twenty-Fourth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de malautia del pulmo e de tos.	On Cauterization of Lung Disease and Cough.
Quan tos e malautia de pulmo so de humiditatz fregas e le malaute no ha febre ni tisic e es malautia antiqua, lahoras cauterisa aquel am dos cauteris sobre la furcula en les locz depremegutz leontz e buoytz; e am autra cauteri en le mieg loc del pietz entre dos mamillos; e sia le cauteri clavilh segon la forma precedent.	When cough and lung disease are caused by cold humors and the patient does not have fever or phlegm, but is an old illness, then cauterize that with two cauteries on the furcula in the depremented locations, one above and one below; and with another cautery in the middle location of the feet between two mamillae; and let the cautery be claw-like according to the previous form.
E si vols, sia la tua cauterizacio punctan am le cauteri que es apelat puncta, la forma del qual precedeys en la ponctacio de dolor de aurelhas.	And if you wish, then be your cauterization punciform with the cauteries that are called puncta, in the shape which precedes in the puncturing of earache.
E sian puntz entro cays ad aquels; e aprop cura aquel am aquo meteys que es precedit entro que sia sanat.	And be points inserted into those, and then cure that with water which is preceded by it until it is healed.
E ya sia le cauteri haventz tres ramps quar cauterizacio es am aquel: am una veguada podes far tres cauteris segon aquesta forma:	And already the cauteries have three humps where cauterization is done with that: once you can make three cauteries according to this form:
Capitol .xxv.	Twenty-Fifth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de titillic que es le cap del ajutori.	On Cauterization of Titillation which is the head of the Help.
Quan le cap del ajutori es dislocat per causa de humiditatz lubricas e no es fermat en la hora del sieu retornament deves la sua dislocacio entro que sia a lu aquo costuma de retornar, e aprop per un petit movement es deslocat ayssi que s’endeve, ayssi cum nos havem testificat, lahoras cove que primieyrament redusiscas la dislocacio, e aprop le malaute sia reversat sobre le sieu dos o sobre le latz sa; e aprop eleva la codena la qual es en la partida dedintz del citillic a las partidas desus am les ditz de la tua ma sinistra, si la junctura es dislocada a las partidas dedintz.	When the head of the Help is dislocated due to lubricating humors and does not remain fixed in its return moment, and then for a small movement it becomes dislocated again, just as we have testified, then it is necessary to reduce the dislocation first, and then the patient should be returned to their original position or onto their right or left side; and then elevate the code which is in the posterior part of the citillic to the upper parts with the fingers of your left hand if the juncture is dislocated towards the back.
E aprop igneys le cauteri havent dos caps; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	And then ignite the cautery having two heads; and this is its form:
E aprop cauteriza la codena entro que penetre aquela entro al autre latz; e vindra la figura de cauterizacio lahoras de iv caps cauteris.	And then cauterize the code so that it penetrates into the other side; and the figure of cauterization will be like this: with four heads of cauteries.
e so aquel subtils segon la quantitat de tenta; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	and so those subtleties according to the quantity of tent; and this is its form:
E alcunas veguadas es ajustat segon aquest comte i per que son les cauteris .viii.	And some times it is adjusted according to this count, and because there are eight cauteries.
E aprop pausa sobre le cauteri porys cuytz am sal, e aprop fay adherir le malaute a trenquilitat, e lo membre no sia maugut per alcun temps entro que sia confortat.	And then pause over the cautery with porous citruses and salt, and then make the patient adhere to tranquility, and let the member not be decayed for any time until it is comforted.
E si la dislocacio es a las partidas desus e tart es fayt aquo, lahoras cauteriza sobre le muscle am cauteri clavilh o am motz cauteris puntan, quar la junctura es confermada e la humiditat es romauguda e le malaute es sanat.	And if the dislocation is in the upper parts and tartness is made there, then it is necessary to cauterize on the muscle with claw-like cautery or with pointed puncture cauteries, because the juncture is confirmed and the moisture is dried up and the patient is healed.
Capitol .xxvi.	Twenty-Sixth Chapter.
De cauterizacio del stomac.	On Cauterization of the Stomach.
Quan veno en l’estomac freg e motas humiditatz entro que aquel extrazo de la sua compleccio e so multiplicatz raumases a lu, e si tu continuas las manieyras de curacio e no confereyso, lahoras cove que le malaute sia sobre le sieu dos ressupinat, e extenda las suas mas e las suas coysas, e aprop cauteriza aquel am tres cauteris: an un cauteri dejos le pietz per la quantitat d’un dit am cauteri clavilh, e am dos cauteris dejos del dos costatz del cauteri, entro que vengua la figura de cauteri triangulada; e elonga entre els que no sian ajustatz que faran poyredura.	When cold humors come out in the stomach and many moistures are multiplied there, and if you continue the methods of healing and do not confirm it, then it is necessary that the patient be placed on their back with their legs extended and their clothes loosened, and then cauterize that with three cauteries: one leaving a space for the foot as long as the width of a finger with claw-like cautery, and two cauteries leaving the sides of the stomach, so that the figure of triangular cauterization is formed; and elongate between them so that they do not intersect and cause pressure.
E si la profunditat del cauteri la quantitat de les dos terses de la grocesa de la codena.	And if the depth of the cautery is equal to the quantity of two-thirds of the thickness of the code.
E sia la figura del cauteri segon aquesta forma ses addicio, E si vols, cauteriza am gran cauteri en le mieg loc del estomac segon aquesta forma; et aquest sia un cauteri segon la forma de cercle segon aquesta forma:	And the figure of the cautery will be according to this form, with addition, And if you wish, cauterize with a large cautery in the middle location of the stomach according to this form; and that will be one cautery according to the shape of a circle, according to this form:
E sia cauterizat l’estomac punctan ad aquel que de aquest cauteri es spaventat: e es que tu senhes sobre l’estomac punt segon la quantitat que voles am tenta, e aprop cauteriza aquel am cauteri en les puntz; e aprop cura aquel am la curacio qu’es precedita entro que sia sanat.	And then cauterize the stomach punctiform to that which is frightened by this cautery: and it is that you sense on the stomach point by point according to what you wish with tent, and then cauterize that with a cautery in the points; and then cure that with the healing which precedes it until it is healed.
Capitol .xxvii.	Twenty-Seventh Chapter.
De cauterizacio del fietge fret.	On Cauterization of the Frozen Feet.
Quan endeve en le fietge dolor per fregiditat o per humiditat o per grossa ventositat entro que de la sieua normal compleccio sia getat per egressio superflua, e es curat le malaute am aquo que havem dit e no comfereys, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia ressupinat sobre la sua cervitz, e senhes am tenta tres cauteris segon aquesta forma et aquesta quantitat meteyssa sobre le fietge dejos dels ipocondres, la hon perve le decubit de home.	When there is pain in the foot due to coldness or moisture or excessive ventilation so that it departs from its normal state by excessive excretion, and the patient is not cured with the water which we have said, then it is necessary that the patient be placed on their back with their head elevated, and sense three cauteries according to this form and this quantity mixed with tent, and place them on the foot left of the hip bones, where the man's position lies.
E sia l’espazi le qual es entre quascun cauteri segon la grossetut del dit, e sia le cauteri segon la longitut del cors dreyta.	And let the space between each cautery be according to the thickness of the finger, and let the cauteries be placed according to the length of the right arm.
E no compremas la tua am le cauteri mot.	And do not compress your hand with the moving cautery.
E si la quantitat de aquo que es adhurit la quantitat de la maytat de la specitut de la codena, e no y sia pus ajustat; e si le malaute stant sobre les pes de lu; e si no es estant, lahoras sia jassent, le qual ja ha extendudas las suas coysas, e eleve les sieus brasses.	And if the quantity of water that is absorbed is equal to the quantity of the maturity of the codena, and not yet adjusted; and if the patient stands on his feet; and if he is not standing, then lie down, which has already stretched out its clothes, and elevate its arms.
E es aquesta la forma del cauteri:	And this is the form of the cautery:
E a tu es possible que cauterizes aquestz cauteris am cauteri cutellar, quan es am tu subtilitat e prudencia en l’art.	And it is possible for you to cauterize those cauteries with a cutlery-like cautery, when it is according to your subtlety and prudence in the art.
E guarda te que trop no procesiscas en la cauterizacio, e sia adhurida la specitut de tota la codena per que sia adhurit tot le cors e pervengua entro als budels, quar la codena aqui es subtil; e sapias aquo.	And beware that you do not process too much in the cauterization, and let the subtlety of all the code be absorbed so that it is absorbed into the whole body and reaches within the veins, for the code here is subtle; and know this.
Capitol .xxviii.	Twenty-Eighth Chapter.
De perforacio de apostema del fietge am cauteri.	On Perforation of Abscess on the Foot with a Cautery.
Quan endeve excitura o apostema en le fietge e voles saber si aquel apostema es en le carn del fietge o en la tunica de lu, lahoras si es en la carn del fietge, le malaute atrobo gravitat e dolor ses acuitat.	When there is an excrescence or abscess on the foot and you want to know if that abscess is in the flesh of the foot or in the skin, then if it is in the flesh of the foot, the patient will have a heavy and intense pain.
E si es en la tunica del fietge, am la dolor es acuitat gran e vezes que ja afatiguatz les metges la cura de lu.	And if it is in the skin of the foot, with great pain and at times that fatigues even the physicians with its cure.
Donc cove que·l malaute sia enversat sobre la sieua cervit; e aprop senha le loc de l’apostema am tenta; e aprop igneys le cauteri le quel es asemblat a rag, la forma del qual a precedit en l’autra pagina.	Therefore it is necessary that the patient be placed on their back with their head elevated; and then sense the location of the abscess with tent; and then ignite the cautery which is shaped like a rag, the form of which has been preceded in the other page.
E cauteriza am aquel i cauteri entro que tota la codena sia comborida, entro que pervengua al ciphac, entro qu’en yesca sania.	And then cauterize with that and cautery until all the code is burned away, until it reaches the bone, until in which you will see healing.
E aprop cura aquel per curacio dels autres apostemas entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with the healing of other abscesses until it is healed.
E no cove que de aquesta forma de cauteri use sino aquel del qual le estudi en l’art de medicina es prolonguat, e en las mas del qual motas malautias an conogut; mays aquest am esperiment alcunas veguadas sia ardit sobre aquesta operacio, mays empero leyssa aquela deves nos, e es miels.	And it is not necessary to use this form of cauterization unless one has studied in the art of medicine and many diseases have been known; but rather, try it occasionally with some boldness, but always leave room for doubt, and that is better.
Capitol .xxix.	Twenty-Ninth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de plauresi.	On Cauterization of Pleurisy.
Diyssero les antics cauteri de las razitz de aristologia a plauresi frega segon aquesta manieyra esser fazedor, e es aquest que tu prenguas de las razitz de aristologia longa secca una razit pun longua que es trobada, e sia de la grossetut del dit.	They will say that the ancient cauteries of the roots of aristology are made for pleurisy with a coldness according to this manner, and it is this: take one root of aristology, long and dry, which is found, and be of the thickness of a finger.
E aprop submergeys aquela en oli e eysen aquela al foc, e aprop cauteriza per un cauteri en aquel loc le qual es entre la continuacio de la furcula am le col; e am dos cauteris petitz dejos guidazi, un pauc declinans a la partida que es dejus la barba, e am dos cauteris en aquo que es declinant entre la quinta costa e la cizena, declinant un pauc a las partidas detras; e am autre cauteri en le mieg loc del pietz; et am autre sobre l’estomac, et am tres cauteris de las partidas detras; et am un cauteri en aquel loc le qual es entre las dos spallas, e am dos cauteris dels dos latz del pietz, dejos le cauteri le qual es entre doas spallas.	And then immerse that in oil and ignite it at the fire, and then cauterize with a small cautery in that location which is between the continuation of the furcula and the neck; and with two small cauteries, one slightly declining towards the side below the beard, and another two cauteries declinating between the fifth rib and the navel, declining slightly behind; and another one in the middle of the foot; and another one on the stomach; and three small cauteries on the back; and one cautery in that location which is between the two shoulders; and two small cauteries from both sides of the foot, leaving out the cautery which is between the two shoulders.
E no cove que compremas la tua ma am le cauteri, ans sia en le manifest de la codena en obra.	And it is not necessary to compress your hand with the cautery, but rather let it be in the manifest of the code in work.
E ja diyssero alscus antics que so alscus dels homes les quals uson de cauteri de ferr semblant a ray e igneysso aquel, e meto aquel en aquel loc le qual es entre las costas, entro que pervenguam am aquel ad aquel apostema e sia foragetada sania, ayssi cum havem dit en l’apostema del fietge.	And already some ancient ones have said that they are also some of the men who use a cautery made of iron similar to a ray and ignite it, and place it in that location which is between the ribs, until it reaches the abscess and is purged with pus, just as we have said in the abscess of the foot.
Mays en aquesta perforacio am cauteri no es ses temor, quar hu mor tantost ho accideys en le loc fistula a la qual no es sanacio.	But in this perforation with a cautery there is no fear, for when it happens soon after it becomes a fistula which does not lead to healing.
Capitol .xxx.	Thirtieth Chapter.
De la cauterizacio de la melsa.	On Cauterization of the Melancholy.
Quan tu curas la malautia de la melsa am aquo que havem dit de la curacio en la divisio e no confereys la tua curacio, lahoras cauteri en lu es segon tres manieras, las quals totas son dreyturieras, de las quals la una es que fassas tres cauteris o quatre linhan segon la longitut de la melsa segon la figura dels cauteris del fietge, la figura dels quals ha precedit.	When you cure the disease of melancholy with the water which we have said in the division and do not confirm your cure, then cauterize in that place according to three ways, all of which are purgative, of which one is to make three or four lines running along the length of the melancholy, just as the figure of the cauteries on the foot has preceded.
E sia entre quascun cauteri la grossetut d’un dit o un pauc mes, e la manieyra del cauteri sia la manieyra la qual havem dita en le cauteri del fietge engualment.	And let the thickness between each cautery be the thickness of a finger or a little more, and the manner of the cautery be the manner which we have said in the cautery of the foot equally.
E no compremas la tua ma am le cauteri; e le malaute sia eves sobre lo sieu dos.	And do not compress your hand with the cautery; and let the patient be elevated on their back.
E es autra manieyra de cauterizar, so es que tu igniscas le cauteri haventz dos vertimentz, la qual causa havem dita en le capitol de dislocacio del muscle, e elava la codena la qual es en le endreyt de la melsa la hon perve le jazer del malaute sinistre.	And there is another manner of cauterizing, so that you ignite the cautery having two wick-like ends, which we have said in the chapter on dislocation of the muscle, and elevate the code which is in the end part of the melancholy, where the patient's left side becomes quiet.
E sia la tua elevacio am la qual elevas la codena segon la longuesa del cors, per que sian faytz cauteris segon la latitut del cos.	And let your elevation be the one by which you elevate the code according to the length of the body, so that the cauteries are made according to the latitude of the body.
E aprop entromet les dos vernimentz, ignitz mot, en aquel entro que am aquels penetres la codena de la autra part.	And then insert the two wick-like ends, ignite them slowly, into that which you will pierce with the code from the other side.
E aprop extrayt le cauteri; e donc son faytz quatre cauteris.	And then extract the cautery; and thus four cauteries are made.
E si voys, cauteriza am cauteri havent tres vernimentz.	And if you wish, cauterize with a cautery having three wick-like ends.
E aprop tu cura le cauteri pus que aia laysat de getar brac per trops jorns, quar mays es comferent que las autras causas precedentz en la curacio.	And then cure the cautery more than it has already laid down of getting worse for too many days, because it is more certain that the other previous causes are in the cure.
Capitol .xxxi.	Thirty-First Chapter.
De cauterizacio de ydropici.	On Cauterization of Hydrocephaly.
Cauteri no catz en ydropici sino en alcinte3 propriament.	Cauteries are not used in hydrocephaly, but rather on the proper part alone.
Quan tu curas le ydropic am las manieyras de curacio las quals havem ditas en la divisio e no confereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que aquel cauterizes am quatre cauteris en le cercuit del embelic e am un cauteri sobre l’estomac, e am autre cauteri sobre le fietge, e am autre cauteri sobre la melsa, e am dos cauteris entre les spondils del dos, e un cauteri en lo dreyt del pietz, e am autre cauteri sobre l’estomac.	When you cure the hydrocephalus with the methods of healing which we have said in the division and do not confirm your cure, then it is necessary that one cauterizes with four cauteries around the navel, and one cautery on the stomach, and another on the foot, and another on the melancholy, and two cauteries between the vertebrae of the back, and one cautery in the right side of the foot, and another on the stomach.
E la quantitat de la profunditat del cauteri sia propdana a la spicitut de la codena.	And the quantity of the depth of the cautery be proportional to the subtlety of the code.
E aprop layssa le cauteri ubert per so que gete brac per lonc temps.	And then leave the cautery untouched for such a time that it may become worse over a long period.
E no evacuas le malaute de curacio aprop le cauteri am aquo que cove per que sian agreguadas a lu doas entencios, e sira festinada a lu am ajutori sanacio.	And do not evacuate the patient from the cure near the cautery with water which is necessary for two intentions, and be hastened to him with the help of healing.
La forma del cauteri am lo qual es cauterizat lo ventre sia clavilh segon que la forma de aquel es desus precedent, e es aquel am le qual es cauterizat le dos sia olivar segon qu’es precedent a la sua forma.	The form of the cautery with which the belly is cauterized is claw-like according to its previous shape, and it is that with which the back is cauterized is olive-shaped according to its previous form.
Capitol .xxxii.	Thirty-Second Chapter.
De cauterizacio de pes e de las coyssas.	On Cauterization of Feet and Shoes.
Quan les pes so apostematz en ydropitz e so repletz de aygua sitrina, cove que cauterisas les pes sobre le dos del pe in nocrati aquo que es entre le auricular e le anular, e eleva la tua ma am le cauteri e no torses aquel; e aprop eleva la tua ma, e no retornes aquela de tot, quar l’aygua satrina rezuda.	When the feet are abscessed in hydrophobia and filled with stagnant water, it is necessary that you cauterize the feet on the back of the heel with a cautery in nocturnal water which is between the auricular and anular, and elevate your hand with the cautery and do not twist it; and then elevate your hand, and do not return to all, because the stagnant water resists.
Es le cauteri segon aquesta forma: E aprop fay sobre las doas coyssas dos cauteris, e en quascuna coysa sia feyt cauteri am la extremitat del cauteri cutellar.	It is the cautery according to this form: And then make two cauteries on each shoe, and in each shoe make a cautery at the extremity of the claw-like cautery.
E sia le cauteri segon la longitut de la coyssa: i dejos le denolh e l’autre jos le mieg loc de la coyssa; e sobre quascuna coyssa dos cauteris.	And let the cauteries be according to the length of the shoe: one at the toe and the other at the middle of the shoe; and on each shoe, two cauteries.
E layssa la plagua uberta ses curacio per lonc temps per so que alcuna aygua resuda de lu.	And leave the wound open without healing for a long time because some water will ooze out from it.
E aprop cura le am aquelas causas las quals havem ditas.	And then cure with those causes which we have said.
Capitol .xxxiii.	Thirty-Third Chapter.
De cauterizacio de cos de ventre.	On Cauterization of the Belly.
Quan cos de ventre es per freg e per humiditat entro que debelice las vertutz, so es la vertut digestiva e retentiva, las quals so en l’estomac e en les budels, e es curat aquo am las manieyras de curacio e no confereys, e vezes le malaute suffertan cauteri de vertut exhiberant, lahoras cauteriza aquel am gran cauteri sobre le sieu stomac segon que a precedit en la cauterizacio del estomac, am le cauteri del cercle e am quatre cauteris en le cercuit del embelic subtils, am cauteri clavilh subtil; e am cauteri sobre le alcatin sobre alozis gran, o am dos cauteris.	When the belly is afflicted by cold and moisture so that the virtues are debilitated, it is necessary to exhibit virtue to show that the patient will suffer from a cautery. Then cauterize that with a great cautery on the patient's stomach according to what preceded in the cauterization of the stomach, with the circle cautery and four small cauteries in the navel subtils, with claw-like cautery subtlety; and with a cautery over the skin over the aloes grand, or two cauteries.
E si vezes las humiditatz exhuberants e le malaute aquo tollerant, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre le pentenilh e sobre les budels, e fort leu ajustant dos cauteris sobre l’estomac e prop dels inguonas, quar es curacio perficent de juvament de la qual no erras.	And if the humidities are excessive and the patient can tolerate it, then cauterize that over the intestines and over the bowels, and slightly adjusting two cauteries on the stomach and near the inguinal regions, because it is a perfect cure of which you will not err.
Capitol .xxxiv.	Thirty-Fourth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de emorroydas antiquas.	On Cauterization of Old Hemorrhoids.
Quan so en la natura derier emorroydas antiquas o una de humors grossas fregas o de humiditatz corrompudas, e son curadas am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no confereys la tieua curacio, lahoras cauterisa am tres cauteris sobre le pus dejos spondilh del dos petit e petit triangular, e am cauteri desus le ombelic cays per dos ditz.	When in nature old hemorrhoids or one of gross humors or corrupted moistures come to an end, and are cured with what we have said in the division and do not confirm the patient's cure, then cauterize with three cauteries on the pus left between the vertebrae of the small back and small triangular, and with a cautery above the navel which falls by two fingers.
E si doptas que l’estomac de lu sia enfregidat e la vianda de lu no sia degerida, e la cara de lu vezes apostemada, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre l’estomac am gran cauteri segon que es precedit; e am un cauteri sobre fietge, e am autre cauteri sobre la melsa de lu am cauteri clavilh, e leyssa le cauteri per alcun temps ubert, e aprop cura lu entro que sia sanat.	And if you think that the patient's stomach is chilled and their food not digested, and their face often abscessed, then cauterize that on the stomach with a great cautery according to what has preceded; and with one cautery on the foot, and another on the melancholy of them with a claw-like cautery, and leave the cautery untouched for some time open, and then cure them until they are healed.
Capitol .xxxv.	Thirty-Fifth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de atheyl aprop la abscizio de lor.	On Cauterization of Athletes near the Abscession of Their Wounds.
Quan tu abscindes atheyl, lahoras tu igneys le cauteri que es asemblat a ray.	When you abscess athletes, then ignite the cautery that is shaped like a ray.
Aprop entremet aquel ignit en aquel atheyl abscis, e ultima la tieua ma entro que pervengua le cauteri al orifici de la vena de la qual ve la sanc.	Then insert that ignited cautery into the abscessed athlete, and finally rest your hand until the cautery reaches the opening of the vein from which blood flows.
E fay aquo una vetz o doas, quar si achieyl son trops, lahoras cauteriza quascun de lor segon que havem recontat, e aprop cura aquels am aquo que confereys a lor dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And make it once or twice, for if athletes are many, then cauterize each of them according to what we have recounted, and finally cure those with what confirms their wounds until they are healed.
E si cauterizas am gran cauteri sobre alquatin, es mays derier en juvament.	And if you cauterize with a great cautery on someone, it is more certain in judgment.
Capitol .xxxvi.	Thirty-Sixth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de fistolas que son faytas en la natura derie en las partidas de lu.	On Cauterization of Fistulas that are made in the natural parts of the body.
Quan la natura no obeziys a la obra la qual havem recomtada en son loc, e·l pacient es espaventat per aquo, sia sanat am cauteri.	When nature does not obey the work which we have recommended in its place, and the patient is frightened by this, then heal with a cautery.
Donc quan ad alcun ve fistola en la natura derier, e es antiquada, corro sania de lu e humiditatz corrompudas, e donc aquo que es pus digne que cove es que proes aquela am tenta subtil, e aprop conoys la quantitat de la profunditat de lu am la devant dita tenta.	Therefore, when one has some fistula in the natural parts which is old and corrupt, with pus and corrupted moistures, and therefore what is most worthy that it cures is to probe that with a subtle tent, and then know the quantity of its depth with the preceding said tent.
Aprop igneys le cauteri que es semblant a ray.	Then ignite the cautery which is shaped like a ray.
E aprop met aquel cauteri ignit en aquesta fistula, e segon la quantitat en la qual intrec la tenta.	And then place that ignited cautery into this fistula, and according to the quantity in which the tent has penetrated.
E itera sobre aquela le cauteri entro que sian comburitz aquels cors corrumputz tost una veguada o dos o tres, segon la quantitat de la tua necessitat.	And repeat the cautery on that until those corrupted bodies are burned away in one, two, or three sessions, according to the quantity of your necessity.
E guarda te de combustio de nervi e de vena; o si fistula va al cors de la vesica o al cors del budel, lahoras guarda te de totz aquels locz; e no fassas aquo sino quan la fistula es en loc carnos e cogitas que no es penetrant.	And beware of combustion of nerves and veins; or if the fistula goes to the bladder or bowel, then beware of all those places; and do not make it so unless the fistula is in a fleshy and palpable place that is not penetrating.
E aprop cura le loc entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the place until it is healed.
E si le loc es sigillat, e so abscindidas de lu las materias, e roman ayssi per lonc temps, lahoras sapias que ja es curat entierament.	And if the place is sealed, and all materials have abscessed from it, and remains thus for a long time, then know that it has been fully cured.
E si las materias no so de lu ostadas, lahoras sapias que es penetrant o en le preon de lu os corromput, o cays aquo de aquelas causas de las quals vindra rememoracio en son loc.	And if the materials are not gone from it, then know that it is penetrating or in the prone position of corrupting one's flesh, or falls into those causes of which a reminder will come in its place.
Capitol .xxxvii.	Thirty-Seventh Chapter.
De cauterizacio dels ronhos.	On Cauterization of the Tonsils.
Quan en les ronhos endeve dolor per freg o per grossa ventozitat, e per aysso le coyt del malaute es amermat, lahoras cove que cauterizes aquel sobre les ronhos am cauteri sobre quascun ronho am cauteri clavilh del qual precesic la rememoracio.	When in the tonsils there is pain from cold or from excessive ventilation, and because of this the patient's throat is dry, then it is necessary that you cauterize that on the tonsils with a cautery on each tonil with a claw-like cautery of which the remembrance precedes.
E fort leu cauterizam am le segon un petit dejos, per que vindran tres cauteris liniatz, e donc siran mays deriers en juvament.	And then cauterize with a small cautery in the second one, so that three lined-up cauteries will come to be, and therefore they will be more certain in judgment.
Capitol .xxxviii.	Thirty-Eighth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la vesica.	On Cauterization of the Bladder.
Quan accideys en la vesica debelitat e mollificacio per freg e per humiditatz ayssi que·l malaute la urina no retengua, lahoras cauteriza aquel en la partida pus dejos sobre la vesiqua, la hon comensan les pels del pentenilh, e cauteriza am un cauteri en la partida dreyta, e am autre en la senestra de lu.	When debilitation and mollification occur in the bladder due to cold and moistures such that the patient's urine does not retain, then cauterize that in the most posterior part of the bladder, where the hairs of the intestines begin, and cauterize with one cautery on the right side and another on the left.
E sia la longitut de quascun cauteri segon la cantitat dels not del pous; e cauteriza aquel am cauteri en la partida pus bassa del dos, o am dos cauteris si es necessitat.	And let the length of each cautery be according to the number of the bones of the foot; and cauterize that with a cautery in the most lower part of the back, or with two cauteries if necessary.
E sia cauteri clavilh segon que es procesit.	And let it be a claw-like cautery according to what has been processed.
Capitol .xxxix.	Thirty-Ninth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la mayra.	On Cauterization of the Shoulder.
Quan veno en la mayra freg e humiditatz, e per aysso es prohibida enpreignacio, e son corrompudas las mestruas de lu, e es tardada la provocacio de lor, e accideys dolor deves le haveniment de lor, lahoras cove que·l loc sia cauterizat am tres cauteris en le circuit del ombelic, ayssi cum havem dit en le cauteri de la vesica; e am cauteri sobre le loc pus dejos del dos, o am dos cauteris, e sia le cauteri clavilh.	When cold and moistures come to the shoulder, and because of this, there is no preoccupation, and the menstrual cycles are corrupted, and the provocation of them is delayed, and it happens that pain occurs in the movement of them, then it is necessary that the place be cauterized with three cauteries in the circuit of the navel, just as we have said in the cauterization of the bladder; and with a cautery on the most posterior part of the back, or with two cauteries, and let the cautery be claw-like.
Capitol .xl.	Fortieth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la dislocacio de l’anqua.	On Cauterization of the Dislocation of the Hip.
Quan humiditatz moucozas so efundudas a la partida de la anqua, e so faytas causas del yssiment del sieu loc, e senhal de lu es que la coyssa es prolonguada sobre l’autre quan so comparadas entre lor.	When moistures are effused into the part of the hip, and are caused by the symptoms of the same place, and a sign of it is that the shoe is prolonged over the other when they are compared between them.
E le loc de la dislocacio es atrobat en lu quays boyt.	And the location of the dislocation is found in the quarter where the buttock lies.
Adonc cove que cauterizas le malaute sobre la partida de la anqua de lu am cauteri a sercle semblant, pus que tu auras senhat am tenta en le cercuit de la partida ayssi cum es revolguda, e per so que la partida caia el mieg loc del cercle.	Then it is necessary that you cauterize the patient on the part of the hip with a circular cautery resembling a circle, as you have marked with a tent in the circuit of the same part, and because the part falls into the middle of the circle.
E sia le cauteri del qual precedit la forma en la cauterizacio del estomac.	And let it be the cautery whose form preceded in the cauterization of the stomach.
E si aquest cauteri no es a tu present, lahoras cauteriza aquel am tres cauteris am cauteri olivar gran.	And if this cautery is not with you at hand, then cauterize that with three cauteries and one large olive-shaped cautery.
E sia fayt le cauteri segon la quantitat de la ispicitut de tota la codena; e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And let the cautery be made according to the quantity of the subtlety of all the code; and then cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .xli.	Forty-First Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la vena sciatica.	On Cauterization of the Sciatic Vein.
Quan dolor ve en la partida de anqua, e so causa de lu freg et humiditatz, le malaute es curat am aquo que havem dit e no confereys, e aquo es antiquat, lahoras cove que tu lacses le malaute de humors grosses am pillulas fetidas o am pillulas artificials o semblantz; e aprop cauteriza aquel.	When pain occurs in the part of the hip, and its cause is cold and moistures, the patient is cured with what we have said and does not confirm, and this is old, then it is necessary that you release the patient from gross humors with fetid pills or artificial pills or similar ones; and then cauterize that.
E la manieyra del cauteri en aquela es segon dos manieyras: o cauteri am medicinas comburentz, o cauteri am foc.	And the method of the cautery in that is according to two methods: either a cautery with burning medicines or a cautery with fire.
Sira segon dos manieyras scientas, de las quals es la una que cauterizes aquel sobre la partida de l’ancha de lu am tres cauteris triangulatz segon aquesta forma; e fay am aquels bona profunditat.	There are two scientific methods, one of which is to cauterize that on the part of the hip with three triangular cauteries according to this form; and make good depth in those.
E sia le spazi le qual es entre cascun cauteri la quantitat de la grossitut del dit e si le cauteri olivar o gran.	And let the space between each cautery be the quantity of the thickness of the finger, and if it is an olive-shaped or large cautery.
Mays alcunas veguadas sia le cauteri sobre le mieg loc sobre le cap de l’anquan per que son quatre cauteris.	But sometimes there are four cauteries on the middle part of the hip, so that they are on the head of the anquana.
E si vols, cauteriza am le cercle del qual es precesida la forma en la cauterizacio de la dislocacio de l’anqua, la i que sia cercle continent e comburey la ispicitut de tota la codena.	And if you wish, cauterize with the circle whose form precedes in the cauterization of the dislocation of the hip, that it may be a circular container and burn away the subtlety of all the code.
E aquesta es la manieyra de cauteri in ciatiqua quan dolor es adherent al anqua e no es estenduda entro a la coyssa.	And this is the method of cautery for sciatica when pain is attached to the hip and not extended into the coss.
Mays si es estenduda entro a la coyssa, lahoras cauteriza aquel am dos cauteris sobre la coyssa sobre le loc al qual envireys le malaute que es la dolor; e am un cauteri sobre la cavilha per quatre ditz un pauc deves la part cilvestra.	But if it is extended into the coss, then cauterize that with two cauteries on the coss on the spot where the patient feels the pain; and with one cautery on the hip for four fingers a little above the hairy part.
E si le cauteri cutellar, e sia la profunditat del cauteri segon la quantitat de la ispicitut de la codena.	And if the cautery is cutaneous, and let the depth of the cautery be according to the quantity of the subtlety of the code.
E si le malaute envireys que la dolor es estenduda entro al loc prop les ditz des pes, lahoras cauteriza aquel aqui on envireys am cauteri per tres puntz o quatre o mays si indigeys de aquel.	And if the patient says that the pain is extended into the place near the big toes, then cauterize that here where it hurts with a cautery for three or four points, or more if needed.
E si le malaute envireys dolor esser dejos le donolh ves la coyssa, lahoras cauteriza aquel aqui am un cauteri cutellar.	And if the patient says that the pain is below the donal bone near the coss, then cauterize that here with one cutaneous cautery.
E guarda te en tota cauterizacio que no ultimes am le cauteri en tant que comburas nervi o gran arceria, e que per aquo a tu es sobre le malaute mal noccument o contraccio.	And be careful in all cautery that you do not leave the cautery until you burn nerves or large arteries, and because of this, it may harm your patient more than it helps.
E yeu ja e vist un e autre de aquels les quals cauterizero sobre la cavilha e ultimero en la cauterizacio, e la cama foc inflada entro que la tumor aconseguit lo pe, e foc perforat e corromput tot le pe.	And I have seen one or another of those which you will cauterize on the hip and ultimately in the cautery, and the inflated fire burning inside until the tumor reaches the top, and the perforated and corrupted foot.
E aprop accidic fort solucio de ventre, e aprop aquo la mort.	And thus there will be a sudden solution of the stomach, and thus also death.
E si la dolor es en dos partidas ensemps cauteriza quascuna segon aquesta manieyra.	And if the pain is in two parts together, then cauterize each one according to this method.
E diysero les savis alcus en la cauterizacio de anqua cauteri del qual aquesta es la manieyra: fay semblant a cercle de ferr del qual le cercuit sia la maytat de un palm; e sia deves le sieu orrifici segon la grossesa de un os de datil o mens un pauc.	And thus the wise men say in the cauterization of the hip, that this is the method: make it resemble a circle of iron, the circumference being half of a palm; and let the opening be according to the thickness of an almond or slightly less.
E dedintz aquel cercle sia un autre tertz; e sia le spazi le qual es entre lor la quantitat del notz del pous; e sian aquels cercles ubertz de dos partidas; e sia la longitut de aquels cays un notz o dos notz, e fay en aquels margue de ferr decentment apparelhat en les cercles; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	And in the center of that circle be another circle; and let the space between them be the quantity of the bones of the foot; and be those circles about two parts; and let their length be one bone or two bones, and make in those margins a decent iron clothing in the circles; and this is the form of it:
Aprop sia ignit en le foc entro que s’enrogesisca e gete scintillas, e aprop sia pausat sobre la partida del anqua, le malaute colcat sobre le latz sa.	And let it be ignited in the fire until it reddens and produces sparks, and then let it rest on the part of the hip, the patient lying on their side.
E donc cauteriza aquel am tres cauteris redontz en una veguada.	And therefore cauterize that with three circular cauteries in one go.
E aprop layssa aquel per tres jorns; aprop emplastre aquel am boder e layssa la plagua uberta per trops dias; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then let that rest for three days, apply an emplaster to it with a border and leave the wound open for many days; and then cure that with ointments until it is healed.
Diys Albucasis : o, filhs, de aquesta specia de cauteri pauc havem usat per la terror del reguardament de lu, e per aquo que paucs havem trobatz les quals reguardan sobre lu.	Thus says Albucasis: Oh, sons, of this type of cautery we have used but few times because of the terror of the regard for it, and therefore few of those who look upon it.
Mays dels bos cauteris a lu qui les sufferta, et atroba am aquel le loc de lu.	But of the best cauteries to that place which suffered them, and finds with it the location of the same.
Mays cauteri am medicinas adhurentz es que tu fassas dos cercles haventz armula perforada en la qual deyssen le guaffo de la porta de ferr; sia la longuitut de la paretz en la nauteza de lor sian dos nozes o quays aquels.	But the cautery with medicines that adhesions, is that you make two circles having an armula perforated in which they should be placed the guaffo of the door of iron; let the length of the walls be in the naughtiness of theirs be two bones or as many as those.
E si le spazi le qual es entre quascu la quantitat de la grossitut del dit; e sian ubertz dejos e desus, e sian que contenguan se entre lor segon aquesta forma:	And if the space between each one is the quantity of the thickness of the finger; and be above and below, and be that they contain themselves between them according to this form:
E aprop pausa sobre la partida de la anqua le malaut jasent sobre le latz sa, e comprem la tua ma sobre la partida de la anqua; e aprop pren de aygua cauda e fon la entre dos cercles, e la qualiditat de aquela sia am le foc petit a petit, e te aquela per la quantitat de una hora, e sufferta le malaute la mordicacio e la adhustio de lu — quar aquel atrobo mordicacio ayssi cum de foc — entro que cesse la mordicacio.	And then let it rest on the part of the hip, the patient lying on their side, and press your hand on the part of the hip; and then take hot water and pour it between two circles, and let its quality be like a small fire gradually, and let it stay for the quantity of an hour, and suffer the patient's mordication and adjustment of it - because that atrocity is as if from fire - until the mordication ceases.
E aprop eleva la tua ma am le instrument et abstergeys l’aygua cauda de tota la anqua am aygua dousa.	And then lift your hand with the instrument and wash away the hot water from all of the hip with lukewarm water.
E aprop leyssa aquel per tres jorns e pausa sobre aquel boder entro que sia la negror de la adhustio remauguda, e leyssa aquo per alcus jorns, e correra de lu poyredura; aquest es derier en juvament.	And then let it rest for three days and pause on that border until the blackness of the adjustment is renewed, and let it rest again for some days, and flow from it purulence; this is the final in judgment.
E aprop cura aquel am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with ointments until it is healed.
E si la dolor es extenduda entro la coyssa o la camba, fay a lu estatua en lu que contengua aygua segon que es feyt en la anqua engualment.	And if the pain is extended into the coss or the leg, make it so in that location where it contains water according to what is done in the hip in equal measure.
E aquesta es la manieyra de aygua cauda, e yeu ja he scrit aquela en le tractat de la rectificacio de medicinas.	And this is the method of hot water, and I have already written that in the treatise on the correction of medicines.
Recipe de alcali e de caus no extinta de amdos ana partida una, e trissa les e pausa en una ola nova de la qual la partida dejos sia perforada per un petit trauc, segon la quantitat que intre en lu ray.	Recipe of alkali and of causes not extinct in both parts, one on each side, and mix them together and pause in a new bowl of which the left part is perforated by a small hole, according to the quantity that enters into the ray.
E pausa dejos le fons de la ola autra ola enveyriada, e gete sobre aquel alcali e caus viva de aygua doussa la qual cobra aquels per un dit, e pus que tu compremes aquels am la tieua ma per bona compressio, e leyssa la hola que deyssenda de lu aygua aguda en la partida dejos a la ola enveyriada.	And pause the bottom of one bowl in another bowl filled with lukewarm water, and pour upon that alkali and living causes of hot water which absorbs them by a finger, and then press those with your thumb for good compression, and let the hole that descends from the sharp water into the left part of the bowl filled with lukewarm water.
E aprop ajusta tota aquela aygua, e geta la sobre autra caus viva e autre alcali renovelatz, quar aquela lahoras sira de mot forta acuitat, la qual es aministrada en motas operacios de medicina e en cauterizacio dels autres membres, quar operacio fa de foc.	And then adjust all that water, and pour it over another living cause and another alkali renewed, for those things are now of great fiery intensity, which is administered in many operations of medicine and in the cauterization of other members, for this operation does by fire.
E so de las medicinas alcunas am las quals es cauterizat ancha, ayssi cum tezizic e mel anacrat e caus am sabo enayssi que sian mesclatz.	And thus of some medicines with which the hip is cauterized, such as turpentine and manna, and causes with saffron, mixed together in a way that they are blended.
E Gualia recontet de un home dels antics la operacio e la curacio am la qual es curada dolor de anqua e de vena sciatica, e magnifiquet mot be esser de aquel, e diys que no hac necessitat de autra curacio, e quar es sanat per una veguada ayssi cum recomtec, quar fort leu aquel intrec en banh e eysic ja sa d’aquel.	And Gualia recounts the story of a man from ancient times who underwent an operation and cure with which he was cured of hip pain and sciatic vein pain, and magnified much about that, saying that there was no need for another cure, and since he was healed in one go just as recommended, because it was very easy to do so.
Et es que sia pres de certarragi vert, e si no es atrobat vert, sia presa figua recent; e mot sia trissada am un pauc de grays e sia pausat sus la anqua en la qual es la dolor, o en la coyssa, o en la camba, e sia liat.	And thus it is that he is pressed with a certain type of vertebra, and if not found to be green, then he is pressed with a recent fig tree; and much is mixed with a little bit of gray and is paused on the hip where there is pain, or in the coss, or in the leg, and is tied.
E sia layssat per la cantitat de tres horas o per la quantitat que·l malaute centa cedacio de la adhustio.	And let it be left for the quantity of three hours or for the quantity that the patient gives up the adjustment.
E aprop met aquel en banh e donc quan le cors de lu sia enrozat, entromet aquel en le sol, quar la dolor cessa e es sanat.	And then put it in water and thus when the body of him is reddenated, enter that into the earth, because the pain ceases and he is healed.
E sapias que no cove que alcu use de cauteri am aquestas medicinas sino aprop la evacuacio del cors.	And know that it is not necessary for anyone to use this cautery with these medicines except in the case of evacuation from the body.
Mays ja Escorides diysec que quan am fenda de cabra la vena stretica es cauterizada, aprofieyra a lu mo be; e sia le cauteri am lu segon aquesta manieyra: sia presa lana e sia enbeguda en oli antic, e sia pausat entre le pous del pe e entre le fossil.	But already Escorides has said that when there is a wound in the goat's vein, it is cauterized by afflicting the moon; and let the cautery be done according to this method: take wool and soak it in old oil, and place it between the toes of the foot and between the fossils.
E aprop pren fenda de cabra secca e emflasma aquela am foc entro que sia fayta carbo; e aprop pausa lu sobre la lana e leysa la entro que sia estengida.	And then take dried goat's skin and inflame it with fire until it is made into charcoal; and let the cautery be done by placing the charcoal on the wool and letting it extend.
E aprop itera aquo, e no cessas far aquo entro que·l scintiment de la mordicacio pervengua entro al anqua e repausa la dolor.	And then repeat this process, and do not cease to do so until the sensation of the mordication reaches into the hip and relieves the pain.
Et aquesta manieyra de cauteri es apelat cauteri de vaquas.	And this method of cautery is called "cauteri de vaquas".
Capitol .xlii.	Chapter XLII.
De cauterizacio de dolor de dos.	On the Cauterization of Pain in Two Parts.
Alcunas veguadas dolor es en le dos per tropas causas, cum per cazement o per percucio o per superflua evacuacio, e per causas ad aquelas semblantz, per infusio de materia frega e humida.	At times pain is in the two parts due to numerous causes, such as by falling or striking or excessive evacuation, and by causes similar to those, namely the infusion of wet and humid matter.
E cauteri no catz sino en aquesta sola specia la qual es fayta per efusio de materia frega.	And let it not be cut off except in this one species which is made by effusion of wet matter.

E sia fayta cauterizacio am cauteri de punt.	And let it be a cauterization with pinpoint cautery.

Capitol .xliii.	Chapter XLIII.
De cauterizacio al comensament de gilbositat.	On Cauterization at the Beginning of Gillyosity.

Many times this disease begins in small children; and the sign of its beginning in children is that it occurs on their structure in the leg, causing elevation and movement.

que prengua le cauteri sobre tota partida del spondilh engualment.	that takes the cautery on all parts of the vertebra equally.

Capitol .xliv.	Chapter XLIV.
De cauterizacio de podagra e de dolor de juncturas.	On Cauterization of Gout and Pain in Joints.
Quan dolor de juncturas son faytas per humors fregas les quals so enfundutz a quascun membre del cors, lahoras quan veno dolors en los pes, de costuma dels metges es que aquo apelen podragua propriament.	When pains in joints are caused by wet humors which are lodged in each member of the body, it is customary for doctors to call this condition gout properly.

E si las dolors pugan entro al donolh e·l dos, lahoras aministra le cauteri le qual havem dit en le sieu capitol.	And if the pains rise into the tendon and the back, then administer the cautery which we have said in its own chapter.
E si las dolors so en las mas tant solament, e es apelada suagra, lahoras puncta en le circuit dels focils ayssi cum se revolvo, puncta en aquels dos linhas.	And if the pains are only in the mass and is called syringa, then point in the circle of the tendons as they revolve, pointing to those two lines.
E si reman de las dolors en les ditz, lahoras puncta en le cercuit dels focils sobre quascun notz e sobre la pinche de la ma.	And if the pains remain in the said joints, then point in the circle of the tendons on each bone and on the pinch of the hand.
E si las dolors pugan aprop alscus jorns als coydes o als muscles, lahoras cauteriza les quascus de tota part dels ajutoris.	And if the pains rise to nearby days in the hips or muscles, then cauterize all of them on all parts of the aids.

Capitol .xlv.	Chapter XLV.
De cauterizacio de rompeduras.	On Cauterization of Wounds.
Quan endeve rompedura en les angonars e diysendo les budels denant l’atela al genetiu, e aquo es comensan de aprop, lahoras cove que tu mandas al malaute layssar la sua comestio en le sieu dia e que use de causas leniens per so que la fenda deyssenda del sieu ventre.	When an open wound appears in the groin and says goodbye to the navel, and this is where it begins to approach, then you must tell the patient to stop eating for a day and to use soothing causes so that the wound will descend from its belly.
E aprop segua le malaute entre las tuas mas sobre le sieu dos, e comanda a lu que tengua le sieu ale entro que sia foro getat o aparesca l’atela o·l budels.	And then follow the patient between your hands on their back, and command them to keep their arm bent until there is a hole or the cord or the bag appears.
E aprop retorna aquel am les tieus ditz e senha am tenta la ruptura sobre le os del pentenilh am senhal la extremitat del qual sia semblant a la maytat de cercle a las subiranas partidas del cors.	And then return that place with your said fingers and signal the rupture over the bone of the shoulder blade, signaling the extremity of which is similar to the middle of a circle on the divided parts of the chest.
E aprop igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And then ignite the cautery which has this form:
entro que sia mot rog e gete cintilhas.	until it is but a small spark and gives out sparks.
E aprop reduzeys le budel o l’atela a la sua conquavitat, e aprop pause la sua ma sobre le loc per so que le budel no yesqua.	And then reduce the bag or cord to its natural size, and then place your hand on the location so that the bag does not burst.
E tu ja has ubert entre las coyssas del malaute e dejos lu as pausat un coyssi, et autre servent sia sus las cambas de lu, e autre sus le pietz de lu, le qual tengua las suas mas.	And you have placed between the patient's cosses and left one there to rest, another serves on his legs, and another on his feet, which has its own masses.
E aprop pausa le cauteri sobre aquel senhal am la tua ma am cauteri stan dreyt, e te aquel entro que am lu consieguas le os del pentenilh entro al mieg del duiduni; e itera am aquel autra veguada si a tu aquel no has conseguit en la primieyra veguada entro al os.	And then pause the cautery on that signal with your hand holding the cautery straight, and place it there until you reach the bone of the shoulder blade in the middle of the dueduni; and repeat that procedure another time if you did not achieve it in the first instance into the bone.
E observa saviament del ysiment del budel en la hora de la tua cauterizacio, que no comburas aquel budel per so que sobre le malaute no vengua in mort o autre gran malicia.	And observe wisely the shape of the bag at the time of your cautery, lest you burn that bag and the patient comes to harm or great evil.
E sapias que quan tu am le cauteri no atenhas le os, no confereys la tua operacio.	And know that when you are applying the cautery do not touch the bone, nor compromise your operation.
E cove que·l cauteri dels enfants sia subtil segon le gran e la mesura de lor.	And it is necessary that the cautery of children be subtle according to their age and measure.
E aprop cura le loc del cauteri per tres dias am boder entro que sia remauguda la scara del foc.	And then cure the location of the cautery for three days with ointment until the scar of fire is renewed.
E aprop cura aquel am les autres enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that place with other remedies until it is healed.
E le malaute sia jasent sobre le sieu dos per xl dias entro que sia sigillat le loc e la plagua.	And the patient lies on their back for 40 days until the wound and the plague are sealed.
E cove que pauses le nutriment de lu segon la longitut del temps de la curacio de lu le qual le linesca le ventre de lu, e que le budel no yesca fora deves le esforsament de guerir.	And it is necessary that you pause the patient's nourishment according to the length of time of their cure, which stretches their belly, and that the bag does not burst forth from the effort to heal.
E aprop quan se vol levar aprop xl dias, lahoras aministra liament decentment fayt, e tengua aquel per autres xl jorns.	And then, after 40 days, gradually administer a decrease in the remedy, and keep it thus for another 40 days.
E sia mermat de trebalh e de replecio de vianda e de beure, e de votz vehementz, quar quan usa de aquest regiment de sanacio entiera sira sanat.	And thus be reduced in work and replenishment of food and drink, and in violent voices, because when you use this regimen of entire healing, it will be healed.
E yeu diyre la curacio de las rupturas en las autras partidas del ventre, e so al comensament, e vols que no treguan, lahoras cauterisa la ruptura d’aquel am cauteri redon segon la quantitat de lu, e sia aquo que es exhurit de la codena ayssi cum la tersa partida de lu; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que havem dit, e no es ajustat.	And I say the cure for ruptures in other parts of the belly, and thus at first, and you wish not to delay, then cauterize the rupture with that redon-shaped cautery according to its quantity, and it is this which is exhorted from the code just as the third part of it; and then cure that place with what we have said, and do not adjust.
E ja diyssero alcus primiers que ruptura sia cauterizada am cauteri triangular segon aquesta forma, pus que es senhada am tenta:	And it has already been said by some firsts that a rupture should be cauterized with a triangular cautery according to this form, since it is signaled in the attempt:
e es pausada linha que eys per la latitut en le latz pus sobira de la ruptura, e autra linha al desus; e depausa la tua ma am un cauteri clavilh, mays le primier cauteri es pus leugier e milhor.	and it is a paused line that goes through the latitude in the hip above the rupture, and another line above; and place your hand with a claw-shaped cautery, but the first cautery is lighter and better.
Capitol .xlvi.	Chapter XLVI.
De cauterizacio de torcio.	On Cauterization of Twist.
Quan endeve en alscus membres per cazement o per percussio dolor e persevera aquela dolor per lonc temps e no comfereys al u curacio am medicinas, lahoras cove que cauterizes am cauteri de punt.	When an injury occurs in some member by falling or striking and the pain persists for a long time and does not yield to cure with medicines, then it is necessary that you cauterize with pinpoint cautery.
E sia le cauteri de tot membre segon la magnitut e la parvitat de lu, e vertut e develitat de lu, e locacio de torcio e dolor de lu.	And it is the cautery of each member according to its magnitude and smallness, virtue and revelation, location of twist and pain.
Donc si·s sanat per le primier cauteri, bo es; e sino, lahoras itera sobre lu le cauteri; quar de costuma de aquelas dolors es que sian punctatz de membre ad aquel membre le qual apropinque al u, per que cove que consieguas aquels am cauteri entro que·l malaute sia sanat.	Therefore, if it is healed by the first cautery, good is; and otherwise, then repeat the cautery on it; for it is customary with those pains to be punctured in the member that approaches the one, so that you must achieve those with cautery until the patient is healed.
Capitol .xlvii.	Chapter XLVII.
De cauterizacio de lepra.	On Cauterization of Leprosy.
Les lebros alcunas veguadas am cauteri per mot gran juvament, e magerment si la specia de lepra que es fayta per putrefaccio de flacma e de melencolia.	The lepers sometimes require cauterization for a great benefit, and more so if the species of leprosy is made by the putridity of blood and melancholy.
E donc cum tu vols cauterizar aquel, considera si la lepra es comussan e as aquela curada am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no deysen, ni esta, e temes sobre le malaute que la corrupcio comprehenda tot le cors de lu e tota la compleccio de lu, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre le cap am v cauteris: am un en le mieg loc del cap, e am le segon pus dejos de lu, eves le front a la fi dels cabels; e amdos sobre dos corns; e am un detras, sobre la nuca o servitz.	And therefore, when you wish to cauterize that place, consider if the leprosy is common and has been cured with what we have said in the division and not delayed, nor stopped, and fear for the patient that corruption will encompass all of their body and all its composition, then cauterize it on the head with seven cauteries: one in the middle location of the head, and the second a little behind, up to the forehead; and two on each earlobe; and one behind, on the back of the neck or the nape.
E ultima la tua ma am le cauteri un pauc entro que emprema en le os una petita empressio, e de lu sian deslocadas las scorsas, per so que la expiracio de grossas vapors sia alleujada de lu; e cauteriza sobre la melsa segon que es precesit.	And finally, place your hand with the cautery a little bit until it presses on the bone and leaves a small impression, and from there the scabs are dislodged, so that the expiration of gross vapors is alleviated from them; and cauterize over the swelling according to what has been said.
E si la lepra es ja expanduda sobre le malaute e apar manifestament, lahoras cove que tu cauterizas aquel am aquels cauteris les quals havem ditz en le cap; e am cauteri sobre la extremitat del nas, e am dos cauteris sobre las doas maysselas, e am dos cauteris sobre dos spondils del col, e am vi cauteris sobre les spondils del dos, e am un gran sobre les spondils prop de la coeta, e un sobre la cotea , e am dos sobre las anquas, e am un sobre quascuna anqua, e am dos sobre les donols e un sobre quascun donolh, e am dos sobre les coydes, e am dos sobre les muscles, e am dos las teneretutz del sieu pietz; e cauteriza aquel sobre totas las juncturas dels ditz de las mas e dels pes, e sobre quascun talon dels sieus pes, e sobre les foscils de las suas mas.	And if the leprosy has already expanded over the patient and appears manifestly, then it is necessary that you cauterize that place with those cauteries which we have said in the head; and with one cautery on the tip of the nose, and two on both elbow joints, and two on both vertebrae of the neck, and six on the vertebrae of the back, and one great one on the vertebrae near the coccyx, and one on the coccyx itself, and two on each hip joint, and one on each hip, and two on each ankle, and one on each toe, and two on each calf, and one on each muscle, and two on each tendons of the legs; and cauterize that place on all the joints of the said limbs and feet, and on each heel of their feet, and on the tendons of their arms.
E guarda te dels nervis les quals so sobre le talo que no comburas aquels.	And beware of the nerves which are on the ankle, lest you burn those.
E alcunas veguadas es cauterizat am un cauteri sobre le os del pentenilh e am autre sobre la boca del stomac, e autre sobre le fietge.	And sometimes it is cauterized with a cautery on the bone of the shoulder blade and another on the mouth of the stomach, and another on the liver.
E sapias que quant mays ajustas cauteris, tant es mays juvatiu e mays conferent; e sapias que le malaute no ha en le cauteri dolor, ayssi cum han les sas, per so quar le cors de lu ja es stupefayt.	And know that the more you adjust the cauteries, the more beneficial and conformable it is; and know that the patient does not have pain in the cautery, just as they do in their own flesh, because their body has already been stupified.
E cove que les cauteris sian grans o paucs segon les membres e las juncturas segon que es precedit de las specias dels ferramentz.	And it is necessary that the cauteries be great or small according to the members and joints, as is preceded by the species of instruments.
E aprop cura le cauteri am farina de errs coyta am mel e am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the cautery with flour of earthworms mixed with honey and other remedies until it is healed.
Capitol .xlviii.	Chapter XLVIII.
De cauterizacio de stupor.	On Cauterization of Stupor.
Quan alcun membre es stabozit o adormit e es curat am medicinas, olis e emplastres, e no es sanat, lahoras tu cauteriza aquel membre stabozit am cauteris segon que merita la grandesa del membre o la parvitat de lu.	When some member is stuporized or drowsy and is cured with medicines, oils, and poultices, and it is not healed, then you must cauterize that member with cauteries according to its magnitude or smallness.
E sia lo tieu cauteri intrant la ispicitut de la codena un pauc.	And your cautery should enter the subtlety of the code a little bit.
E aprop cura aquel am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that place with remedies until it is healed.
E alscunas veguadas es cauterizada alcuna stupor le qual endeve a las mas e als pes, e als spondils del dos e ves le eysiment dels nervis les quals mavon aquel membre, e es remauguda la stupor.	And sometimes it is cauterized some stupor which occurs in the arms and legs, and in the vertebrae of the back, and the tension of the nerves which govern that member is released, and the stupor is renewed.
Mays no prusuma sobre aquo sino aquel que es savi en la anotomia dels membre e de la egressio dels nervis tot le cors moventz.	But do not presume on this unless you are knowledgeable in the anatomy of the members and the exit of the nerves throughout the entire moving body.
Capitol .xlix.	Chapter XLIX.
De cauterizacio de albaras que es morfea.	On Cauterization of Moles that are Morfæa.
Quan albaras es antiqua e no comfereys a lu alcu dels enguentz de medicina, lahoras tu cauteriza sobre aquela am cauteri preon un pauc segon la quantitat de la specitut de la codena entro que sia remauguda la blancor e la color de lu, e la color de lu sia mudada.	When moles are old and do not yield to any of the remedies of medicine, then you must cauterize over them with a preon-shaped cautery a little bit according to the quantity of the subtlety of the code, until the whiteness and color of it are restored, and the color of it is changed.
E aprop cura aquel am farina de errs e de lentilhas am oli rozat e am folhas de arnagrosa, e am sanc de colomba o am sanc de yronda, da cascuna sia una partida e totas sian mescladas, e aprop sia linit un drap e sus le loc sia pausat entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that place with flour of earthworms and lentils mixed with rose oil and leaves of arnica, and with the blood of pigeon or the blood of swallow, each being one part and all being mixed together; and apply a cloth and place it on the location until it is healed.
Capitol .l.	Chapter L.
De cauterizacio de cranc.	On Cauterization of Crabs.
Quan canser es comensan e vols aquel ostar, lahoras cauteriza aquel am cauteri de cercle en le circuit de lu ayssi cum es revolgut.	When cancer is beginning and you want to cut it out, then cauterize that place with a circle-shaped cautery in the circuit of it just as it revolves.
E diysero les savis que sia cauterizat am lo derier cauteri en le mieg loc; mays a mi no es vist aquo, quar temi que sia ulcerat, e yeu ja e vist aquo alcunas veguadas.	And they say that it should be cauterized with the last cautery in the middle location; but to me, I have not seen this, for I fear that it will become ulcerated, and I have already seen this some times.
E es pus dreyturier que sia cauterizat en le circuit de lu am cercle ayssi cum avem dit, o am motz cauteris.	And it is better to be cauterized in the circuit of it with a circle just as we have said, or with many cauteries.
Capitol .li.	Chapter LI.
De cauterizacio de adubilati.	On Cauterization of Adulterations.
Quan alcun adubilati es tardat en maturacio, e aysso es per la superfluitat fazen aquela, o per etat del malaute, quar es vielh en decrepitat, de pauc sanc, o per le temps, e tu vols festinar en la maturacio de adubilati; lahoras cauteriza en le circuit de lu am motz cauteris petitz punctan; e aprop leyssa aquela quar ela fastinara en maturacio.	When some adulterations are delayed in maturation, and thus it is due to the superfluity making it so, or because of the condition of the patient, which is old and decrepit, with little blood, or because of time, and you want to hasten the maturation of adulterations; then cauterize in the circuit of it with many small punctate cauteries; and then let that be as it will mature in its proper time.
Mays si tu vols la perforacio de lu am cauteri, lahoras tu igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma de lu: e depausa aquel en le mieg loc de adubilati entro que penetre la codena.	But if you want the perforation of it with a cautery, then ignite the cautery of which this is the form; and place that in the middle location of the adulterations until the code pierces.
E si le cauteri en aquel loc que es pus dejos, per so que le cors del brac sia alleujat; e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if the cautery is applied in that location which is more behind, because the body of the arm is relieved; and then cure that place until it is healed.
Capitol .lii.	Chapter LII.
De cauterizacio de corrodent.	On Cauterization of Corrosions.
Corrodent es corrupcio ambulant en le membre, la qual corrodeys aquel ayssi cum a foc comedent lenha secca.	Corrosion is corruption that walks in the member, which corrupts it just as fire consumes dry wood.
Donc si vezes aquel corrodent en loc le qual sufferte cauteri am foc, lahoras tu igneys cauteris clavils motz paucs, e grans segon que es convenent en aquel loc en le qual es corrodent.	Therefore, if you find that corrosion in a location where it is suitable for cautery with fire, then ignite small to great number of claw-shaped cauteries, and apply them according to what is convenient in that location where the corrosion is.
E aprop cauteriza aquel de tota partida entro que erradiques tota la corrosio e no romangua alcuna causa de lu.	And then cauterize that place entirely until you eradicate all the corrosion and there remains no cause of it.
E aprop leyssa aquel per tres dias, e pausa sobre les locs cauterizats solpre trissat am oli mesclat entro que las scaras sian totas eradicadas e tota la corrupcio.	And then leave that place alone for three days, and pause over the locations that have been cauterized with a mixture of oil and soap until all the scars are eradicated and all corruption is removed.
E aprop cura aquel am enguentz carn engendrantz.	And then cure that place with flesh-generating remedies.
Mays si aprop tres dias vezes que la carn nasca sana en la qual no es corrupcio, bo es; mays sino, lahoras itera le cauteri sobre aquo que es romas en les locs corrumputz.	But if after three days the flesh grows healthy and there is no corruption in it, good is; but if not, then repeat the cautery over that which remains in the corrupted areas.
E corrodent es medicat alcunas vetz am medicina aguda, quar aquela es meza en loc de cauteri.	And corrosion is treated with some sharp medicines, because it is a halfway point between cautery and medicine.
Mays empero cauteri am foc es de pus leugier juvament.	But however, cautery by fire is of greater benefit.
E yeu ja e dit la curacio de lu am medicina aguda en la divisio, e donc pren aquela quan de lu auras endegencia.	And I have already said the cure with sharp medicine in the division; therefore take it when you have need of it.
Capitol .liii.	Chapter LIII.
De cauterizacio de claus e dels autres semblants.	On Cauterization of Knots and other Similarities.
Motas veguadas endeve a las partidas dejos del pe malautia que s’apela clau, e es causa grossa, fentrada, la qual ladeys le pe; e cauteri en aquels es segon dos manieyras, so es cauteri am foc e cauteri am aygua cauda.	Many times there is a growth in the leftover parts of the foot that is called a knot, and it is a big, deep cause which lames the foot; and cautery is done on those according to two methods, that is, with fire and with hot water.
Mays cauteri am foc es que igniscas le cauteri concau semblant a pena de voltor, le qual sia feyt de ferr segon la quantitat la qual contengua le clau de tota partida, e sia de subtils marguas.	But the cautery with fire is when you ignite the concave-like cauteri resembling a small wheel, which is made of iron according to the quantity that contains the knot of all parts, and it should be of fine margins.
E aprop pausa aquel ignit sobre le clau, e aprop revolveys la tua ma am le cauteri en le circuit del clau entro que·l cauteri pervengua a la profunditat del clau.	And then pause that which is ignited over the knot, and then revolve your hand with the cautery in the circuit of the knot until the cautery reaches the depth of the knot.
E leyssa aquel per tres dias entro que comense getar brac.	And then leave that place alone for three days until the knot begins to fall off.
E aprop emplastre aquel am malvas salvatges trissadas am sal, e leyssa le emplastre sobre aquel per una nuoyt, quar aquel sira eradicat de las suas razitz.	And then apply that place with wild marjoram leaves mixed with salt, and leave the poultice on that place for one night, so that it is eradicated from its roots.
E aprop cura le loc am enguent de carn generatiu entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that place with flesh-generating remedies until it is healed.
E si so no-convertitz, e motas veguadas accideysso en la superficia del cors, majorment en las mas e les pes, lahoras cove que tu aministres en aquels cauteri am aygua, e es que prenguas una quannula de eram o de ferr o de pena de voltor, e pausa aquela sobre le clau; e aprop geta en la quanula de aygua cauda pauca cantitat, e rete la tua ma, e tu revolveys aquela am compressio de la tua ma de tot, e sia enpremut le marge de la canula en la razit del clau, e atrobara la aygua cauda via al preon de la razit del cau; e espera le malaute un pauc la mordicacio de l’aygua cauda per una hora, e aprop remau aquela, quar le clau am las suas razitz sira erredicat.	And if it does not convert, and many times it occurs on the surface of the body, mostly in the arms and legs, then you must administer cauterization with water, and this is done by taking a hollow reed or iron rod or a wheel-shaped piece, and placing that on the knot; and then take a small quantity of hot water, and pour it into the canula, and hold your hand, and revolve that with compression of your hand all over, so that the margin of the canula is pressed against the root of the knot, and let the hot water flow back through the reed to the root of the cau; and wait for the patient a little while for the mordicating effect of the hot water for one hour, and then remove it, because the knot with its roots will be eradicated.
E ayssi fe am aquels la i aprop l’autre entro que venguas sobre totz les quals de lor so en le cors.	And thus do this to those and the other one until you come to all of them on whose body it is.
E aprop cura aquels pus que las razitz dels claus so erradicadas am aquo dels enguentz les quals la carn ve engenran.	And then cure those places where the roots of the knots are eradicated with this water of remedies which causes flesh to regenerate.
Capitol .liiii.	Chapter LIV.
De cauterizacio de tremor.	On Cauterization of Tremors.
Quan endeve ad alcu tremor per freg en le nervi o per febre de causa frega, o per autra causa semblant, lahoras cove que tu cauterises aquel am quatre cauteris o am v sobre les spondils del dos, entre quascun spondilh am un cauteri; e am cauteri en le pietz de lu, e sobre l‘estomac de lu, am cauteri olivar.	When there is a tremor due to fright in the nerves or due to fever caused by fright, or for another similar reason, then it is necessary that you cauterize that place with four or five cauteries placed between each vertebra of the back; and with one cautery on the legs and over the stomach of the patient, with an olive-shaped cautery.
E la tremor de lu se repausa e festina la sanetat de la malautia frega.	And the tremor ceases and hastens the recovery of the patient from the frightful illness.
Capitol .lv.	Chapter LV.
De cauterizacio de albati accidentz al cors.	On Cauterization of Accidental White Spots on the Body.
Quan en le cors so espellitz albati, e so pustulas fendas las quals so feytas de materias grossas corruptas; donc cove al comensament cum apareyso, que sia cauterizat sobre tot cap de la fistola am cauteri subtil am fustz de mirt, la extremitat del qual es estenduda am foc; o am razitz de erestologia longua; o am cauteri lentecular.	When white spots are formed on the body and pustules burst open which are made of thick corrupted matter; therefore it is necessary at first as it appears, that a subtle cautery be applied to the head of the fistula with a myrtle-shaped cauteri whose end is extended in fire; or with the roots of long-lasting erestology; or with a lentecular cautery.
E alscunas veguadas es cauteri ademamil al comensament de la sua expulcio segon aquesta manieyra; e no so cregudas, e es disrumpuda la superfluitat fazens aquels, et sana de aquels.
