And sometimes it is necessary to cauterize again at the beginning of its expulsion according to this method; and do not believe, and the superfluity making those things ceases, and cures those.
Mays empero cove que aquo sia fayt aprop evacuacio am fleubotomia.	But however, it is necessary that this be done properly with evacuation by phlebotomy.
Capitol lvi.	Chapter LVI.
De cauterizacio de fluex de sanc accident per incisio de arceria.	On Cauterization of Accidental Bleeding due to Incision of Artery.
Tropas veguadas endeve fluex de arceria que es inciza deves la plagua la qual endeve deforo, o deves la incizio de apostemas o cauteri del membre, e alor semblantz, e es dificil remaura aquel.	Many times there is bleeding from an artery which is cut by the wound or by the incision of apostemes or cauteries on the member, and then similar things happen, and it is difficult to stop that bleeding.
Donc cum accideys ad alcu aquo, lahoras tu·t coyta am la tua ma a l’orrifici de la arceria, e pausa sobre aquel le tieu dit endic estrenh aquel motas veguadas entro que sia ostat le fluex del sanc dejos le tieu dit, e que non yesqua.	Therefore, as it happens with some water, then you must take your hand to the orifice of the artery and place on that the said cauteri, and apply it many times until the bleeding stops and there is no more.
E aprop pausa en le foc les cauteris olivars paucs e grantz, per nombre motz, e exsuffla sobre aquels entro que sian mot ignitz.	And then pause in the fire with small and large olive-shaped cauteries, by number of points, and blow over them until they are thoroughly ignited.
E aprop pren de aquels un petit o un gran segon le loc e la plagua en la qual es rompuda la arteria, sobre aquela vena festinantment pus que auras remaugut le tieu dit, e te le cauteri entro que sia abcindit e restreyt aquel sanc.	And then take one small or one large cautery from those, according to the location and wound where the artery is broken, and place it on that vein hastening more than you have previously applied the said cautery, until the bleeding is stopped and contained.
E si le sanc es expellit de l’orrifici de la arteria quan tu remaues le tieu dit e extringeys le cauteri, lahoras pren la un autre cauteri coytadament dels cauteris les quals en le foc son preparatz, e donc no cesses fer aquo un aprop autre entro que le sanc sia restrengit.	And if the blood is expelled from the orifice of the artery when you remove the said cautery and extinguish it, then take another cautery carefully from among the cauteries that are prepared in the fire, and therefore do not cease to do this repeatedly until the bleeding is stopped.
E guarda te que no comburas le nervi que aqui es, e que vengua sobre le malaute autra malicia.	And beware that you do not burn the nerves which are here, and that you bring other evil upon the patient.
E sapias que quan de l’arteria flueys sanc, lahoras no es possible en aquels restrenge la sanc, e majorment quan l’arteria es gran, si no am una de quatre manieyras: o am cauteri ayssi quo dit havem, o am extraccio quan no es extrayta, quar quan es extrayta las extremitatz de lu miels son comburidas e es restreyt le sanc, o que sia liat am fiel o am liament per fort strectura, o que sian pausadas sobre lu medicinas de las quals la vertut es restringir la sanc; e sian strengudas am pulvinar am costriccio decent.	And know that when blood flows from the artery, it is not possible to stop the bleeding in those cases, and especially when the artery is large, unless by one of four methods: or with a cautery as we have said, or by extraction when it is not extracted, because when it is extracted the extremities of it are burned and the bleeding is stopped, or that it be tied with thread or ligament by strong constriction, or that medicines which have the virtue of restricting blood flow be applied to it; and they must be strengthened with a poultice and decent constriction.
Mays aquel que aministra restriccio decent de lu am liament e am strictura am draps o per posicio de causas comburentz e de semblantz, no comfereys sino tart.	But he who administers restraint by way of ligament and constriction with cloths or by position of causes that burn and similar things does not yield quickly.
Mays si aquo endeve ad alcu e no sia le metge present ni medicina, lahoras obre am pausament del dit indic sobre le orrifici de aquela vena ayssi cum havem dit, e entenda a la gran costreccio de lu entro que le sanc sia ostat de la sobirana partida de la plagua, e sobre la arceria le dit no sia remaugut; e de sobre la arceria sia aspergit am aygua frega de mot gran fregiditat entro que·l sanc sia congilat e engrossat; e mays cossire en que ha de cauteri o de medicina necessitat.	But if this happens in some place and there is no doctor present or medicine, then work with a pause of the said cautery on the orifice of that vein just as we have said, and understand the great constriction of it until the bleeding stops from the highest part of the wound, and over the artery let it not be removed; and on the artery be sprinkled with cold water of great coolness until the blood is congealed and thickened; and further in what has to do with cauteri or medicine needed.
Comensa la segonda partida.	The second part begins.
De incisio e perforacio e ventozas e de fleubotomia e de plaguas e de lor semblants.	On Incision, Perforation, Ventoses, Phlebotomy, Wounds and their Similarities.
Aquestas son paraulas de Albucazis.	These are the words of Albucasis.
Ja havem dit en le primier capitol tota malautia en la qual cauteri am foc es convenient e am medicina comburent, e las occasios e las causas de lu, e les instrumentz en aquels necessaris am las formas dels cauteris; e he ordenatz les capitols de la subiranetat del cap entro als pes.	We have already said in the first chapter about all diseases in which cautery with fire is suitable and with medicine that burns, and the occasions and causes of it, and the instruments necessary for those things in the forms of cauteries; and we have arranged the chapters of the subordination of the head to the feet.
E yeu procesire en aquest capitol per aquela meteysa guisa, per que sia alliujat lo querent aquo, lahoras sobre aquo que aura demandat.	And you will proceed in this chapter by that same manner, so that it may be helpful to the one seeking it, namely on what he has requested.
E denant que yeu comense aquo, cove, fils, que aprenguatz que en aquest capitol es per terror aquo que es en le capitol primier de cauterizacio.	And before you begin this, it is necessary, sons, that you learn that in this chapter it is about terror, which is in the first chapter of cauterization.
E per aquo que cove que sia en lu gran cautela, quar en la operacio la qual es en aquest capitol motas veguadas catz evacuacio la qual es am sanc am le qual esta la vida deves la aspersio de la vena o incisio sobre l’apostema o apercio de exsitura o puracio de la plagua o extraccio de sageta o incizio de peyra e a lor semblantz.	And therefore it is necessary that there be great caution, because in the operation which is in this chapter, many times evacuation occurs, which is with blood, and to which life belongs, and so the sprinkling of the vein or incision on the apostema or warning of existence or purification of the wound or extraction of splinter or incision of peyra and their similar things.
E de totz aquels so acompanhatz temor e tremor e en le mas de lor catz la mort.	And among all those, there is accompanied fear and trembling, and in most of them death.
E yeu amonesti vos que sobre vos no caia aquo en le qual es esitacio, quar alcunas veguadas cazo deves vos manieyras de homes am manieyras motas de malautias.	And you are warned that this should not fall on you, because sometimes the case requires the methods of men with many diseases.
E de lor es alcu que s’irays am la sua malautia e es leugiera deves lu la mort, e aysso per la vehemensia de aquo que troba de sa malautia, e per longuesa de la malautia de lu, e am la malautia es paor la qual significa mort.	And some of them flee from their disease and it is light for them to die, and thus because of the vehemence of this that they find in their disease, and due to the length of their illness, and with the disease there is fear which means death.
E de aquels es le qual dona a tu son aver e ditta, tu esperant am aquel sanetat, e la sieua malautia es perniciosa.	And one of them is the one who gives you their property and wealth, while you are expecting their health, and their disease is deadly.
E donc no cove que tu consentas en aquel que ve a vos del qual es aquesta manieyra; e la vostra cautela sia major que covesitat e la vostra rapacitat; e no presumatz alcuna causa sobre aquo sino aprop sciencia certa la qual virifica aquo deves vos, e al qual perve successio lausabla.	And therefore it is not necessary that you consent to him who comes to you with this manner; and your caution should be greater than covetousness and rapacity; and do not assume any cause about this without proper certain science which verifies what you are, and by which you will have a praiseworthy succession.
E usatz en la curacio de totz vostres malautes de pronosticacio e indicacio de lu al qual es salut convertida, quar en aquel es a vos ajutori sobre adquisicio de fama e de memoria, de lausor e de gloria.	And use in the cure of all your diseases prognosis and indication from that which is converted to health, for in that is aid to you on acquisition of fame and memory, praise and glory.
O, filhs, Dieus en vos spire le sieu entendement e no oste a vos direccio e proteccio, quar aquo es en la sua ma.	Oh, sons, God inspires his understanding in you and does not withhold direction and protection from you, for this is in his hand.
E yeu e ordenat aquest capitol distingent per capitols segon que precedit en le capitol de cauteris, de la cura del cap entro als pes, per que sia a vos alleujat aquo que demandatz de aquo e del qual havetz necessitat.	And you have arranged this chapter distinct by chapters according to what preceded in the chapter on cauteries, from the cure of the head to the feet, so that it may be helpful to you in what you request and need.
Capitol primier.	Chapter I.
De la curacio de aygua la qual es contenguda en le cap dels enfantz.	On the Cure of Water which is contained in the Head of Children.
Sapias que aquesta malautia motas veguadas endeve als enfantz deves le enfantament e quan la noyrissa estrenh le cap del enfant ses livitat.	Know that this disease often occurs in children, especially during childbirth, when the midwife tightens the child's head.
E alcunas veguadas endeve per causa amaguada la qual no es saubuda.	And sometimes it occurs due to a hidden cause which is not known.
Mays yeu no vi aquesta malautia sino en les enfantz; e a totz aquels les quals yeu vi se coytec la mort, e per ayssi es a mi vist layssada obra en aquels.	But I have not seen this disease except in children; and all those whom I have seen have been brought to the point of death, and thus it has been shown to me as a work that is left undone in them.
E yeu e vist que un enfant le cap del qual era d’aygua omplit, e·l cap de lu era totjorn ayssi magnificat entro que ceser no podia sobre si meteys per la grandesa del sieu cap, e mays que la humiditat fe aucmentada entro que foc mort.	And I have seen that a child whose head was filled with water overflowed, and the head of him was always thus magnificently swollen to the point where it could not be contained on its own, but rather increased in moisture until it became hot death.
E aquesta humiditat o es agreguada entre la codena e l’os, o es agreguada dejos le os sobre le ciphac.	And this moisture either accumulates between the vertebrae and the bone, or accumulates behind the bone above the spine.
Quar la operacio en aquel si la humiditat es entre la codena e l’os e le apostema es pauc, lahoras cove que tu fendas en le mieg loc del cap am una fissura en la latitut, e sia la longitut de la fissura cays dos notz entro que corra la humiditat, e aquesta es la forma del spatum:	For the operation in that case if the moisture is between the vertebrae and the bone and the apostema is slight, then it is necessary for you to make an incision in the middle of the head with a fissure in the latitude, and the length of the fissure should be two nights so that the moisture may flow, and this is the form of the spatum:
E donc si la humiditat es mays augmentada e l’apostema es major, lahoras son aqui dos fissuras segon aquesta manieyra:	And therefore if the moisture is further increased and the apostema is greater, then there are two incisions in this manner:
E si la humiditat es dejos le os, senhal de lu es que tu vezes la comissuras del cap ubertas de tota partida e l’aygua es spremuda quan tu compremes aquela am la tieua ma a las partidas dedintz e no es aquo a tu amaguat.	And if the moisture is behind the bone, then the sign of it is that you should cut open the commissures of the head from all sides and the water will be squeezed out when you compress that with your hand on the parts inside and it is not hidden from you.
Cove que tu fendas en le mieg loc del cap am tres fissuras segon aquesta manieyra:	It is necessary for you to make an incision in the middle of the head with three incisions in this manner:
e aprop la inscizio extratz ne tota la humiditat; e aprop strenh las fissuras am draps e plumassols; e aprop enbroca aquo de sobre am vi e oli entro al quint dia, e aprop deslia le liament e cura la plagua am tentas e enguentz, e strenh le cap am equalitat; e mange le malaute am vianda secca de pauca humiditat entro que·l membre sia confortat e sanat.	And then apply the incision and extract all the moisture; and then strengthen the incisions with cloths and poultices; and then envelop this in a wrapping of vinegar and oil for five days, and then release the ligament and cure the wound with tentas and enguentz, and strengthen the head with equality; and feed the patient with dry food with little moisture until the member is comforted and healed.
E es autra manieyra de incisio, que consideras hon apar la magnitut del apostema e la colleccio de l’aygua, quar alcunas veguadas es mays en le occipicii, o en la partida denant, o en la destra, o en la sinistra; e donc aten am la incizio on appar le apostema e la replecio de l’aygua, e fen aquo segon que a tu es miels possible.	And there is another way of incision, which you should consider according to the magnitude of the apostema and the collection of water, for sometimes it appears more in the occiput, or in the front part, or on the right side, or on the left side; and therefore attend to the incision where the apostema appears and the replenishment of water, and make it so that it is most suitable for you.
Et observa que no inscindas la arteria e endevengua flueys de sanc e mora le malaute per aquel flux de sanc am evacuacio de humiditat.	And observe that you should not incise the artery and thereby cause bleeding of blood, and let the patient die from that flow of blood with evacuation of moisture.
Capitol .ii.	Chapter II.
De inscisio de las arterias las quals so aprop las aurelhas, apeladas hilasseysse.	On the Incision of the Arteries which are near the Ears, called Hilasseysse.
Capitol segon.	Chapter III.
Quan endeveno ad alcu catars o raumas als huelhs o al pietz, e es antiquat aquo, e no confereys en aquo la curacio de las medicinas, lahoras la deriera curacio en aquest es incizio de aquelas dos arterias.	When it happens to some that they have catarrhs or wounds in the eyes or feet, and this is old-fashioned, and does not conform with the cure of medicines, then the final cure in this case is incision of those two arteries.
E donc cove quan tu vols inscidir aquelas que le malaute raza lo sieu cap, e aprop fregua le loc am drap aspre per so que aparan las arcerias, e aprop sia strengut le col del malaute am alcu drap; e aprop considera on polsa la vena; e les locs de quascuna sobre les locs les quals so aprop las aurelhas depremutz, e tant se occultan sino en alcus homes.	And therefore it is necessary when you want to incise those that the patient's head swells, and then gently rub the location with a rough cloth so that the arteries appear, and then strengthen the neck of the patient with some cloth; and then consider where the vein pulsates; and the locations of each over the locations which are near the ears, repressed, and only in some men.
E aprop senha sobre la arceria am tenta, e aprop inscideys quascuna am le spatum de quascuna partida agut am inscizio pervenient entro al os, e sia aquo per la latitut del cap.	And then sign on the artery with a tentacle, and then incise each one with the spatula of each side approaching to the bone, and be it so for the latitude of the head.
E si vols, entromet le spatum dejos la arteria e trenqua aquala a las inciden a las partidas desus.	And if you wish, enter the spatula below the artery and cut it at the incisions on each side.
E sia la longitut de la inscizio cays dos ditz ajustatz, quar quan alcuna vena es inscizida le sanc es eyssit am egressio pulsatil, le qual saut deforo per saut frequent.	And be the length of the incision about two inches adjusted, for when some vein is incised, the blood flows out with pulsatile egression, which jumps forth frequently.
Mays si la arceria no apareys al cintiment, lahoras cove que tu mesures de la aurelha la quantitat del spazi de tres ditz, e aprop senha am tenta, e fen entro al os.	But if the artery does not appear at the incision, then it is necessary for you to measure from the ear the quantity of space of three fingers, and then sign with a tentacle, and enter into the bone.
E aquo que cove getar del sanc es quantitat de vi unc., e fort leu ne geta de lu mays o mens, e tot aquo es segon la quantitat la qual appareys de la vertut del malaute e de la replecio de la arceria de lu.	And as much blood as is needed to be gotten is one vessel's worth of blood. and not too little or too much is gotten from the patient, and all this is according to the quantity which appears of the virtue of the disease and the replenishment of the artery in him.
E aprop considera la plagua, e donc si reman sobre le os alcuna causa del ciphac, lahoras inscindys aquo per so que no endevengua apostema caut.	And then consider the wound, and therefore if some cause of the spine remains on the bone, then incise this so that it does not develop into a painful apostema.
E aprop strenh la plagua am plumassols e am liamentz de drap de li, e aprop cura aquela am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then strengthen the wound with poultices and ligatures of linen cloth, and then cure it with ointments until it is healed.
Capitol .iii.	Chapter III.
De extraccio de las arcerias las quals so en las templas.	On the Extraction of the Arteries which are in the Temples.
Quan ad alcu accideys emigranea antiqua o catertz agutz, per humiditatz agrimonials e per qualiditat en les lacertz des templas, o sodo antiqua vehement e semblantz ad aquels, e es medicat am las manieyras de curacio de medicina e aquo no comfereys, lahoras nos hem sproatz en aquestas malautias extraccio de las arcerias en les templas, o cauterizacio de aquelas ayssi cum havem mostrat.	When to some it happens that ancient emigration or sharp catarrh occurs, due to humid and grueling conditions in the temples, or old-fashioned violent symptoms similar to those, and is medicated with the methods of medicinal cure, but this does not conform, then we have resolved to extract the arteries in the temples, or cauterize them thus as we have shown.
E la manieyra de la operacio e extracio de aquelas es que·l malaute raza les pels les quals son en les templas; e entenda a la arceria apparent en le templar quar ela es a tu mostrada per le sieu pols, e·s occultada sino en paucs homes per vehemencia de freg.	And the method of the operation and extraction is that the patient shows the arteries which are in the temples; and understand the apparent artery in the temple because it is shown to you by its pulsation, and it is hidden from most men except for a few due to the vehemence of the friction.
E si a tu es occultada, lahoras le col del malaute sia strengut am alcun drap; e aprop fregua le loc am un drap aspre o evapora le loc am aygua cauda entro que aparesca a tu la arceria manifestament.	And if it is hidden from you, then the neck of the patient should be strengthened with some cloth; and then gently rub the location with a rough cloth or evaporate the location with warm water until the artery becomes manifest to you.
E lahoras tu pren le spatum del qual aquesta es la forma:	And then take the spatula of which this is the form:
E aprop tu scorja la codena am aquel am facilitat entro que pervenguas a la arceria; e aprop geta en lu onti e extratz aquela a las partidas sobiranas entro que extraguas aquela de la codena e descobras aquela de las tunicas las quals so dejos aquela, de tota partida.	And then gently scrape the vertebra with that spatula with ease until you reach the artery; and then get into it and extract that part above all, and extract it from the vertebra and uncover those tunics which are below it, on all sides.
Mays si la arteria es subtil, lahoras envolveys aquela am la extremitat del oncii, e aprop inscindeys de aquela una partida segon la quantitat per la qual sian alonguadas las extremitatz de lu e sian contraytas, e no endevindra flux de sanc, quar si no so inscididas no pujara le sanc de tot.	But if the artery is fine, then wrap it around with the extremity of the onyx, and then incise one part of that according to the quantity by which its extremities are lengthened and contracted, and do not allow a flow of blood, for if they are not incised, the blood will not rise at all.
E aprop evacua del sanc de vi unc. entro a tres.	And then evacuate one vessel's worth of blood. into three.
E si la arceria es gran, lahoras cove que tu lies aquela en dos locs am fiel dopble fort de ceda o am cordas a lonc, e no coyte a lu putrefaccio denant la consolidacio de la plagua e endevengua flux de sanc.	And if the artery is large, then it is necessary for you to ligate that in two places with a double knot of thread or with cords as long, and do not allow putrefaction before the consolidation of the wound and prevent blood flow.
E aprop incideys la superfluitat la qual es entre dos liamentz; e fay aquo en aquela hora o aprop autra ora.	And then incise the superfluity which is between two ligatures; and do this at that hour or at another hour.
E si vols, cauteriza aquela am cauteri entro al os am cauteri cutellar entro que sian incididas las extramitatz de lu, e stara en loc de aquela meteyssa obra.	And if you wish, cauterize that with a cauterizer into the bone and with a cauterizer in the shape of a knife, so that the extremities are incised, and remain in its place as an intermediate work.
E es milhor obra sino que·l malaute aia febre o es de escalfada compleccio; quar cauteri es de aquelas causas que ajudan a las humiditatz finidoras, e donc es milhor en juvament.	And it is better work if the patient has fever or is of scalded complexion; for cauterization is one of those causes that helps to finish off the humidities, and therefore it is better in judgment.
E cove aprop la extraccio de las arcerias que huomplas le loc de coto antic, e sian pausatz sobre lu polvils decentement fayt, e aprop sia curat am medicinas seccas fazen naysser la carn e am calguas entro que sia sanat.	And it is necessary to carefully extract the arteries that fill up the old cut, and let them be placed on the polyps decently made, and then let it be cured with dry medicines making the flesh appear and with some ointment until it is healed.
E si mentre obres autra veguada endeventa flux de sanc de la arceria, lahora tu te coyta a restrenger aquel sanc, o am cauteri, o que omplas le loc de coto, e strenh la tua ma entro que sia restreyt le sanc.	And if while you are working on another occasion there occurs a flow of blood from the artery, then immediately grasp to stop that blood, or with cauterization, or by filling up the old cut, and strengthen your hand until the blood is stopped.
E si deguna causa de aquelas no es a tu present, lahoras pausa le tieu dit sobre le loc entro que·l sanc sia congilat, e enbroca le loc am aygua de vehement fregiditat entro que la acuitat repausa, e sia strengut segon que cove.	And if any of these causes is not present to you, then pause your hand on the location until the blood is congealed, and envelop the location with warm water of fervent heat so that the sharpness may rest, and be strengthened according to what is necessary.
E aquo que es pus leugier en extraccio de arceria es que tu cauterizes la vena am aquest cauteri haventz dos cotels, pus que tu has senhat les dos locs am tenta, e depausa quascus, mot ignitz, entro que pervenguan al os e inscindan la vena en dos locs, per so que sia elonguat aquo que es entre las extremitatz de lu, quar no son consolidadas de tot am aquest cauteri.	And what is easier in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cauterizer having two blades, because you have marked the two locations with a tentacle, and then lay each one aside, entirely extinguished, until they reach the bone and incise the vein in two places, so that what is between its extremities may be lengthened, for it is not completely consolidated by this cauterization.
E aquesta es la forma del cauteri:	And this is the form of the cauterizer:
E sia la acuitat dels dos cotels esemps.	And the sharpness of the two blades is an example.
Mays empero si so mendres acuitat que dos cotels es milhor, quar si so agudas cum dos cotels propera a quascuna freg, e no enscideysso la carn am velocitat.	But if it has less sharpness than two blades, then it is better, for if it is as sharp as two blades near each other, and does not cut the flesh with speed.
Donc cum en aquels es alcuna grossitut, es tenguda la calor del foc en aquels e la carn es abscindida leugierament.	Therefore, since in those there is some thickness, it is held that the heat of the fire is kept in them and the flesh is cut away slightly.
E aquesta obra es milhor en tota obra e pus leugiera.	And this work is better than all other works and easier to accomplish.
E sia le spazi le qual es entre dos cotels la quantitat de la grossesa del dit.	And the space between the two blades should be equal to the thickness of the said digit.
Capitol quart.	Chapter IV.
De la cura de cors de lagremas agudas e aciduas dels huels.	On the Cure of Corrupted Eyes with Sharp and Acid Tears from the Ears.
Quan so lagremas aciduas, e es le cors de aquelas venas las quals so sobre le test del cap deforo, e no comfereys en aquo alcuna causa de la curacio de medicina, e vezes la cara del malaute ja enrogesir e sent en le sieu front deambulacio ayssi cum si era deambulacio de formiguas, e·ls huels de aquel so extenuatz, humitz enayssi que ja les pels de lor son conodutz, e las parpelas so scalfadas per la acuitat de las lacrimas, les antics agro mesties en la curacio de aquelas de aquesta operacio, e nompnero aquela curacio am spassa.	When there are acid tears, and the eyes of those veins which are above the forehead of the head protrude forth, and do not conform to any cause of medicinal cure, and the face of the patient is already inflamed and feels in its own forehead a wandering like that of ants, and the ears of that person are exhausted, moistened and worn out as if their skin was condensed, and the eyelids are scarred by the sharpness of the tears, those ancient agrumists mixed in the cure of these with this operation, and called it "spassa" curation.
E es que tu comandas al malaute rayre les pels les quals son en le sieu front, e aprop inscideys en le front tres fissuras engualment distans segon la longitut del front.	And it is that you command the patient to tear off the skin which is on his forehead, and then incise three fissures equally distant along the length of the forehead.
E si’ la longitut de la fissura cays dos ditz: la una fissura sia engualment distant a la longitut del nas en le mieg loc del front, e la segonda segon la longitut un petit del movement dels lacertz les quals so en le lacrimal, e la tersa del autre part.	And if the length of the fissure is two fingers: one fissure should be equally distant from the length of the nose in the middle of the forehead, and the second according to the length of a little finger movement of the eyelids which are in the lacrimal, and the third on the other side.
E guarda te de la incizio de las arcerias las quals so en dos latz, e elongua la tua ma de la continuacio de amdos las mandibulas.	And beware of the incision of the arteries which are in two sides, and stretch your hand from the continuation of both jawbones.
E si’ l’espazi de quascuna inscizio la quantitat de tres ditz ajustatz.	And if the space between each incision is equal to three fingers adjusted.
E si’ a tu una pessa d’espongua apparelhada o draps seccatz motz am les quals exsiccas le sanc.	And if you have a piece of sponge apparatus or dry cloths, moistened and saturated with which the blood is absorbed.
E aprop entremet le spatum de dos agudas extremitatz, del qual aquesta es la forma de la inscisio de lu:	And then insert the spatula of two sharp extremities, of which this is the form of the incision:
que es de la partida des templas entro a la segonda inscizio.	which is from the side of the temples to the second incision.
Exxcorja am aquel tota la codena la qual es entre dos incizios am le ciphac le qual es sobre le os, e aprop fay aquo de la inscizio migera entro a la segonda inscisio.	Scrape away with that all the cord which is between two incisions on the spine which is above the bone, and then make this move of the incision to migrate into the second incision.
E aprop stratz ne aquest spatum e entromet en la primieyra inscizio autra vetz un autre instrument le qual es apelat cutellar, agut de una part e del autre no agut.	And then place this spatula aside and insert another instrument called "cutellar", sharp on one side and not sharp on the other.
E pausa le latz de aquel agut deves la carn annexa deves la codena, e le latz de lu leon dintz le os, e empelley aquel entro que pervengua a la fissura migera, e abscindeys am aquel totz les vaysels que descendo del cap als huels.	And pause the blade of that cutellar so as to cut through the flesh attached to the cord, and the blade of it cuts down into the bone, and push that forward until it reaches the middle fissure, and cut away with it all the vessels that descend from the head to the ears.
Mays que sia continuada la inscizio ad aquo appar de la codena, e aprop fay aquo en la fissura migana entro al autra fissura.	But continue the incision up to where the cord appears, and then make this move in the middle fissure into another fissure.
E pus que corr del sanc quantitat engual, exprem les locs de las pessas del sanc congilat.	And since there is a quantity of blood that has coagulated, express the places of the pessaries where the blood has been collected.
E aprop pausa en quascuna fissura calgua de coto vielh, e pausa sobre aquels polvils enbegutz en vi e oli e vi agre, e vegas que no endevengua apostema caut.	And then pause in each fissure the old cut and pause over those polyps begotten in wine and oil and vinegar, and be careful that it does not develop into a painful apostema.
E en le tertz dia deslia le liament e aministra gran enfusio de aygua cauda o tebeza, e aprop cura aquo am enguent bazilicon am oli rozat e autres entro que las plaguas sian sanadas.	And on the third day release the ligature and administer great enthusiasm of warm water or tub, and then cure it with ointment made from basilikon oil and other things until the wounds are healed.
Capitol .v.	Chapter V.
De la cura de lagramas per catartz e als huels descendentz de las partidas dedintz del cap.	On the Cure of Lagrams by Catarrh and to the Ears, which descend from the parts behind the head.
Quan ad alcu veno catartz agutz e continuantz, e vezes les huels del malaute extenuatz petitz, e ja le reguardament de lor es debelitat, e las palpebras ulceradas e de lor cazo les pels, e en le preon del cap es dolor aguda ledent e extrenutacio consequent, lahoras sapias per aquestz accidentz que las materias e catartz no veno sino de motas venas de las partidas dedintz procedent.	When there occurs in some patient sharp and continuous catarrh, and the ears of that person are exhausted and small, and already the regard of them is debilitated, and the eyelids are ulcerated and their skin peeled away, and in the forehead of the head there is acute pain leading to exhaustion, then it is necessary to understand by these accidents that the matters and catarrh do not come from only a few veins but from many parts behind proceeding.
E la milhor curacio en aquels es aquesta: que comandes al malaute que raza lo sieu front, e aprop inscideys en aquel una fissura al mieg loc del front, un petit per la latitut (e comensa am la fissura del templar senestre entro al dextre templar; e sia inscisio entro al os; e eslongua la tua ma dels lacertz del templas lesquals son maugutz deves la mastigacio), entro que sia le os descubert.	And the best cure for these is this: that you command the patient to scratch his forehead, and then incise a fissure in the middle of the forehead, a little bit for the latitude (and start with the fissure of the left temple into the right temple; and be the incision into the bone; and stretch your hand over the eyelids of the temples which are above the mastigatio), until the bone is uncovered.
Exsicca tot le sanc am espongua o am drap secc e aprop repleys entre las doas labias de la fissura am coto vielh o am draps de li.	Absorb all the blood with sponge or dry cloth and then fill it between the two lips of the fissure with old cut or dry cloths.
E aprop estrenh desus am polvils enbegutz en vi e oli per so que no endevengua apostema caut.	And then strengthen above on those polyps begotten in wine and oil, so that it does not develop into a painful apostema.
E quan deslias aquo e veses que l’apostema ja es diminuit, lahoras cove que fregua le os entro que comensa en lu nayser carn, e aprop cura aquel am regiment exsiccatiu le qual fassa neysser la carn, ayssi cum si tu prenes de farina de froment dos partidas e de colofania quatre partidas e mescla o, e de lor sia fayt emplastre e sia aministrat en aquestas plaguas a de la carn nativitat.	And when you have removed that and see that the apostema has decreased, then it is necessary to rub the bone until it begins to produce flesh, and then cure it with an emollient regimen which makes the flesh appear, just as if you take two parts of wheat flour and four parts of colophony and mix them together, and from it make a poultice and administer it in these wounds for the nativity of flesh.
Capitol .vi.	Chapter VI.
De la cura de aquo que catz en las aurelhas.	On the Cure of that which catarrhous in the Ears.
Tota causa que catz en las aurelhas es una de quatre specias, quar o es peyra mineral o causa semblant a peyra, ayssi cum ferr e veyre, o es de planta ayssi cum ceze o fava, o es causa fluxtibla ayssi cum aygua e vi agre e a lor semblantz, o alcuna bestia.	All causes that occur in the ears are one of four species, because either it is mineral or something similar to mineral, like iron and copper, or it is from plants, such as cheese or fava, or it is a fluid cause, like water and vinegar and their semblances, or some animal.
E donc quan peyra catz en l’aurelha o autra causa semblant de aquelas causas que no ajustan ne creysso en l’aurelha, e pausa la aurelha al solelh, e si vezes la peyra, lahoras distilla en aquela alcuna causa de oli violat o sizami, e aprop aministra la extraccio de lu, e fay le stornudar am condizi, e oppila las nars deve le aveniment de stornutacio.	And therefore when mineral or some similar cause occurs in the ear that does not adjust or believe in the ear, and pauses the ear at the sun, and if the mineral is sometimes present, it is necessary to distill in that certain causes of oil of vitriol or sassafras, and then administer the extraction of it, and make the stornudation in conditions, and open the nostrils before the event of stornutiation.
E aprop pausa en le circuit de la aurelha alscunas pessas de drap o lana, e dextendas la aurelha a las partidas desus, quar motas veguadas es foro-getada am aquestas causas.	And then pause in the circuit of the ear with some pieces of cloth or wool, and extend the ear to the upper parts, because many times it is forgotten about these causes.
E si no n’es getada, lahoras aministra extraccio de lu am le instrument apelat gesti epicicarios subtil del qual aquesta es la forma:	And if not, then administer the extraction with the instrument called "gesti epicicarios" which is subtle and has this form:
E si es foro-getada am gesti, bo es; e sino, lahoras aministra la extraccio de lu am onci subtil de pauca duplicacio.	And if it is forgotten about the "gesti", then so be it; and otherwise, then administer the extraction with the onyx of subtle duplication.
E donc si no es foro-getada per aquo, lahoras fay una canula de aram e entromet la extremitat de la canula en le trauc de la aurelha e claus a l’enviro de la canula am cera e am oli mollificada per so que no sia ubert sino la canula.	And therefore, if not forgotten about this, then make a tube of iron and insert the tip of the tube into the hole of the ear and seal around the tube with wax and softened oil so that only the tube is free.
E aprop extratz am le tieu vent am fort atraccio, quar tropas veguadas cum aquo que havem recontat.	And then extract with great force of attraction, because many times as we have recounted.
Mays si no es foro-getada en aquesta manieyra, lahoras pren de halka alumbat o de vecz aparelhat am le qual son preses les ausels una patita quantitat, e pausa aquel en la extremitat de ray, e aprop envolopa sobre aquel coto decentment pausat.	But if not forgotten in this manner, then take of holly lit or of prepared wax with which the birds are caught, and put that into the tip of the ray, and then wrap around it decently paused.
E aprop entromet aquel en le trauc de la aurelha am facilitat, e aprop excicca la aurelha de la humiditat.	And then insert that into the hole of the ear with ease, and then dry out the ear from its humidity.
E donc si no es foro-getada am totas las causas las quals havem recontadas, lahoras tu coyta a talhar aquela denant que endevengua apostema caut o espasme.	And therefore, if not forgotten about all the causes which we have recounted, then you should beware of cutting it before it develops into a painful apostema or spasm.
E la manieyra de talhar aquela es que tu al comensament sancnes le malaute de la vena sephasica e extratz del sanc segon la mannieyra de la vertut de lu, e aprop fay aquel cezer entre las tuas mas e converteys l’aurelha a las partidas desus, e fen am petita fissura en la razit de la aurelha deves lo greys de lu en le loc be premegut de lu.	And the method of cutting it is that you first anoint the patient with the sap of the vena sephasica and extract the blood according to the manner of the virtue of it, and then make that cease between your hands and convert the ear into the upper parts, and make a small fissure in the root of the ear above the grey hair.
E sia la fissura de figura lunar entro que pervengua a la peyra, e, la peyra atrobada, osta aquela si podes am instrumentz apropriatz; e aprop cos la fissura en aquela hora am velocitat, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And the fissure should be of lunar shape until it reaches the peyra, and when the peyra is darkened, stop that if possible with appropriate instruments; and then close the fissure in that hour with speed, and cure that until it is healed.
E si la causa cazent en la aurelha es un dels gras que creysso e so inflatz, lahoras aministra la curacio e la extraccio de lu; mays si no obezeys a tu ad eyssiment, lahoras tu pren spatum teune subtil segon aquesta forma:	And if the cause occurs in the ear is one of the fat that creases and is inflamed, then administer the cure and extraction of it; but if not obedient to your sight, then you take a spatula of fine iron according to this form:
e aministra am aquel la abscizio de aquel gra lo qual es cazut en l’aurelha.	and administer with that the removal of that fat which has fallen into the ear.
E no fassas aquo quan cogitas que aquel ja es humectat per la vapor del aurelha, e pausa aquel en motas pessas, e prop extratz ne aquelas am les oncis o am gesti subtil, o ab inscizio ayssi co dit havem, quar es alleujada la extraccio de lu.	And don't do that when you think that it is already moistened by the vapor of the ear, and pause it in many pieces, and then extract from those with onyx or with subtle instruments, or with incision as we have said, because it is facilitated the extraction of it.
Mays en l’aygua la qual es intrada en l’aurelha cove que·l malaute use de sternutacio am condizi al comensament, e omple la sieua aurelha am alcu coto vielh, e jagua sobre aquela aurelha en la qual es l’aygua, e si per aquo es foro-getada, bo es; e sino, lahoras pren tropas peyras teunas e leons segon la longitut del dit, e calfa aquelas en le foc un pauc, e le pacient entrometa una de aquelas en le trauc de la sua aurelha e saute sobre la un pe sieu de aquela partida e percussia am una autra peyra sobre la peyra la qual es dintz la aurelha.	But in the water which is entered into the ear, it is necessary for the patient to use stornutation in conditions at first, and fill his own ear with some old cut, and then pour oil over that ear where the water is, and if forgotten about this, so be it; otherwise, take many iron pears and lemons according to the length of the finger, and heat those in the fire a little, and the patient inserts one of those into the hole of his own ear and sits on top of it with another pear over the pear which is behind the ear.
Donc no cesse aquo am peyra entro que tota l’aygua sia foro-getada.	Therefore, do not cease this process until all the water has been forgotten.
E ja l’aygua sira foro-getada enayssi que tu prenguas de papier o de gonc .i., e met la una extremetat de lu en l’aurelha e estendas l’autre extremitat am foc entro que sia comburit le may de lu.	And already the water will be forgotten in such a way that you take of paper or of cotton, etc., and place one end of it in the ear and stretch the other end to the fire until the middle part of it is burned.
E prop met i autre gonc e fay aquo tantas veguadas entro que tota l’aygua sia foro-getada, e stratz aquel am canula ayssi co desus es dit de la peyra extrasadora.	And then place another cotton and make it so many times until all the water is forgotten, and stretch that with a tube just as described above about the extracting pear.
Mays en la extraccio de bestia intrant en aquela aurelha, si es a petit cos, ayssi piussa e a lu semblant, cura aquel ayssi cum havem dit en la divisio; mays si es de gran cos la qual causa apar al sen del vezement, lahoras aministra la extraccio de lu am gesti e oncis, e la causa de lu es pus leugiera de totas las autras causas que cazo en l’aurelha.	But in the extraction of beasts that enter into that ear, if it is small-sized, just like a little one and similar to it, cure it as we have said in the division; but if it is from great-sized, which appears on the side of the swelling, then administer the extraction with instruments and onyx, and the cause of it is more easily removed than all other causes that occur in the ear.
Mays en la extraccio de verm engendrat en la aurelha, quan tu curas aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e en le tractat de distillacios e no comfereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que tu reguardes la aurelha al solelh.	But in the extraction of worms born in the ear, when you cure it with that which we have said in the division and in the treatise on distillations, and do not conform your treatment, then it is necessary to look at the ear to the sun.
E donc si apar aqui alcuna causa dels verms, lahoras extratz aquel am gesti o am onci subtils, mays si no apar deguna causa, lahoras pren una canula dejos streyta e desus ampla de la qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And therefore, if any cause of worms appears here, then extract that with instruments or subtle onyx; but if no cause appears, then take a tube made of stretched and widened material, the form of which is this:
E entromet la extremitat subtil en la aurelha segon la quantitat la qual suffertar puesca le malaute; e aprop sucgeys am aquela per succio fort, e fay aquo motas veguadas, entro que totz les verms sian foro-gitatz.	And insert the subtle end into the ear according to the quantity that the patient can tolerate; and then suck it out with strong suction, and make it many times, until all the worms are forgotten.
Mays si no obezeysso a tu al ayssiment, lahoras tu opila e claus en le circuit de la canula am cera ayssi cum havem dit; lahoras aministre distillacios las quals han ja esproadas les antics en la curacio dels verms, e atrobaras aquo en le tractat de distillacios.	But if not obedient to your sight, then you open and close the circuit of the tube with wax as we have said; then administer distillations which the ancients have already tried in the cure of worms, and find it in the treatise on distillations.
E sia la tua efusio am la qual efundas les olis medicinas en la aurelha am aquest strument del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And this is your effusion with which you pour the medicinal oils into the ear with this instrument, the form of which is this:
E fay aquela de argent o de eram, dejos streyt, en le qual sia un petit trauc, e am pla desus.	And make that of silver or of lead, stretched, in which there is a small hole, and with a plate on top.
E donc sia cum empellent a que es en la conquavitat de la canula de continent aqui on sira necessari.	And thus it will be like as we have impelled that which is in the continuity of the tube, here where it is necessary.
E si vols, pren le ray e envolveys en la extremitat de lu decentment coto, e aprop gieta oli en la concavitat del auziment, o suc de alcuna herba, o aquo que vols de aquestas medicinas en la canula — e aquela es en la aurelha —, e aprop entromet le ray am coto desus e exprem am la tua ma aquel am compressio temprada de lu entro que l’oli sia expellit en la concavitat del auziment e le malaute senta le oli dedintz.	And if you wish, take the ray and wrap it around the end of it decently cut, and then pour oil into the cavity of the ear, or juice from some herb, or whatever you want from these medicines in the tube -- and that is in the ear --, and then insert the ray with a cut above and compress it with your hand gently so that the oil is expelled into the cavity of the ear and the patient feels the oil outside.
E aquo que sia enfundut en la aurelha sia ja scalfat am foc un petit.	And what is inserted into the ear is already scorched with fire a little bit.
E guarda te que la causa la qual distillaras en l’aurelha no sia trop frega, quar las medicinas de aurelha no suffertan aquo.	And beware that the cause which you will distill in the ear is not too hot, because the medicines of the ear cannot withstand this.
Capitol .vii.	Chapter VII.
De curacio de opilacio de aurelhas.	On the Cure of Ear Blockage.
Alcunas veguadas alcus enfantz yeysso dels ventres de lors mayres no-perforatz, e aquo ja accideys en alcus homes, opilacio en le meat de la aurelha per plagua o per carn nada en aquela; e aquesta opilacio alcunas veguadas es fayta en le preon del trau de la aurelha la qual no consiec le vezement, e alcunas veguadas es en las partidas defora.	Sometimes children are born with blocked ears from their mothers' unperforated vents, and this also happens to some men, blockage in the ear canal due to injury or flesh not perforated in that; and sometimes this blockage occurs in the prominence of the nose of the ear which does not consent to the swelling, and sometimes it is outside.
E aquela que accideys en le preon de lu, la qual no comprehen le vezement, es en las majors disposicios de dificil sanacio.	And that which occurs in the prominence of it, which does not understand the swelling, is in the greatest difficulties of difficult healing.
E en aquela en qual consegueys le vezement, cove que tu pauses la aurelha del malaute al solelh e reguarda en aquela.	And in that where you can understand the swelling, it is necessary to pause the ear of the patient at the sun and look into it.
E donc si vezes oppulacio apparent, obre aquela am espatum subtil del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And therefore, if there appears obvious swelling, open that with a subtle spatula of which this is the form:
Si’ la extremitat de lu en la qual sia petita la latitut, del qual la una partida sia aguda e l’autra no; e le spatum sia de dos latz leon per so que no fassa lizio al aurelha.	If the end of it in which there is a small latitude, where one part is sharp and the other is not; and the spatula has two lion-like edges so that it does not cause damage to the ear.
E donc si la opilacio es per carn nascuda en la aurelha o en le meat de lu, lahoras te aquela am oncis subtils e incidiys aquela vehement facilitat entro que sia ostada tota la carn.	And therefore, if the blockage is due to flesh born in the ear or in the canal of it, then take that with subtle onyx and cut that away with vehement facility until all the flesh is removed.
E si opilacio es en le preon de la aurelha, lahoras pren ray subtil leon e escalfa aquel am foc un pauc, e aprop met aquel en le meat de l’aurelha.	And if the blockage is in the prominence of the ear, then take a subtle iron rod and heat it slightly with fire, and then insert that into the canal of the ear.
E donc si as scentit oppulacio am aquo que le malaute atroba am facilitat, per gravetat de ausir, esforsa la oppressio de lu am facilitat; e guarda te que no plagues les nervis del aurelha.	And therefore, if you have felt obstruction with that which the patient has obtained with facility, due to gravity of air, force the oppression of it with facility; and beware that you do not hurt the nerves of the ear.
E aprop pausa en l’aurelha drap de li segon la quantitat del ample del trauc lo qual tu as envolvutz en l’enguent egipciac; e fay aquo per alcus jorns entro que sias segur de la consolidacio de la plagua; o que prenguas qualgua e enfon aquela en ayguaros e pulveriza sobre lu segi trissat e usa de lu; e si vezes la aurelha ja esser apostemada, lahoras cove que tu estraguas la qualgua e permutes aquela am autra qualgua la qual tu envoloparas en cerot que sia fayt am oli rozat, entro que sia le apostema caut cedat; e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And then pause in the ear with cloth of lead according to the quantity of the width of the hole which you have wrapped around it in Egyptian ointment; and make this for several days until you are sure of the consolidation of the wound; or take some powder and mix it with water and sprinkle it on top, and use it; and if the ear is already inflamed, then it is necessary to remove the powder and replace it with another powder which you wrapped around it in rose oil, so that the inflammation subsides; and then cure it until it is healed.
Mays si accideys flux de sanc, lahoras submergeys esponga o drap en aygua frega e pausa sobre la aurelha, e usa del autra curacio la qual restrengeys le flux del sanc, la qual es dita en le tractat de distillacio.	But if there is a flow of blood, then submerge the sponge or cloth in hot water and pause it over the ear, and use another cure which restricts the flow of blood, which is described in the treatise on distillation.
Capitol .viii.	Chapter VIII.
De cura de athezil le qual endeveno a las palpebras.	On the Cure of Athazel Which Occurs to the Eyelids.
Athezil les quals endeveno a las paupebras dels huels alcuna veguada so humitz, alscunas veguadas son secs.	Athazels which occur on the eyelids of humans sometimes are humid, and at other times they are dry.
Donc cove que tu tenguas aquels am tenhalhas o am onci, e inscindas aquels am espatum de las suas razitz, e aprop pausa sobre les locs segi trissat.	Therefore, it is necessary to take those with tentacles or onyx, and cut them with an instrument of their own roots, and then pause over the places as described.
Mays si dolor am flux de sanc veno, lahoras tu cauteriza aquels am cauteri lanticular subtil.	But if pain accompanied by a flow of blood occurs, then you should cauterize those with a lunar cautery instrument.
E la milhor cauterizacio es aprop las inscizios e tropas veguadas retornam quan reman alcuna causa de sas razitz; e quan so cauterizadas am foc, aquelas razitz son comburidas e no retornan.	And the best cauterization is to do it around the incisions and many times return when there remains some cause of their roots; and when they are cauterized with fire, those roots are burned and do not return.
Capitol .ix.	Chapter IX.
Cura de grandeyssa que veno a las palpebras dels huels.	On the Cure of Grandeyss Which Occur on the Eyelids of Humans.
Motas veguadas endeve en las palpebras dels huels alcuna causa la qual es asemblada a grandissa en sa fortalicia e duricia, e per so grandissia es apelada.	Many times it occurs on the eyelids of humans some cause which is assembled to grandess in its strength and hardness, and because of that grandess it is called.
E es agreguacio de humiditat grossa en la palpebra dejos e desus.	And it is an accumulation of great moisture above and below the eyelid.
Donc la opperacio en lor es que consideras lahoras si la grandissia es procedent en lu en aquo que apar de la palpebra e es mauguda a tota partida; e la causa de lu es leugiera.	Therefore, the operation on them is that you should consider whether the grandess is proceeding from it in what appears to be the eyelid and is spreading to all parts; and the cause of it is light.
Donc fen sobre aquela am fissura per la latitut, e aprop escorga aquela de tota partida am facilitat entro que evasesca, e aprop suspen aquela am onci e abscindeys aquela.	Therefore, make an incision in it with a fissure by latitude, and then carefully examine all parts with facility until it is evacuated; and then suspend it with onyx and remove it.
Mays si a tu no es apparelhada la incizio de lu si no pus que penetras la palpebra am inscizio pauc a pauc, lahoras aquo no notz en deguna causa.	But if you are not accustomed to making the incision of it, nor can you penetrate the eyelid with an instrument little by little, then there is no cause noted.
E si la figura es gran, lahoras tu l’ajusta am sutura; e cura aquela entro que sia sanada.	And if the figure is large, then you should adjust it with a suture; and cure that until it is healed.
E si es pauca, a tu no sobrevindra mal per aquela quar l’anguent de lu restaura aquela e encarna.	And if it is small, then you will not suffer harm from that because the ointment of it restores that and incarnates.
E si la grandissia es declinant a las partidas dedintz de la palpebra deves la superficia dedintz, lahoras evesa la palpebra e suspen la grandissia am onci, otra que tu indigescas de incizio, e prem aquela de tota part, e si la palpebra per inscizio es alonguada, aquo no notz en deguna causa.	And if the grandess is declining to the outer parts of the eyelid you must remove the surface outwardly; then and there ease the eyelid and suspend the grandess with onyx, unless you are accustomed to incision, and press it all around; and if the eyelid by incision is lengthened, there is no cause noted.
E aprop la incizio, lava le huel am aygua salada; e cura le loc am aquo que encarna entro que sia sanat.	And then wash your hands with salted water; and cure the place with that which incarnates until it is healed.
Capitol .x.	Chapter X.
De la cura axcirnah en la palpebra desus del huel.	On the Cure of Axirnah in the Eyelid above the Eye.
Axcirnath es grays le qual es engendrat en las tunicas de la palpebra desus, e majorment endeve als enfantz, agrava les huels de aquels et accideyso a lor catartz le mayti; e no podon reguardar la claror del solelh per aquo quar lagremas se coytan ad aquels.	Axcirnah is a grayish growth which is generated in the tunics of the eyelid above, and most often occurs in children, causing their eyes to become inflamed and leading to their cataracts being affected; and they are not able to gaze at the brightness of the sun because tears flow into them.
E per so tu vezes aquels jaser sobre les lors caras tot temps, e sobre les lors caras dormen; e so a las palpebras de lor dejos les sobrecils humidas, las quals ja ha cuberta imflacio, e iminencia de accernac apparent es en l’uelh; e que quant tu premes le loc am les tieus ditz, tu centes accernac entro aquels.	And therefore you should wet those eyes constantly on their faces, and they sleep on their faces; so that the eyelids of theirs below are covered with humidified swelling, which has already been inflamed, and there is apparent danger of cataract in the eye; and when you press the place with those fingers you said, you will bring about healing within them.
E alcuna manieyra de opperacio es en aquel que le malaute pausa le sieu cap en le tieu se, e aprop pausa drap de li e de lu fay calgua, e fay de lu cercle segon la quantitat la qual contena arthernach de tota partida, e aprop pausa aquel sobre aquela e prem am les tieus ditz de tota per que sia agreguat arcernac en le mieg del cercle, e aprop fen en le mieg de aquela humiditat am spatum inscident am fissura per la latitut, e la fissura no sia major que la fissura que es fayta en flaubotomia.	And some method of operation is in him who makes the patient put his head into a circle made from cloth and lead, and then puts on a mixture of lead and oil, and makes a circle according to the quantity which contains arthernach of all parts; and then puts that on top and presses with those fingers you said of all parts so that it is aggregated arcernac in the middle of the circle, and then ends in the middle of that humid atmosphere with an instrument incised by a fissure for latitude, and the fissure should not be greater than the one made in flaubotomia.
Mays en le preon cove que tu fendas la codena tota entro que pervenguas ad arcernach, quar en las mays desposicios proceseys arcernach per fissura segon la forma de grayseza blanca.	But in the prominence it is necessary that you open the code entirely until you reach arcernach, for in the most suitable procedures arcernach is processed by fissure according to the form of white gersa.
Donc extratz aquela am draps los quals tu as envolopatz entre les tieus ditz a las partidas deforo e revolv entre la ma dextra e sinistre entro que sia dispargut.	Therefore, extract that with cloths which you have wrapped around the fingers of yours in the outer parts and revolve between your right and left hands until it is dispersed.
E guarda te que no ajustes en la fissura per so que am le spatum no pervenguas al huel e ladescas aquel.	And beware that you do not adjust in the fissure because with the instrument you may not reach the eye and it will be lost.
Mays si no apar a tu arternach en le comensament de la fissura, mays que tu ajustes en la fissura un petit am fecilitat entro que procesisca arternach; e aprop extratz aquela ayssi quo havem dit; e aprop submargeys draps de li en aygua e vi agre e pausa les sobre le loc e estrenh aquels am polvils.	But if there is no arthernach in the beginning of the fissure, then you should adjust slightly in the fissure with facility until arthernach processes; and then extract that as we have said; and then submerge cloths of lead in water and vinegar, and make them wet and pause them over the place and strengthen those with powders.
E so alcus que trissan sal e pausan aquel en la conquavitat de la fissura per so que aquo que es remas de aquela humiditat.	And thus, some that are left over from that humidity pause in the cavity of the fissure for this reason.
E aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that until it is healed.
Mays si accideys en le loc apostema caut, lahoras cura aquel am emplastres cedatils entro que sia sanat.	But if there occurs an inflamed apostema in the place, then cure that with ointments which subside until it is healed.
Capitol .xi.	Chapter XI.
De manieyras de tactimi del huel.	On Methods of Palpation of the Eye.
Quan en las palpebras dels huels so natz pels ajustatz dejos les pels naturals e so antiquatz, lahoras aquels noso al huel e fan endevenir manieras de malautias ayssi cum lacrimas assiduas e mollificacio de palpebras e tela entro que aquo sia causa de destruccio del huel que s’apela tactinir del huel, e cura se en quatre manieyras: o per cauteri am foc; o am medicina acuta segon que denant es dit en le capitol de cauteri; o es fayt atactini per inscizio e sutura; o per cannas segon que yeu diyre.	When in the eyelids of humans there are born natural folds and they become ancient, then those no longer belong to the eye and cause ways of illnesses such as constant tears and softening of the eyelids and skin until it is a cause of destruction of the eye which is called palpation of the eye, and cure itself in four ways: or by cauterization with fire; or by acute medicine according to what is said before in the chapter on cauterization; or made to be palpated by incision and suture; or by canals according to what I will say.
E donc cove que tu pauses le cap del malaute en le tieu se; aprop converteys la palpebra del uelh am la tua ma sinistra, e si es convertida, bo es; e sino, entromet agulha en aquela en la qual sia fiel de la partida pus dejos de la palpebra, e fay penetrar la agulha am fiel desus, e aquo sia — prop del marge de la palpebra en le qual naysso les pels — prop dels pels, e tira le fiel a las partidas desus am la palpebra, e converteys aquela am le ray.	And therefore it is necessary that you put the patient's head in the said circle; then turn the eyelid of the eye with your left hand, and if it is turned, good is; and otherwise, insert a needle into that part which is faithful to the outermost side of the eyelid, and make the needle penetrate from above, and thus it will be — close to the edge of the eyelid where there are no hairs — close to the hairs, and pull the thread upwards with the eyelid, and turn that with the ray.
E aprop fen en la partida dedintz de la palpebra dejos les pels ajustatz am spatum inscidentz del lacrimal major entro al lacrimal mendre; e aprop extratz le fiel e pausa dejos la palpebra polvilhs petitz de coto o de drap, e aprop senha sobre la palpebra am tenta, e sia ayssi cum figura de fuelha de mirt.	And then end in the outermost part of the eyelid below the hairs, adjusted with an instrument incised by the lacrimal major into the lacrimal duct; and then extract the thread and pause below the eyelid with small powders of coton or cloth, and then sign above the eyelid with a tent, and it should be as follows: like the figure of myrtle foliage.
Mays empero cove que sia la figura segon la quantitat de helevacio de la palpebra, quar aquo ja es diversificat en les homes, quar de aquels es le quals indigeys que sia inscidit de la palpebra gran quantitat segon la quantitat per la qual la palpebra es mollificada.	But however it is necessary that the figure be according to the quantity of elevation of the eyelid, for this is already diversified in men, for some of them require that a great quantity of the eyelid be incised according to the quantity by which the eyelid is softened.
E aprop fen am le spatum sobre las doas linhas las quals has senhadas, e comensa del lacrimal major entro al lacrimal menor.	And then end with the instrument on two lines which you have marked, and begin from the lacrimal major into the lacrimal minor.
E si’ la tua fissura prop dels pels naturals ayssi cum es la grossetut del rey.	And if your incision is as wide as the natural folds of hair, like the thickness of a king.
E aprop met le onci en un dels dos angles de la codena, e aprop excoria aquela tota, e aprop ajusta am la scitura las doas labias am gula o fiel de lana subtil, e abstergeys le sanc, e fay adherir aquo que superflueys dels fiels sobre dos sobrecils am alcunas causas enviscans, si voles far aquo, e sino, non cures.	And then put the onyx in one of the two angles of the code, and then excoriate that entire area, and then adjust with the suture the two lips to the palate or thread of fine wool, and wash away the blood, and make adhere that which superfluously remains from the threads over two eyelids with some causes visible, if you wish to do so, and otherwise, do not cure.
E aprop leyssa la sutura dels fiels entro a tres dias o quatre, e aprop cura aquo.	And then loosen the suture of the threads within three or four days, and then cure that.
E si vols, layssa la plagua ses sutura, e cura aquela am aquo que exsicca e constrenh, quar la palpebra es alevada deves la sigillacio de la plagua e la agreguacio de lu; mays sutura es milor E donc aysso diysso les antics de taxanir.	And if you wish, leave the wound open without suture, and cure that with that which dries up and constrains, for the eyelid is raised above the sealing of the wound and the aggregation of pus; but suture is better. And thus I say to those who are accustomed to taxanir.
Mays empero en lu sia sollicitut sobre le malaute, e es de bona operacio, e no es en lu temor.	But however, in this there is solicitude for the patient, and it is of good operation, and not from fear.
E es autra manieyra en taxmir, e es que senhes sobre la palpebra figura ayssi cum fuelha de mirt, e aprop eleva la palpebra am tres uncis segreguatz e congreguatz segon aquesta forma:	And there is another method in taxanir, and it is that you sign on the eyelid a figure like myrtle foliage, and then raise the eyelid with three separated and gathered threads according to this form:
Mays si no es possible aquo, tener les uncis, e aquo no es engualhat, lahoras pren una agula en la qual haia fil e met aquela en le mieg de la figura, e entromet le autre fiel prop le lacrimal major, e·l fiel segon prop le lacrimal mendre, e ajusta entre les tieus ditz les fiels am equalitat, e aprop am aquels eleva la tua ma am elevacio engual, eleva tota la codena sobre la qual es senhat ayssi cum havem recomtat.	But if it is not possible to take the threads, and it is not equalized, then take one needle with thread and put that in the middle of the figure, and insert the other thread near the lacrimal major, and the second thread near the lacrimal minor, and adjust between the fingers you said the threads with equality, and then with those elevate your hand with elevation equal to it, elevate the entire code over which is signed as we have recounted.
E aprop ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am sutura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And then adjust the two lips of the wound with suture, and cure that until it is healed.
Mays si accideys apostema deves la tua inscizio o la tua fissura, seda aquel apostema am cerot e a lu semblantz, e am enguentz.	But if there occurs an inflamed apostema due to your incision or your fissure, soothe that apostema with cerote and similar substances, and with gentle remedies.
E alcunas veguadas endeve a la palpebra que·ls sieus pels sian convertitz, adonc cove que tu uses en aquela de aquo que havem dit de inscizio; mays sutura en quascus es mays artificial.	And sometimes it happens that the eyelid is converted into hair, then it is necessary that you use in that what we have said about incision; but suture is more artificial.
Ataxinir am cannas es segon aquesta forma:	Taxanir by canals is according to this form:
e es que tu convertas la palpebra e scindas la figura qu’es dedintz segon que he recontat; e aprop per art fay doas cannas o doas astelas subtils de las quals longitut sia segon la longitut de la palpebra e la latitut de lor sia mendra de la latitut del spatum.	and it is that you convert the eyelid and divide the figure which is below according to what I have recounted; and then, by art, make two canals or two thin tubes of which the length is according to the length of the palpebra and the latitude of them is less than the latitude of the spatium.
E tu ja has inscidit en las extremitatz de quascunas partidas, la on tenes les fils.	And you have already incised at the extremities of each part, where you have the threads.
Aprop agregua quascuna am subtilitat subre aquo que superflueys de la palpebra del huel, e constres las cannas de quascunas partidas am fort strictura, e layssa aquela per alcus jorns, quar la codena per la strictura morira e sira denegada e se poyrira entro que per si meteyssa cayra.	And then add each one with subtlety above that which superfluously remains of the eyelid of the eye, and constrict the canals of each part with very strict constriction, and leave it for a few days, for the code will die and become denuded and will be absorbed into the skin within which it has fallen.
Mays si es tardat, lahoras trenca la am las toroyras, e aprop cura la plagua entro que sia sanat.	But if it is delayed, then break the thread and leave the torn parts, and then cure the wound until it is healed.
Donc cum es solidada, la palpebra es elevada e les pels no pungo.	Therefore, when it is solidified, the eyelid is raised and the hairs do not prick.
E aquesta es la forma de doas cannas las quals faras segon aquesta forma:	And this is the form of two canals which you will make according to this form:
e haia la quantitat de la longitut e de la latitut ni mays ni mens.	and have the quantity of length and latitude neither more nor less.
Capitol .xii.	Chapter XII.
De elevacio de pels pungentz en le huel am agula quan le pel es dur.	On Elevation of Pricking Hairs in the Eye with a Needle when the Hair is Hard.
Quan son pels no-naturals, durs e aspres e pungentz les huels, lahoras la operacio en lu es que tu prenguas agula subtil e pauses en aquela fiel de ceda subtil e leon, e aprop que tu ajustes las extremitatz de lu e nozes quascu en manieyra mot subtil.	When the hairs are unnatural, hard, and rough, and prick the eyes, then the operation in this case is that you take a fine needle and pause it in that thread of silk or linen, and then adjust the extremities of it and note each one in a manner very subtle.
E sia la longitut dels fiels de quantitat de una palma.	And let the length of the threads be of the quantity of one palm.
E aprop tu compon2 autre fiel subtil dejos lu en breu, e nuza las extremitatz de aquel si tu·t vols.	And then compose another fine thread below it in brief, and join the extremities of that if you wish.
E aprop pause le malaute le sieu cap en le tieu se, e sia prop del solelh per que la tua obra sia declarada, quar es operacio subtil e menuda.	And then place the patient's head in the said circle, and be near the sun so that your work is declared, for it is a subtle and minute operation.
E aprop intromet la agulha en la razit del pel ajustat la qual ha necessitat de engen, e fay aquela penetrar en la palpebra festinantment entro que extraguas aquela desus le pel natural.	And then insert the needle into the root of the hair adjusted to which it is necessary for engineering, and make that penetrate the eyelid promptly until you extract it above the natural hair.
E aprop tire le pel entro desus e intromet aquel en alixati, e sian les pels un o dos o tres e no mays.	And then pull out the hair above and insert that into alignment, and be the hairs one or two or three, but not more.
E aprop tira la tua ma am aquel entro que·l pel sia fora-gitat am alixolati en la palpebra am le pel natural.	And then pull out your hand with that until the hair is outside and aligned in the eyelid along with the natural hair.
Mays si es atirat alixalati e non es gitat le pel, atiraras alixati a las partidas dejos am le fiel le qual tu has compost am aquela, entro qu’en sia gitat alixalati del trau sobira.	But if it is pulled out of alignment and the hair is not expelled, then pull out the alignment to the parts below with the thread which you have composed in that, until it is aligned with the above the surface.
E vegas aquela am la visio del huel, quar lahoras tu gitaras alixati e lo fiel, e grotan quascu e clautz le huel, e laysse le claus per dos dias o tres, entro que·l pel adheresca al sieu loc e nasque sobre aquel bona carn.	And then gaze at that with the vision of the eye, for then you will pull out the alignment and the thread, and grind all and clean the eye, and leave the closure for two or three days, until the hair adheres to its place and grows on top of it good flesh.
E si es mays breu le pel, lahoras tu ajusta un pel lonc dels pels naturals, e es elevat am aquel, o que·l leysses entro que sia alonguat aprop alcu spazi, e lehoras tu eleva aquel.	And if the hair is too short, then you adjust one long hair from the natural hairs, and it is raised with that, or let it rest until it is lengthened to some space, and then you raise that.
Capitol .xiii.	Chapter XIII.
De la cura de ehacratir la qual ve en la palpebra desus.	On the Cure for Pterygium which appears on the Eyelid above.
Quan ve en le huel ehacratir, e es contraccio de la palpebra quan es contrayta en sus, o a dextra o a sinistra partida, per mala consolidacio de plagua o de seccio o de cauteri, e es apelada leporina, e aquesta ahercrati o es natural o accidental, e es fayta per consolidacio de plagua o de seccios o de cauteri, o per semblantz a lor malcuratz.	When pterygium appears on the eye, and it is contraction of the eyelid when it is contracted in its own direction, or to the right or left part, due to bad consolidation of wound or section or cauterization, and it is called leporina, and this pterygium either is natural or accidental, and it is made by consolidation of wound or sections or cauterization, or by resemblance to their maladies.
May la manieyra de la operacio en lu es que tu fendas aquela consolidacio e que separes las labias de lu, e pauses en lu en aquo que es entre aquelas una meca de drap de li, e ligues aquelas entro que sian sanadas.	The method of the operation in this case is that you cut through the consolidation and separate the lips of it, and pause in it where there is a gap between them of cloth or linen, and tie those together until they are healed.
E no cove que tu uses de curacio de lu de las causas las quals exsiccan, constrenho; quar si tu fas aquo retorna alixacratir pus mal que nulh temps no foc habantz.	And it is not good that you use any cure for it from the causes which dry up and constrict; for if you do so, it will return to pterygium even worse than before at no time whatsoever.
Usa en aquela de causas que mollifico ayssi cum es fenugrec, e embroca am la aygua en la qual son coytz altea e semensa de li, o enguent dyaquilon, le qual sia liquefayt am alcu dels olis, e submergeys en aquel la meca, e cura am aquel.	Use in it causes that soften, such as fenugreek, and mix with the water in which are cooked almonds and sesame seeds of linen or aquilon ointment, which is liquefied with some oils, and immerse in that the cloth, and cure with that.
E lo tesaur de la tua curacio es que tu perforsses am tot engen que no sia consolidat segon la forma que foc al comensament.	And the treasure of your cure is that you perforate all that is not consolidated according to the form in which it began.
E aquesta operacio la qual havem dita, no es sino alcuna rectificacio de ehalixacrati que no retorna la forma del loc segon que foc denant.	And this operation which we have said is only some correction of pterygium that does not return to the form of the place according to what was before.
Capitol .xiiii.	Chapter XIV.
De la cura de ehacrati le qual es fayt en la palpebra dejos.	On the Cure for Pterygium which is made in the Eyelid below.
Aquesta alxacrati la qual es fayta en la palpebra dejos, la qual es nompnada vertadierament alxacrati; e es de lu alcuna natural, autra accidental.	This pterygium which is made in the eyelid below, which is truly called alxacrati; and it is of some natural, others accidental.
Mays accidental es fayta per plagua o per scissura o per cauteri o per autres semblantz.	But accidental is made by wound or section or cauterization or other such things.
E la via de la operacio de lu es que tu prenguas una agula en la qual haga fil doble, e fiques aquela en la carn, e que la fassas passar del lacrimal de senestre entro al lacrimal dextre, entro que·l fil pervengua en las doas extremitatz de la carn.	And the way of the operation is that you take a needle with double thread, and insert it into the flesh, and make it pass from the left lacrimal to the right lacrimal, until the thread reaches both ends of the flesh.
E aprop exten la carn a las partidas desus am la agula e cus aquela am la agula, e inscideys am spatum ample.	And then extend the flesh to the upper parts with the needle and cut it with the needle, and incise with a spatula wide.
E donc si retorne la figura de la palpebre segon que cove, bo es; e sino, pren le ray e pausa aquel en la figura fenduda, e am aquel converteys la palpebra, e fen las doas fissuras en le latz de la palpebra dejos.	And then if the figure of the eyelid returns according to what is good, it is well; and otherwise, take a thread and pause it in the divided figure, and with that convert the eyelid, and close both incisions on the lower eyelid.
E sian las extremitatz de las doas fissuras de dos angles de la inscizio, la qual has fayta entro que concurren, e sia de lor fayt angle entro que quan se congreguan sia fayta figura de lor.	And let the ends of both incisions be at two angles of the incision which you have made until they converge, and be of their own making angle, so that when they come together it forms a figure.
E aquesta figura es letra greca: la landa.	And this figure is the Greek letter: lambda.
E aprop osta la carn aquela per la quantitat que es le latz de lu agut dejos de lu, aquo que siec la palpebra.	And then secure the flesh with that quantity which is the edge of the lower eyelid, so that it secures the eyelid.
E aprop ajusta las partz seperadas e cos aquelas am le fil de lana; e aprop cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit de las medicinas mollificativas e de las calguas entro que sia sanat.	And then adjust the separated parts and sew them together with wool thread; and then cure those with what we have said of softening medicines and poultices until it is healed.
E si alxacrati endeve per fissura o sutura o cauteri, lahoras cove que tu fendas am fissura plana sobre les pels de la palpebra segon que es precedit.	And if pterygium develops through incision or suture or cauterization, then it is necessary that you cut with a flat incision on the hairs of the eyelid according to what has been previously said.
E aprop separa am la calgua entre doas labias segon que havem dit.	And then separate with a poultice between two lips according to what we have said.
En la suma del sermo de la cura de alxacrati quan es desus o dejos, que corra en lu operacio, segon que es preparat de la forma de alxacrati, e aquela es en forma de motas diversitatz.	In the sum of the sermon on the cure of pterygium when it is above or below, that which runs in this operation, according to what is prepared from the form of pterygium, and that is in the form of various moles.
