And I had already cured a woman of an abscess which was located in her gullet, which abscess tended to become fiery red, with little sensation, and had already closed off the gullet, and the woman was breathing very tightly, and had already forbidden herself from eating or drinking water, and had almost reached death if I had not acted for a day or two.
E l’apostema ja tant havia pugat que havia mezes dos ramps entro que eyssiro per dos traucs.	And the abscess had so swollen that it had formed two ridges and was about to burst through two holes.
Donc yeu me cuytegui fisturalment e fiquegui en un de lor onci, e tiregui aquel, e atirada es de lu gran porcio, e aprop yeu incidigui aquela de on comprendegui del autre trau, e aprop yeu obrigui la boca de lu, e compremegui la sua lengua, e aprop yeu fiquegui le onci en aquela apostema.	Therefore I carefully cut open the fistula and remained in one of them, and pulled out that abscess, and it was drawn out with a great deal of discharge, and then I incised the other one from where it comprehended the other hole, and then I opened her mouth, and grasped her tongue, and then I placed the onion into that abscess.
E aprop yeu abscizi gran partida de lu, e no corria de lu sino un pauc de sanc.	And then I carefully cut out a great part of it, and there was only a little bleeding.
Donc absolut es le guolayro de aquela femna, e comensec tantost beure aygua, e aprop presec vianda, donc yeu no cessegui inscidir de aquela apostema motas vetz per lonc temps, e succesia apostema en loc de aquel, le qual inscizia entro que es prolonguat aquel.	Therefore the gullet of that woman was absolutely free, and she began to drink water soon after, and then I carefully prescribed food for her. And so I did not cease to incise that abscess many times over a long period, and successive abscesses appeared in its place, which I incised until it was prolonged.
Donc yeu engen agui e cauterizegui le guolayro de lu, donc astec de addicio; e aprop yeu perambulegui e no saubi que fec Dieus de aquela aprop mi.	Therefore I went and cauterized the gullet of her, therefore above addition; and then I walked away and did not know what God had done for me.
Capitol .xxxvii.	Chapter XXXVII.
De inscizio de huvela quan es apostemada.	On the Incision of an Umbilical Abscess when it is Apostemated.
Quan catarr deysen a la huvula, e es apostemada e es longa, lahoras ela es nompnada perpendicular; e si es en la partida dejos grossa e redonda, e lahoras ela es apelada buba.	When the umbilical cord is diseased in the navel, and it is apostemated and is long, then it is called a "perpendicular" one; and if it is on the side that is thick and rounded, then it is called a "bubble".
Mays quan es curada am aquo que havem dit en la divisio, e no comfereys la tua curacio, e eyssament ja vezes que apostema caut ja es ostat de lu e es subtil, lahoras cove que tu inscidas aquela que es agreguadas redonda; e si es ad aquela longitut, e es sanguina, de fusca color o de negre, e no es a lu centiment, lahoras cove que tu temtes la inscizio de lu, quar en aquela es temor sobre le malaute.	But when it is cured with what we have said in the division, and your cure does not agree with it, and it happens that the abscess has already gone away from there and is subtle, then you must incise that which is added on roundly; and if it reaches that length, and is sanguine, fiery red or black, and has no sensation in it, then you must fear the incision of it, because in that place there is fear for the patient.
E quan tu vezes aquela segon la manieyra que yeu he dita de la sua blancor e longuesa, que tu fassas sezer le malaute e premas la lengua de lu am instrument del qual procesic la sua forma e aprop fica le onci en la nuva, e tira aquela en jos e inscideys aquela am un de dos instrumentz les quals e ditz en la inscizio de dos mellas.	And when you incise that according to the manner which I have said of its whiteness and length, then you make the patient sit and take hold of his tongue with an instrument whose form is this: And carefully place the onion in the navel, and pull it down and incise it with one of two instruments which are mentioned in the incision of two notches.
E cove que no inscidas aquela sino aquo que es ajustat sobre le terme natural ses addicio, quar si tu inscides de lu mays, lediyras le sieu parlar.	And it is necessary that you do not incise that, but only as much as is adjusted to the natural term without addition, because if you incise too much, you will deprive him of his speech.
E aprop la inscizio, usa de aquo le qual havem recomtat en la inscizio de dos mellas, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And then carefully incise it with that which we have mentioned in the incision of two notches, and cure that one until it is healed.
Mays si era le malaute espaventat per la inscizio de lu, cove que use de engen en la cauterizacio de lu ses temor, e la manieyra del cauteri en lu no es sino am aygua aguda, e es que tu pauses le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop prem la lengua de lu am le instrument le qual havem dit, e aprop pren de l’aygua la qual havem dita en le capitol de cauterizacio, e comfeys am aquela caus viva, e pausa aquela no spessa ni subtil, e de aquela omple la concavitat de l’estrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	But if the patient is frightened by the incision of it, then you must use great care in the cauterization of it without fear, and the manner of the cauterization is nothing but with sharp water, and that you pause the head of the patient in your sight, and carefully grasp his tongue with the instrument which we have mentioned, and take from the water which we have said in the chapter on cauterization, and confine it to that living cause, and pause that no thick or subtle, and fill that concavity with the instrument whose form is this:
Sia la extramitat de lu conquavitat en la qual sia pausada la medicina ayssi cum la conquavitat de culher de ray, e pausa le strument am la medicina sobre la vula, e·l malaute jagua sobre le sieu latz per so que corro saliva o musellage de la boca de aquel per la intrinscequa medicina, per so que no deyssenda de aquela deguna causa sobre le golayro de lu e que ledesca aquel.	And let the edge of it be in the concavity in which the medicine is paused, just like the concavity of a spoon, and pause the instrument with the medicine on the navel, and the patient will stretch out his hand over his own side so that he may pour saliva or mouthwash from his mouth into that concavity through the intrinsic medicine, so that none of those causes will descend onto the gullet of him and trouble it.
E aprop te la tua ma am la medicina, e exprem aquela sobre la uvula per l’espazi de miega hora entro que vegas aquela esser denegrada e sedada per la mordicacio de la medicina.	And then carefully take your hand and the medicine, and express that onto the uvula for a space of half an hour until you see it to be discolored and sedated by the biting of the medicine.
E si vols, prengues coto e envolopes aquel sobre la extremitat del ray, e submergeys le coto en la medicina, e entrometas le ray am le coto en una canula de sobre entro que·l coto adheresca en aquela canula, e fay aquo tantas vetz entro que consiegues aquo que vols de la cauterizacio de la uva, e aprop leyssa aquela quar ela se seccara e cayra aprop tres dias o quatre.	And if you wish, take a cloth and wrap it around the extremity of the ray, and immerse the cloth in the medicine, and insert the ray with the cloth into a syringe or needle, and make sure that the cloth adheres to the syringe or needle, and do this as many times as you need until you achieve what you want from the cauterization of the uvula, and then let it be so that it dries out and falls off about three days or four.
E si indigeysses que iteras la medicina, itera aquela, e aprop la cauterizacio abstergeys en le circuit de la uva am coto enbegut en boder, e mondifica am aquel aquo que es en le circuit de lu de la medicina, e sia lavat am aygua frega, e sia curat deforo am embrocacio, e dedintz am guarguarismes entro que sia sanat.	And if you need to iterate the medicine, iterate it, and then carefully cauterize it in the circuit of the uvula with cloth wrapped around it, and clean off any residue from the circuit of the medicine, and wash it thoroughly with vinegar water, and treat it externally with embrocation, and internally with gargling, until it is healed.
E aquesta especia de curacio es pus salva que inscizio e pus long de temor.	And this kind of cure is even more saved than incision and less long in fear.
Alcunas veguadas es curada la uvuola am aquo que es pus subtil que cauteri e inscizio, quar es curat am subfumigacio en aquesta manieyra: recipe calament, ysop, origua, ruda, scicados arabic, camamilla, broyda e semblant ad aquels de las erbas, e ajusta totas aquelas causas, o alcunas de lor, en una ola, e sian submergidas am vi agre, e bulhan; e la ola sia be lutada am lut decentment, e sia en le mieg loc de la ola un trauc, sobre le qual sia pausat un instrument conquau de aram segon aquesta manieyra; sia fayt de argent o de aram.	Sometimes the uvula is cured with something even more subtle than cauterization and incision, because it is treated by subfumigation in this manner: take calament, myrrh, origanum, ruda, Arabic scicados, camomile, broth, and similar herbs to those of plants, and mix all those causes, or some of them, into a bath, and let them be submerged in vinegar water, and boil; and the bath should be well stirred with a decent stirring, and there should be a hole in the middle of the bath, on which should be placed an instrument made of iron or steel according to this manner.
E sia entromesa la extremitat en la boca del malaute entro que la vapor poge a la uvula sobre la quanula, entro que la uvula sia mot ofuscada.	And the extremity should be inserted into the mouth of the patient so that the vapor rises to the uvula on the quinsy, until the uvula is quite obscured.
E aprop itera sobre aquela motas veguadas entro qu’es secca, e guarda te que no fassas aquesta curacio al comesament de l’aveniment de apostemas, quar trop ajustaria en le apostema, e no cove que tu fassas aquo, sino deves la declaracio de apostema de lu caut.	And then repeat this process many times until it is dry, and be careful not to apply this cure at the beginning of the appearance of abscesses, because it would be too intense for the abscess, and you should not do that, but rather declare the appearance of the abscess first.
Mays si no es a tu present aquest instrument, lahoras pren una cana e compon en la extramitat de lu un clos de huou, per so que la boca del malaute sia comborida, quar le closc del huou prohibeys la vapor comburir la boca.	But if you do not have this instrument, then take a reed and compose in the extremity of it a bundle of cotton, so that the mouth of the patient may be closed, because the closure of the cotton prevents the vapor from burning the mouth.
E aquesta curacio es bona am salut.	And this cure is good for health.
Capitol .xxxviii.	Chapter XXXVIII.
De extraccio d’espinas e de aquo que adhereys en le golayro e de las autras causas.	On the Extraction of Thorns and of what adheres in the Gullet and of other Causes.
Motas veguadas adhereys en le guolayro o spina de peys o alcuna autra causa.	Many times something adheres in the gullet or thorn from a fish or some other cause.
Adonc cove que tu extraguas aquo que de aquels es apparent, sobre le qual catz la vista, pus que tu premes la lengua am instrument denant solelh, per so que a tu sia declarat aquo que es en la guola.	Then you must extract what is apparent from those things that are seen above the gullet, because you grasp the tongue with an instrument in front of the sun, so that it may be declared to you what is in the throat.
E aquo que no apar e es a tu occultat en le guolayro, cove que tu fassas vomir le malaute denant que la vianda sia degerida en l’estomac, quar fort leu la causa annexsa le golayro sira foro-getada per vomit; o que deglusia le malaute una pessa de nap o de razit de laytuga o un boci de pa sec; o prengua una pessa de sponga marina sequa leon, e lia aquela fortment am fiel, e aprop le malaute transglussia aquela, quar cum perve al loc en le qual so spinas e es extrahuda, lahoras so foro-getatz.	And what does not appear and is hidden to you in the gullet, then you must make the patient vomit before the food has been digested in the stomach, because the attached cause to the gullet will be forgotten by vomiting; or that the patient drinks a potion of nape or of razit of laytuga or a bowl of dry bread; or takes a piece of marine sponge, and binds it tightly with a thread, and then makes the patient swallow it, so that when it reaches the place where the thorns are and is extracted, then they will be forgotten.
E mays pren una anguila e be am fiel liada, e sia dedintz mesa e soptament sia extrayta; o pren un porr e soptament le metas e soptament l’en tratz.	And then take a snake and bind it tightly with a thread, and place it inside the patient's mouth and then pull it out; or take a fork and place it inside the patient's mouth and then pull it out.
Mays si no so foro-getatz am aquelas causas las quals havem ditas, lahoras husa de un instrument de plom segon aquesta forma:	But if those causes are not forgotten as we have said, then take an instrument of lead according to this form:
E sia pus gros que ray un petit, e en la extramitat de lu sia conquavitat la qual tu entrometas en la sua guola am facilitat.	And be more thick than a reed, a little one, and in the extremity of it be a concavity which you insert into the patient's gullet with ease.
E el aga le sieu cap elevat en sus, e guarda te que·l tocament del sieu os de la gola, per so que endevengua a lu cos e am aquela que enpellesca le os o la spina, o que aquel le metge am la sua ma.	And it will make the patient's head rise upwards, and be careful that the touch of its bone in the throat is gentle, so that it does not disturb the flesh or the spine, or put pressure on the bone or the thorn.
Mays empero que·l malaute aquel entrometa es miels, per la sua sciencia del loc de la causa annexa e enpellisca en jos, e tira la sua ma am le instrument en sus, tot aquo segon la quantitat la qual es a lu preparada entro que sia foro-getada.	But meanwhile, the patient will move that part of his body into a sweet position, by virtue of his knowledge of the location of the attached cause and its descent below, and pull his hand with the instrument towards him, all according to the quantity which is prepared in advance until it is forgotten.
Capitol .xxxix.	Chapter XXXIX.
De extraccio de sancguisugua annexsa al golayro.	On the Extraction of Blood from the Gullet.
Quan es medicada sanguisugua am aquo que havem dit en la divisio de la curacio am medicinas e no comfereys, considera lahoras en le guolayro del malaute al solelh, pus que tu aias compremuda la lengua de lu am instrument le qual a tu havem recomtat.	When blood is medicated with what we have said in the division of cure with medicines and does not agree, then consider that in the gullet of the patient to the sun, because you have grasped his tongue with an instrument which we have recommended.
Donc si tu vezes la sancguisugua, extratz aquela am onci petit o am gesti subtils decentment.	Therefore, if you see blood, extract it with a small onion or with subtle gestures decently.
E si no es a tu possible estrayre am aquel, lahoras pren una canula concava e entromet aquela en lo guolayro del malaute, e aprop pausa en la concavitat de la canula un ferr ignit, e fay aquo tantas vetz (entro que la sancguisugua sia morta e se osta del guolayro) e abstengua se le malaute tot lo jorn de aygua.	And if it is not possible to extract it with that, then take a concave syringe and insert it into the patient's gullet, and carefully pause in the concavity of the syringe an iron hot instrument, and do this many times (until the blood is dead and comes out of the gullet) and abstain from giving the patient water all day.
E aprop prengua una veyria plena de aygua frega, e obra la boca de lu en aquela, e lava la boca am aquela; e no trasglucia de aquela alcuna causa e maugua l’aygua una hora aprop autra am la sua ma, quar la sancguisugua tantost cum sent l’aygua catz.	And then take a vial full of vinegar water, and work the patient's mouth with that, and wash the mouth with that; and do not let any cause emerge from that and spoil the water for an hour afterwards by putting it in the patient's hand, because the blood will soon come out when it feels the water.
Mays si no es foro-getada am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras subfumigua le malaute am cimetz o am assafetida per le instrument le qual havem recomtat en la sufumiguacio de uvula.	But if it is not forgotten as we have recommended, then subfumigate the patient with camphor or with assafetida by the instrument which we have recommended in the subfumigation of the uvula.
Fay aquo, so en quar cayra.	This is how it will be, and then it will fall out.
E es un’autra manieyra de operacio en sufumiguacio de aquela, es que tu prenguas una ola en la qual sian carbos ignitz e la ola sia cuberta am una cobertora en le mieg de la qual sia un trauc, e sia compausat en aquel trauc la extremitat del instrument; e aprop dega desus la subfumigacio; e pause le malaute la sua boca en la extremitat de la canula, e claugua la sua boca per que la subfumiguacio no sia foro-getada entro que sapias que la subfumigacio es pervenguda a la sancguisugua, quar la sancguisugua tantost cayra.	And there is another manner of operation in the subfumigation of that, which is: you take a bath in which are hot coals and the bath is covered with a cloth in the middle of which is a hole; and the extremity of the instrument is composed in that hole; and then carefully wait above the subfumigation; and have the patient's mouth open at the extremity of the syringe, and close their mouth so that the subfumigation is not forgotten until you know that the subfumigation has reached the blood, for the blood will soon fall out.
E si no catz, lahoras tu itera la subfumiguacio motas vetz, e abstengua le malaute de beure, e mange causas saladas e alhs, e no begua aygua, e ayssi necessari es que am aquest regiment sia fora-getada.	And if it does not fall out, then you must iterate the subfumigation many times, and abstain from giving the patient water to drink, and give them salty causes and salted foods, and not give them vinegar water, and so it is necessary that with this regimen it will be forgotten.
E aquesta es la forma del instrument am le qual es trayta sancguisugua del guolayro quan es vista; e es semblant a forceps ayssi cum vezes, sino quar es en lu alcuna curvitat:	And this is the form of the instrument with which blood is drawn from the gullet when it is seen; and it is similar to forceps like those, but with some curvature.
le qual sia mesa al guolayro, e la extremitat de lu es semblant a bec de ciconia, que es guanta, en la qual es aspretat de lima, per so quar, quan comprem alcuna causa, aquela no leyssa.	The one that is placed in the gullet, and its extremity is like a stork's beak, which is grasped, in which a lime is sharpened, so that when it compresses any cause, that one does not loosen.
Capitol .xl.	Chapter XL.
En le qual es la suma del sermo en apercio de apostemas e en seccio de lor.	In which is the summary of the sermon in warning against abscesses and their section.
Les apostemas so motas specias, de motas manieyras, segon que ve rememoracio de lor, de quascuna en aquest libre.	Abscesses are many species, of many manners, according to the memory of them, each one in this book.
E so diversas en perforacio e seccio de lor per doas manieyras, de las quals la una es per la specia de apostemas en si meteys; e per aquo que comprem de las humiditatz.	And thus diverse in perforation and section of them by two manners, of which one is by the species of abscesses themselves; and therefore that they comprehend the humors.
E la segonda manieyra es prop les locs en les quals accideys del cos, quar le apostema accident en le cap es autra de la apostema accident en le cul; e le apostema en le loc carnos accident es autra del apostema accident en junctura; e a quascun de lor es son juguament per operacio.	And the second manner is according to the places in which they occur in the body, because an abscess that occurs on the head is another from one that occurs on the tailbone; and an abscess in a fatty location is another from one that occurs at a joint; and each of them has its own judgment by operation.
E mays de apostemas so alcunas las quals cove que no sian perforadas sino aprop maturacio de la sania en aquels o compliment de lor.	And besides, some abscesses are such that they must not be pierced, but rather allowed to mature and heal on their own.
So autras apostemas les quals cove que sian traucatz quan son cruzes, e no son maturatz segon lor compliment, ayssi cum apostemas que son propdas a las juncturas, quar apostema quan ve prop junctura, lo esser de lu es prolonguat entro que·s poyreys aquo que es en le circuit de lu, e fort leu son corromputz les liamentz o les nervis de aquela junctura, per que es fayta causa de contraccio de aquel membre; o es apostema prop de membre principal, e si tu tardas la perforacio de lu entro sia madurat nosira al membre principal; o es prop le cul, donc perfora aque no-madurat; e no cove que·l perforas cru, de no-complida degestio, sino aquel que es prop del cul, per so que no poyresca le preon de lu e sia elonguat a las partidas dedintz del cul, e sia fayta fistula, o que sia fayt en le terme de lu que no sia sanat.	And some abscesses are such that they must be pierced when they are crossed, and not allowed to mature according to their natural course, just like those abscesses that are near joints, for an abscess that occurs near a joint is prolonged into the circuit of the joint, and then it is corrupted by affecting the ligaments or nerves of that joint, causing contraction of that member; or it is an abscess near the main limb, and if you delay the puncture until the abscess has matured on the main limb, or it is an abscess near the anus, so pierce it when not yet mature; and do not pierce a green abscess, without proper digestion, but only that which is near the anus, in order to avoid prolonging the passage of stool and causing a fistula, or that it becomes a condition that cannot be cured.
Mays cove que tu sapias la hora de la perforacio de la apostema, e aysso es quan es maturat.	But you must know the time of puncturing the abscess, and thus is when it has matured.
E sapias que es madurat quan es la cedacio de la dolor e la cessacio de la febre, e aprop la diminucio de la rogor e de la pulsacio, e la acuitat del cap del apostema, e les autres senhals.	And you must know that it is mature when there is cessation of pain and fever, and accordingly the decrease in swelling and pulse, and the sharpness of the tip of the abscess, and other signs.
E quar cove que sapias la perforacio cazer en le loc pus dejos del apostema e de pus venient de curacio de la eminencia.	And thus it is necessary to know that the puncture should be made in the most dependent part of the abscess and closest to the cure of the prominence.
E perforacio tostemps sia per le lonc de la carn o del cors, si las apostemas son en las partidas de las mas o dels pes, e en loc dels lacertz, de las cordas dels nervis, de las arcerias; e, al derier, en totz locs enguals en les quals no es reflecio; quar en aquels que so reflectitz, usa de perforacio segon aquel membre.	And puncture should be made through the length of flesh or muscle if the abscesses are in the parts of the arms or legs, and in areas of the loins, cords of nerves, or tendons; and finally, in all locations where there is no reflection; because in those that are reflected, use puncture according to that member.
Mays quan le apostema es en loc carnos, lahoras miels es que leysses la perforacio de lu entro que sia confermada la digestio de lu segon compliment, ayssi quo havem dit; quar si tu perforas aquel denant aquo, es prolonguat le cors del poyre de lu e de mota sordicia, e fort leu las labias de lu so enduradas e la profunditat de lu.	And when the abscess is in a fatty location, then it is better that you wait until the perforation of it is confirmed by the digestion of it according to its natural course, as we have said; because if you puncture it too soon, it will prolong the process of the body's discharge and much pus, and therefore the lips of the abscess will be hardened and its depth increased.
Mays alcus apostemas so perforatz segon la latitut de la carn o del cos deves la necessitat, o segon aquo del qual lo membre indigeys.	But some abscesses are punctured according to the necessity of the location of the flesh or muscle, or according to what the affected member demands.
E cove que administres petita perforacio , e·n les apostemas grans gran perforacio e ampla o motas seccios segon la diversitat de la grandesa dels apostemas.	And it is necessary to administer a small puncture, and in large abscesses, a large puncture or multiple sections according to the diversity of the size of the abscesses.
E autras so dels apostemas en les quals cove que la codena sia conquavada e sia encidida, quan es fayta ayssi quo pan e fayta es en terme que ja stigua, ayssi cum aquel que accideys en trops de dubelec e de bubos.	And some abscesses are such that the cord needs to be concaved and incised, when it is done in a way that is already stated, like those that occur in troops of boils and buboes.
E de aquels so que so insciditz am seccio havent tres angles; e de aquels es en le qual es inscidit ayssi cum figura de fuelha de mirtra, ayssi cum las apostemas dels angonars.	And some abscesses are such that they are incised with a section having three angles; and of those is the one which is incised like the figure of a myrtle leaf, as with those abscesses of the gout sufferers.
E de lor so en les quals es administrada seccio redonda e seccio lunar, e semblantz ad aquels.	And some abscesses are such that they receive a circular section and a lunar section, and resemble those.
Mays aquel al qual no es cap ayssi cum son apostemas leons superficials, cove que tu perforas aquel am perforacio superficial, o plana tant solament.	But as for the one that is not like those abscesses of lions, which are superficial and do not have a deep or complex shape, it is necessary to pierce it with a superficial puncture or only a flat one.
E cove quant le apostema es gros e ya ha colligit mota sania, que perfores aquel e no te coytes que extraguas tot le poyre en aquela hora; habantz extratz de aquel una partida, e aprop opila le apostema entro al autre dia, e aprop extratz una partida major, e aprop fa aquo motas veguadas segon graduacio entro que sia foro-getat.	And it is necessary when the abscess is large and has collected much pus, that you pierce it and do not hesitate to extract all the pus in that hour; having extracted one part, and then stop the abscess until the next day, and then extract a larger part, and so on many times according to gradation until it is forgotten.
E majorment si·l malaute es de freol vertut, o femna prens, o enfant petit, o viel en decrepitut, quar l’esperit animal motas vetz es resolvut am la egressio de la sania, e fort leu mor le malaute, e tu operte les.	And especially if the patient is a young child, or an elderly person in decline, because the animal spirit many times is resolved through the egression of pus, and then the patient will die, and you should intervene.
Don guarda aquest capitol am gran cautela, e aprop la tua perforacio en la qual perforas aquestz apostemas, cove que abstergescas las plagues e consideras donc si la plagua del apostema es pauca, o es una seccio plana, lahoras tu aministra las qualguas de li o de coto antic; e si le apostema es gran, e las fissuras de la perforacio son motas, lahoras cove que tu pauses meca en quascun trauc entro que pervenguan ensemps.	Therefore, keep this chapter with great caution, and carefully perform the puncture in which you pierce these abscesses, so that you cleanse the plagues and consider whether the plague of the abscess is small, or is a flat section; then administer those of like or similar things; and if the abscess is large, and the fissures of the perforation are many, then it is necessary to pause in each track until they are together.
E si en le apostema es abscindit una partida de la codena o has concavada aquela en le circuit, lahoras cove que tu la complescas de coto viel o de fil fayt de drap de li, ayssi cum quan has traytz pans o razizos, ses humiditat; e strenh aquel entro al tertz dia; e aprop proceseys aquel e cura le am aquo que cove dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And if in the abscess one part of the cord has been severed or has been concaved in the circuit, then it is necessary to complete it with old cloth or a thread made from linen fabric, just as when you are binding pans or razors, its moisture; and strengthen that within three days; and accordingly process it and cure the patient with the same method until they are healed.
Mays si accideys flux de sanc en la hora de la operacio tua, lahoras tu aministra aygua frega e vi agre en les quals mules un drap de li, e pausa aquel sobre le loc del fluxs del sanc motas veguadas.	But if bleeding occurs during your operation, then you should administer vinegar water and wine mixed with linen cloth, and pause that over the location of the bleeding many times.
Mays si persevera le fluxs del sanc, lahoras cove que tu aministres regiment e curacio e polveras las quals he recomtadas en motz locs de aquest nostre libre e de divisio.	But if the bleeding persists, then it is necessary to administer a regimen and cure, and dust those which I have recommended in many places of this our book and division.
Mays si es en temps de hivern, e·l loc de la apostema es loc de motz nervis, lahoras cove que tu enfundas pulvils en vi e oli caut, e pauses aquels sobre les locs.	But if it is in the time of winter, and the location of the abscess is a place of many nerves, then it is necessary to wrap powders in vinegar and oil, warm them, and pause them over those locations.
E si es en estiu, e les locs son carnoses, lahoras cove que tu pauses pulvils enbeguts am aygua e oli o am vi e oli, e tot aquo sia freg entro que sia le ters dia, ayssi cum havem dit, e lahoras cove que tu deslies le apostema e abstergescas aquel e aministres en la curacio de lu aquo que a lu conveneys entro que sia sanat.	And if it is in summer, and the locations are fleshy, then it is necessary to pause powders wrapped in water and oil or vinegar and oil, and all should be cool within three days, just as we have said, and then you must loosen the abscess and cleanse it, and administer the cure according to what is suitable for it until it is healed.
E aysso es aquo que es necessari de la cognicio de la curacio de apostemas universalment, mays segon la via de distinccio ja he dit de tot apostema en qual manieyra es via de la cura de lu per capitols singularment.	And thus this is what is necessary for the knowledge of the cure of abscesses universally, but according to the way of distinction that I have said about each abscess in which manner is the way of its cure by chapters separately.
Capitol .xli.	Chapter XLI.
De seccio de apostemas les quals veno en la codena del cap.	On the Section of Abscesses that occur in the Cord of the Head.
En la codena del cap petitz apostemas, e so de specias de nodes les quals conteno tunicas que so a lor factz ; e las specias de lor so motas.	In the cord of the head small abscesses occur, and there are species of nodes that contain tunics which are according to their facts; and the species of them are many.
E de lor son pingas, e de aquelas so que conteno humiditat semblant a lima.	And among them are pustules, and those that contain moisture similar to lime.
E de aquelas so las quals conteno humiditat semblant a pols, et asemblantz a lor; e de aquelas so que son lapideas, durs.	And among them are those that contain moisture similar to powder, and resembling their own kind; and those that are lithoid, hard.
E en la seccio de totz, e en la extraccio de aquels no es temor, cum deves la exteccio de aquels no fa contrariat arceria.	And in the section of all, and in the extraction of those, there is no fear, as you should not make the extraction cause contraction of the artery.
E la operacio en seccio de aquels es que tu esproes aquels am instrument la forma del qual ve aprop aysso, le qual es apelat entromes, entro que sapias que contengua.	And the operation in section of those is that you express them with an instrument whose form is similar to this, which is called an entrume, until you know what it contains.
Quar si aquo que conte es humiditat, lahoras scindeys aquel am seccio segon la longitut per seccio superficial segon aquesta forma:	Therefore, if what is contained is moisture, then cut it with a section according to its length, in a superficial section following this form:
E comensa en la seccio de la linha de .B. entro a la linha de .G. Donc cum la humiditat es evacuada, lahoras tu excoria aquela pel que conte aquela humiditat, e no leysses de aquela alcuna causa de tot, quar tropas veguadas retorna, si roman de aquela alcuna causa.	And begin in the section of the line .B. up to the line .G. Then, as the moisture is evacuated, cut off that portion which contains that moisture, and do not leave any cause behind, for many times it returns, if some cause remains.
E aprop submergeys coto en enguent egipciach, si es present, e sino, en aygua e sal; e umpleys am aquel la plagua e layssa aquel entro ad autra dia, quar am aquo corrodeys tot so que es romas de aquela pellicula.	And accordingly, submerge the cloth in Egyptian ointment, if present, and if not, in water and salt; and fill it with that and leave it for another day, for by this, you will corrode all that remains of that skin.
E aprop itera sobre aquel coto am enguent egipciach segondament e tersament si indigeyses de lu, entro que·t comfides que no y haia romas alcuna causa de aquela pellicula; lahoras cura la plagua am enguent entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly, iterate over that cloth with Egyptian ointment secondly and thirdly if it is needed of it, until you are confident that there is no remaining cause of that skin; then cure the wound with ointment until it is healed.
E si apostema conte nodi gras, lahoras tu inscideys aquel segon aquesta forma:	And if the abscess contains fatty nodes, then cut into it according to this form:
am seccio havent forma de crotz, e geta oncis entre doas labias de la seccio e scorsa aquel de tota partida, e esforsa la tua vertut en extraccio de la tunica la qual conte aquel.	with a section having the form of a cross, and cut into it between two lips of the section and scrape off all that part, and strain your virtue in extracting the tunic which contains that.
Mays si a tu arceria fa contrarieta, lahoras fay aquo que yeu t’e recontat primieyrament.	But if your artery becomes contracted, then do what I have recounted to you first.
E semblantment fay en le apostema lapificat de seccio e de curacio segon que a tu havem dit; e seccio sobre apostema lapificat es pus leugiera, quar es de pauc sanc e de pauca humiditat.	And similarly do with the lithoid abscess of section and cure according to what we have said; and the section over the lithoid abscess is more gentle, because it has little blood and little moisture.
E alcunas vetz so alcus de aquestz apostemas les quals so en le cap en alcus homes am los quals de tot no es humiditat; la qual causa es quar yeu inscindigui sobre un apostema en le cap de una femna vielha e atrobegui le apostema ayssi cum peyra sorda, aspra, blanqua, la qual no podia esser trinquada, e si a alcu fos am aquela percussit, plaguera aquel.	And sometimes there are cases of these abscesses which are in the head of some men who do not have moisture; and this cause is because you incise over an abscess on the head of an old woman and break open the abscess like a deaf, harsh, white palsy that could not be shaken off, and if any force was applied to it, it would become infected.
Mays en les autres apostemas accidentz en le cap otra aquest no es aquest capitol, ayssi cum les apostemas que veno als caps dels enfantz e deves las razitz de las aurelhas, mays la seccio de aquestz totz sia seccio superficial.	But in other abscesses that occur on the head, it is not this chapter, such as those that occur on the heads of children and in the crevices of the ears, but the section of all these shall be superficial.
E pausa la perforacio de aquels de la partida pus bassa de lor per so que sia alleujat le cos de la sania a las partidas pus bassas.	And pause the puncture at the lower part of them, so that it may be alleviated the body from the pus to the lowest parts.
E aprop cura aquelas am aquo que conveneys ad aquel de curacio.	And accordingly, cure those with what is suitable for its cure.
Capitol .xlii.	Chapter XLII.
De seccio de scrophulas las quals accideyso en le col.	On the Section of Scrofulas which occur in the Neck.
Motas veguadas endeveno aquestas apostemas en le colh e en las aysselhas e en les angonars; e alcunas veguadas accideyso en las autras partidas del cos.	Many times these abscesses occur in the neck and armpits and shoulders; and sometimes they occur in other parts of the body.
E so aquelas que accideysso en le colh, e so motas que so engendradas entre lor, e tota scrofula de aquelas es dintz la sua tunica propria, e ayssi cum en les nodis e apostema del cap, ayssi cum havem recomtat.	And those that occur in the neck, and many which are generated between them, and all the scrofula of those is surrounded by its own tunic, just as with the nodes and abscesses of the head, just as we have recounted.
E las specias de aquestas scrophulas son motas, quar de aquelas so alcunas lapideas, e de aquelas so que conteno humiditatz, e de aquelas so malignas las quals no obeseysso a curacio.	And the species of these scrofulas are many, for some are lithoid, and some contain moisture, and some are malignant which do not yield to cure.
Donc en aquela la qual tu vezes de bona disposicio en le Tocament, de la qual la color de aquo que es manifest es propda a la color de la codena, e es mauguda a tota partida, e no es annexsa am le nervi del colh, ni am las venas, ni am la arceria, e no es preonda, cove que tu inscidiscas aquela am siccio superficial de la partida desus a la partida dejos del cos de la linha de .G. entro la linha de .B., e scorja aquela de tota partida, e exten dos labias de la codena am onci, o am motz oncis si has necessitat de aquels, ayssi cum havem dit en las apostemas del cap, e extratz aquela petit a petit.	Therefore, in that one which you find to be of good disposition in the Tocament, whose manifest color is akin to the color of the cord, and is spread out over all parts, and not annexed to the nerve of the neck, nor to the veins, nor to the artery, and does not swell, then you should incise it with a superficial section from above to below the body along the line of .G. up to the line of .B., and scrape off that part completely, and extend two lips of the cord with one or many oncements if necessary, just as we have said in the abscesses of the head, and extract it little by little.
E es mays cautela que no sia inscidida la vena o nervi.	And be more cautious so that the vein or nerve is not cut.
E sia le spatum no mot agut, que no ajuste a tu la tua ma am inscizio, o que enquiete le malaute, e que inscidas aquo que no es necessari inscidir; quar si inscideysses vena o arceria e prohibeys tu de la tua operacio, lahoras pausa en la plagua vetriol trissat o autras polveras las quals ostan fluxs de sanc, e estrenh la plagua, e layssa aquel entro que·s repausa la acuitat de la apostema e sia mollificada la plagua e comense esser poyrida.	And be careful not to cut too deep, lest you adjust your hand to your own mark or wound the patient, or else you would inscribe something that is not necessary to inscribe; for if you cut into a vein or artery and prohibit your operation, then pause in the wound, whether it is a bruise or other powder that stops bleeding, and strengthen the wound, and leave it until the sharpness of the abscess has subsided and the wound has become softened and begins to heal.
Quan le sanc es abscindit.	When the blood is severed.
Donc retorna a la tua operacio entro que l’aias complida.	Therefore, return to your operation until you have completed it.
E aprop inquireys am le tieu dit indic si es romas alcuna causa de las autras petitas scrophulas, donc inscideys aquelas e munda aquelas.	And accordingly, inquire about the sign given by your teacher if there is any remaining cause of other small scrofulas, then incise those and clean them.
E si es en la razit de la scrophula gran vena, cove lahoras que no inscidas aquela scrophula de la sua razitz.	And if it is in the root of the large scrofula, then it is necessary that you do not incise that scrofula from its roots.
Abantz cove que lies aquela am fiel doblat fort e que leysses aquela entro que caia per si ses nocument.	Therefore, bind it with a double thread and leave it until it falls off on its own without causing harm.
E aprop omple la plagua de coto vielh le qual tu has ja submirgit en enguent egipciac, e aprop cura aquel.	And accordingly, fill the wound with old cloth which you have already submerged in Egyptian ointment, and accordingly cure that.
E si inscides aquela scrophula tota, lahoras cove que tu ajustes las doas labias de la plagua e cuzas2 tantost pus que no y ha romasa deguna superfluitat.	And if you incise that scrofula completely, then it is necessary that you adjust the two lips of the wound and close them as soon as possible so that there remains no superfluous excess.
Mays si tu vezes que haia romasa superfluitat per la grandeza de la scrofula, cove que tu entendas a inscidir la razit de aquela, e astrayra aquela e aministra sutura e aquo que es dit.	But if you find that there remains excess due to the greatness of the scrofula, then it is necessary that you understand how to incise its root, and extract it, and administer suture and what is said.
E aquela de las scrophulas que conteno humiditatz, perfora aquela am perforacio superficial aqui la on appar a tu le loc de maturacio de lu, e pausa perforacio de aquo que siec le pus bas del cos, ayssi cum havem dit.	And that of the scrofulas which contain moisture, pierce it with a superficial puncture at the location where you find the point of maturation of it, and pause puncture at the lowest part of the body, just as we have said.
E aprop aministra perforacio, calguas am enguent e semblantz ad aquels, per so que corroda aquo que es romas de la corropcio.	And accordingly, administer puncture with ointment and similar substances to those, in order that it may corrode what remains of the corruption.
E aprop quan tu vezes la plagua ja esser mundada, lahoras tu cura aquela am enguent de carn generatiu entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly, when you find that the wound is already cleansed, then cure it with ointment of generated flesh until it is healed.
Capitol .xliii.	Chapter XLIII.
De seccio del pilhot del apostema accident dintz le guolayro.	On the Section of Pilling off the Abscess which occurs in the Groin.
Diyssero les antics aquesta seccio en le epilhot, e no vist alcu hom en nostra terra que aquela aia fayta.	The ancients have described this section in the pillography, and I have not seen any man in our land who has practiced it.
E aquesta es la inscriptura del sermo de aquels.	And this is the inscription of the sermon of those.
Mays en les homes haventz esquinencia, cove que sia esquivada la extraccio del epilhot, cum per aquo no sia fayt juvament per so quar totas las venas e las majors del malaute so aqui.	But in men with hemorrhoids, it is necessary to avoid the extraction of the pillography, because through this, there would be no advantage for the patient, since all the veins and main vessels are here.
Mays en aquels que han apostemas cautz en la boca o guolayro o dos aurelhas, quan la malautia no es en la cana, cove husar de la seccio de epilhot a fugir la perdicio la qual es fayta per perfocacio.	But in those who have abscesses located in the mouth or groin or both ears, when the disease is not in the cane, it is necessary to use the section of pillography to flee from the destruction which is caused by perforation.
Donc cove quan volem aquo, que inscidam le epilhot dejos tres cercles dels cercles del epilhot, o quatre am petita seccio per la latitut en aquel que es entre dos cercles per quantitat, que la seccio sia en ciphac, no en la cartillage, e aquest loc es convenent a seccio, quar es privat de carn e les vayselhs de sanc de lu son luhen.	Therefore, when we want to do this, we must incise the pillography behind three circles of the pillography, or four with a small section along the latitude in that which is between two circles by quantity, so that the section be in ciphac, not in cartilage, and this location is suitable for section, because it is deprived of flesh and the vessels of blood are nearby.
E si le metge es pauruc, cove lahoras que extenda la codena del golayro am onci, e aprop fenda la codena entro que pervengua a la canal, mays evite les vaysels de sanc si vetz de aquelas alcuna causa.	And if the doctor is fearful, then it is necessary that he extends the cord of the groin with one incision, and accordingly cuts the cord into the channel, but avoids the vessels of blood if he sees any cause.
E aprop inscida li ciplach segon que havem recomtat; e es significat sobre la seccio de la canal per le flacma le qual es de aquela eyssit am aquo que es de lu disromput e per la abscizio de la votz.	And accordingly, incise the ciphac according to what we have recounted; and it is signified about the section of the channel by the flame which is from that place and comes forth with water which is broken down and by the absorption of the voice.
E layssa la plagua uberta per alcun temps.	And leave the wound open for some time.
Donc cum la hora es remauguda en la qual perforacio es temuda, agregua doas labias de la codena de la plagua, e cus aquela sola ses la cartillage.	Therefore, as the hour is re-matured in which puncture is feared, add two lips of the cord of the wound, and close it alone except for the cartilage.
E aprop administra medicinas que fan naysser la carn entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, administer medicines that make the flesh to heal, until it is healed.
E diyssec Albucasis que la summa del sermo le qual havem recomtat, exposicio no es sino que veias que alcus de aquetz apostemas ja han opilat lo guolayro del malaute, e le malaute es vengut entro a mort, e le ale de lu es entresecat, e alcus van a inscidir le epiglos per so que respire le malaute sobre le loc de la plagua per alcuna respiracio, e sia salvat de mort.	And Albucasis says that the summary of this sermon which we have recounted is nothing but to see that some of these abscesses have opened up the groin of the patient, and the patient has come to death, and the pulse of life is interrupted, and some are about to incise the epigastrium so that the patient may breathe over the location of the wound by some respiration, and be saved from death.
E per aquo comandero layssar la plagua uberta entro que sia consumida la malicia de la malautia; e es la malicia de lu per tres dias; e donc lahoras comandero cosi la plagua, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And therefore, I command to leave the wound open until the evil of the disease is consumed; and this evil lasts for three days; and therefore, I command that way the wound, and cure it until it is healed.
E aquo que yeu he vist per mi meteys, es que una sirventa pres un cotel e mesec le en le sieu golayro e inscidic am aquel una partida de la cana del pulmo, e yeu fu apelat a la curacio de lu, e atrobegui la mugen ayssi cum es mugit del moridos, e descubrigui la plagua e atrobegui le sanc le qual era yssit de la plagua petit.	And what I have seen with my own eyes is that a servant took a cote and placed it in his groin and incised a part of the canal of the lung, and you were called to its cure, and opened up the mouth as if it was crying out like one who is dying, and discovered the wound and opened up the blood which was flowing from the small part of the wound.
Donc yeu fo confessat que aquela no havia inscidit vena ni guidegi, e le vent yssia de la plagua, e curegui aquela entro que foc sanada.	Therefore, you were confessed that it had not cut into a vein nor a nerve, and the wind was coming from the wound, and cured it until it was healed.
E no accidic a la sirventa si no rauquiera en la votz, e aprop alcus dias retornec ad miloracio de las suas dispozicios.	And there was no harm to the servant except that he grew hoarse in his voice, and accordingly some days returned to better disposition.
E ara dic yeu que en la seccio del epilhot no ha temor.	And now I say to you that in the section of pillography, there is no fear.
Capitol .xliv.	Chapter XLIV.
De seccio sobre apostema le qual accideys en le golayro defora, e es apelat hernia del golayro.	On the Section of Abscess which occurs in the Groin outside and is called Hernia of the Groin.
Aquest apostema nompnat hernia del golayro es apostema gran segon la color del cors, e es mot en las femnas.	This abscess is named Hernia of the Groin and is a large abscess according to the color of the body, and it is more common in women.
E es segon dos manieyras, quar o es natural o accidental.	And it is according to two manners, either natural or accidental.
E en le natural no es engen de curar.	And in the natural one, there is no way to cure it.
E l’accidental es segon dos manieyras del qual la un es semblant a nodes grasses, e l’autra manieyra es semblant apostema le qual es fayt per nodacio de arteria, e en aquel es temor.	And the accidental one is according to two manners of which one is similar to fatty nodes, and the other manner is similar to abscesses that are caused by the constriction of an artery, and in that one there is fear.
E no cove que·s fassa presumpcio a lu cum ferr sino en aquel que es petit.	And it is not necessary to make assumptions about it unless it is small.
E tu proha aquel e investigua aquel am le dit, e si atrobas lu semblant a nodi gras, e no es suspendut am alcuna de las venas, lahoras tu inscideys aquel ayssi cum les nodes, e extratz aquel am aquo que conte lu de la pel e bursiclam; e sino, lahoras es perscrutat tot le sieu esser, e aprop cura le loc am aquo que cove de curacio entro que sia sanat.	And you should proceed with that and investigate it according to the dictum, and if you find it similar to fatty nodes, and it is not suspended from any of the veins, then you should incise it as one would incise nodes, and extract it with what contains the skin and bursa; and otherwise, you should scrutinize all its being, and accordingly cure the location where it needs to be cured until it is healed.
Capitol .xlv.	Chapter XLV.
De seccio de las specias de nodes.	On the Section of the Species of Nodes.
Dels nodes so motas specias e yeu ja he dit totas las specias de lor en la divisio.	Of the nodes, many species and you have already said all their species in the division.
E cove que yeu recomte assi la diferencia entre node e exitura cum fassa dubitacio.	And it is necessary that you recount thus the difference between a node and an excrescence, so as to dispel doubt.
Donc yeu dic que am exitura es caliditat e febre e dolors vehementz entro que es sedada la ebullicio de la superfluitat; e es complida putrefaccio que lahora cessa la febre, la dolor e la calor.	Therefore, you say that with an excrescence there is heat and fever and violent pains until the ebullition of the superfluity is calmed; and it is completed putrefaction which then ceases the fever, the pain, and the heat.
Mays am node no es caliditat ni febre ni dolor, e conte aquel ciphac leon le qual es al u sac propri.	But with a node there is no heat or fever or pain, and it contains that ciphac lion which is in its own sack.
E es segon la color del cors, e le comensament de lu es cum un ceze e es fayt ayssi cum vace, sia major o minor, e son segon dos specias, quar o so grassas e conteno humiditat, e las colors de la humiditat son motas, segon que yeu diyssi en la divisio.	And it is according to the color of the body, and its beginning is like a cheese and is made thus as a vessel, whether major or minor, and they are two species, either fatty and containing moisture, and the colors of the moisture are many, according to what you said in the division.
Donc cove, quan pervenas a la curacio de node, que exprohes aquel e inquiras aquel al comensament am sturment le qual es apelat intromes, segon que vindra la sua forma en le capitol le qual es aprop aquest.	Therefore, when you come to the cure of a node, that you expose it and inquire into its beginning with a instrument which is called an intrumentum, according to what will come forth in the chapter which is appropriate to this.
E es manieyra de inquisicio de apostemas e de totz nodes, e es que tu prenguas aquest sturment e entromet aquel en le loc pus humit le qual atrobas en le apostema, e tu revolveras les tieus ditz am aquel petit a petit entro que sapias que·l sturment ja ha penetrat la codena.	And it is the manner of inquiring into abscesses and all nodes, that you take this instrument and introduce it into the most humid location which you find in the abscess, and you turn the points of the instrument little by little until you know that the instrument has penetrated to the cord.
E aprop ultima la tua ma segon la mesura de la grandeza del apostema, e aprop extratz le entromes e considera aquo que es yssit en le vestigi de lu.	And accordingly, your hand should be last according to the measure of the greatness of the abscess, and accordingly extract the intrumentum and consider what is situated in its vestige.
E si es fora-getada la humiditat corrent, de qualque color sia, lahoras tu le inscideys am seccio superficial segon que he dit en les autres apostemas.	And if the moisture current is forgotten, of whatever color it may be, then you should incise it with a superficial section according to what I have said in other abscesses.
E si del vestigi de l’intromes no hieys humiditat, lahoras sapias que es gras.	And if from the vestige of the intrumentum there is no moisture, then you should know that it is fat.
E secca sobre lu am seccio havent forma de crotz segon aquesta forma:	And dry it over with a section having the form of a cross according to this form:
ayssi cum t’e ensenhat, e suspen aquel am oncis, e excorja la codena de tota part am facilitat, e guarda la pel o sac, si podes, sobre aquel e extraguas aquela sania am le node.	Thus as I have taught you, and suspend it with one incision, and excise the cord from all parts with ease, and preserve the skin or sack, if possible, over that and extract that pus from the node.
Mays si es romput en la operacio, no es possible extrayre aquela sana, e motas veguadas endeve aquo, e lahoras tu la extratz a pessas entro que de lu no romangua denguna causa.	But if it is broken in the operation, then it is not possible to extract that pus, and many times it happens so, and accordingly you should extract it piecemeal until there is no longer any cause from it.
Quar si de lu roman denguna causa, pauc o trop, le node retorne segon le mays.	For if from it remains no cause, a little or too much, the node will return to its former state.
E si tu vezes que de lu roman alcuna part petita, lahoras comple la plagua de alcunas polveras corrosivas agudas e strenh la plagua, e pausa sobre aquela que sede apostema caut, e cura aquel del autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	And if you find that from it remains some small part, then complete the wound with certain corrosive powders acute and strengthen the wound, and pause over that which is seated apostema cautiously, and cure that from other cure until it is healed.
E si es node gran, lahoras tu cus las doas labias de lu e cura aquel am aquo que encarna.	And if it is a great node, then you should close the two lips of it and cure it with that which nourishes.
Mays si vena pulsatil es a lu contraria, o no-pulsatil, lahoras tu coyta e huemple le loc de zegi trissat que es vetriol e leyssa aquel streyt per dos dias o per tres entro que·s poyresca la plagua e que repause la ebullicio del sanc; e aprop retorna a inscindir aquo que es romas del node.	But if the pulsating vein is opposite to it, or non-pulsating, then you should compress and apply pressure to the location of threefold stitches that are vertigo-like, and let that rest for two or three days until the wound is quieted and the ebullition of blood ceases; and accordingly return to incising what remains of the node.
Capitol .xlvi.	Chapter XLVI.
De las formas del sturmentz necessaris en seccio e perforacio.	On the Forms of Instruments necessary in Section and Perforation.
De aquels so las formas dels intromesas, e so de tres specias, que de aquels es alcu gran, e de lor es migier, e de lor es petit.	Of those, the forms of intruments are three species, that is to say, some are great, some medium, and some small.
La forma de intromes gran es aquesta:	The form of great intrument is this:
La forma de intromes migier es aquesta:	The form of medium intrument is this:
La forma de intromes petit es aquesta:	The form of small intrument is this:
Sian faytz de ferr, de alfulud, de extremitatz cayradas decentment, per so que festino le intrament en les apostemas.	They are made of iron, of alfulud, and of curved extremities descending, in order that the instrument may be inserted into abscesses.
E aquestas so las formas dels experientz, e son nompnatz albered, e un de aquels es apelat berid.	And these are the forms of instruments, and they are named "albered", and one of them is called "berid".
E so de tres especias, quar de lor es gran, migier e pauc.	And there are three species, that is to say, some are great, some medium, and some small.
La forma de experient gran, forma de lu:	The form of great instrument, the shape of it:
La forma de experient migier, forma de lu:	The form of medium instrument, the shape of it:
La forma de experient pauc, forma de lu:	The form of small instrument, the shape of it:
Conveneysso que sian per aquels apostemas e exituras e fistulas e bubos per so que entre aquelas so dels osses e de autras causas.	Conveniently, these are for those abscesses and excrescences and fistulas and boils, because among them there are of bones and of other causes.
E so faytz redontz, grosses, leons, ayssi cum grans agulhas am las quals son cosidas las selhas, e son faytas de eram citri, o de eram o de ferr, o de argent, E las milhors so quan so faytas de eram citri.	And thus they are made of redontz, grosses, leons, just like great needles with which the seams are sewn, and they are made of terra citri, or of earth or iron or silver, And the best ones are when they are made of terra citri.
E son faytz les experient de plum negre, les quals se acordan que per aquels sian ubertas las fistulas en la conquavitat de las quals so reflexios, que sian reflectidas am la sua levitat am aquelas refleccios.	And they are made of black plume instruments, which are adapted to those in which the fistulas are located in the concavity of which there are reflections, which are reflected in their lightness with those reflections.
E so de tres specias, quar alcus de lor so loncs, e dels autres migiers, e dels autres breus, segon la quantitat del ample de la fistula e de la strictura de lu.	And there are three species, that is to say, some of them are long, and some medium, and some short, according to the quantity of the width of the fistula and its constriction.
Forma del experient gran de plom:	Form of the great instrument of lead:
Forma del experient migier de plom:	Form of the medium instrument of lead:
Forma del experient petit de plom:	Form of the small instrument of lead:
Las formas dels oncis so de motas specias, quar de aquels so alcus simples, als quals es una curvitat solament, e so de tres specias: grans, paucs e migiers.	The forms of the needles are many species, that is to say, some are simple, which have only one curvature, and there are three species: great, small, and medium.
E de lor so uncis orps, e so de tres specias.	And among them are orphic needles, and there are three species.
E de aquels so uncis haventz doas curvaturas, e so de tres specias.	And among them are needles with two curvatures, and there are three species.
E de lor so haventz tres curvaturas, e so de tres specias.	And among them are needles with three curvatures, and there are three species.
E totz aquetz so necessaris en lor loc.	And all these are necessary in their place.
Forma de unci simple gran, forma de lu:	Form of a simple great needle, the shape of it:
Forma de unci simple migier:	Form of a simple medium needle:
Forma de unci simple pauc, forma de lu:	Form of a simple small needle, the shape of it:
Forma de unci orp gran:	Form of an orphic great needle:
Forma de unci orp migier, forma de lu:	Form of an orphic medium needle, the shape of it:
Forma de unci orp pauc, forma de lu:	Form of an orphic small needle, the shape of it:
Forma de unci gran havent dos curvaturas:	Form of a great needle having two curvatures:
Forma de unci migier havent dos curvatas:	Form of a medium needle having two curvatures:
Forma de unci pauc havent dos curvaturas:	Form of a small needle having two curvatures:
Forma de unci gran havent tres curvaturas:	Form of a great needle having three curvatures:
Forma de unci migier havent tres curvaturas:	Form of a medium needle having three curvatures:
Forma de unci pauc havent tres curvaturas:	Form of a small needle having three curvatures:
E aquestas so las formas dels scalpels am les quals son seccatz e scorjatz les nodes e le apostemas, e so de tres specias, quar de aquels es gran, migier, e pauc.	And these are the forms of scalpels with which nodes and abscesses are sectioned and excised, and there are three species, that is to say, some are great, some medium, and some small.
Forma de scapel gran:	Form of a great scalpel:
Forma del scapel migier:	Form of a medium scalpel:
Forma de scapel pauc:	Form of a small scalpel:
Las extramitatz de aquels am les quals es fayta seccio so agudas e las autres extramitatz so no-agudas, e no so pausadas en tal manieyra, sino per que sia fayt juvament en la excorjacio dels nodes la temor de inscizio de vena o de nervi, e per aquels sia sanat le malaute e atrobe tranquilitat un petit per la adustio la qual atroba deves la excoriacio del apostema.	The extremities of those with which section is made are sharp and the other extremities are not sharp, and they are not paused in such a way that there is no fear of cutting into a vein or nerve, and by them the patient is cured and obtains tranquility for a little while due to the adjustment found necessary for the excision of the abscess.
E aquestas son las formas de almagidas, e so de tres specias: gran, migier e pauc, ayssi cum veyras.	And these are the forms of ligatures, and there are three species: great, medium, and small, just like veins.
La forma de magda gran:	The form of a great ligature:
Forma de magda migier:	Form of a medium ligature:
Forma de magda pauc:	Form of a small ligature:
Sian faytas de eram e so semblantz de ray am le qual e fayt alcofol.	They are made of terra and resemble rays with which alcohol is made.
E es en la extramitat lada punctada am spatum occultada e en aquela corr a las partidas dedintz e defora, quan tu vols, ayssi cum veses.	And it has on the pointed end a hidden point and in that it goes through the parted parts within and without, as you see.
Las formas de spatimis, les quals so amaguatz entre los ditz deves la perforacio dels apostemas e no les percebo les malautes, e so de tres specias: gran, migier e pauc.	The forms of spatimis, which are hidden between the said points for the perforation of abscesses and do not perceive the patients, and there are three species: great, medium, and small.
E aquestas so las formas de aquels:	And these are the forms of those:
Las formas de ventozas am las quals es abscindit le flux del sanc, e so de tres specias; gran, migiera e pauca; las formas de lu:	The forms of ventozas with which the flow of blood is arrested, and there are three species: great, medium, and small; the forms of it:
Sian faytas de eram citri, redondas am alcuna longitut , e sian subtils.	They are made of terra citri, rounded in some length, and are subtle.
E cove que sian aquestas specias de ventosas deves tu grans, migieras e paucas, per so que per aquelas abscindas flux de sanc am velocitat en necessitat, e lahoras quan a tu primieyrament no es medicina.	And it is necessary that you have these species of ventozas, great, medium, and small, in order that through them the flow of blood may be arrested with speed when needed, and therefore, when your first remedy is not medicine.
Enpero no uses de aquelas ad abscidir sanc en tot loc del cors, e non uses sino en locs carnoses, ayssi cum en les lacertis de las cambas e de las coyssas, e en les lacertz dels brasses, e de las mamillas e del ventre e dels engonars, e semblantz a lor dels lacertz carnoses humitz.	However, you should not use them to arrest blood in all parts of the body, and you should only use them in fleshy locations, just like in the skin folds of the thighs and groins, and in the armpits and nipples and belly and groin areas, and similar to those of fleshy human skin.
E alcunas veguadas son faytz de aquels strumentz autres petitz semblantz scorsas de fisacs segon aquesta forma; per les quals lo sanc es abscindit quan es fayt per fleubotomia, o deves inscizio de vena o de arceria.	And sometimes they are made of those small instruments resembling scissors according to this form; by which the blood is arrested when it is cut through phlebotomy, or due to incision of a vein or artery.
E alcunas veguadas son faytas redondas segon aquesta forma:	And sometimes they are made rounded according to this form:
Capitol .xlvii.	Chapter XLVII.
De la cura de las mamillas dels homes las quals so asembladas de femnas.	On the Cure of Men's Breasts which are assembled like Women's.
Alcunas veguadas so infladas las mamillas de alcus homes deves le compliment del dormir cum comensan esser pellutz, e aprop so infladas las mamillas, e so asembladas las mamillas de las femnas, e romano apostemosas, lejas.	Sometimes the breasts of some men become swollen as they begin to sleep, and accordingly they become swollen, and the breasts like those of women, apostematosed, distant.
E ad aquel que avoreys aquo, cove que inscidisca aquelas am seccio lunar segon aquesta forma, de la linha de .B. entro a la linha de .G., e aprop excorja la groceza tota, e aprop uempla la plagua de medicament encarnatiu, e aprop ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am cosidura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And to that one who has this condition, it is necessary to incise those parts with a lunar section according to this form, from the line of .B. to the line of .G., and accordingly excise all the swelling, and accordingly fill the wound with an incarnate medicine, and accordingly adjust the two lips of the wound with stitching, and cure that one until it is healed.
Mays si la mamilla declina a las partidas dejos e es mollificada per la sua magnitut ayssi cum endeve a las femnas, lahoras sia fendut en dos latz sieus pus sobiras, am dos seccios semblantz a figura lunar, de las quals quascuna sia contenguda en l’autra deves la fi de quascuna, entro que sia que la linha major contengua la menor segon aquesta forma de la linha de .B. e la linha de .G. E aprop excorja la codena la qual es entre dos labias de la plagua, e osta la pingueza, e aministra aquo que havem dit de la sutura e de las polveras aquo que es necessari en la curacio entro que sia sanat.	But if the breast declines to its parts and is softened by its magnitude, just like in women, then it should be cut into two equal parts, with two sections resembling a lunar figure, of which each one should be contained within the other until the end of each one, so that the major line contains the minor according to this form from the line of .B. to the line of .G. And accordingly excise the cord which is between the two lips of the wound, and stop the swelling, and administer that which we have said about suturing and powders which are necessary for the cure until it is healed.
E si tu non conpleysses la inscizio de aquo que cove inscidir per la inquietut del malaute, e per flux de sanc, lahoras cove que huemplas la plagua de coto submergit en enguent corrosiu e layssa aquel entro que aquo corroda que es romas de la grayssa, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if you do not complete the incision of that which should be cut because of the unease of the patient and the flow of blood, then it is necessary to fill the wound with a submergent potion in corrosive oil and leave that one until the corroded part that remains of the grayness, and accordingly cure that one until it is healed.
Capitol .xlviii.	Chapter XLVIII.
De perforacio de apostemas que veno dejos le titillic.	On the Perforation of Abscesses that come forth with Lichenification.
Aquetz apostemas que veno dejos le titillic so de las specias de scrophulas, durs, las quals conte una pel que es sac.	Those abscesses that come forth with lichenification are of the species of scrofulae, hard ones, which contain a bag of skin.
E de aquelas so alcunas que conteno humiditatz; e aquelas que conteno humiditatz cove que sian inscididas am seccio lunar segon aquesta figura: de la linha de .G. a la linha de .B. E cum es tot evacuat aquo que es en le apostema de la sania, lahoras tu le comple de coto viel e leysa le entro al autra dia.	And some of those contain humidity; and those that contain humidity must be incised with a lunar section according to this figure: from the line of .G. to the line of .B. And when all the pus is evacuated from the abscess, then you should fill it with good oil and leave it until the next day.
E aprop le coto sia ostat e sia curat am enguent convenient ad aquo, entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, the oil should be stopped and the wound should be cured with a suitable poultice for that, until it is healed.
E si le apostema de las specias dels nodes es, e de las scrophulas, lahoras tu scindeys sobre aquel ayssi cum havem dit en la seccio sobre las scrophulas engualment.	And if the abscess is of the species of nodes and scrofulae, then you should cut over it just as we have said in the section on scrofulae similarly.
May si la plagua es extenduda en aysso que yesca poyredura, lahoras administra en lu cauteri segon que en aquo havem denant dit.	And if the wound is extended in such a way that it becomes a poultice, then you should administer to it a cautery according to what we have said before.
Capitol .xlix.	Chapter XLIX.
De seccio de apostemas que accideysso per arceria o per vena.	On the Section of Abscesses that occur through Artery or Vein.
Quan arceria es rompuda, e la codena es consolidada la qual es sobre aquela, lahoras motas veguadas accideys apostema E les senhals per les quals es conoguda que imflamacio e apostema sian per la arteria o per vena: quar quan apostema es per arceria es lonc agreguat en le preon del cors; e que quan inpelleysses le apostema am les tieus ditz, sentes en lu quays sia stridor.	When an artery is broken and the cord which is above it becomes consolidated, then many times an abscess occurs. And the signs by which it is known that inflammation and abscess are due to the artery or vein: for when an abscess is caused by an artery, it is long aggregated in the precordium of the body; and when you impelate the abscess with those said ties, you will feel a stridor in it.
E aquel que es per vena es redon al manifest del cors.	And that which is caused by a vein is rounded to the manifest of the chest.
E seccio sobre aquest apostema es error, e majorment en aquel que es dejos las aysselhas, e en les angonars, e en le col, e en motz locs del cors; e es mot gran, donc cove que la sua curacio am ferr sia esquivada, e aquel que es en las extramitatz, o al cap, cove que sia evitat.	And the section on this abscess is an error, and most especially in those that are situated near the armpits, groins, neck, and many other places of the body; and it is very great, therefore it is necessary to avoid its cure with iron, and that which is located in the extremities or at the head should be avoided.
Mays sobre aquel que es de lor per imflacio de l’orrifici de la arceria, scindeys en la codena seccio en le lonc; e aprop huebre la seccio am uncis e aprop la arceria, e deliura de las tunicas entro que sia descuberta.	But on that which is due to the inflammation of the orifice of the artery, you should cut in the cord section in length; and accordingly, you should make the section with scissors and accordingly apply it to the artery, and deliver from the tunics until it is uncovered.
E aprop met sobre aquel agulha e fay aquela penetrar entro al autre latz, e estrenh la arceria am fiel doble en dos locs, — la qual causa yeu a tu eyssenhegui en extraccio de doas arcerias les quals so en les templars.	And accordingly, you should sew that thread and make it penetrate into the other side, and tighten the artery with a double thread in two places, — which cause is to your eyesight in extracting two arteries which are in the temples.
E aprop punh le loc le qual es entre dos liamentz am spatum entro que yesca le sanc tot que es en lu, e sia dissolvut le apostema.	And accordingly, you should push the place which is between two ligaments with a spatula until the blood that is in it flows out and the abscess is dissolved.
E aprop administra curacio en la qual es engendrat poyre entro que caian les liamentz; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz convenientz ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, you should administer a cure in which fire is generated until the ligaments fall away; and accordingly, you should cure that one with suitable poultices for it until it is healed.
E si es apostema per seccio de vena, lahoras cove que tu tenguas am la tua ma aquo que es a tu possible del apostema am la codena, e aprop intromet la agulha dejos le loc le qual tu has tengut dejos la tua ma, e fay aquela penetrar; e sia en aquela fil doble entro que tu extraguas aquel del autre latz, e aprop ligua le apostema am bo liament segon que yeu he dit a tu en le liament de uva4 de doas partz am doas extremitatz del fil.	And if it is an abscess due to section of a vein, then you should hold the place with your hand on the abscess and the cord, and accordingly introduce the needle below the location which you have held with your hand, and make it penetrate; and be in that file double so that you can extract that one from the other side, and accordingly tie the abscess with a double ligament according to what I have said to you about the ligature of two parts with two extremities of the thread.
Mays si temes que extraguam le fil, lahoras entromet le fiel am aquela agula dejos tot le apostema deves la inscizio de la agulha primieyra, e strenh les tieus fiels en quatre locs.	But if you fear that the thread will be extracted, then accordingly introduce a thread with that needle below all the abscess so that the incision of the first needle is made, and tighten the four threads in those places.
Aprop secca le apostema en le mieg loc de lu entro que quan es yssit aquo que es en lu, lahoras tu inscideys la superfluitat de la codena, e layssa aquo que de lu es liat.	And accordingly, cut the abscess in the middle of it so that when what is in it is evacuated, you should incise the superfluity of the cord, and leave what remains tied.
E aprop pausa sobre lu pulvil le qual has submergit en vi e oli, e aprop administra la curacio la qual es fayta am calguas e enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, apply to it the poultice which you have submerged in vinegar and oil, and accordingly administer the cure made with some and powders until it is healed.
Capitol l del apostema le qual accideys per torcio de nervis.	Chapter L of the Abscess that occurs due to Torsion of Nerves.
Ayssi cum accideys apostema en arceria e en vena, e semblantment accideys apostema en les nervis quan accideys en lor percussio o accideys per trebal superfluable, e per semblantz.	Just as an abscess occurs in the artery and vein, so too does an abscess occur in the nerves when it occurs through percussion or excessive travail, and similarly.
E es fayt le mays de lu en les locs dels adjutoris o del talo, o en tot loc en le qual so maugudas las juncturas.	And it is made the most in the places of the assistants or the heel, or in any place where the joints are bad.
E es apostema greu, e es asemblat a la color del autre cors, e es en las majors de lu disposicios ses de lor e quan es streyt am vehementia, sent en lu le malaute semblant stupor.	And it is a great abscess, and is akin to the color of another body, and is in the greater part of it disposed to its place, when it is stretched with great vehemence, and then in it the patient seems stupid.
E no es apostema agreguat en le preon del cors, e per so es dejos la codena, e el es maugut a tota partida e no va a las partidas denant ni detras.	And it is not an abscess aggregated in the precordium of the body, and therefore it remains outside, and it is bad on all sides and does not go to any parts before or behind.
Donc aquo de aquels que es en las juncturas no cove que sia envasit am ferr, quar fort leu endevenguera contracio.	Therefore, the one that is in the joints should not be sewn with iron, for very lightly it would bring about contraction.
Mays aquel que es en le cap o en le front fen la codena am spatum.	But the one that is on the head or forehead should have the cord cut with a spatula.
Mays si es apostema pauc, lahoras te aquel am les forfecs e abscindeys aquel de razitz.	But if it is a small abscess, then you should take it away with forceps and cut it from the roots.
E si es gran, lahoras tu le suspen am unci, e excorja aquel, e aprop osta aquel; e ajusta la plagua am sutura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if it is great, then you should suspend it with scissors, and excise that, and accordingly stop that; and adjust the wound with sutures, and cure that one until it is healed.
Capitol .li.	Chapter LI.
De seccio de apostema le qual accideys de cheil que accideys al ventre.	On the Section of Abscess which occurs in the Abdomen.
Endeveno ad alcus homes motas veguadas en les ventres de aquels e en las autras partidas del cors de aquels theils les quals son apelatz funguals per similitut de aquels am funges, dels quals la razitz es subtil e·l cap de aquel es gros; e ja las labias de aquels so conversas, e es de aquels que es petit, e es de aquels que es mot magnificat.	I have observed in some men many times that certain parts of their bellies and other parts of their bodies are called fungals by similarity to those with fungi, whose roots are subtle and the head is thick; and the lips of these are conversed, and it is of those that are small, and it is of those that are very magnificent.
