E yeu ja e vist un, e en le ventre de lu eran dos theils les quals eran mays a funges semblantz, e no era diferencia entre aquels blancs, de menuda razitz.	And I have also seen one, and in the belly of it were two thorns which were more like fungi, and there was no difference between those white ones with fine roots.
E ja las labias de aquels eran enversadas e se fendian, e humiditat corria de aquel tot temps.	And the lips of those were turned inward and split open, and moisture flowed from it all the time.
Donc yeu inscidegui aquels e atrobegui en la un en pes quays xviii unc. e l’autre quays vi unc.	Therefore, you should incise them and cut into one in pieces that weigh 18 ounces. and the other weighs 6 ounces.
E la operacio en la inscizio de lor es que consideres lahoras si·l malaute es humit, e la color de atheil es blanca, humit, de subtil razitz; lahoras tu le inscideys am spatum lat, e sian en la presencia tua cauteris en le foc, quar motas veguadas deves la seccio de lu es expellit mot sanc; e si te ventz le sanc, cauteriza aquel.	And the operation in the incision of them is that you consider at the time if the patient is humid, and the color of the thorn is white, humid, with fine roots; then you should cut into it with a spatula late, and have cauterizers in the presence of fire, because many times the section of it is expelled with much blood; and if you see the blood flowing, cauterize that.
E si vezes le malaute pauruc e temeros, guarda te de inscizio am ferr; mays lahoras pren fiel de plom recent fayt, e strenh am aquel atheil, la manieyra del qual es aquela que havem dita; e leyssa aquel per dos dias.	And if the patient is weak and trembling, be careful not to cut with iron; but rather take a lead thread freshly made, and tighten it on that thorn, in the manner which we have said; and leave it for two days.
E aprop ajusta en la strictura del fil de plom; donc, no cesses strenher le plom granre devetz en theil, entro que sia abscindit e cayha per se ses trebalh.	And accordingly adjust it in the constriction of the lead thread; therefore, do not cease to tighten the lead thread greatly on that thorn, until it is cut off and falls away by its own travail.
Mays si theil es de grossa razitz, lahoras en la inscizio de lu es alcuna causa de temor e de paor, e majorment en aquel que es en le ventre.	But if the thorn is of great root, then in the incision of it there is some cause for fear and dread, and especially in that which is in the belly.
Mays possibla es que tu inscindas la maytat de lu , e aprop cauteriza aquel per que no retorne.	But possible is that you cut off most of it, and accordingly cauterize that so that it does not return.
E aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanada la plagua.	And accordingly, cure that one until the wound is healed.
E guarda te que tu no presumas inscidir theil le qual es de fusca color, de pauc sentiment, de leg reguardament, quar aquel es absi cancros.	And be careful not to presume to cut that thorn which is of a dark color, with little sensation, and little regard, for it is absolutely cancerous.
E yeu vindre am rememoracio de cranc aprop aysso.	And you will find memory of a cancerous abscess accordingly.
Capitol .lii.	Chapter LII.
De curacio de eminencia del umbilic.	On the Cure of an UMBILICAL HERNIA.
Eminencia del umbilic es fayta per motas causas; o per fissuras del ciphac le qual es sobre le ventre, e yeys de lu la tela o budel segon que endeve en las autras rupturas; o per sanc le qual flueys de vena o de arceria segon que es denant dit, o per ventositat coarctada en lu.	An umbilical hernia is caused by many reasons; or by fissures of the cicatrix which is above the belly, and eyes of it bursting forth as if it were a bag or pouch according to what has been said in other ruptures; or by blood flowing from a vein or artery according to what has been said before, or by ventosity constricted in there.
Mays si es per fissura del ciphac e per yssiment de la tela, lahoras la color del apostema es semblant a la color del cors; e es leon ses dolor, e aprop appar de divers situament.	But if it is due to a fissure of the cicatrix and bursting forth of the bag, then the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the body; and there is no pain, and accordingly appears in different situations.
E si es per egressio del budel, lahoras le situament de aquel am lu de aquo que havem recontat, de mays vehement diversitat, e cum tu premes aquel am les tieus ditz es occultat, e aprop retorna; e fort leu es am lu so, e es magnificat mot deves le introt de banh e vehement trebalh.	And if it is due to the bursting forth of the bag, then the situation of that with respect to water which we have recounted, and more vehement diversity, and as you press that with the threads said, it is concealed, and accordingly returns; and very soon it will be in its place, and is magnified much with regard to the introgression of blood and vehement travail.
Mays si per humiditat, lahoras es leon e no es occultat quan premes am la tua ma, ni es constrengut, ni es cregut.	But if it is due to humidity, then the situation of that one is like an onion and not concealed when you press with your hand, nor constrained, nor crept.
E si es per sanc, lahoras am aquestz senhals apareys le apostema a negror declinant.	And if it is due to blood, then accordingly, the abscess appears with these signs declining towards blackness.
Mays si es per carn nada, lahoras es apostema greu, gros e dur, e es ficat segon una quantitat.	But if it is due to nothing but flesh, then accordingly, the abscess is a great one, large and hard, and is situated according to a certain quantity.
Mays si es per ventositat, lahoras le tocament de lu es leon.	But if it is due to ventosity, then accordingly, the touch of it is like an onion.
E la operacio en lu es que consideras lahoras si la eminencia de l’umbilic es per sanc de arceria, o de vena, o per ventositat; lahoras cove que sias prohibit de la curacio de lu, quar en aquela es temor e paor ayssi cum t’e ensenhat en le capitol en le qual he dit les apostemas per arceria e per vena.	And the operation in that case is to consider at the time if the umbilical hernia is due to blood from an artery, or a vein, or ventosity; accordingly, you should be prohibited from curing it, for in that case there is fear and dread just as I have taught you in the chapter on abscesses caused by arteries and veins.
E si la eminencia del umbilic es per le budel o per la tela, lahoras cove que comandes al malaute que tengua le ale sieu, e sia stant extendut; e aprop senha am tenta en le circuit de tot le umbilic, e aprop comanda a lu que stia envers entre las tuas mas sobre le sieu dos, e aprop circunda am spatum lat en le circuit del umbilic sobre le loc le qual has senhat am la tenta; e aprop exten la maytat del apostema a las partidas desus am unci gran; e aprop lia en le circuit am fiel fort o am ceda e la manieyra del liar decent.	And if the umbilical hernia is due to the bag or the pouch, then accordingly, you should command the patient to hold his breath and be standing upright; and accordingly, make a sign with your tent in the circuit of all the umbilic, and accordingly, command him to stand between your arms on his right side, and accordingly, circle around with a spatula wide in the circuit of the umbilic over the place which you have marked with your tent; and accordingly, extend most of the abscess upwards with scissors large; and accordingly, tie it in the circuit with a strong thread or cord and the manner of tying decent.
E aprop huebre le mieg del apostema extendut sobre le liament e intromet le dit tieu en aquel indic e quereys le budel; e si tu l’as atrobat ni guardat per le liament, lahoras tu extratz alxorati e impelleys le budel a las partidas dedintz del ventre.	And accordingly, cut the middle of the abscess extended over the ligament and introduce the said thread into it and seek out the bag; and if you have not found nor guarded by the ligament, then accordingly, you should extract the remaining portion and push the bag towards the parts inside the belly.
E si has atrobada la tela, lahoras pren aquel am unci; e inscideys las superfluitatz de lu.	And if you have reached the pouch, then accordingly, take it with scissors; and cut out the superfluities of it.
Mays si es contraria a tu arceria o vena, lahoras circunda aquel mot, e aprop retorna a la tua operacio; e pren dos agulhas e met en aquelas dos fiels fortz e entromet dos agulhas en le circuit le qual has feyt entorn le apostema en manieyra de crotz, las quals fassas penetrar; e aprop strenh le apostema en quatre partidas sobre las agulhas.	But if it is contrary to your artery or vein, then accordingly, circle around that much, and accordingly return to your operation; and take two needles and put them in those two strong threads and introduce two needles into the circuit which you have made around the abscess in a cross-like manner, so that they will penetrate; and accordingly, tighten the abscess in four parts over the needles.
E si tu vols, osta las agulhas e leyssa le loc entro que poyresca la carn extenduda e caia per si; o inscideys aquel quan es subtiliat e se poyreys, e aprop cura aquel am aquo que cove dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And if you wish, stop the needles and leave the place until the flesh extended falls away by itself; or cut it when it is softened and falls apart, and accordingly cure that one with water as needed until it is healed.
E si la eminencia del ombilic es de carn nada en lu o per humiditat, lahoras cove que tu conquaves le apostema ayssi cum havem dit e estraguas le sanc o la humiditat, la qual atrobas en lu, e aprop cura aquel am aquo que cove e que consolide le loc.	And if the umbilical hernia is caused by flesh nothing in that place or due to humidity, then accordingly, you should conquer the abscess as we have said and extract the blood or humidity which you find in it, and accordingly cure that one with water as needed and consolidate the place.
Capitol .liii.	Chapter LIII.
De curacio de cranc.	On the Cure of Cancer.
Ja havem dit, en la divisio, de specia de cranc e en qual manieyra es via a la curacio de lu am medicinas, e que es squivador en lu la curacio am ferr per so que no sia ulcerat; e havem dit cranc engendrat en la mayra e cautela de la curacio de lu.	We have already said in the division, about the species of cancer and how it should be treated with medicines, and that it is a warning to avoid curing it with iron because it would not be ulcerated; and we have also said that cancer is generated in the majority and caution of its cure.
E diyssero les antics que alcunas veguadas cranc es en loc on es possibla la eradicacio de lu, ayssi cum de cran le qual es en las mamillas o en la coyssa e a lor semblantz dels membres allocat a estrayre tot aquel, e majorment quan es comensant petit.	And the ancients said that sometimes cancer is in a place where it is possible to eradicate it, such as in the breast or armpit and its likenesses of limbs allocated to extract all of it, and especially when it starts small.
Mays quan es antiquat e es gra, no cove que te propries a lu, quar yeu non pogui sanar de aquel alcu ni no he vist autre, ni que sia pervengut ad aquo.	But when it is old and great, you should not take ownership of it, for I have not seen anyone cure it completely or partially, nor has it been passed down to this day.
E la operacio en lu es quan es allocat ayssi cum havem dit, es que tu precedescas e laysses le malaute e purgues de colera negra alcunas veguadas, e aprop sagna aquel, si es atrobada replecio manifesta.	And the operation in that case is when it is allocated as we have said, which is to precede and leave the patient and purge them with black cholera several times, and accordingly sign it, if there is a clear manifestation of repletion.
E aprop prepara le malaute am preparacio en le qual sia locat am operacio, e aprop prohiceys en le trauc uncis les quals cove ad aquel; e aprop concava de tota part am la codena sego bona perexcrutacio entro que no romangua alcuna causa de las razitz de lu.	And accordingly, prepare the patient with preparation in which it is located for the operation, and accordingly prohibit in the tract of scissors those that are needed for it; and accordingly, concave all parts with a good cord for thorough excision so that no cause remains for the roots of it.
E layssa correr le sanc, e no abscidas aquel leugierament, e exprem les locs, e abstergeys le sanc gros tot am la tua ma o am instrument am le qual es a tu possible dels instruments.	And accordingly, let the blood flow and do not cut it slightly, and express the places, and wash away the gross blood with your hand or with an instrument that is at your disposal among the instruments.
Mays si a tu fa contrarietat de sanc gros inscizio de vena o de arceria, lahoras cauterisa aquela entro que·l flux del sanc sia cessat, e aprop cura aquel am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	But if there is a contrariety of gross blood incision in the vein or artery, then accordingly cauterize that one until the flow of blood ceases, and accordingly cure that one with another treatment until it is healed.
Capitol .liv.	Chapter LIV.
De curacio de ydropici.	On the Cure of Hydroceles.
Nos ja havem recomtat, en la divisio, de las specias de ydropici de l’aygua, e les senhals de quascuna especia, de la curacio de lu am medicinas.	We have already recounted, in the division, about the species of hydroceles of water and their signs, as well as the cure for it with medicines.
E aquela la qual es curada am ferr no es sino la specia de althitas sola, e no es aproximat am ferr a la specia de timpanistres ni a la especia de yposarcha, quar aquo es mortal.	And that one which is cured with iron is not but the species of hydroceles alone, and it is not approached with iron to the species of tympanic sac or to the species of hydropsy, for this is mortal.
E quan tu ja has medicat aquesta especia de ydropici timpanistre am medicinas e no comfereys la tua medicacio, lahoras considera, quar si al malaute ja es conseguida debelitat, o es am aquel autra malautia otra ydropici, ayssi cum si es en lu tos o cos de ventre e semblant ad aquels, lahoras guarda te que no le mediques am ferr, quar temor es sobre aquo.	And when you have already medicated this species of hydroceles tympanic sac with medicines and your treatment has not been confirmed, then accordingly consider, for if the patient is already debilitated, or has another malady, such as in the lungs or belly and similar to those, then accordingly be careful not to treat it with iron, for fear is over that.
Mays si tu vezes le malaute de vertut exuberant, e am lu no es autra malautia sino ydropici tant solament, e no enfant ni vielh, lahoras la manieyra de la operacio de lu es que tu eleves le malaute entre las tuas mas, e le ministre aprop lu exprema le ventre de lu am la sua ma, enpellen la aygua a la partida dejos del pentenilh, e aprop pren spatum spinos segon aquesta forma:	But if you treat the patient with abundant virtue, and in it there is no other malady except hydroceles alone, and not infant or old, then accordingly the manner of the operation for it is that you lift the patient between your arms, and minister to him accordingly, expressing the belly of him with his own hand, filling the water at the exit of the pentenilh, and accordingly take a spatula with spines in this form:
sia de dos partz agudas lonc, de aguda extremitat ayssi cum spatum; mays empero sia en lu alcuna brevitat petit a petit, per so que en la operacio am aquel no passes entro al budel, e que ledas aquel.	to be of two sharp parts long, with an acute extremity like a spatula; but however, there should be in it some smallness little by little, so that in the operation on it, one does not penetrate into the bag and leaves it.
E aprop considera si la generacio de ydropici es de part dels budels, quar lahoras cove que tu am la seccio te alonhes del ombelic per la quantitat de tres ditz a las partidas dejos, en le dreyt de lu sobre le pentenilh.	And accordingly consider if the generation of hydroceles is from one of the bags, for then you should take with the section to be away from the navel by three times as much as the parts left behind, on the right side of it above the pentenilh.
Mays si la generacio de hydropici es per malautia del fietge, lahoras la tua seccio sia sinistra del ombilic per tres ditz.	But if the generation of hydroceles is due to liver disease, then accordingly your section should be on the left side of the navel by three times.
E si la generacio de lu es per la melsa, lahoras la tua seccio sia en le las dreyt.	And if the generation of it is due to the spleen, then accordingly your section should be in the right side.
E no cove que la tua seccio sia sobre le costat sobre le qual vol jaser le malaute per que no corron las superfluitatz ad aquel loc freul.	And it is not necessary that your section be on the side on which the patient wishes to lie down, so that the superfluities do not flow into that place freely.
E aprop perfora am le instrument tota la codena, e aprop entromet en aquela seccio, e eleva la tua ma am le spatum entre la codena e·l siphac, e tu excorja aquel; e si’ la quantitat de una ungla o enviro.	And accordingly perforate the entire cord with an instrument and enter into that section, lift your hand with a spatula between the cord and the sac, and excise it; and if the quantity of one fingernail or thereabouts.
E aprop perforo le ciphac entro que pervengua le spatum al loc vuoyt, e es loc de l’aygua.	And accordingly pierce the cicatrix until the spatula reaches the place where you want it to be, and it is the location of the water.
E aprop extratz aquel e entromet un instrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	And accordingly extract that one and enter with an instrument whose shape is this:
e es semblant a canula de argent subtil; es fayt de argent o de eram o de lato leon, al qual en la partida pus bassa de lu es un petit trauc, e en les costatz de lu so tres traucs: dos de una partida e un del autra partida; e fayta es la extremitat de lu insciza segon la manieyra de pluma, ayssi cum vezes:	and it is similar to a silver canula; it is made of silver or copper or bronze, at which the bottom part has a small hole, and on both sides there are three holes: two on one side and one on the other side; and the tip of it is cut according to the manner of a feather, as follows:
E en la extramitat de lu pus sobirana es armilla, quar quan le instrument perve al aygua, lahoras aquela tantost deysen sobre le instrument, donc evacua de l’aygua en la ora miega quantitat, quar si tu evacuas de aquela mes que no cove en la hora, fort leu mor le malaute per resolucio del sieu spirit animal, o accideys a lu cincopi que es appropinquada la mort.	And in the uppermost part of it is an eyelet, because when the instrument reaches the water, then that one immediately falls on top of the instrument, and thus evacuates a moderate quantity of water, for if you evacuate more than what is needed at this time, soon the patient will die from resolution of their animal spirit, or else you will cause harm to them which is approaching death.
Mays evacua de aquela segon la quantitat de la vertut de lu e segon que significan a tu las disposicios del malaute de la vertut del pols de lu e de la bontat de lu.	But evacuate as much as the virtue of it and according to what your dispositions indicate for the patient's vitality, pulse, and goodness.
E aprop extrats le instrument, e rete l’aygua la qual causa es quar tantost es retenguda per la codena la qual rete le trauc que es sobre le ciphac del qual e recomtat a tu que perfores aquel segon aquela manieyra.	And accordingly extract the instrument, and retain the water which is retained because it is held back by the cord which retains the hole that is above the cicatrix of which we have said to you that you should pierce it in this manner.
E aprop itera le instrument al autra dia si vezes le malaute tollerant aquo, e extratz de la aygua petita quantitat, e fay aquo per alcus jorns sobre temor, e guarda te de error entro que no romangua de l’aygua sino pauc.	And accordingly iterate the instrument to another day if the patient can tolerate it, and extract a small quantity of water, and make this go on for some days with caution, and be careful not to err until there is very little water left.
Mays si tu temes sobre le malaute, e leyssas de l’aygua gran quantitat, lahoras cura aquel am sepultura en arena cauda, e mota suzor en banh, e al solelh espere per lonc temps; e cura aquel am medicinas dessicativas entro que sia sanat.	But if you fear for the patient, and leave a great quantity of water, then accordingly cure it with burial in hot sand, and moisten with warm bath, and expose to the sun for a long time; and cure it with desiccative medicines until it is healed.
E cauteriza sobre le stomac, e la melsa e·l fitge aprop la extraccio de l’aygua, segon que yeu he recontat en aquo que es precedit.	And cauterize on the stomach, and the spleen and liver accordingly with the extraction of water, according to what we have recounted earlier.
Capitol .lv.	Chapter LV.
De la curacio dels enfants les quals so natz les locs de la urina no-perforatz.	On the Cure of Children Who are Born with Undescended Testicles Not Perforated.
Alcunas veguadas alcun dels enfantz es eyssi del ventre de la sua mayre e·l cap de la sua mixtio no es perforat (o es trauc streyt o no es en son loc).	Some times some of the children are born like that, from the belly of their mother and the head of their mixture not perforated (or it is a narrow hole or not in its place).
Donc cove coytar am perforacio de lu tantost que es nascut am spatum mot subtil segon aquesta forma:	Then accordingly, make a small incision on the child as soon as it is born with a spatula made of subtle bronze in this form:
E aprop pausa en le trauc un clavil subtil de plom e ligua aquel, e te per tres jorns o per .iiii.tre.	And accordingly, pause in the hole a small clip made of subtle lead and tie it, and let it be for three days or for four times.
E quant vol urinar sia remaugut e hurine; e aprop retorne aquel.	And when it is time to urinate, it should be renewed and reformed; and accordingly, return that one.
E si tu no pauses le plom, ja es possible que la urina la qual va sobre le loc, no leysa aquest claure.	And if you do not pause the lead, it is possible that the urine which flows over the place will not allow it to close.
Mays aquel del qual le trauc es streyt sia medicat am clavil de Plom, ayssi cum havem dit, per trops dias entro que sia amplificat.	But that one of which the hole is narrow should be treated with a lead clip, as we have said, for many days until it is enlarged.
Mays aquels en les quals es le trauc no en son loc, so leditz, la qual causa es quar de aquels, aquel que es nat e·l trau es deves la fi del cap de la vergua per que no pot urinar a las partidas dedintz, entro que eleva la vergua am la sua ma a las partidas desus; e no es a lu generacio, per so quar le sperma no pot pervenir a la mayre segon rectitut, e es malautia mot laga.	But those in whom the hole is not in its place are led astray, which is because from them, that which is born and thrusts forth is due to the end of the head of the foreskin so that it cannot urinate into the parts behind, until it lifts the foreskin with its own hand to the parts above; and this is not a generation, for which reason the sperm cannot reach the mother according to rectitude, and it is a miserable disease.
E la manieyra de la operacio en lu es que·l malaute sia envessat sobre le sieu dos, e aprop exten le cap de la vergua de lu am la tua ma sinistra am vehement extraccio, e inscideys le cap del cap de la vergua del loc del perpucii am spatum agut, ayssi cum es inscizio de pluma, o que tu ne razas alcuna partida, per so que·l mieg de lu vengua semblant al cap de la vergua e que le trauc caia en le mieg loc segon que cove.	And the manner of the operation in this case is that the patient be laid on his back, and accordingly extend the head of the foreskin with your left hand with a violent extraction, and incise the head of the foreskin at the location of the perineum with a sharp spatula, just as a feather is cut or if you cut out some part, so that the middle of it becomes like the head of the foreskin and the hole falls in the middle place according to what is needed.
E guarda te que en la tua operacio de flux de sanc, quar motas vetz accideys aquo; e pausa te a lu am aquo que abscindeys le sanc, e cura la plagua entro que si’ sanada.	And be careful that in your operation of blood flow, for many times this happens; and pause at the place where you cut the blood, and cure the wound until it is healed.
Capitol .lvi.	Chapter LVI.
De albater le qual accideys en le prepucii en le cap de la vergua e de corropcio e negror e adherencia del prepucii del cap de la vergua.	On the Foreskin which Accidents in the Prepucii of the Head of the Foreskin, and on Corruption, Blackness, and Adhesion of the Prepucii to the Head of the Foreskin.
Motas veguadas accideys aquest albater en la vergua e es eminencia de carn laga.	Many times this foreskin becomes inflamed in the head of the foreskin and is an excessive prominence of flesh.
E de aquela una es maligna e autra es no-maligna.	And one of these is malignant, and the other is non-malignant.
No-maligna, cove que suspendas am unci subtil e abscindas aquela entro que aquela mondes tota; e aprop pausa sobre aquela coto submirgit en enguent egipciac; e aprop aquel, cura le am enguent diafinicon entro que sia sanat.	Non-malignant, it is necessary to suspend with a subtle thread and cut it so that all of it becomes free from the foreskin; and accordingly pause over it for three days in an Egyptian ointment; and accordingly cure it with another ointment, day by day, until it is healed.
E si albater es maligna, de lega color, lahoras cove que tu aministres cauteri aprop la inscizio de lu e la razio de lu.	And if the foreskin is malignant, with a foul color, then accordingly you must administer caustics around the incision and the surrounding area.
Mays si albater es en le prepuci del cap de la vergua no-circumcis, e la una partida de albater es dedintz le prepucii e l’autra partida es defora, lahoras cove que tu ostes albater le qual es dedintz al comensament entro que es consolidat; e lahora tu cura aquel deforo, quar quan tu curas aquel ensemps le prepuci, no es asegurat que no sia trinquat.	But if the foreskin is in the prepucii of the head of the foreskin not-circumcised, and one part of the foreskin is inside the prepucii and the other part is outside, then accordingly you must remove the foreskin that is inside at first until it is consolidated; and afterwards you cure the one that is outside, for when you cure both together with the prepucii, it is not certain that it will not be torn.
E ja eysamen accideys en les genetius e en le prepuci negror e corruccio, adonc cove que tu conquavas tot aquo que ja es denigrat e que ja se vol corrompre o que ja es corrumput; e aprop lineys sobre aquel aprop aquo am mel, le qual es contusit am farina de scorsa de milgrana e de errs trissatz e crivellatz.	And already many accidents occur in the genitals and prepucii, namely blackness and corruption; therefore it is necessary to conquer all this which is already denigrated and which already wants to corrupt or has corrupted; and accordingly line on top of that with a mixture made from honey, which is mixed with flour of scoria of millet and of errors trampled and crushed.
E aprop cura aquel am l’autra curacio entro que sia sana.	And accordingly cure it with another remedy until it is healed.
Mays si endeve flux de sanc, lahoras aministra cauteri lunar segon aquesta forma:	But if there is bleeding, then accordingly administer lunar caustics in this form:
quar cauteri juvatiu es a dos disposicios ensemps, so es a flux de sanc e a la plagua quan es corrumpuda.	for the caustic juice is good at two dispositions together, that is to say in bleeding and in a wound when it is corrupted.
E si le cap de la vergua es corrodut e es destruit tot en la hora, lahoras cove que tu intrometas en lo meat del prepucii una canula de plom per so que le malaute urina per aquela.	And if the head of the foreskin is destroyed and all in an instant, then accordingly it is necessary to introduce a lead tube into the meatus of the prepucii so that the patient may urinate through it.
En la adherencia del prepucii am le cap de la vergua (et aquesta adherencia no accideys sino en aquel del qual le prepucii es sa, e sobre lu no es exhigida circumcizio; e quan accideys adherencia per plagua o per apostema) cove que excorjas am spatum obtus entro que sia dissolvut le liament e sia deliurat le cap de la vergua de tota partida.	In the adhesion of the prepucii to the head of the foreskin (and this adhesion only occurs in one who has an uncircumcised prepucii, and on whom no circumcizion has been performed; and when adhesion occurs due to a wound or abscess) it is necessary to excise with a blunt spatula until the bond is dissolved and the head of the foreskin is completely freed from all parts.
E si es dificil desirnir aquelas exquisidament, lahoras cove que tu excorjes am spatum alcuna causa del cap de la vergua e del prepucii, e aysso es quar le prepucii, quan es subtil, fort leu es perforat per la sua subtilitat leugierament.	And if it is difficult to remove those excrescences exactly, then accordingly it is necessary to excise with a spatula some cause from the head of the foreskin and the prepucii, and thus it is because when the prepucii is subtle, it is easily perforated by its subtlety lightly.
E aprop separa entre·l prepucii e·l cap de la vergua am dra7 de li subtil, le qual ja es mulhat en l’aygua frega per que no adherescan autra veguada.	And accordingly separate between the prepucii and the head of the foreskin with a thread of subtle lead, which has been moistened in water so that they will not adhere again.
E aprop sia curat am vi stiptic entro que sia consolidat.	And accordingly it should be cured with a vinegar-strengthened remedy until it is consolidated.
Capitol .lvii.	Chapter LVII.
De mundificacio dels enfants e de la curacio de aquo que accideys ad aquels de circumcisio.	On the Circumcision of Children and the Cure of What Occurs to Them in Circumcision.
Circumcisio no es solucio de continuitat ayssi cum las autras plaguas: mays empero cum sia de la nostra operacio e de nostra voluntat, e lus de aquela sia propriament en les enfants, es necessari que asignem en aquela milhor operacio e via pus leugiera perdusent a salut.	Circumcision is not a solution of continuity like other wounds: but since it is our operation and our will, and the purpose of which is properly in children, it is necessary that we assign to it a better operation and way that is more gentle and less hurtful to health.
Donc dic que les antics no diyssero circumcisio en alcu dels lors libres, quar no n’usan en las suas leys, e no es sino quar havem aquisit per speriment, la qual causa es que yeu he atrobat la major partida dels artifexs e dels barbies usar circumcisir e mundificacio am novacula e am torores; e usan de liament am fiel e de inscizio am la ungla.	Therefore I say that the ancients did not write about circumcision in any of their books, because they did not use it in their laws, and this is only because we have discovered through experience, which reason is that you have found that most of the artists and barbers use circumcising and cleansing with a new razor and with toreros; and they tie with a thread and inscribe with a nail.
E yeu ja he prohadas totas aquestas manieras e no atrobegui milhor mondificacio am forfexs, am liament am fiel que en mondificacio cum la ungla, quar motas vetz efugeys la codena pus desus, quar la codena del prepucii a dos tunicas, e roman la tonica pus dejos, e fort leu es forsat ad autra inscizio e dolor sicura.	And I have already forbidden all these methods and did not find better cleansing with razors, threads that tie with a thread like the nail in cleansing, because many times the cord above has fled, because the cord of the prepucii has two tunics, and the tonic is left behind, and soon it will be forced to another incision and certain pain.
E am mundificacio le qual es fayta per alphecati, e es digital, del qual usan les sabatiers, no es segurada la inscizio de la extremitat del membre viril, quar fort leu intra en le trau de lu.	And the cleansing method that is made by aliphatic acid, and is digested, which is used by barbers, is not assured of the incision at the end of the virile member, because soon it will enter into the wound.
Mays en la operacio am ungla, fort leu obazeys ferr e corromp la tua operacio.	But in the operation with a nail, soon iron will be oxidized and corrupt your operation.
E la codena del enfant es breu per natura, e motas veguadas nays en tal manieyra que no ha necessitat de mondificacio, e yeu he vist aquel.	And the cord of the child is short by nature, and many times it is such that there is no need for cleansing, and I have seen this.
Mays de la mondificacio que·s fa am forfexs e liamentz am fiel, la bontat, experiment descrobic a mi, quar las forfexs so de proporcional inscizio, per aquo quar la acuitat que es desus es ayssi cum la acuitat que es dejos; e donc cum tu premes la tua ma so proporcionadas dos acuitatz, e inscideysso segon una comperacio en un temps; e es fayta compressio del fiel am figura contenent la codena de la vergua de tota partida, am le qual no catz error de tot.	But the cleansing that is done with razors and threads with a thread, the goodness of it has been discovered by me through experience, because the razors are of proportional incision, for which reason the acuity above is as the acuity below; and therefore when you press your hand so proportionally two acuities, and inscribe accordingly in one time; and it is made compression of the thread with a figure containing the cord of the foreskin from all sides, with which there is no error at all.
E la manieyra de la operacio primeyra es que tu fassas estar le enfant majorment si es de aquels que entendo un petit, que no fassas sino que tu lies le fiel en la sua vergua tant solament, e que leysses aquel entro al autra dia.	And the first manner of the operation is that you should make the child stay in a state of quietude, whether it is one of those who understand a little or not, and that you should only lay the thread on the foreskin so long as necessary, and then leave it alone until the next day.
E aprop fay aquel alegrar en tota aquela manieyra que es a tu possibla de aquo que recep la sua intelligencia.	And accordingly make the child happy in all that manner which is possible to you, according to what it receives its intelligence.
E aprop fa aquel estar entre las tuas mas estatuir preparadament, e no sia ges cezent; e occulta las forfexs en la tua ma o dejos le tieu pe, que l’enfant no veia aquelas ni degun autre dels instruments.	And accordingly make the child sit between your arms, well prepared and not at all frightened; and hide the razors in your hand or in your lap, so that the child does not see them or any other instrument.
E aprop entremet la tua ma a la vergua de lu e suffla en la codena, e tira aquela entro que sia eyssit le cap de la vergua, e aprop mondifica aquel de aquo que es agregat en ela de sordicia.	And accordingly place your hand on the foreskin of him and blow into the cord, and pull it until the head of the foreskin is out, and accordingly cleanse that which has accumulated in the area of the foreskin.
E aprop lia le loc signat am fiel dobla, e aprop ligua pus bas de aquel un petit le segon liament, e aprop te am le dit pous e endic tieu le loc del liament dejos am bona retencio, e inscideys entre dos liaments.	And accordingly place the marked spot with double thread, and accordingly tie a small piece of it as a second ligature, and accordingly tie it on the said point with good retention, and inscribe between two ligatures.
E aprop eleva la codena sus leugierament e estratz le cap de la vergua; e aprop leyssa le sanc corre petit e petit, quar es milhor ; e pausa polvera desus e sobre la polvera pausa drap en le qual es spandut mugol de huou coyt en ayguaros concosit am oli rozat recent bo; e layssa aquel sobre aquel entro al autra dia; e cura aquel am curacio entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly lift the cord slightly and pull out the head of the foreskin; and accordingly let the blood flow little by little, for it is better; and pause powder above and on top of the powder, a cloth spread with yolk of egg mixed with oil recently roasted beef; and leave that on that until the next day; and cure that with a remedy until it is healed.
La forma de las forfexs a mondificacio, aquesta es la forma:	The form of the razors for cleansing, this is the form:
Sian las unas extramitatz no-talhantz e las autras sian talhant, que non sia yssit le ram del clau, e sia la longitut de las doas acuitatz ayssi cum la longitut de dos manubres engualment.	Be the outer edges not cutting and the inner ones cutting, so that there is no space left for the hinge of the lock, and be the length of both acuities as the length of two equal hands.
Mays la error en mundificacio es quar fort leu efugeys la codena intrinseca tota, o partida de lu deves la inscizio.	But the error in cleansing is that soon the inner cord will be entirely or partially cut off from its inscription.
Donc cove que tu extendas aquela de la tua hora am la tua ungla denant la apostemacio del loc e que inscidas aquela segon equalitat.	Therefore it is necessary that you extend that of your hour with your finger before the apostema of the place and that you inscribe it according to equality.
E si no la podes tenir am la tua ungla, lahoras extratz aquela am unci e inscideys aquela.	And if you cannot hold it with your finger, then accordingly extract it with a thread and inscribe it.
Mays si son passatz tres dias, e roman aquo que es imflat dejos la vergua apostemat, lahoras tu leyssa aquo entro que sia cedat le apostema caut, e excorja aquel am fecilitat, e inscidex aquel segon que a tu es preparat.	But if three days have passed and the foreskin has become inflamed again, then accordingly you should let it be for a little while until the inflammation is subsided cautiously, and then excise it with facility, and inscribe it according to what is prepared for you.
E guarda te del cap de la vergua, quar no nosera a lu aquo.	And beware of the head of the foreskin, for it will not be at all in that place.
E donc cura aquel am aquo que la plagua consolida de las polveras las quals havem recomtadas en le tractat de las polveras.	And therefore cure that with the water which has consolidated from the powders which we have recommended in the treatise on powders.
E si es inscidit de la codena sobre mesura, e obezeys a las partidas desus, aquo no notz a lu.	And if it is inscribed by the cord with measure, and submits to the parts above, then this will not be noticed at all.
E mays cura aquel am aquo que havem dit entro que sia sanat.	And therefore cure that with the water which we have said until it is healed.
Capitol .lviii.	Chapter LVIII.
De curacio de urina retenguda en la vesiqua.	On the Cure of Retained Urine in the Bladder.
Retencio de urina en la vesica es fayta per oppulacio fayta per peyra o per sanc congilat, o per poyre o per carnada, e semblantz ad aquels de aquo que havem dit de las manieyras de curacio en la divisio.	Retention of urine in the bladder is caused by oppression made through fear or blood congested, or through pouring or fleshiness, and it resembles those cases which we have said about the manners of cure in the division.
E si no es dissolvuda la urina, e veses retencio de lu esser per peyra le qual ja es en le col de la vesica, lahoras cove que le malaute sia encorbat sobre les sieus denolhs.	And if the urine is not dissolved, and you see retention of it being caused by fear which is in the neck of the bladder, then accordingly the patient should be encouraged on his own desires.
E aprop conponeys les pes de aquel sobre le sieu dos e extendas le sieu ventre de la partida pus desus del sieu dos, e le malaute estrengua le sieu ale tant quant es a lu possible.	And accordingly place the patient's feet on his own back and stretch out his belly from the upper part of his back, and the patient should strain his arm as much as is possible to him.
Donc lahoras le col de la vesica es costreyt ha espulsio de la peyra a las partidas detras, per que la urina es absolta.	Therefore accordingly the neck of the bladder is constricted for expulsion of the fear to the parts behind, so that the urine is eliminated.
E si no es dissolvuda am aquo que havem dit he vehement es fayta la causa sobre le malaute, lahoras cove que aministres extraccio de lu am instrument le qual es apelat siringua, del qual aquesta es la forma: Sia de argent e sia subtil leon conquau, ayssi cum canula de pena de ausel am subtilitat de ray lonc en similitut d’un palm e mig, al qual sia cana subtil en le cap de lu.	And if it is not dissolved with what we have said, then the cause is vehement and made upon the patient, accordingly it is necessary to administer extraction of it by instrument which is called syringe, the form of which is as follows: It should be made of silver and a subtle lead combined, like a canula of an eagle's quill with subtlety of ray long in similitude of half a palm, with a thin cane in its head.
E la manieyra del eyssiment de la urina per aquel es que prenguas le fiel doblat e lies en la extramitat de lu lana o coto per bona liadura; e entrometas las extramitatz del fiel en la partida dejos de la ciringua, e inscideys am las forfexs si superflueys alcuna causa de la lana, mays intromet la en la canula am vehemencia E aprop enongeys la ciringua am boder e am album de huou.	And the manner of extracting urine with that is as follows: You take the doubled thread and tie it in the extremity of the lanolin or cotton for good binding; and then you insert the ends of the thread into the posterior part of the syringe, and inscribe with razors if any superfluous cause of the lanolin exists, but instead introduce it into the canula with vehemence And accordingly you should pour the ciringua into the border and album of egg.
E fay cezer le malaute sobre la selha, e embroca la vesiqua de lu e la vergua am olis umitz, e oli de oliva e ayguaros.	And make the patient sit on the seat, and wrap the bladder of him and the foreskin with olive oil and egg yolks.
E aprop entromet la ciringua am facilitat entro que pervengua a la razit de la vergua; e aprop dobla la vergua desus a la partida del embelic; e aprop empelleys la ciringua dintz aquela; e aprop empelleys aquela entro que pervengua a la vesica, e aquela centa le malaute esser pervenguda a la causa vuoda, e no es fayt asso segon aquest orde, sino le meat en le qual va a tortuositat.	And accordingly insert the syringe with ease until it reaches the root of the foreskin; and accordingly double the foreskin above at the part of the belly; and accordingly push the syringe into it; and accordingly push it in until it reaches the bladder, and that will cause the patient to be relieved from the desired cause, and not made as such according to this order, but rather the way it goes to tortuosity.
E aprop exten le fiel am la lana petit a petit, quar la urina siec la lana.	And accordingly stretch the thread with the lanolin little by little, because the urine will soak the lanolin.
Aprop extratz aquela e fay per curacio urina, e usa ciringua, no cesses fer aquo e usa ciringua entro que sia evacuada la vesica e le malaute atrobe alleviacio.	And accordingly extract that and make for urine cure, and use syringe, do not cease to do so and use syringe until the bladder is emptied and the patient obtains relief.
Capitol .lix.	Chapter LIX.
De qualitat de clisterizacio de la vezica am clampcedra e am semblantz instrumentz les quals sian acordants ad aquo.	On the Quality of Cathartics for the Bladder with Clampseed and similar instruments which are in accord with that.
Quan accideys en la vesica ulceracio o apostema, o sanc congilat en aquela, o es coartat poyredura, e vols en aquela destillar ayguas e medicinas, lahoras sia fayt am instrument le qual es apelat clampcedra, e aquesta es la forma de lu:	When ulceration or apostema occurs in the bladder, or blood congestion in it, or it is constricted by pouring, and you want to make it distill with waters and medicines, then accordingly use an instrument which is called clampcedra, and this is its form:
sino que en la extramitat de lu es sorda, so es clausa.	except that at the extremity of it there is a stopper, so it is closed.
Et en aquela so tres traucs: dos de la una partida , ayssi quo vezes.	And in that there are three holes: two on one side, like times.
En le comensament es loc concau, en le qual es aquo que es enpellit, e sia segon quantitat que oppile aquel, ses addicio, entro que quan alcuna causa es ab aquel tirada de las humiditatz, sia atirada, e quan es expellida, am aquo sia atirada, e quan es expellit lonc, segon que fa clampcedra am la qual es phicat naphta en las batalhas de mar.	In the beginning it is a concave place, in which there is water that is poured in, and it should be according to the quantity that oppresses it, without addition, until when some cause is pulled out by the humidities, it will be pulled out, and when it is expelled, with water it will be pulled out, and when it is expelled long, as the clampcedra does to which naphta is poured in the battles of the sea.
Donc cum tu vols prohicir humiditatz en la vesica, entromet la extremitat de clapcedra en la humiditat, e atira am aquel aquo que es empellit a las partidas desus, quar la humiditat es atirada en la conquavitat de clapcedra.	Therefore, when you want to provoke humidities in the bladder, insert the extremity of the clampcedra into the humidity, and pull out with that water which is poured into the upper parts, because the humidity is pulled into the concavity of the clampcedra.
E aprop entromet la extramitat de clapcedra en la vergua segon que havem recomtat en la ciringua; e aprop empelleys la humiditat am aquo que empelleys, quar aquela humiditat perve a la vesica tantost, e le malaute cent aquela.	And accordingly insert the extremity of the clampcedra into the foreskin according to what we have recommended in the syringe; and accordingly pour out the humidity with water which pours out, because that humidity comes to the bladder soon, and the patient will be relieved.
Forma del cristeri subtil am le qual la vesica es cristerizada, e es aquela la forma:	The form of the cathartic instrument with which the bladder is cathartized, and it is this form:
E sia fayta de argent o de lato, de la qual le cap pus aut sia semblant a petita pluma, e dejos lu cana dedintz liament.	And it should be made of silver or lead, the head being similar to a small feather, and with a thin cane inserted into the ligature.
E aprop pren vesica de moto, e pausa en aquela la humiditat que vols cristirizar en la vesica, e aprop lia aquela entre dos am fort liguatura am fiel doble, e escalfa aquela humiditat sobre le foc.	And accordingly take the bladder of motion, and pause in it the humidity that you want to cathartize in the bladder, and accordingly tie it between two with a strong ligature made of double thread, and warm up that humidity over the fire.
E aprop entromet la extremitat del cristeri en la vergua.	And accordingly insert the extremity of the cathartic instrument into the foreskin.
E aprop estrenh la tua ma sobre la vesica am la humiditat am strectura descent entro que·l malaute centa que aquela humiditat ja es pervenguda a la vesica.	And accordingly place your hand on the bladder with the humidity stretched downwards until the patient feels that that humidity has reached the bladder.
Mays si a tu no es present vesica, lahoras tu pren una pessa de parguames e fay de aquel cercle; e perfora aquel de tota la sua retonditat; e aprop entromet fiel fort en aquels traucs, ayssi quo so revolgut; e aprop agregua le cercle ayssi quo es agreguat alsofatur, pus que tu pausas en aquel aquo que tu vols de las humiditatz, e olis e ayguas.	But if you do not have a bladder, then accordingly take a piece of parchment and make a circle from it; and perforate that all around its entire circumference; and accordingly insert a strong thread into those holes, just as they are revolved; and accordingly add the circle in such a way that it is added also to the other parts, so that you pause on that which you want of the humidities, oils, and waters.
E aprop tu lia aquel en le instrument e fay am aquel ayssi cum has fayt am la vesica, e exprescio am la tua ma entro que la humiditat pervengua a la vesica.	And accordingly tie that to the instrument and make it like you did with the bladder, and express it with your hand until the humidity reaches the bladder.
Capitol .lx.	Chapter LX.
De extraccio de peyra.	On the Extraction of Fear.
Nos ja havem dit en la divisio las specias de peyra e curacio de lu am medicinas, e la diferencia entre peyra engendrada en los ronhos e peyra engendrada en la vesica, e les senhals de aquela.	We have already said in the division the species of fear and cure of it with medicines, and the difference between fear generated in the lungs and fear generated in the bladder, and the signs of it.
E havem dit la peyra en la qual catz operacio am ma, e seccio.	And we have said about the fear in which one can perform an operation with hand and section.
E la peyra engendrada en la vesica propriament es aquela que es ficada en la vesica.	And the fear generated in the bladder properly is that which is placed in the bladder.
E yeu so narrant aquel am exposicio manifesta e abreviacio.	And you will narrate it with a manifest exposition and abbreviation.
Donc dic que peyra engendrada en la vesica majorment ve als enfantz; e dels senhals de lu es que la urina que es eyssida de la vesica es semblant a aygua en la sua subtilitat, e apar en aquela arena; e le malaute fregua la sua vergua, e motas veguadas pen, e aprop es dressada; e am aquo yeys foro le cul en motz de aquels.	Therefore I say that fear generated in the bladder mostly appears to children; and among its signs is that the urine that comes out of the bladder is like water in its subtlety, and appears in that sand; and the patient trembles his foreskin, and many times looks pale, and accordingly is dressed; and with this you will find the tail in moles of those.
E es laugiera la sanacio dels enfants de aquela entro que han conseguitz xiiii ans; e es dificil curacio en les viels.	And it is easier to cure children of that until they have reached 14 years old; and it is difficult to cure the elderly.
Mays en les joves es migiera per aquo quar es entre aquels.	But in young people, it is easier for this reason because it is between those.
E de aquel del qual la peyra es major e la curacio es pus leugiera; E si es pauca, es contraria ad aquela.	And of that which fear is greater and cure is more easy; And if there is little, it is contrary to that.
Donc cum pervenem a la curacio de aquela, cove al comensament de aquela que mondifiquem le malaute am cristeri le qual extragua tota la fenda la qual es en les sieus budels; quar aquela fenda alcunas veguadas prohibeys la envencio de la peyra deves la inquisicio de lu.	Therefore, when we come to the cure of that, it is necessary at the beginning of that to cleanse the patient with a cathartic instrument which extracts all the fissure that is in their intestines; for that fissure sometimes hinders the formation of fear by the investigation of him.
E aprop sia pres le malaute am les sieus pes e sia contosit e maugut enjos per so que la peyra descenda al preon de la vesica, o que saute de loc aut alcunas veguadas.	And accordingly be present the patient with their feet and be comforted and strengthened by rest for so that fear may descend to the bottom of the bladder, or sometimes jump from one place to another.
E aprop fay aquel cezer entre las tuas mas preparat, e las mas de lu sian dejos las coysas de lu, per so que la vesica tota sia fayta declinant a las partidas dejos.	And accordingly make that person sit between your arms prepared, and those of him are left with his things, for so that the bladder is made to decline entirely to the posterior parts.
E aprop perquier aquela e tota aquela deforo.	And accordingly pour out all that and everything outside.
Donc si sentes la peyra en l’espazi, lahoras tu te coyta tantost am seccio sobre lu.	Therefore, if you feel fear in the space, then accordingly you should crouch down soon with section on him.
E si no catz de tot dejos le tieu tocament, lahoras cove que tu untes am oli le tieu dit indic de la ma sinistra, si malaute es enfant, o le dit miga si es jove complit, e entrometas aquel en le sieu cul.	And if you do not feel completely the presence of his touch, then accordingly it is necessary that you anoint with oil the said indication of your left hand, whether the patient is a child or a young adult in full bloom, and insert it into their anus.
E perquier de la peyra entro que stia dejos le tieu dit.	And pour out fear until it stays behind your said indication.
E converteys aquela petit a petit entro al col de la vesica.	And convert that little by little into the neck of the bladder.
E aprop prem sobre aquel am lo tieu dit, e expelleys aquel a las partidas defora ves le loc del qual vos la seccio.	And accordingly press on that with your said indication, and push it out into the posterior parts outside of the location from which you took the section.
E comanda al ministra que prema la vesica am la sua ma; e comanda a un autra ministra que am la sua ma dextra extenda les genetius a las partidas desus, e am la sua autra ma remaugua la codena la qual es dejos les genetius, en partida del loc en le qual se fa la seccio.	And command the minister to press on the bladder with her right hand; and command another minister to extend the legs upwards with her left hand, and with her other hand to relax the cord which is below the legs, in a part of the location where the section is being made.
E aprop entromet espatum be inscident del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And accordingly insert a spatula which is incident to this form:
e scindeys en lu aquo que es entre·l cul e·ls genetius, no en le mieg loc, abantz al latz de la coyssa sinistra; e sia la seccio sobre aquela peyra e·l tieu dit sia en le cul, e sia fayta seccio transversa, per que la seccio defora sia ampla e dedintz streyta segon la quantitat que egrecio de la peyra sia a lu possibla, e no major, quar fort leu comprem le tieu dit le qual es en le cul la peyra deves la seccio, e es foro-getada ses defacultat.	And accordingly insert a spatula which is incident to this form:
E sapias que de la peyra es alcuna a la qual so angle e margers, per que le eyssiment de lu es fayt deficil per aquo.	And know that of the fear there is some which has an angle and margin, for which the emission of it is made difficult by this.
E de aquela aquo es leon semblant a glan, e es redonda, e es fayt de lu leugier eyssiment.	And of that fear there is one which resembles a grain, and is round, and is made for easier emission.
Donc si es aquela al qual so angles e marger, ajusta en la fissura.	Therefore, if it is this type with angle and margin, adjust it in the fissure.
E si no es ayssi foro-getada, lahoras cove que tu engenes sobre aquel, o que strenguas sobre aquel am gesti decentment, la extremitat del qual sia ayssi cum lima am le qual strenguas sobre la peyra, e no evasesca de lu; o que entrometas dejos lu instrument subtil de curvada extremitat.	And if it is not so, then accordingly you must generate on that, or strengthen on that with decent gestures, the extremity of which should be like a file with which you strengthen on fear, and do not escape from there; or insert below that subtle instrument with curved extremity.
Mays si tu no podes sobre aquel, lahoras tu amplifica le trauc un petit, e si tu veus flux de sanc, abscindeys en strenh aquel am vitriol trissat.	But if you cannot do so, then accordingly you should amplify the hole a little bit, and if you see a flow of blood, cut off the strength with vitriol powder.
Mays si la peyra es mays de una, lahoras al comensament tu impelleys la ma a la boca de la vesica, e aprop inscideys sobre lu; e aprop impelleys un petit aprop aquo; e semblantment fay si son motas mays de doas.	But if the fear is more than one, then accordingly at first you will push your hand into the mouth of the bladder and insert it on that; and accordingly push in a little bit above that; and similarly do so if there are many more than two.
E si es peyra mot gran, lahoras ignorancia es que tu inscidas aquel am gran seccio, quar accideys al malaute una de doas causas: o que mora o que endevengua a lu destillacio de urina continuabla, per aquo quar le loc no es de tot consolidat.	And if it is great fear, then ignorance is that you insert that with great section, because it happens to the patient one of two causes: or that they die or that they are unable to undergo continuous urine distillation, therefore where the location is not entirely consolidated.
Mays aministra expulcio de lu entro que sia fora-getada, o engenia en la fractura de lu am las forfexs entro que extragua aquela en pessas.	But administer expulsion of it until it is forgotten, or generate in the fracture with razors into which it extracts that in pieces.
Donc cum tu auras cumplit la tua opperacio, lahoras omple la plagua de enses de aloe e de sanc de drago, e strenh aquel.	Therefore, when you have completed your operation, then accordingly fill the wound with the juice of aloe and dragon's blood, and strengthen that.
E pausa sobre aquel drap enfus en oli e vi, o en oli rozat e aygua frega, per so que apostema caut sia cedat.	And pause on that cloth infused in oil and vinegar, or in rosy oil and water, for so that the apostema may be calmed.
E aprop resupina le malaute sobre le sieu col, e no deslias le liament entro al tertz dia.	And accordingly lay the patient on his back, and do not loosen the ligature for three days.
E cum aquel auras desliat, embroca le loc am aygua e mot oli, e aprop cura aquel am enguent diafinicon e am enguent diabazilicon entro que sia sanat.	And when that has been loosened, wrap the wound with water and some oil, and accordingly cure it with divine ointment and devilish balsam until it is healed.
Mays si en la plagua accideys apostema caut, adhust e corrosiu, e de aquel semblantz ayssi cum si le sanc es en la vesica congelat, e per lu es la hurina prohibida (e aquo es conogut per la egressio del sanc am urina), a donc entromet lo tieu dit en la plagua e extratz aquel sanc, quar si roman provoca la vesica a corropcio de la vesica e de lu putrefaccio.	But if in the wound there occurs apostema, acute and corrosive, and of that it appears as if blood is congealed in the bladder with frost, and because of that urination is forbidden (and this is known by the egress of blood with urine), then accordingly insert your said indication into the wound and extract that blood, for if it remains it will provoke the bladder to corruption and putrefaction.
E aprop lava la plagua am vi agre, aygua e sal, e am opposicio a tota specia, am aquo que conveneys a lu de la curacio entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly wash the wound with vinegar, water, and salt, and with opposition to all species, with what is suitable for its cure until it is healed.
E cove en las horas de tota la curacio que tu lies amdos las coyssas e ajustes las medicinas las quals so pausadas sobre le loc.	And accordingly in all the hours of your cure, you should lie down with both the legs and adjust the medicines which are paused on the wound.
E si la peyra es petita e es en le meat de la vergua, e es ficat en lu, e eyssement de urina es prohibit, lahoras cura aquel am aquo que yeu recomti denant que pervenguas a seccio, quar tropas veguadas per aquesta curacio yest acusat de seccio; e ja yeu e esproat aquo, e es que tu prenguas un perforador de ferr alfelut, del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And if the fear is small and is in the head of the foreskin, and is fixed there, and emission of urine is prohibited, then accordingly cure that with what you recommended before reaching section, for many times accused by this cure; and now I have tried it too, and it is that you take a perforator made of iron alloy, whose form is as follows:
de triangulada extramitat, agut, ficat en fust.	with a triangular extremity, sharp, fixed in wood.
E aprop pren fiel, e lia am aquel la vergua dejos la peyra per so que no retorne a la vesica.	And accordingly take the thread and tie it to that foreskin below the fear, for that reason that it may not return to the bladder.
E aprop entromet le ferr en la vergua, perforant am fecilitat entro que·l perforador vengua ad aquela peyra.	And accordingly insert the iron into the foreskin, perforating with ease until the perforator comes to that fear.
E revolveys le perforador am la tua ma en aquela peyra petit a petit, e tu perforsa la perforacio de lu entro que fassas aquel del autra part penetrar; quar la urina tantost es absolta.	And accordingly turn the perforator with your hand in that fear little by little, and you will make the perforation of it until you make that other part penetrate; for the urine is soon abolished.
E aprop prem la tua ma sobre aquo que es romas de la peyra de la partida deforo de la vergua, quar aquela es trinquada, e es foro-getada am la urina, e le malaute es sanat.	And accordingly press your hand on that which is remaining of the fear from the outside part of the foreskin, for that is tightened, and forgotten with urine, and the patient is healed.
Mays si aquesta curacio no es a tu aparelhada per alcuna causa la qual prohibeys de aquela, lahoras lia un fiel dejos la peyra, e autra fiel desus la peyra.	But if this cure is not adapted to your equipment for some reason that prohibits it, then accordingly tie a thread below the fear, and another thread above the fear.
E aprop encideys sobre la peyra en aquela vergua entre doas liaduras.	And accordingly insert yourself on the fear in that foreskin between two ligatures.
E aprop extratz aquela.	And accordingly extract it.
E aprop deslia le liament e mondifica le sanc congilat, le qual es fayt en la plagua.	And accordingly loosen the ligature and cleanse the congealed blood which is made in the wound.
E no es necessari liament de fiel dejos la peyra, sino per que no retorne a la vesica, e l’autre liament desus sino, quar quan es desliat le fiel aprop la egrecio de la peyra, la codena retorna a son loc e cobra la plagua.	And it is not necessary to tie the thread below the fear, except that it may not return to the bladder, and the other thread above, so that when the thread is loosened near the emission of the fear, the cord returns to its place and covers the wound.
E per aquo es a tu necessari quan lias le fiel desus, que tu eleves la codena a las partidas desus, o que retorne deves le tieu compliment, e cobra la plagua ayssi co havem dit.	And therefore it is necessary for you when you have tied the thread above, that you lift the cord to the upper parts, or that you return to your previous complement, and cover the wound as we have said.
Capitol .lxi.	Chapter LXI.
De extraccio de peyra de las femnas.	On the Extraction of Fear from Women.
Peyra en las femnas pauc es engendrada.	Fear in women is rarely generated.
Mays si ve peyra ad alcuna de aquelas, lahoras dificil es la curacio de lu, e es prohibida per tropas manieyras.	But if fear appears in some of them, then it is difficult to cure it and is prohibited by many methods.
La una de lor es quar la femna fort leu es verges.	One of their reasons is that the woman is very ashamed.
E la segonda es quar tu no trobas femna be scient que descroba si meteyssa al metge quan es casta, o es de las femnas haventz maritz.	And the second reason is that you cannot find a woman who is well-versed in the art of childbirth and who would deliver herself to the doctor when she is chaste, or who has no husband.
La tersa es quar tu no hatrobas femna be sabent aquesta art, majorment la operacio am ma.	The third reason is that you cannot find a woman who is skilled in this art, especially the operation with hand.
E la quarta es que·l loc de la seccio sobre peyra en las femnas es longinc del loc de la peyra, per que indigeys de seccio preonda, e en aquela es temor.	And the fourth reason is that the location of the section on fear in women is too far from the location of the fear, so you need a preceding section, and in this there is fear.
Mays si necessitat provoca a tu ad aquo, lahoras cove que tu prenguas una femna metga be scient, e pauc es atrobada.	But if necessity prompts you to this, then accordingly it is necessary that you take a midwife who is well-versed and not easily found.
Mays si tu es privat de aquela, lahoras cerca metga quast e subtil, o presenta una femna matrona be esenhada en le feyt de las femnas, o femna que en aquesta art ennueys partida del art.	But if you are deprived of her, then accordingly look for a midwife who is skilled and subtle, or present a woman matron who has been initiated in the art of women, or a woman who has divided from this art.
Donc fay aquela present, e comanda a lu que fassa tot aquo que tu li mandaras, de la enquisicio sobre la peyra al comensament; la qual causa es que reguarde si la femna es verges, lahoras cove que meta lo sieu dit en le cul de lu e quiera la peyra.	Therefore, present her and command her to do all that you will tell her from the beginning of the inquiry on fear; which cause is that she should look if the woman is chaste, then accordingly put your said indication in her rectum and desire the fear.
Donc si atroba aquela, coarte aquela dejos le sieu dit, e lahoras comanda a lu que inscida sobre aquela.	Therefore, if you find that, cut it below your said indication, and then command her to insert it on that.
Mays si no es verge, lahoras comanda a la matrona que entrometa lo sieu dit en le conh de la malauta e enquiera sobre la peyra, pus que pausa la sua ma sinistra sobre la vesica, e comprem aquela am bona comprecio.	But if she is not chaste, then accordingly command the matron to insert her said indication into the anus of the patient and inquire about the fear, since she will place her left hand on the bladder and compress it with a good compression.
Donc si atroba aquela, lahoras cove que gradantment maugua aquela de l’orrifici de la vesica a las partidas dejos am somman de la sua vertut entro que pervengua am aquel a la razit de la coyssa.	Therefore, if you find that, then accordingly it is necessary to gradually relax that from the orifice of the bladder down to the lower parts with the summit of her virtue until it reaches the rectum of the wound.
E aprop inscida sobre aquela apposicio de la maytat del conh deves la razit de la coyssa de qualque part sia a lu parada e cent la peyra en aquela partida, e·l dit de lu no sia remaugut de la peyra coartan dejos lu.	And accordingly insert it on that opposition of the majority of the anus to the rectum of some part so that the fear is in that part, and the said indication of yours not be relaxed from the fear cut off below.
E la seccio sia pauca al comensament; e aprop entrometa lo ray sobre aquela seccio, e si sent la peyra, lahoras ajuste en seccio segon la quantitat la qual sap que la peyra sira getada de aquela.	And the section should be small at first; and accordingly insert the ruler on that section, and if you feel the fear, then adjust to section according to the quantity which you know will cause the fear to be driven from there.
E sapias que las specias de peyra son motas: quar de aquelas es pauca e gran, e leon e aspra, e longua e redonda, e havent ramps.	And know that the species of fear are many: for some are small and great, and lion-like and harsh, and long and round, and having ridges.
Donc tu sapias quantas specias so de lu per aquo que tu signifiques sobre aquo que vols.	Therefore, you know how many species there are of it by this which you signify on what you want.
E si tu veus flux de sanc, ajusta en le loc vetriol trissat e te aquela per una hora entro que sia abscindit le sanc, e aprop retorna a la tua operacio entro que la peyra sia fora-getada.	And if you see a flow of blood, adjust with vitriol powder on that location and keep it for one hour until the blood is stopped, and accordingly return to your operation until the fear is forgotten.
E fay que prepares am tu dels instrumentz les quals e ditz en la extraccio de peyra en les homes, per so que sias ajudat per aquels en la tua operacio.	And make sure to prepare with you the instruments which are mentioned in the extraction of fear from men, for that reason that you will be helped by them in your operation.
E si tu veus flux de sanc, e sabes que la expulcio del sanc es de la arceria que es insciza, lahoras tu pausa polvera sobre le loc e estrenh aquel am pulvils e strictura descent, e no iteras aquo; e layssa la peyra e no extraguas aquela, quar fort leu morira la malauta.	And if you see a flow of blood and know that the expulsion of blood is from the instrument inserted, then accordingly you pause powder on that location and strengthen it with powders and strictures descending, and do not iterate this; and leave the fear alone and do not extract it, for very soon the patient will die.
E aprop cura la plagua.	And accordingly cure the wound.
Donc cum es cedada la acuitat del sanc aprop alcus jorns, e·l loc se poyreys, lahoras tu retorna a la tua operacio entro que la peyra sia fora-getada.	Therefore, when the sharpness of blood has ceased after some days, and the location is well, then accordingly you return to your operation until the fear is forgotten.
Capitol lxii.	Chapter LXII.
De seccio sobre ernia acoza.	On the Section on Hernia in the Abdomen.
Hernia ayguoza no es sino agregacio de humiditat en le ciphac blanc lo qual es dejos la codena dels genetius contenent le huou, e es nompnat ciphac.	Hernia in the abdomen is nothing but an accumulation of moisture in the white apron which is below the cord of the genitals containing the urine, and is called a ciphac.
E alcunas veguadas es en le propri pannicol le qual a lu preparec natura en la partida del huou, entro que sia cuyat que ja es autre huou; e es la codena del genetiu entre le ciphac blanc le qual havem dit, e no es aquo sino tart.	And sometimes it is in the own apron which nature has prepared for the urine in the part of the bladder, until it is full and another urine; and it is the cord of the genitals between the white apron which we have said, and it is not that but a taut cord.
E la generacio de aquest hernia es per debelitat la qual accideys als genetius, per que ad aquels es efundunda aquesta materia, e alcunas vetz accideys per percuscio fayta sobre les genetius.	And the generation of this hernia is due to weakness which occurs in the genitals, for that reason that it flows out from them this matter, and sometimes it happens through a blow made on the genitals.
E aquesta humiditat es havent motas colors, quar la color de lu o es declinant a citrina o a sanguinent, o rog, o es negra feculenta, o es ayguosa blanqua, e es aquo que es mays.	And this moisture has many colors, for the color of it either declines to citrine or sanguine, or red, or is blackish feculent, or white watery, and that is what is most.
E les senhals per les quals es saubut on es aquesta agreguacio de aygua so aquestz: quar si es en le ciphac blanc le qual havem dit, lahoras le apostema es redon declinant un pauc a longitut ayssi cum figura de huou, e appar le genetiu, quar la humiditat conte aquel de tota part.	And the signs by which it is known where this accumulation of water is so: for if it is in the white apron which we have said, then accordingly the apostema is rounded declining a little towards length, and appears like the figure of urine, and shows the genitals, for the moisture contains that from all parts.
E si la humiditat es en le propri pannicol, lahoras le apostema es redon am partida del huou e per aysso hom estima que es autre huou.	And if the moisture is in the own apron, then accordingly the apostema is rounded with the part of urine and by that one estimates that it is another urine.
E si la humiditat es entre la codena dels genetius e·l ciphac blanc, lahoras catz dejos le centiment.	And if the moisture is between the cord of the genitals and the white apron, then accordingly it is cut off below the sentiment.
E cum tu vols la cognicio de la color de la humiditat, lahoras tu esproa la color de la humiditat en le apostema am entromes cayrat del qual la forma es precedida; e segon aquo que es eyssit en le vestigi del entromes, jutga de aquo que es dedintz lu.	And when you want to know the color of the moisture, then accordingly you try out the color of the moisture in the apostema by inserting a stick from which the form is preceded; and according to that which is found in the vestige of the stick, judge what it is below.
Donc quan nos vinem a la curacio de lu am ferr, lahoras cove que comandem al malaute que sia fleubotomat si aquo es a tu possibla, e vezes le cos de lu ple.	Therefore, when we come to the cure of it with iron, then accordingly it is necessary that you command the patient to be flebotomized if this is possible for you, and sometimes fill up his body.
E aprop sia resupinat sobre le sieu dos sobre alcuna causa un pauc auta, e pausa dejos lu motz draps.	And accordingly lie on your back on some cause a little above, and pause below him many cloths.
E aprop setz tu sobre la part sinistra de lu, e comanda al ministra que segua a la dextra de lu, le qual extenda la sua vergua a hun de dos latz a la codena dels genetius e a la partida del mirac del ventre.	And accordingly sit you on the left side of him, and command the minister to follow on the right side of him, which will extend her hand to one or two sides to the cord of the genitals and to the part of the navel.
E aprop pren spatum lat e scindeys la codena dels genetius del mieg loc per la longitut entro prop le pentenilh.	And accordingly take a spatula late and cut the cord of the genitals in half through the middle location, to the length almost up to the pubic bone.
E sia fayta la seccio segon rectetut engualment distant de la linha que deveseys la pel dels genetius, entro que pervengua al ciphac blanc comprehendent.	And be made the section according to equal measure distant from the line which should be drawn on the skin of the genitals, until it reaches the white apron inclusive.
E excorja aquel, e observa, e guarda te per aysso que tu no inscidas aquel; e la tua excoriacio am la qual aquel excorjas per partida jassia que sia suspenduda am le huou mays e subtilment escruta am la excoriacio segon la quantitat a tu possibla.	And excise that, and observe, and be cautious for yourself that you do not insert it; and your excision with which that is excised by partition below, so that it is suspended in the urine more and subtly scrutinize the excision according to the quantity possible.
E aprop perfora le ciphac ple de aygua am perforacio ampla, e extratz tota l’aygua.	And accordingly pierce the white apron full of water with a wide perforation, and extract all the water.
E aprop separa entre doas labias de la seccio am uncis, e exten le ciphac a las partidas desus; e no toques la codena les genetius comprehendent, e inscideys le ciphac en aquela manieyra que es a tu possible.	And accordingly separate between two lips of the section with uncles, and stretch the white apron to the upper parts; and do not touch the cord of the genitals inclusive, and insert the white apron in that manner which is possible for you.
E inscideys aquel am la sua totalitat o en pessas, e majorment le sieu latz subtil, quar si tu no perscrutas exquisidament la inscizio de lu, no es fayta segurtat que la aygua no retorne.	And insert it with its totality or in pieces, and more so the subtle sides, for if you do not scrutinize the insertion of him carefully, there is no surety that the water will not return.
Mays si le huou procezeys de aquela defora de la sua codena en la ora de la tua operacio, lahoras quan tu auras complida la seccio del ciphac, retorna dedintz aquel, e aprop ajusta las doas labias de la codena dels genetius am sutura, e aprop cura aquel ayssi cum las autras plagua, entro que sia sanat.	But if the urine proceeds from that outside of its cord in the hour of your operation, then when you have completed the section of the white apron, return to it, and accordingly adjust the two lips of the cord of the genitals with suturing, and accordingly cure it just like the other wounds, until it is healed.
E si atrobas le huou corromput per autra malautia, lahoras cove que tu lies les vayssels les quals so sore le suspensori, e extrat le huou, e aprop cura aquel am aquo que havem dit.	And if you find the urine corrupted by another disease, then accordingly it is necessary that you loosen the vessels which are sore the suspender, and extract the urine, and accordingly cure it with what we have said.
Mays si l’aygua es agreguada en doas partidas esemps, lahoras sapias que doas son las ernias; donc inscideys aquela partida segon que has feyt en l’autra engualment; e si es a tu vist que sia una opera, lahoras tu la fay.	But if the water is accumulated in two separate parts, then you know that there are two hernias; therefore, insert that part according to what you have done in the other equally; and if it seems to you that it is one operation, then you do it.
E aprop tu abstergiys le sanc, e entramet en las seccios lana submersa en oli o en oli rozat; e pausa deforo autra lana la qual tu as submersa en vi e oli, e expandeys aquela sobre dos genetius e·l mirac del ventre; e pausa desobre draps doblatz e pulvils, e lia aquels desobre am liament le qual es segon aquesta forma:	And accordingly you wash away the blood, and insert into the sections wool submerged in oil or rose oil; and pause before another wool which you have submerged in vinegar and oil, and spread it over two genitals and the navel; and pause above folded cloths and powders, and bind those above with a ligament according to this form:
e aprop sian preses dos draps e sian humplitz de lana carmenada segon aquesta semblansa; e sian faytas las extremitatz am les quals es premut de coto o de lana humida, e sian agreguatz am strectura en le braguier de las braguas, e la una de las extremitatz prengua del cul entro al dos, e la segonda prengua a la partida del pantenilh, e dos extramitatz sobre dos coyssas dejos e dos extramitatz autras sobre dos angonars, e tota extrictura sia ajustada en le braguier de las braguas.	and accordingly two cloths are pressed and filled with Carmenated wool according to this likeness; and the extremities are made with those which are premuted of cotton or wet wool, and added to the structure in the waistband of the breeches, and one of the extremities takes from the anus to the thigh, and the second takes from the part of the pubic bone, and two extractions above two cresses below and two other extractions above two garters, and all the structure is adjusted in the waistband of the breeches.
