E alcunas veguadas aquesta hernia es medicada artificialment am cauteri en loc de seccio am ferr; e es que tu prenguas cauteri cutellar subtil e que inscidas am aquel la codena dels ginitius, e es ignit segon que havem recomtat entro que sia descubert le ciphac blanc contenent la aygua, e lahoras tu pren cauteri segon aquesta forma:	And sometimes this hernia is medicated artificially with a cauterizer in the place of section with iron; and it is that you take a cauterizer cutlery subtle and insert it into the cord of the genitals, and ignite according to what we have recounted, until the white apron containing the water is discovered, and then you take the cauterizer according to this form:
e es asemblat a letra greca.	and it is assembled in Greek letters.
E aprop perfora am aquel ciphac, e es ignit entro que tota la humiditat sia fora-gitada.	And accordingly pierce through that white apron, and ignite until all the humidity is exhausted.
E aprop exten le ciphac am uncis, e excorja am uncis, e excorja am cauteri subtil ignit; e inscideys aquel segon que es a tu possible entro que eradiques tot lu; e guarda te del huou que·l foc no·l toque.	And accordingly stretch the white apron with uncles, and excise with uncles, and excise with a subtle cauterizer ignited; and insert that into what is possible for you until it radiates all of it; and be cautious not to let the fire touch the urine.
E sapias que aquesta operacio es pus salva e pus longinqua de flux de sanc, e milhor que operacio am seccio.	And you know that this operation is more saved and longer in terms of blood flow, and better than an operation with section.
Mays si a tu fa contrarietat apostema caut en la hora de seccio o en hora de cauteri, o flux de sanc, lahoras cove que tu cures qual contrarietat fa a tu per aquo, am curacio la qual conveneys a lu segon que es dit.	But if it happens to you that an apostema is caught in the hour of section or at the hour of cauterization, or blood flow, then accordingly it is necessary that you cure which contrariety makes for you by that, with a treatment which is suitable for him according to what has been said.
Mays si le malaute es pauruc, e no spera la segonda operacio per la sua horribilitat, lahoras administra perforacio segon que yeu recomti aquo; e es quan es certificat deves tu, per aquo que havem dit de las significacios, que aquela hernia es ayguosa.	But if the patient is poor and does not hope for a second operation due to its horror, then accordingly administer perforation according to what we have recommended here; and it is when you are certified by this signification that the hernia is watery.
Lahoras cove que tu fassas sezer le malaute sobre alcuna cezelha elevada, aprop perfora le apostema en la partida pus bassa de lu am spatum lat, e pausa la perforacio segon la longitut del cos.	Then accordingly you should make the patient lie on some elevated ceiling, and pierce the apostema in the lowest part of him with a spatula late, and pause the perforation according to the length of the body.
E sia la apercio ampla entro que corro tota l‘aygua.	And be the aperture wide enough for all the water to flow out.
E aprop pausa sobre le loc coto e lia aquel e layssa aquel, per so que corro le romanent de l’aygua.	And accordingly pause on the place cotton and bind it and leave it, in order that the remaining water may flow out.
E aprop cura aquel entro que la plagua sia sanada.	And accordingly cure that until the wound is healed.
Mays si contrarietat es a la egrecio de l’aygua en aquela hora tu perforas aquela: e aquo no es fayt sino per aquo quar le pannicol blanc en le orrifici de la plagua fa contrarietat e prohibeys le eyssiment de l’aygua, lahoras cove que tu metas en la plagua pena o instrument am la qual es extrayta l’aygua dels ydropitz, la forma del qual es precedida; o ajusta en la opprecio de la plagua un petit.	But if contrariety is against the flow of water in that hour you pierce it: and this is not done except for this reason because the white apron in the orifice of the wound makes contrariety and prohibits the exit of the water, then accordingly it is necessary to put into the wound a pain or instrument with which the water is extracted from the hydropisies, the form of which is preceded; or adjust a small one in the opposite part of the wound.
E sapias que l’aygua retorna, e es agueguada aprop vi meses o enaviro aquels; e cum es agreguada, lahoras sia perforat segon aquela meteyssa manieyra, quar le malaute ayssi passara les sieus dias.	And you know that the water returns, and is accumulated accordingly for about 2 months or thereabouts; and when it is accumulated, then accordingly it should be pierced according to that manner of procedure, in order that the patient may thus pass his days.
Capitol .lxiii.	Chapter LXIII.
De seccio sobre hernia carnosa e la curacio de lu.	On the Section about Fleshly Hernia and its Cure.
Sapias que en la seccio sobre aquesta hernia es temor perdusent a pernicia en las majors disposicios; per que a mi es vista la dimissio de lu e esser salvat per aquela milhor.	Know that in the section about this hernia there is fear of being lost to perdition in greater dispositions; therefore, it has been seen by me the dismissal of him and being saved through that which is better.
E yeu so rememorant la operacio en aquela e las specias dels apostemas.	And you should remember the operation in this case and the species of the apostemes.
Donc, dic que l‘apostemas natz en les cos dels quals les genetius so conponutz e es fayt aquo per motas causas: o per superfluitat aguda agra, la qual es efundida als genetius, o per percuscio.	Therefore, I say that the apostemes are born in those whose genitals are composed and it is made so by many causes: or by acute and bitter superfluity, which is poured into the genitals, or by impact.
E es la color de la apostema segon la color del cos, e no es atrobat en lu dolor, e es apostema greu.	And it is the color of the apostema according to the color of the body, and it is not found in him pain, and it is a grave apostema.
E fort leu es apostema lapificada, del qual la color es fosca, e no es centiment a lu.	And very often it is a fatty apostema, the color of which is dark, and there is no sentiment in him.
E alcunas veguadas es fayt per nodacio de las arcerias, e per imflacio de aquelas ayssi quo ja es perceubut la rememoracio de lu, o per imflacio de venas.	And sometimes it is caused by blockage of the arteries, and by inflammation of those so that already there is a recollection of him, or by inflammation of veins.
Mays aquo que es per imflacio de arcerias es conogut per la dispercio de la apostema quan compremas aquela am les tieus ditz; e no cove que aquel toques.	But that which is caused by inflammation of the arteries is known by the distribution of the apostema when you compress it with those said ties; and it does not need for him to touch.
Mays aquel que es fayt per imflacio de vena no es dispergut de lu alcuna causa deves la compressio am les ditz.	But that which is caused by inflammation of the vein is not dispersed from him for any reason, even with compression using those said ties.
E ja es possible que sobre aquesta specia sia fayta seccio e sobre les autres carns; e es que tu inscida la codena dels genetius, e aprop esten le huou a las partidas desus, e extratz aquel del ciphac blanc, e deliura le suspensori dels vaysels, e ligua les, e inscideys le suspensori pus que tu deliuras aquel de tota partida de las partidas del huou.	And it is possible that on this species a section should be made and on the other flesh; and it is that you insert the cord of the genitals, and accordingly stretch the urine to the upper parts, and extract that from the white apron, and deliver the suspender of the vessels, and bind them, and insert the suspender more than you deliver that of all part of the parts of the urine.
Donc si l’huou ja es am aquelas carnadas consolida, lahoras cove que tu extraguas le huou e inscidas aquel.	Therefore, if the urine is already consolidated with those fleshly matters, then accordingly it is necessary that you extract the urine and insert it.
E si es adherencia entro alcuna causa del ciphac, o entre aquo que es entre les bayssels, lahoras cove que tu deliures tota aquela adherencia e inscidas aquela per inscizio redonda.	And if there is adhesion due to some cause of the white apron or between what is between the vessels, then accordingly it is necessary that you deliver all that adhesion and insert it with a rounded insertion.
Mays si es nativitat de carn en le loc de la adherencia la qual es detras, lahoras cove que tu inscidas tot aquo que es de lu, e extraguas le huou ayssi cum havem dit.	But if it is a natural growth of flesh in the place of adhesion which is behind, then accordingly it is necessary that you insert all that is of him, and extract the urine just as we have said.
Donc cum es complida la tua operacio, lahoras omple la plagua de lana imfuza en oli rozat e vi; e aprop cura aquela am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	Therefore, when your operation is complete, then accordingly fill the wound with wool infused in rose oil and vinegar; and accordingly cure that with another cure until it is healed.
Capitol .lxiv.	Chapter LXIV.
De la curacio de hernia que es de vitz.	On the Cure of Hernia which is of Vine.
Vit es apostema envolut per alcuna envolucio semblant a broto am mollificacio dels testiculs, e es fayt dificil movement exercitiu e deambulacio sobre le malaute.	Vine is an aposteme enveloped by some wrapping resembling a sprout with softening of the testicles, and it is made difficult for the patient to perform movements, exercise, and walking.
E en la curacio de aquesta malautia es per temor per aquo del qual es precedida rememoracio.	And in the cure of this disease it is due to fear, because of which memory precedes it.
Empero cove que diguam opperacio en aquela segon que fero les primiers.	However, I must say that the operation in this case should be done according to what I did first.
E dic que cove que fassas sezer le malaute sobre una cezelha elevada; e aprop enpelleys le suspensori dels testiculs a las partidas dejos; e aprop te la codena dels genetius am les tieus ditz am les baysels que so probdas a la vergua; e tengua aquels autre ministre que tu, e extenda aquels am extencio vehement.	And I say that it is necessary to make the patient lie on an elevated ceiling; and accordingly, enfold the suspender of the testicles at the lower parts; and accordingly, take hold of the cord of the genitals with those said ties and vessels which are proved by the sheath; and hold these other ministers that you have, and extend them with a strong extension.
E aprop inscideys am spatum lat agut per seccio traversa en le dreyt dels vaysels entro que sian les vayssels descubertz.	And accordingly insert into the spatula late with a cross section on the right side of the vessels, until the vessels are discovered.
E aprop excorja de tota partida ayssi quo a tu havem dit en extraccio de arceria las quals so en las templas.	And accordingly excise from all parts just as we have said in extraction of arteries which are on the temples.
E aprop fica en aquelas un’agulha en la qual sia fiel doble, e lia aquel en le primier del locs en les quals accideys vit, e lia aquel autra veguada en le derier de lor.	And accordingly place in those an awl with a faithful double thread, and tie that to the first of the places where it occurs, and tie that other time at the last of them.
E aprop inscideys aquels en le mieg loc per seccio dreyta segon la longuesa del cos, e extratz aquo que es agreguat de las humiditatz fetulentas e corruptas.	And accordingly insert those in the middle location by straight section according to the length of the body, and extract that which is accumulated from the foul and corrupted humors.
E aprop cura la plagua am curacio de las autras plaguas en las quals vols sania esser engendrada per so que caian les vaysels les quals noyreysso un de dos genetius, quar no es mal per aquo.	And accordingly cure the wound with the cure of other wounds in which you wish to be generated by that which falls from the vessels which nourish one of two genitals, for it is not bad because of this.
Mays si accideys vit a totz les bayssels, lahoras cove que·ls testicols sian extragutz o que les testicols per aquo se cequo am les vayssels, per que sia privat de tot nutriment per la inscizio dels vayssels, e que sian estaborits, o que cequo per so que no sia juvament am aquels.	But if the vit affects all the vessels, then accordingly it is necessary that the testicles be extracted or that the testicles by this means be joined with the vessels, in order to be deprived of all nourishment by the section of the vessels, and to be extinguished, or to become hardened because it will not be nourished by them.
Capitol .lxv.	Chapter LXV.
De la cura de hernia entestinal.	On the Cure of Hernia Intestinal.
Le adveniment de aquesta hernia es per seccio que endeve en le ciphac extendut sobre le ventre de part dels angunars del mirac del ventre, per que deysendo les budels de aquela ruptura ad alcu dels budels.	The advent of this hernia is due to a section that takes place in the apron extended over the belly from the navel to the groin, so that bursting forth from one of those intestines.
E aquesta ruptura es o del ciphac o de excencio de lu, e accideysso aquestas doas specias per motas causas: o percussio, o per sautz, o per clamor, o per elevacio de alcuna causa greu, o per semblantz.	And this rupture is either of the apron or of excess of him, and it occurs in two species due to many causes: or percussion, or by force, or by noise, or by elevation of some grave cause, or by similarities.
E·l senhal de aquo, quan es per extencio del ciphac, es que accideys pauc a pauc en lonc temps, e no accideys soptament, e es apostema engual entro ves le preon per so quar le ciphac comprem le budel.	And the sign of this, when it is due to extension of the apron, is that it occurs gradually over a long period of time, and does not occur suddenly, and it is an aposteme which grows evenly within the prepuce because the apron compresses the intestine.
E le senhal de lu es quan es per seccio del ciphac, quar al comensament fa accidir dolor vehement sobtament; e es apostema divers aparent dejos la codena propdana aparent, e aquo es per eyssiment del budel, e·l cos de lu a las partidas deforo del ciphac.	And the sign of him is when it is due to section of the apron, because at the beginning it causes sudden and violent pain; and it is an aposteme which appears differently underneath the apparent cord, and this is because of the intestine's protrusion, and his body goes out to the parts outside the apron.
E alcunas veguadas es fora-getat am le budel la tela, e es apelada aquesta hernia entestinal zirbal.	And sometimes it is forgotten in the intestine's membrane, and this is called intestinal hernia cirrhotic.
E alcunas veguadas es fayta am ventositat, e alcunas veguadas corr en le budel fenda, e aqui es retenguda, e es am aquo gran pernitia3 del malaute, e alcunas veguadas fa endevenir dolor malvada e majorment quan es premut.	And sometimes it is made with ventosity, and sometimes it runs into the intestine's fissure, and here it is retained, and this is accompanied by great pain for the patient, and sometimes it makes a wicked and greater pain when it is pressed.
E en la curacio de las especias de aquesta malautia am ferr es temor, per que cove que sia esquivat le cazament en aquela.	And in the cure of this disease's species with iron there is fear, because it is necessary to avoid the mistake in that.
E la manieyra de la operacio de aquela es que comandes al malaute que redugua le budel am la sua ma a las partidas dedintz de la sua conquavitat si obezeys al sieu retornament, e aprop sia envessat sobre le sieu col entre las tuas mas, e eleva las cambas de lu.	And the manner of the operation in that is that you command the patient to reduce the intestine with his own hand to the parts outside of his conqueror if he obeys his returnment, and accordingly it should be enveloped over his back between your hands, and raise the patient's legs.
E aprop sten la codena la qual siec la codena dels testicols a las partidas desus, e inscideys la codena dels testicols tota per le lonc; e aprop fiqua en doas labias de la seccio uncis segon que indigeysses a hubrir la seccio am aquels.	And accordingly take hold of the cord which cuts off the cord of the testicles to the upper parts, and insert the cord of the testicles all along; and accordingly place in two lips of the section uncis according to what is needed to open the section with those.
E si’ la seccio segon la quantitat que a tu sia possible que de aquela le huou sia foro-getat.	And if the section is according to the quantity that it is possible for you to forget from that, the urine should be forgotten.
E aprop excorja aquela ciphaqueth les quals so dejos la codena dels testicols, entro que sia descubert le ciphac blanc dur de quascuna partida.	And accordingly excise those apron-like things which are underneath the cord of the testicles, until the white hard apron is discovered in each part.
Lahoras tu entromet le tieu dit en aquo que siec le testicol, en aquo que es entre ciphac blanc, le qual es dejos la codena del huou, e entre le ciphac segon, e absolve am aquel’adherencia que es en la partida detras del huou.	Then accordingly you should tie the said thread to that which is tied to the testicle, in that which is between the white apron and the one that is underneath the cord of the urine, and between the second apron, and absolve from that adhesion which is in the part behind the urine.
E aprop mau am la ma la codena dels testicols a las partidas deforo, e am aysso exten le ciphac blanc en sus am la ma sinestra, e eleva le huou am le ciphac a la partida de la seccio; e comanda al ministre que extenda le huou ensus e tu dissolveys la adherencia que es detras am solucio complida.	And accordingly take hold of the cord of the testicles with your left hand, and extend the white apron on top with your right hand, and raise the urine to the part of the section; and command the minister to extend the urine upwards and you dissolve the adhesion that is behind with complete solution.
E cerqua am les tieus ditz que lay no sia alcuna causa del budel envelopat en le ciphac blanc dur.	And search for those said threads so that there may be no cause of the intestine being enveloped in the white hard apron.
Mays si tu atrobas de lu alcuna causa, lahoras tu enpelleys aquel al ventre dejos.	But if you find any cause from him, then accordingly you should tie that to the belly below.
E aprop tu pren una agulha en la qual sia fiel gros fayt de x fiels, e entromet aquel deves le derier del ciphac, le qual es jos la codena dels testicols, la qual siec seccio; e aprop inscideys las extremitatz las quals emineysso del fiel entro que sian quatre fiels, e aprop compausa alcus de lor sobre alcuna figura en manieyra de crotz; e lia am aquel le ciphac del qual havem dit que es dejos la codena dels testicols am fort liament de dos partz.	And accordingly take a needle with a thread of four threads, and insert that in the last part of the apron, which is underneath the cord of the testicles, where the section is; and accordingly, insert the extremities which protrude from the thread into four threads, and accordingly compose some of them on some figure in manner of a cross; and tie with that the apron which we have said is underneath the cord of the testicles with strong bond of two parts.
E aprop envolveys las extremitatz dels fiels e lia aquelas am liament vehement entro que alcu dels vayssels que noyrrisso aquels no puscan trametre alcuna causa per so que de aqui no accida apostema caut.	And accordingly envelop the extremities of the threads and tie those with a strong bond, in order that some of the vessels which nourish them may not be able to transmit any cause by which here an aposteme may occur.
E pausa autra veguada liament segon foro le primier liament, lonh de lu mens tres ditz; e aprop aquestz dos liaments layssa del ciphac le qual es dejos la codena dels testicols la quantitat de la grandeza del dit, e inscideys tot le romanent segon redondeza, e osta de lu le huou.	And accordingly pause another bond after the first bond, about three inches away; and accordingly let those two bonds be from the apron which is underneath the cord of the testicles the quantity of the greatness of the thread, and insert all the remaining part according to roundness, and stop the urine.
E aprop inscideys en la partida dejos de la codena dels testicols per seccio de la qual corra sanc e sania ayssi cum havem recomtat en aquo que havem dit.	And accordingly insert into the part underneath the cord of the testicles by section of which blood and pus will flow as we have recommended in that which we have said.
E aprop aministra lana submersa en oli, e pausa en la plagua; e aministra le liament le qual havem recomtat (e alcunas veguadas le ciphac blanc es cauterizat, le qual havem dit aprop la inscizio de lu temen de flux de sanc, quar motas veguadas accideys aquels) e leyssa le liament entro que per si caia.	And accordingly apply wool soaked in oil to the wound; and pause there; and apply the thread which we have recommended (and sometimes the white apron is cauterized, which we have said should be done at the incision of the wound to prevent blood flow, because many times those apostemes occur) and let the thread fall into place.
Mays si le cazement de lu es tardat, lahoras de aygua cauda sia embrocat, e pausa sobre aquel entro que caia segon que havem dit.	But if the mistake of him is delayed, then accordingly cold water should be poured, and pause over that until it falls according to what we have said.
E aprop cura la plagua am l’autra curacio de las plaguas entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly cure the wound with another cure of wounds until it is healed.
Capitol .lxvi.	Chapter LXVI.
De hernia ventosa.	On Hernia Ventosa.
En aquesta hernia no e vist alcu que sia estat ardit sus la curacio de lu am ferr.	In this hernia, it has not been seen that anyone has been burnt by the cure with iron.
E les primiers diyssero que es fayta ayssi cum havem recomtat en la hernia que es am vi; la qual es que tu lies les vayssels aprop la seccio sobre aquela am fecilitat de lu; e aprop secca en le mieg loc en enviro le apostema am aquo que obro aquel, entro que caian les vayssels.	And the first ones said that it is done just as we have recommended in the hernia which is with wine; which is that you tie the vessels accordingly at the section on that side with felicitous ease; and accordingly cut in the middle location around the aposteme with water that brings about that, until the vessels fall.
E cura la plagua segon que havem dit entro que sia sanada.	And cure the wound according to what we have said until it is healed.
Capitol .lxvii.	Chapter LXVII.
De la disropcio que es fayta en les anguonars.	On the Disproportion that is made in the Navel.
Alcunas veguadas endeve ruptura en les angonars ayssi cum havem dit, e emineys le loc.	Sometimes a rupture occurs in the navel just as we have said, and protrudes the location.
E no deyssen als genetius alcuna causa dels budels al genetius; e si deyssen, aquo es pauc; e retorna s’en en totas horas.	And there is no reason for the genitals to be affected by the intestines at the genitalia; and if there is, it is slight; and returns to its normal state in all hours.
Mays si es prolonguat le temps am aquo, es ajustada fissura en le ciphac entro que deysenda le budel en le ciphac; e accideys aquo per la extencio del ciphac le qual es en le angonars ayssi cum havem dit, la qual causa es quar le ciphac es estendut, e aprop es mollificat e·l loc es apostemat e emineys.	But if the time is prolonged with this, there is an opening in the apron into which the intestine descends; and this occurs because of the extension of the apron which is in the navel just as we have said, which cause is that the apron is stretched, and accordingly it becomes softened and the location apostematises and protrudes.
E la cura de lu es am cauteri ayssi quo es precedida la narracio de lu.	And the cure for this is with a cauterizing tool just as the narrative of this has described.
E alcunas veguadas es curada am ferr segon aquesta manieyra: e es que·l malaute jagua sobre le sieu dos entre las tuas mas, e aprop secca le loc de la ruptura dels apostemas emineys am seccio per la latitut segon la quantitat de tres ditz.	And sometimes it is cured with iron according to this manner: and it is that the patient lies on his back between his thighs, and accordingly cuts the location of the rupture of the apostemes protruding by section along the width in a quantity of three fingers.
E aprop strenh le ciphac blanc que es jos la codena entro que sia descubert.	And accordingly strengthen the white apron that is underneath the cord, until it is discovered.
E aprop pren le ray e pausa aquel sobre le loc eminent del ciphac, e prem aquel al preon del ventre.	And accordingly take the reed and pause it over the protruding location of the apron, and press it against the belly's fold.
E aprop cus le dos locs eminentz sobre la extremitat del ray del ciphac, e ajusta am la sutura un de aquels am l’autre.	And accordingly close the two protruding locations on the tip of the reed of the apron, and adjust them with a suture one to the other.
E aprop extratz la extremitat del ray, e no inscidas del ciphac de tot, ni no extenda le huou, ni autra causa ayssi cum yeu te fi saber en la curacio de hernia entestinal.	And accordingly extract the tip of the reed, and do not insert it into the apron completely, nor extend the urine, nor any other cause just as you would want to know in the cure of intestinal hernia.
E aprop cura aquela am la curacio de las plaguas, e cum inscideyses les fiels, mundifica aquela e restaura la plagua entro que sia consolidada; quar le ciphac es contrayt e no es ajustada la eminencia de ruptura.	And accordingly cure that with the cure of wounds, and by inserting the threads, cleanse it and restore the wound until it is consolidated; for the apron has contracted and the protrusion of rupture has not been adjusted.
E cauteri es milhor en aquest loc, quar es pus propda a salut.	And cauterization is better in this location, since it is closer to health.
Capitol .lxviii.	Chapter LXVIII.
De mollificacio de la codena dels testiculs.	On Softening of the Cord of the Testicles.
Motas veguadas la codena dels testiculs en alcus homes es mollificada per aysso quar las carns que so entre aquela son mollificadas, e es fedat le reguardament de lu.	Many times the cord of the testicles in some men is softened because the flesh which is between that is softened, and it is fitting for him to take care.
Adonc necessari es ad aquel que es preguat en la curacio de lu que fassa jazer le malaute segon le sieu dos, e enscida tota la codena la qual es mollificada sobre la codena natural; e aprop que ajuste doas labias am la sutura.	Therefore it is necessary for the one who is taking care of him in his cure to make the patient lie on his back, and insert all the softened cord which is above the natural cord into it; and accordingly adjust two lips with a suture.
E si vols, cus en le comensament la superfluitat de la codena mollificada am tres cozeduras o quatre e am ferma sutura.	And if you want, cut off the excess of the softened cord with three or four cauterizations and a firm suture.
E aprop inscideys entre las suturas; e aprop cura per curacio de las autras plaguas entro que sia sanat e caian les fiels.	And accordingly insert between the sutures; and accordingly cure by curing of other wounds until it is healed and the threads fall.
Capitol .lxix.	Chapter LXIX.
De castracio.	On Castration.
Sapias que castratio en nostre ley es excomengada, mays per causa es legut a mi que·m remembre de lu en aquest libre; e no es necessaria la rememoracio de lu sino per doas manieyras, de las quals es la una per so que aquo sia en la sciensa del metge quan es enterroguat de aquela, que sapia la curacio de lu al qual accideys; e l’autra manieyra es que nos motas vetz havem necessitat de castracio de autras bestias per les juvamentz nostres per aquelas, ayssi cum de motos, e de bocs, e de porcs, e de semblantz a las bestias.	Know that castration in our law is excommunicated, but by reason it is written to me that I remember of it in this book; and it is not necessary to remind of it except by two manners, of which one is because of what this is in the knowledge of the doctor when he is asked about it, knowing the cure for him who suffers from it; and the other manner is that many times we have needed castration of other animals for our uses through them, just as with horses, and bulls, and pigs, and similar to these animals.
E donc dic que castracio es fayta en dos manieyras: o per atrissio, o per fissura a seccio.	And therefore I say that castration is done in two manners: either by emasculation, or by incision at the section.
Mays en aquela que es fayta per atrissio, la via de la opera es que nos fassam cezer la bestia en aygua cauda entro que·ls genetius de lu sian mollificatz e sian linhitz e que pendan.	But in that which is done by emasculation, the way of the operation is that we make the animal lie down in cold water until its genitalia are softened and relaxed, and hang.
E aprop pren aquels am la tua ma entro que sian resols e no apparescan dejos le tocament.	And accordingly take them with the help of your hand into where they are resolved and do not appear to be left behind by the touch.
Mays en castracio fayta per fissura e seccio, cove que tu tenguas la bestia e premas la codena dels testicols de lu am la ma senestra.	But in castration done by incision and section, it is necessary that you hold the animal and press the cord of the testicles with your left hand.
E aprop lia le suspensori, e inscideys sobre quascun huou am una seccio entro que dos huous proceseysso.	And accordingly tie the suspenders, and cut on each side with one incision until two incisions process.
E aprop inscideys aquels pus que auras quascu excorjat.	And accordingly cut those more than you would have excoriated.
E no leysses sobre aquels del ciphac alcuna causa, sino le ciphac subtil le qual es sobre les vazes.	And do not leave any cause on those of the apron, except for the subtle apron which is above the vessels.
E aquesta manieyra de castracio es milhor la qual es fayta per atrissio, quar atrissio fort leu layssa alcuna causa dels testicols per que la bestia desira coyt.	And this manner of castration is better which is done by emasculation, because emasculation leaves no cause for the testicles so that the animal desires to copulate.
E aprop cura la plagua entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly cure the wound until it is healed.
Capitol .lxx.	Chapter LXX.
De la cura de hermafrodozia.	On The Cure of Hermaphrodism.
Hermafrodozia en les homes es segon dos manieyras: la una es quar o appar en aquo que siec l’espazi en la codena de testiculs, en aquel que es entre dos testiculs figura quar cunh de femna en la qual so pels.	Hermaphrodism in men is according to two manners: the one is when it appears as a space in the cord of testicles, in that which is between two testicles, a figure like that of a woman's vulva.
E alcunas veguadas de aquel corr urina le qual es en la codena dels testiculs.	And sometimes from it flows urine which is in the cord of the testicles.
Mays en las femnas es una specia: e es que·l conh de la femna sobre le pentenilh es ayssi cum dos testiculs de home un pauc de tot yminiheys a la partida deforo ayssi cum le perpucii de home e dos testicols.	But in women, there is a species: and it is that the vulva of a woman on her pubic mound is like two testicles of a man, almost all of them being placed outside just as the male genitalia are.
E la curacio es de tres specias: de dos dels homes e de una specia de las femnas.	And the cure is of three species: two of men and one of women's.
E es que cove que tu inscidas aquelas carns ajustadas entro que efuga la emprecio de aquela, e aprop que cures aquelas am curacio de las autras plaguas.	And it is that you must insert those adjusted flesh into where it escapes the impression of that, and accordingly cure those with the cure of other wounds.
E en la segonda specia dels homes de la qual yeys urina la qual es en la codena dels testiculs, no es curacio ni opperacio en lu.	And in the second species of men from which urine flows which is in the cord of the testicles, there is no cure nor operation in it.
Capitol .xxi.	Chapter XXI.
De lentinge e de carn eminent per causas de las femnas.	On Swelling and Flesh Elevation due to Causes of Women.
Lentige fort leu es ajustada sobre causas naturals entro que es etressat e es fayt leg le reguardament; e alcunas veguadas es magnificada en alcunas femnas en tant entro que es spandit ayssi cum en les homes e perve entro al coito.	Swelling is slightly adjusted on natural causes until it becomes exhausted and makes the regulation firm; and sometimes it is magnified in some women to such an extent that it spreads like in men and penetrates into coitus.
Adonc cove que tu tenguas la superfluitat de lentinge am la tua ma o am unci e inscidas.	Therefore it is necessary for you to take the excess of swelling with your hand or with a tool and insert it.
E no ultimes en inscizio, majorment en le preon de la razit, per so que no endevengua flux de sanc.	And do not stop in inserting, especially at the pubic region, so that there may not be a flow of blood.
E aprop cura aquela am curacio de las plaguas entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly cure that with the cure of wounds until it is healed.
Mays carn nascuda es carn que nays en le horrifici de la mayre entro que umple aquel, e fort leu es eyssit a las partidas deforo segon semblansa de coa (e per aquo alscus primiers appelero aquo “malautia caudada”); donc cove que nos inscidam ayssi cum inscidem lentinge, e curem aquela entro que sia sanada.	But born flesh is flesh that grows in the horrificity of the mare until it fills it, and slightly rises to the outer parts according to the shape of a hen (and for this reason some first call this "diseased swelling"); therefore it is necessary for us to insert as we insert swelling, and cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .lxxii.	Chapter LXXII.
De curacio de alratica.	On The Cure of Ulceration.
Alratica es que le conh de la femna no sia perforat, o sia le trauc petit.	Ulceration is when the vulva of a woman is not perforated, or if it is slightly torn.
E es o natural o accidental.	And it is either natural or accidental.
Accidental es per malautia la qual ha precedit, e aquela es fayta o per carn nada ajustada o per ciphac subtil o espes.	Accidental is due to disease that has preceded, and it is caused either by flesh not being adjusted or by subtle apron or thick apron.
E es fayt o en le preon de la mayre, o en les costatz de lu, o en le pus sobira de lu, o en le pus bas de lu, e prohibeys de cuoyt e de enprenguacio e de enfantament, e fort leu prohibeys las mestruas.	And it is caused either in the pubic region of the mare, or in its sides, or at the highest part of it, or at the lowest part of it, and prohibits coitus and engagement and childbearing, and very much prohibits menstruation.
E la cognicio de aquela es fayta per reguardament de la metrona, si la oppilacio es apparent, propdana; mays si no es apparent, lahoras tu cerqua aquela am les tieus ditz o am le ray.	And the knowledge of that is made by observation of the uterus, if the opacity is apparent, you can diagnose; but if it is not apparent, you must search for it with those said fingers or with a reed.
Mays si oppilacio es per ciphac subtil, e es propda a las doas labias, lahoras tu coyta e disromp aquela.	But if the opacity is due to subtle apron and is placed on both lips, then you must cut and tear it.
E es que pauses sobre las doas labias pulvils, e aprop pausa les tieus ditz indicz de amdoas las mas encemps.	And it is that you pause over the two lips of dust, and accordingly pause those said indications on both sides.
E la femna sia sobre le sieu dos, las sieuas coyssas extendudas, e aprop exten las doas labias am forsa entro que aquel ciphac subtil sia romput e la oppilacio sia uberta.	And the woman should be on her back, her arms extended, and accordingly extend both lips with force until that subtle apron is broken and the opacity is opened.
E aprop pren lana e enbeu le4 en oli e pausa aquela sobre·l loc, e jagua am home le dia per so que·l loc inscis no sia consolidat.	And accordingly take linen and soak it in oil and pause that over the location, and make the patient lie down at home for a day so that the inserted location is not consolidated.
Mays si le ciphac es gros e espes, lahoras cove que tu inscidas aquel am spatum lat o am fuelha de mirta.	But if the apron is thick and dense, it is necessary for you to insert that with a spatula or with a mulberry leaf.
Mays si la oppilacio es per carnada, lahoras suspen aquela am unci, e inscideys aquela.	But if the opacity is due to edema, then suspend that with a tool, and insert it.
E sian am tu las medicinas que fan cessar flux de sanc ses mordicacio, ayssi cum ahacatia, e sanc de drago, e enses, ajustat am album de huou.	And be familiar with the medicines that stop bleeding without causing injury, such as aconite, dragon's blood, and essence, adjusted with white of egg.
E aprop aministra una canulha de plom ampla per so que la plagua no sia consolidada leugierament.	And accordingly administer a leaden cannula that is wide enough so that the wound does not become slightly consolidated.
E tengua aquela per alcus jorns e aministra calgua de li sec.	And keep that for some days and administer lukewarm water.
E aprop sia curada am l’autra curacio de consolidacio entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly be cured with the other cure of consolidation until it is healed.
E alcunas vetz accideys en la mayre nativitat de autres carns, e lahoras cove que inscidas segon aquesta manieyra.	And sometimes accidents happen in the natural birth of other flesh, and accordingly it is necessary to insert according to this manner.
Mays si aysso es per apostema crancos, a l’apostema crancos le qual es en la mayre no sia fayta contrarietat am ferr en deguna manieyra.	But if it is due to gangrenous aposteme, there should not be any opposition with iron in any manner at the aposteme which is in the mare.
Capitol .lxxiii.	Chapter LXXIII.
De la cura de emorroydas e de tayl e de botor roja que accideysso en le conh de las femnas.	On The Cure of Hemorrhoids and Tail and Red Botch that occur in the Vulva of Women.
Emorroydas so apprecio dels orificis de motas venas entro que de aquelas corro mot sanc continuadament; e cum so antiquadas emorroydas e son fayts theyls.	Hemorrhoids are a swelling of the orifices of many veins until those vessels are corrupted and continue to bleed continuously; and as old hemorrhoids become worse and are made worse by their throats.
E ja yeu he dit en la divisio las specias de aquelas e les senhals de aquelas, e diyre ayssi aquelas que recebo curacio e aquelas que no recebo curacio.	And I have already said in the division the species of those and their signs, and will say also which receive cure and which do not receive cure.
Donc dic que emorroydas e theyls quan so en le preon de la mayre e no apparo al sentiment, lahoras en aquelas no sia fayta curacio am ferr.	Therefore I say that hemorrhoids and throats when they are in the pubic region of the mare and do not appear to the sense, then in those there should not be made cure with iron.
Mays aquelas las quals so en le orrifici de la mayre sobre las quals catz sentiment, so aquelas que so curadas.	But those that are in the orifice of the mare above which one can sense, are those that are cured.
E cove que tu metas la femna en mayso frega e aprop exten atheyl am les forfexs, o am drap aspre, e inscideys aquelas am las razitz.	And it is necessary that you put the woman in a warm bath and accordingly extend her thighs with forceps, or with rough cloth, and insert those into the roots.
E aprop pulveriza sobre aquelas deves le fluxs del sanc de una de las polveras insciscivas ses mordicacio, ayssi cum acassia e semblant ad aquels.	And accordingly powder is spread over those to dry the flows of blood from one of the insertive powders that cause no injury, such as aconite and similar to those.
E aprop enpellesca les sieus pes per una hora, e aprop pausa aquela en aygua freja.	And accordingly press her feet for an hour, and then pause that in cold water.
E si persevera le fluxs del sanc, lahoras fay aquela sezer en decoccio de sumat e de scorsas de milgranas e de gualas e de semblantz.	And if the bleeding persists, then make that person sit in a decoction of Sumatra and Scorzonera of millet, and Gualas and similar plants.
E aprop pren farina de ordi e comfiys aquela am miel e vi agre e fay emplastre am aquo sobre le dos de lu.	And accordingly take wheat flour and mix it with honey, vinegar, and make a poultice with water on the back of him.
E si le sanc es abscindit, bo es; e sino, fay adherir am dos ventozas, e a las mamilhas ses escarificatio.	And if the blood is absorbed, it is good; and otherwise, make adhere two bellows to the breasts with scarification.
E aprop pren lana e submergeys aquela am suc de coliandre o am suc de arnagloza o am suc de guarravier am vi pentit e fay adherir al loc; e aprop cura le loc am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly take linen and submerge that in the juice of Colocynthis or in the juice of Arnoglossum or in the juice of Guaiacum mixed with vinegar, and make adhere to the location; and accordingly cure the location with poultices until it is healed.
Mays athyl rog le qual es de aspre reguardament, cove que tu inscidas aquo que a tu appar de aquel segon que he dit en theyl engualment.	But if the thigh is rough and harsh, it is necessary for you to insert that which appears to you from that according to what I have said in the equal part.
E cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .lxxiv.	Chapter LXXIV.
De perforacio de eyssedura accident en la mayre.	On The Perforation of Accidental Wound in the Mare.
Motas specias de apostemas accideysso en la mayre, ayssi cum cranc e apostema lapident e ulceracios e adhubelat e erpetromens e fistulas emorroyas e raguarrias e thyl e autres apostemas.	Many species of accidental wounds occur in the mare, such as gangrenous and apostematic, ulcerative and adhesion-like, erpetromenous and fistulous hemorrhoids, and rough and other apostemats.
E yeu ja he dit aquestas malautias e las specias de aquelas e les senhals de aquelas, e las curacios de lor en la divisio.	And I have already said these diseases and their species, and their signs, and the cures for them in the division.
E cove que yeu digua en aquest tractat de apostema caut le qual ve en la mayre quan es dels apostemas que collegeysso sania, e si vols saber en qual manieyra se fa la opperacio de lu am ferr.	And it is necessary for you to say in this treatise of gangrenous aposteme which occurs in the mare when one of the apostemats is healthy, and if you want to know how the operation is done on him with iron.
Adonc cove que tu consideres si la dolor de la apostema en le sieu comensament es aguda am percussio e flecma e febre, e vezes aquel enrogezir e si catz sobre aquel le sentiment, lahoras no·t coytes am perforacio de lu, e cura aquel am aquo que ajuda sobre la maturacio entro que cesse la acuitat dels accidentz.	Therefore it is necessary for you to consider if the pain of the aposteme in its beginning is acute with percussion and fluxing and fever, and sometimes that colorizes and if one senses on that location a sensation, then do not cut with perforation of him, and cure that with water that helps on maturity until the acuity of the accidents ceases.
E lahoras cove que tu fassas cezer la femna sobre una cezelha que aia doas cezelhas; e recline sobre le sieu dos e ajusta les sieus pes a la partida pus dejos del ventre, e las sieus coyssas sian expandudas, e pausa les sieus brasses dejos les sieus denols, e lia quascus am liament ad aquo convenient.	And accordingly it is necessary for you to make the woman lie down on a pillow that has two pillows; and recline on her back and adjust her feet at the lowest part of the belly, and her thighs be expanded, and pause her arms below her nails, and tie each one with a string to water conveniently.
E aprop la matrona segua del latz dreyt e aministre le instrument am le qual es ubert le orrifici de la mayre, la forma del qual vindra en aquelas causas que·s faran aprop.	And accordingly the midwife should follow the right way and administer the instrument with which the opening of the mare is covered, the form of which will come in those causes that are done accordingly.
E cove quan vols ministrar aquest instrument que tu fiques am lo ray le preon de la mayre de la femna, e aquo que del instrument es intrat en la mayre no sia mays que·l preon de la mayre e leda le malaute.	And accordingly when you want to administer this instrument, make sure that it is in the ray of the pubic region of the mare of the woman, and what enters the instrument into the mare does not exceed the pubic region of the mare and lead the patient.
Mays si l’estrument es major que·l preon de la mayre, lahoras cove que tu pauses pulvils sobre la textura del preon de la mayre per sso que sia prohibit l’intrament de tot instrument en le preon de la mayre.	But if the instrument is larger than the pubic region of the mare, then it is necessary for you to sprinkle powder on the texture of the pubic region of the mare so that it prohibits the entry of any instrument into the pubic region of the mare.
E cove que tu pauses le vertitge que corr en le strument del latz pus desus e que le ministre tengua le strument e revolva le vertitge entro que sia ubert le orrifici de la mayre.	And accordingly you should pause the vertebra that runs on the instrument above and below, and the one who ministers should hold the instrument and turn the vertebra until it is opened the opening of the mare.
E cum appar la excitura, e es tocada am la ma e es leon e molh, lahoras cove que tu secces aquela deves le cap de lu am spatum lat.	And when the excitation appears, and it is touched by the hand and is rough and moist, then it is necessary for you to dry that with a spatula of fat.
E cum la sania es evacuada, lahoras cove que tu pauses en la plagua una meca submersa en oli rozat o oli vert en le qual sia alcuna stiptisitat; e pausa la calca7 en la seccio en le preon de la mayre.	And when the discharge is evacuated, then it is necessary for you to pause in the wound a poultice submerged in red oil or green oil which has some styptic properties; and pause the pressure in the section of the pubic region of the mare.
E pause deforo la mayre e sobre le pentenilh lana munda submersa en aygua en la qual sian bulidas malvas.	And pause outside the mare and on the pubic mound a clean linen cloth submerged in water in which marigolds are steeped.
E aprop sia curada aprop dos dias am enguent le qual conveneys ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly be cured within two days with poultices that correspond to that until it is healed.
E alcunas veguadas es lavada la mayre e la plagua enayssi que es cristerisat am aygua e mel, e aprop am aygua en la qual es bulhida razit de liri o de aristologia longua, e aprop retorna al enguent.	And sometimes the mare and the wound are washed in this way that is anointed with water and honey, and accordingly with water in which rye or long-leafed Aristolochia has been steeped, and then returns to poultices.
E si la plagua es dedintz en la mayre ameguada, lahoras cove que tu sias prohibit de la curacio de lu am ferr, habantz cura aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio.	And if the wound is opened in the mare with pus, then it is necessary for you to be prohibited from the cure of him with iron, having cured that with water as we have said in the division.
Capitol .lxxv.	Chapter LXXV.
A ensenhar las matronas en qual manieyre les enbrios bius sian medicatz quan yeysso segon figura no-natural.	To teach midwives how to medicate abnormal births when they occur according to a non-natural figure.
Necessaria causa es que la matrona conogua en le comensament la figura del enfantament natural per senhals de lu, e es que quan tu vezas la femna expremar a las partidas dejos e desira odorar le ayre, e sobre aquo es enleujada per aquo que sobre ela es del part, e festina le eyssiment del enbrio, lahoras sapias que aquest part es segon figura natural, e es l’eyssiment de lu sobre le sieu cap, e la segondina am aquel o suspensa o pendent del ombelic.	A necessary cause is that the midwife should know at the beginning the figure of normal childbirth by its signs, and thus when you see the woman expelling at the parting points below and desires to smell the air, and on top of that she is relaxed because what comes out of her is from the part, and hastens the emergence of the fetus, then you should know that this part is according to a natural figure, and it is the emergence of the baby over its head, and the umbilical cord with that or suspended or hanging from the navel.
Donc cum tu vezes aquels senhals, lahoras cove que·l ventre de lu sia compremut per so que l’embrio deysenda leugerament quar quan deyssen sobre le sieu cap, deysen a lu la segondina, e es mondada de aquelas superfluitatz am bona mondificacio.	Therefore, as you see those signs, then it is necessary for the belly of him to be compressed so that the fetus descends slightly when it comes out over its head, and then the umbilical cord should be cut off from those superfluous parts with good cleansing.
Mays aquel que es otra aquest part es no-natural e no-lausable, quar quan le enbrio es eyssit sobre sos pes e·l cos de lu es eyssit devant le cap de lu e·ls pes de lu, e la ma de lu una, o al pe de lu .i., o es eyssit le cap de lu e la ma de lu, o al ventre de lu, e fort leu es convertit sobre le sieu col, e semblant de las figuras de lu no-lausablas.	But that which is another part is non-natural and not permissible, because when the fetus is emerged over its feet and the body of him is emerged before his head and his feet, and one hand or at the foot.1 or is emerged the head of him and one hand or at the belly of him, and very much it is converted over his neck, and similar to the figures of him that are not permissible.
Don necessaria causa es a la matrona que sia savia e subtil en totas aquelas causas, e que·s guarde de error e de decepcio.	Therefore, it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and subtle in all those causes, and to beware of error and deception.
E yeu so mostrant tota figura de aquelas, e qual engen es en aquelas per so que sia significat per aquo e sia stat sobre aquo.	And I show you the whole figure of those, and what engine is in them for so that it is meant by this and stands on top.
Quan le feyt es eyssit sobre le sieu cap per egrecio natural, e aquel es vehement sobre la femna e es fayt a lu part dificil, e vezes la vertut de lu ja debelitada, lahoras fay aquela sezer , o que las femnas tenguan lu, e evapora le conh de lu am fenugrec coyt e am olis humitz.	When the child is emerged over its head by natural excitement, and it is very vehement on the woman and is made to part difficultly, and sometimes the virtue of her is already debilitated, then make that person sit down, or what women have him, and evaporate the vulva with fennel juice and with warm oil.
E aprop entrometa la metrona entre les sieus ditz espatum petit e fenda am aquel la segondina, o secce aquela am la sua ungla entro que corro aquo que es en ela de humiditat.	And accordingly introduce the midwife between the said small spatula and the slit with that umbilical cord, or cut that off with her own nail until the flow of water is in her which is in her of humidity.
E preme le ventre de la femna entro que deyssenda le fet.	And press the woman's belly until it descends the child.
Mays si no deyssen, lahoras cove que la femna sia cristirizada de mucellage de ptilli e mucellage de fenugrec am cizami.	But if it does not descend, then it is necessary for the woman to be anointed with mullein and fenugreek juice mixed with camomile.
E aprop comanda a lu, aprop le cristeri, que sia compremuda e fay aquela stornudar am condisi; e te la boca de lu e·l nas de lu per huna hora, quar le fet sira foro-getat tantost.	And accordingly command him to her, and command the anointing, that it be compressed and make her yawn with conditions; and hold his mouth and nose for one hour, because the child will soon forget it.
E si las doas mas del fet so foro-getadas al comensament, lahoras cove que tu redusiscas aquelas am fecilitat petit a petit.	And if the two hands of the child are forgotten at the beginning, then it is necessary to reduce those with small ease gradually.
Mays si no obezeys al intrament, lahoras pausa la femna sobre una cezelha e leva les pes de lu sus, e aprop concuceys la cezelha sobre la terra; e la femna sia tenguda que no caia deves la concussio.	But if it does not obey the instrument, then pause the woman on a pillow and lift her feet up, and accordingly conceive the pillow on the earth; and the woman should be held so that she does not fall from the concussion.
E si las mas no son dedintz tornadas e morr le fet, lahoras inscideys aquelas e extratz le romament del fet o lia le cors a la ma de lu am drap e extratz aquel am equalitat, quar aquel sira foro-getat.	And if the hands are not returned and the child dies, then insert those and extract the remnant of the child or tie its body to the hand with cloth and extract that in equanimity, because it will soon be forgotten.
De eyssiment del embrio sobre les sieus pes.	On the Emergence of the Fetus over the Feet.
Quan le fet yeys sobre les sieus pes, lahoras cove que tu impelliscas aquels en sus, e aprop convertas le fet petit, e aprop que engualhes aquel, e aprop que prenguas un pe de lu e extendas aquels petit a petit.	When the child emerges over its feet, then it is necessary to push those into them, and accordingly transform the small child, and accordingly equalize that, and accordingly take one foot of him and stretch those little by little.
Mays cum son eyssit entro a las coyssas, lahoras tu comanda a lu que se exprema, e fay aquela extornudar am condizi, quar sira foro-getat si Deus lo vol.	But when they are emerged into the thighs, then it is necessary to command him to be expelled, and make her yawn with conditions, because it will soon be forgotten if God wills it.
E si no es foro-getat am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras tu retorna le fet petit a petit entro que pauses aquel segon figura natural, quar aquel sira lahoras foro-getat am leugier eyssiment.	And if it is not forgotten with what we have recounted, then it is necessary to return the small child gradually until he is paused according to a natural figure, because that will soon be forgotten with a lighter emergence.
E si es prohibit am tot aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras pren de musellage de altea e de goma dissolvuda, e percuteys tot en le mortier per bona percussio, e aprop linieys am aquo le conh de la femna, el pus bas del ventre de lu.	And if it is prohibited with all that we have recounted, then take mullein and dissolved gum, and beat everything together in the mortar for good beating, and accordingly line up with water the vulva of the woman, down below the belly.
E aprop fay aquela cezer en aygua tebeza, entro que consegua les ypocondias.	And accordingly make that person sit in warm water until she achieves relief from her hypochondria.
E cum vezes que las partidas dejos de lu so lenificadas, lahoras fay a lu subfumiguacio de mirta e sub-pausa aquela a lu.	And when the parts below of him are softened, then make to him a sub-fumigation of myrtle and sub-pause that to him.
E quan te la sub-fumiguacio per una hora, lahoras tu la fay sezer sobre una cezelha, e aprop fay aquela stornudar e extrenh la boca de lu, e levas de aquela, e prem la partida pus bassa del ventre de lu am leugiera compressio, quar le fet sira tantost foro-getat.	And when the sub-fumigation has been done for an hour, then make her sit down on a pillow, and accordingly make her yawn and stretch her mouth, and take that away from her, and press the lower part of the belly of her with light compression, because the child will soon be forgotten.
Eyssiment del fet sobre les sieus denols e las suas mas.	Emergence of the Child over its Fingernails and Hands.
Quan le fet eyssira segon aquesta forma, lahoras tu engenies en entrometen las suas mas petit a petit; e aprop la femna stia evessada sobre le sieu col, e les pes de lu pengo en jos, e aquelas sia jasent sobre le lieyt, e complegua las suas mas.	When the child emerges in this form, then you should gently push in his small hands little by little; and accordingly the woman should be laid down on her back, with her feet hanging down, and those [hands] should be lying on the light, and complete his hands.
E aprop prem sobre le ventre de lu petit a petit, e aprop extratz aquo que es dejos les pes de lu de las aurelhas entro que sia preparada en la partida pus dejos.	And accordingly press on the belly of her little by little, and accordingly extract out what is left from the feet up to the ears until it is prepared in the lowest part.
E si le fet no es fora-getat, lahoras pren les pes de lu e mau aquels am movement vehement, e aprop prem aquo que es sobre les ypocondres petit a petit entro que le fet puege a las partidas desus.	And if the child is not forgotten, then take his feet and move them vigorously with those, and accordingly press that which is on the hypochondria little by little until the child can reach the parts above.
E aprop entrometa las suas mas e engualhe le fet petit a petit, e comanda a la femna que se exprema entro que le fet sia foro-getat.	And accordingly enter his hands and equalize the child little by little, and command the woman to be expelled until the child is forgotten.
Eyssiment del fet latutidinalment pendent una de las suas mas.	Emergence of the Child Lateralistically Hanging from One of His Hands.
Sia engeniat en reduccio de la ma de lu, mays si no podes aquela reduzir, lahoras eleva la femna e fe aquela anar.	Be gentle in reducing the hand of him, but if you cannot reduce that, then lift up the woman and make her walk.
E si anar no pot, lahoras fay la jazer sobre le lieyt, e concuteys las coyssas de lu am concussio vehement, e aprop aministra liamentz les quals yeu e recomtatz de mucillages.	And if she cannot walk, then make her lie down on the bed, and conceive the thighs of him with strong concussion, and accordingly administer those remedies which we have recounted and recommended with mullein.
E si es vengut le enfantament, lahoras fay aquela sezer sobre cezelha, e aprop studia sobre la reduccio de la ma, e enguala le fet segon figura natural, e fay stornudar la femna e comanda a lu que comprema a si entro que sia foro-getat.	And if the childbirth is completed, then make her sit down on a pillow, and accordingly study the reduction of the hand, and equalize the child according to natural figure, and make the woman yawn and command him to compress himself until he is forgotten.
Eyssiment del fet sobre·l col expandudas las suas mas e la fassia de lu es al dos de la sua mayre.	Emergence of the Child with expanded hands and the flesh of him at the two sides of his right shoulder.
Cove que la matrona tengua la ma del fet e aprop revolva aquel petit a petit, e eque aquel am facilitat.	It is necessary for the midwife to have the hand of the child and accordingly turn that little by little, and equalize that with ease.
E cum es e quant so es engualhat, e lahoras pausa sobre le conh de lu aquo que havem recomtat de oli e de mucellages.	And when it is and what is equalized, then pause on the vulva of her with that which we have recounted, namely oil and mullein.
E aprop comandas a lu que·s maugua petit a petit, e quan auras feyt aquo, lahoras fay aquela cezer sobre una cezelha e comanda li que sia inclinada sobre le latz dreyt, e aprop comanda a lu que sia compremuda; e fay aquela stornudar am condizi.	And accordingly command him to yawn little by little, and when you have done that, then make her sit down on a pillow and command her to be inclined over the right side, and accordingly command him to be compressed; and make her yawn with conditions.
Exitus foetus praeparati super latus.	Exit of the prepared fetus onto the right side.
Quan deyssen a horrifici de la mayre segon aquesta manieyra, considera, e lahoras tu inscideys la segondina am la tua ungla entro que sia evacuada de la humiditat.	When it emerges in a horrible manner from the mare according to this method, take note, and then insert the umbilical cord with your own nail until it is evacuated of humidity.
E si le fet es suspendut sobre la cara e·l col de lu, lahoras tu inscideys aquela del embelic, per so que no sia retengut e mora.	And if the child is suspended over the face and neck of him, then insert that of the umbilical cord, in order that it may not be retained and die.
E aprop empelleys le fet a las partidas dedintz entro que pauses aquel segon que cove, e manda a la femna que comprema a si alcunas veguadas, e el sira fora-getat am eyssiment leugier, si Dieus o vol.	And accordingly push the child into the parts below until it is paused according to what is necessary, and command the woman to compress herself for some time, and if God wills it, the child will soon be forgotten with a lighter emergence.
Exitus geminorum aut foetuum multorum.	Exit of twins or multiple fetuses.
Sapias que gemels motas veguadas so natz, e alcunas vetz naysso tres o quatre , mays aquo es estranh e tart s’endeve; mays v so causas foro natura, e no vivo.	Know that sometimes twins are born, and some times three or four, but this is rare and not to be expected; however, there are causes natural, and not living.
E conte aquelas, ja sia que sian montiplicatz, una segondina, e son seperatz per ciphac, distingen aquels enter le liguament en l’ombilic de cascun de aquels E alcunas veguadas so foro-getatz ayssi cum es un fet per eyssiment natural leugier, e so eysitz alcunas veguadas per eyssiment no-lausabla ayssi cum havem recomtat.	And among those, whether they are multiple or single, one umbilical cord, and they are separated by ciphac, distinguish them from the ligament in the navel of each of those And some times they are forgotten thus as one fetus for natural emergence lighter, and some times they are born with non-natural emergence thus as we have recounted.
E si son dificils alcus de lor deves le enfantament e perveno ad aquo que havem dit de las figuras no-naturals, lahoras tu cura aquels ayssi cum havem recontat.	And if some of them are difficult to deliver and proceed to what we have said about non-natural figures, then you should cure those as we have recounted.
E si’ la matrona subtil e fassa aquo que fa am facilitat e subtilitat, e am tarditat, e sia ingeniat segon tota figura segon que es a lu preparat de l’engen amenant a salut.	And if the midwife is subtle and does what she does with ease and subtlety, and in delay, and is skilled according to all figures as it is prepared by nature leading to salvation.
Rememoratio eius quod formatur in matrice ex embrionibus et Abortiuntur.	Recollection of what is formed in the womb from embryos and Aborted.
Alcunas veguadas son formatz en la mayre un, e dos, e tres, e quatre, e v, e vi, e vii, e mays x, e ja es deves mi verificat que una femna abortem ne getet vi, e una autra x totz formatz, la qual causa fo fayta per mensuracio dels glorios savis.	Some weeks are formed in one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, and more than ten days; and it is necessary for me to verify that a woman aborts at the seventh day, and another at the tenth day, which was caused by measurement of the glorious sages.
E tot aysso cove que sia en la sciencia de la matrona quar fort leu ad aquela parve semblant de aquo, e donc opause se ad aquo am so que cove.	And all this must be in the science of the midwife because it is a little similar to what has been said, and therefore pause there as much as is necessary.
Capitol .lxxvi.	Chapter LXXVI.
De extraccio del fet quan es mort.	On the Extraction of the Fetus when it is Dead.
Quan tu curas le fet mort am aquo que havem dit en la divisio de la medicacio e no es defora eyssit, e tu yest forsat usar de opperacio am ma, lahoras cove que consideras si la femna es de sana vertut e no es am alcu dels accidentz per les quals sobre ela es temuda perdicio.	When you treat the dead fetus with what we have said in the division of medicine and it is not yet emerged, and you are forced to use operation by hand, then it is necessary that you consider whether the woman has a healthy virtue and is not afflicted with any of the accidents by which peril is feared for her.
Lahoras cove que la femna sia envessada sobre le lieyt sobre le sieu dos, e sia le cap de lu enclinat enjos e las coyssas de lu sian elevadas.	Then it is necessary that the woman be laid down on her back over the bed, and her head inclined downwards, and her thighs elevated.
E·l ministre tengua aquela de doas partz o sia liada en le lieyt per so que·l cos de lu no se extenda deves la extraccio del fet.	And the minister should hold her in two parts or be tied down on the bed for that reason, so that the body of her does not extend during the extraction of the fetus.
E aprop tu humecta la boca de la mayre de lu am olis humitz e am mucellage de altea e de fenugrec e de semensa de li.	And accordingly moisten the mouth of the mare with warm oil, and mullein, and fenugreek, and sesame seed.
E aprop unte la matrona la sua ma am aquels olis e mucellages, e aprop entrometa la sua ma am fecilitat en la mayre, e aprop cerque am la ma loc en le qual fique les uncis en le fet.	And accordingly the midwife should bring her hand with those oils and mullein, and accordingly enter her hand with ease into the mare, and accordingly seek out the exact location where the fingers will be placed on the fetus.
E locs convenient en aquo: adonc tu considera si le fet es preparat que deysenda sobre le sieu cap, e lahoras tu fique les uncis en les huels de lu, o en le col, o en la boca, o en le palat, o dejos la barba, o en la furcula de lu, o en les locs propdas de las costas, o dejos les ypocondres.	And finding the convenient location: then you should consider if the fetus is prepared to emerge on its head, and accordingly place your fingers in the following locations: on the ears of him, or on the neck, or in the mouth, or on the palate, or below the beard, or in the furcula of him, or in the places proper to the ribs, or below the hypochondria.
Mays si le deysendiment es sobre les pes de lu, lahoras en le pentenilh, o en le mieg de las costas.	But if the emergence is on the feet of him, then in the pentalion or in the middle of the ribs.
E cove que tengua le unci am la ma dreyta, e pausa la curvitat de lu en aquel loc le qual es entre les ditz de la ma senestra, e entrometa la ma am facilitat e fique le unci en alcu de aquels locs les quals havem ditz, entro que pervengua a la causa boyda.	And it is necessary to have the fingers of the right hand and pause the curvature of him at that location which is between the digits of the left hand, and enter the hand with ease and place the fingers in one of those locations which we have said, until you reach the cause of the boyd.
E aprop pause e fique en la apposicio de lu un autre unci, o le tertz si es necessitat, per so que sia atraccio engual, e no sia extencio segon la sua rectetut tant solament.	And accordingly pause and place another finger, or the third if necessary, in the opposition of him, to attract equalization, and not be extended according to his straightness only.
Ans sia maugut a tota partida, per so que l’eyssiment de lu sia alleujat ayssi cum es fayt en dent deves la eradicacio de lu.	And it will be good for the whole part, for that reason the emergence of him will be alleviated thus as is done in tooth extraction for the eradication of him.
E cove en lu aquo que es entre lor que la extencio sia mollificada; e si alcuna partida de lu es retenguda, lahoras cove que la matrona unte alcus sieus ditz am oli e entrometa aquels espertament e revolva am aquels aquo que es retengut.	And it is necessary in him that which is between them that the extension be softened; and if some part of him is retained, then the midwife should bring some of his fingers with oil and enter those expertly and turn with water what is retained.
Donc si la partida del fet es fora-getada, lahoras les uncis sian permudatz entra loc le qual sia pus aut; e fay aysso entro que tot le fet sia fora-getat.	Therefore, if the part of the fetus is forgotten, then the fingers should be pushed forward until the location where it is more above; and make so that all the fetus is forgotten.
Mays si la ma es eyssida denant l’autra, e no es possible reduzir aquela per la coartacio de lu, lahoras cove que drap sia envolopat sobre aquela; e aprop extratz aquela entro que tota sia fora-getada, e inscideys aquela o en la junctura de la ma o en le coyde.	But if the hand is emerged before the other, and it is not possible to reduce that by the contraction of him, then it is necessary that a cloth be wrapped around it; and accordingly extract that until all is forgotten, and insert it either in the joint of the hand or in the wrist.
E ayssi cove que fassas en l’autra ma e en les dos pes.	And so it is necessary to do the same with the other hand and both feet.
Mays si le cap del fet es gran, o accideys a lu coartacio en le eyssiment, o es en le cap de lu aygua ajustada, lahoras cove que entrometa entre les ditz espatum spinos e fenda le cap e extragua la aygua, o que discroba aquel am un instrument le qual es nompnat “alundat”, la forma del qual vindra am las formas dels autres instruments en le capitol le qual es aprop aquest.	But if the head of the fetus is large, or if there is contraction in the emergence, or if water is adjusted in the head of him, then it is necessary that you insert between the digits a spatula with spines and cut off the head and extract the water, or use an instrument which is called "alundat", whose form will come from the forms of other instruments in the chapter which is appropriate to this.
E semblantment fassa si·l fet es de gran cap per natura: e lahoras cove que inscida aquel am algematu, o que prengua aquel am alunda ayssi cum havem dit; e aprop extra les osses am les forceps.	And similarly do if the fetus has a large head by nature: and it is necessary that you insert it with an algemate, or take it with an alundat as we have said; and accordingly extract the bones with forceps.
E si le cap es eyssit e es coartat deves la furcula, lahoras sia fendut entro que la humiditat la qual es en le pietz sia efunduda.	And if the head is emerged and contracted at the furcula, then it should be cut open until the humidity which is in the pit is poured out.
Mays si no es complicat, ni obezeys a eyssiment, lahoras tu inscideys le cap tantost segon que a tu sira possible.	But if it is not complicated, nor obedient to emergence, then you should insert the head as soon as possible according to what seems best to you.
E si le dejos del ventre es apostemat o es en lu ydropici, lahoras cove que tu perfores aquel entro que corro la humiditat que es en lu.	And if the afterbirth of the belly is apoplectic or is in him with dropsy, then it is necessary that you perforate that until the humidity which is in him flows out.
Mays si le fet es sobre les sieus pes, lahoras la atraccio de lu es leugiera e la direccio de lu a la boca de la mayre es leugiera.	But if the fetus is on its feet, then the attraction of him is slight and the direction of him to the mouth of the mare is slight.
Mays si es coartat deves le ventre e·l pietz, lahoras cove que tu extraguas aquel am drap le qual auras envolopat sobre la tua ma, e que fendes le ventre e·l pietz entro que corra aquo que es en aquels.	But if it is contracted in the belly and pit, then it is necessary that you extract that with cloth which you will wrap around your hand, and cut open the belly and pit until the water that is in them runs out.
Mays si les autres membres so ostatz e torna le cap, lahoras la metrona entrometa la ma senestra; mays si la boca de la mayre es huberta, lahoras intrometa la ma en le preon de layre, e cerque am aquela le cap, e atira aquel am les ditz entro a la boca de la mayre, e aprop entrometa en lu un unci, o dos uncis, e atire lu am aquels.	But if the other members are stiff and turn back to the head, then put your right hand into it; but if the mouth of the mare is swollen, then insert your left hand into the harp and seek out that head, and attract it with the fingers until it enters the mouth of the mare, and accordingly enter one finger or two fingers into him and draw him with those.
E si la boca de la mayre es coartada per apostema caut le qual accideys a l’u, lahoras cove que no sia trebelhat sobre lu; abantz cove lahoras aministrar efusio de causas humidas grassas.	And if the mouth of the mare is contracted by apoplectic catarrh which happens to him, then it is necessary that you do not trouble him with this; but rather administer effusion of humid and fatty causes.
E aministre emplastres; e segua le pacient en ayguas que mollifican e humectan.	And administer poultices; and follow the patient in waters that soften and moisten.
E si le fet es sobre le sieu costat, lahoras si possible es, sia agulat: e sia aministrat aquo que havem dit en le fet viu.	And if the fetus is on its side, then if possible, it should be punctured: and administer water as we have said in the living fetus.
E si aquo no es possible, lahoras sia inscidit en pessas, e sia extrayt.	And if this is not possible, then it should be inserted into pessaries, and extracted.
E cove que non layssas alcuna causa dedintz de la segondina.	And it is necessary that you do not leave any cause behind the umbilical cord.
E cum tu auras complida tota la tua opperacio, lahoras aministra aquo que havem dit de la curacio en les apostemas cautz les quals accideysso de la mayre.	And when you have completed all your operation, then administer water as we have said for the cure of apoplectic catarrh which happens to the mare.
E si accideys flux de sanc, lahoras deyssendas en ayguas stipticas e aministra l’autra curacio.	And if bleeding occurs, then administer in aqueous stiptics and give the other cure.
E yeu ja e vist una femna en le ventre de la qual era fet mort, e aprop sobre aquel foc autra veguada emprenhada, e aprop foc mort es le fet autre.	And you have already seen a woman in whose womb was a dead fetus, and accordingly on that spot another embryo conceived, and accordingly the dead fetus is another.
Accidit al u aprop lonc temps apostema en le sieu embelic; e inflat es entro que foc ubert, e comensec a getar brac.	It happened to him, accordingly, after a long time an apoplectic catarrh in his navel; and it swelled until a foul odor began to emit.
E yeu fu appelhat a la cura de lu, e medicat a lu per lonc temps, e la plagua no es consolidada.	And you were called upon to cure him, and treated him for a long time, and the wound was not consolidated.
Adonc yeu pausegui sobre lu de alscunas causas emplastra de forta atraccio, e eyssic de lu un os, e aprop passero alcus jorns, e eyssic un autre os; e yeu fu trop meravilhat, cum en le ventre no sia os.	Then you applied some emplasters of strong attraction to him, and extracted from him one bone, and accordingly passed several days, and extracted another bone; and I was too astonished, as in the womb there is no bone.
E adonc yeu cogitegui que eran dels osses del fet mort.	And then you thought that they were the bones of the dead fetus.
Donc yeu enguisigui la plagua, e extrayssi de lu motz osses , la femna existent en las sieuas milhos disposicios, e ja visquec en tal manieyra per lonc temps, correc de lu un petit de brac.	So you cleansed the wound, and extracted many bones from him, the woman existing in her own miserable condition, and already living in such a way for a long time, cried out with a little breast.
E yeu no afermegui asso esser stranh, sino quar en aquo es sciensa e ajutori ad aquo que le metge artifec am la ma per curacio aministra.	And I did not consider it strange, but rather because in that is science and aid to what the physician has in his hand to administer cure.
De las formas dels instrumentz que so necessaris a extrayre le fet.	Of the forms of instruments that are necessary to extract the fetus.
Forma de vertitge am la qual es uberta la mayre:	Form of vertebrae with which the mare is opened:
Aquesta es la forma de strenhedor en le qual so engualhatz les libres, al qual engualhament sian dos virtitges en doas extremitatz de dos futz.	This is the form of strengthener in which are equated the free ones, to which equating are two vertebrae at the two extremities of two feet.
May empero aquesta virtitge cove que sia pus subtil de strictori, e sia fayt o de eba o de fust de boys.	However, this vertebra must be more subtle than the strictor, and be made of ebony or boxwood.
E sia la latitut de quascun fust quays dos ditz e le marge de quascu amdos quays un dit, e la longitut de quascu es un palm e mig; e en le mieg loc de dos fustz so dos ajustaments de aquel meteys fustz les quals ja son fermatz, dels quals la longitut es la maytat de un palm e un pauc mes, e la latitut de quascu es quay dos ditz, o un pauc mes.	And the latitude of each foot is about two digits and the margin of each about one digit, and the length of each is one palm and a half; and in the middle part of the two feet are two adjustments of those fixed feet, which are already secured, of which the length is the majority of one palm and a little more, and the latitude of each is about two digits, or a little more.
E aquestz dos additamentz sian entromeses en la boca de la mayre per que sia uberta am aquels quan tu revolves las doas prescriptas virtigges.	And these two adjustments are inserted in the mouth of the mare so that it is opened with them when you revolve the two prescribed vertebrae.
Forma autra semblant de aquela pus subtil e pus leugiera:	Another form similar to that, more subtle and lighter:
Sia fayta de fustz de eba o de boys segon la semblansa de forceps.	Be made of ebony or boxwood, according to the shape of forceps.
Mays empero en la extremitat de lu so dos additament ayssi cum vezes, e la longitut de aquels additament es quays un palm, e la latitut de quascu es dos ditz.	However, at the end of it there are two adjustments like those times, and the length of these adjustments is about one palm, and the latitude of each is two digits.
E cum tu vols am aquels ubrir la mayre, lahoras tu fay cezer la femna sobre le lieyt les pes pendentz, ubert aquo que es entre las coyssas de lu.	And when you want to open the mare with those, then you should cause the woman to sit on a bed with her feet hanging down, opening what is between her thighs.
E aprop obre la tua ma am le instrument ayssi cum fas am forfexs engualment segon la quantitat que vols de la aprecio de la boca de la mayre entro que la metrona fassa so que vols.
