And accordingly, over your hand with the instrument as you make it for forceps equalizing according to the quantity you want of the appreciation of the mouth of the mare until she makes what you want.
La forma de vertitge la qual diysero les antics:	The form of vertebrae which was said by the ancients:
Forma de impellent am le qual es empellit le fet:	Form of impulse by which the fetus is impelled:
Forma de amisidat2 am le qual es conterit le cap gran	Form of accommodation by which the great head is contained:
E es asemblat a forceps al qual so dentz en la extremitat, ayssi cum vezes, e alcunas veguadas es fayt lonc ayssi cum forceps segon aquesta forma, ayssi cum vezes, al qual so dentz ayssi cum dentz de ressegua am le qual es inscidit e conterit.	And it is assembled to forceps which has teeth at the end, just like times, and some times it is made long just like forceps according to this form, just like times, with teeth just like teeth of a reed into which it is inserted and contained.
Forma de amesidat pauc:	Form of accommodation few:
Forma de unci havent una spina:	Form of finger having one spine:
Forma de unci havent doas spinas:	Form of finger having two spines:
Forma de forceps a la qual so dentz de cerra am le qual le cap del fet sia conterit:	Form of forceps by which the teeth of a comb are contained, into which the head of the fetus is inserted.
Forma de spatum havent dos extremitatz am le qual le cap es abscindit:	Form of spatula having two extremities at which the head is cut off:
Forma de dos espatums latz:	Form of two broad spatulas:
Totz aquels instrumentz so excersitatz, e quan mes so multiplicadas las specias de aquel e so preparadas deves le artifexs, quant es pus leugier a la sua opperacio e pus aut deves les homes per la sua quantitat.	All those instruments are exercised, and when more species of that are multiplied and prepared by the artisans, as it is easier to their operation and more necessary for men in proportion.
E no obres de aquels instrumentz ja sia qua sia deves tu aparalhat, quar la necessitat de aquels no es excusabla.	And do not neglect those instruments however small they may seem to you, because the necessity of them is inexcusable.
De extraccio de la segondina.	Of extraction of the umbilical cord.
Quan la segondina es retenguda deves le enfantament, lahoras cove que tu comandes a la malautae que retengua le sieu ale, e aprop fay aquela stornudar am condizi, e strenh la tua ma sobre la boca de lu e sobre las nars de lu, e si per aysso es defora eyssit, bo es.	When the umbilical cord is retained during childbirth, then it is necessary that you order the patient to retain her breath, and accordingly make her cough with conditions, and strengthen your hand over her mouth and nostrils, and if by this means it is extracted, well it is.
E sino, lahoras tu pren una ola e perfora en la cuberta un trauc e pausa en aquela erbas ubrent la boca de la mayre, ayssi cum calament e ruda e anet e camamilla e scicados arabic e cassia lignea e santaurea.	And if not, then take a cloth and pierce it in the covering of a hole, and pause in that herb which is used to open the mouth of the mare, such as calamus and rue and anise and chamomile and Arab spices and cassia lignea and St. Andrew's.
Totas aquestas erbas o alcunas de lor sian submersas en aygua en la ola, e pausa aquela sobre le foc.	All these herbs or some of them are submerged in water in the cloth, and pause it over the fire.
E aprop pausa una canula de canaviera en la boca de la mayre, e tengua aquela entro que la evapor vengua a la concavitat de la mayre.	And accordingly place a reed cane in the mouth of the mare, and keep it until the vapor comes to the concavity of the mare.
E aprop fay aquela stornudar ayssi cum havem dit, e la segondina sira fora-getada am velocitat.	And accordingly make her cough just as we have said, and the umbilical cord is expelled quickly.
Mays si roman aprop aquesta curacio e no es eyssida, lahoras tu comanda a la matrona que submerge la sua ma sinistra en oli sizami o en micellage de altea, e aprop entrometa aquela en le conh e queresca am aquela la segondina, e cum aquela auras trobada, lahoras pren la e exten aquela pauc a pauc Mays si es annexsa en le preon de la mayre, lahoras entrometa la sua ma segon que havem recomtat, e quan aura trobat la segondina, extragua aquela petit a petit segon rectetut per so que la mayre no caja deves la atraccio vehement.	But if this cure does not work and the umbilical cord is still retained, then you should order the midwife to submerge her left hand in samian oil or in a mixture of altaic herbs, and accordingly insert it into the confluence and seek out the umbilical cord, and when you have found it, take it and stretch it out gradually. But if it is annexed in the womb of the mare, then insert your hand according to what we have recommended, and when you have found the umbilical cord, extract it little by little according to rectitude, so that the mare does not faint from the vehement attraction.
Abantz cove que sia permudada als costatz dreyt e sinestre am facilitat.	But first, it is necessary to be made pliable on both right and left sides with ease.
E aprop sia ajustat en la quantitat de atraccio, quar ela obedira e evasira de adhirencia.	And accordingly, it should be adjusted in the quantity of attraction, because it will obey and escape from adherence.
E si la boca de la mayre es coartada, nos ja havem recomtat la curacio am sturnutacio e am medicacio de la ola am erbas.	And if the mouth of the mare is contracted, we have already recommended the cure by coughing and administering medicine with the cloth and herbs.
Mays si no es fora-getada am totas las causas las quals havem recomtadas, lahoras guarda te que no fetigues sobre aquela en iteracio de abstracio, mays empero cove que aquo que es eyssit de lu a la boca de la mayre lies a la coyssa de la femna, e aprop cristeriza aquela am enguent e tetrafarmacon; quar aquel fara poyrir aquela aprop alcus dias e sira dissolvuda e sira fora-getada.	But if it is not expelled with all the causes which we have recommended, then beware that you do not force anything over there in iteration of abstraction, but rather, it is necessary that what has emerged from him to the mouth of the mare lies at the edge of the woman's bed, and accordingly, plasterize it with a poultice and tetra-pharmacopeia; because that will make it rot away within a few days and be dissolved and expelled.
Mays quan se poyreys, es de lu elevada mala audor al cap, e al estomac, e aquo ledeys la malauta; e adonc cove que sian aministradas sub-fumiguacios e convenientz ad aquo.	But when it rots, it is elevated to a bad authority on the head and stomach, and accordingly leads the patient astray; and then it is necessary that sub-fumigations and conveniences be administered to him.
Mays alcus dels Antics ja so esproatz sub-fumigacio de nazitort e de figuas seccas.	But some of the Ancients have already experimented with sub-fumigation using nitre and dried figs.
Forma de instrument am le qual la femna es sub-fumiguada deves la retentio de mestruas e de la segondina:	Form of instrument by which the woman is sub-fumigated for retention of menstruation and umbilical cord:
Sia fayta de veyre o de eram.	Be made of bay or earthenware.
E sia pausada la extremitat subtil en le conh e la extremitat ampla sobre le foc, e la sub-fumiguacio sia pausada sobre las brazas del foc.	And be placed the slender extremity in the cleft and the broad extremity over the fire, and the sub-fumigation be placed on the arms of the fire.
E tengua aquela entro que sia consumida aquela sub-fumiguacio e itera·n autra.	And keep that until the sub-fumigation is consumed and then iterate another.
De curacio del cul del enfant no-perforat.	Of cure for the child's unperforated anus.
Motz enfantz naysso e les culs de lu no so perforatz, les quals ya ciphac subtil e opilat.	Many children are born without anuses, those which have a subtle and opaque covering.
Adonc cove a la matrona que perfore am le sieu dit aquel ciphac; e sino, perfora aquel am spatum agut, e guarda se que no toque le lacert.	Then it is necessary for the midwife to pierce that subtle covering with her finger; and if not, then pierce it with a sharp spatula, and be careful not to touch the lacet.
E aprop pause sobre aquel lana enfusa en vi e oli; e aprop cura aquel am enguent entro que sia senat.	And accordingly, pause over that with wool infused in vinegar and oil; and accordingly, cure it with a poultice until it is settled.
Mays si temes que sia opilat, lahoras pausa en le trauc una canula per motz dias, e osta la quan le enfant voldra degerir.	But if you fear that it may be obstructed, then pause in the hole a reed cane for many days, and stop when the child will desire to relieve itself.
E ja accideys oppilacio del cul per consolidacio de plagua o de apostema; adonc cove que aquela consolidacio sia inscidida, e aprop sia curada am aquo que avem dit de la curacio e del plom.	And if there is obstruction of the anus due to consolidation of wound or apoplectic catarrh; then it is necessary that this consolidation be incised, and accordingly be cured with the water we have said for the cure and with lead.
De curacio de las fistulas que endeveno dejos.	Of cure for the fistulae which are left behind.
Las fistulas que endeveno en la partida dejos pus bassa so nodacio e grossetut las quals endeveno prop del cul defora o en l’espazi de la una partida.	The fistulae which are left behind in the departure, and which are lower than the navel and thicker on the one side or in the space of the one part, near the anus.
E es una fistula o motas.	And it is a single fistula or several.
E cum aquela nodacio es antiquada e corr de la humiditat aygosa blanca o poyridura subtil, e alcunas veguadas so de aquestas fistulas alcunas penetrantz.	And when that nodule is old and flows with white or yellowish liquid, or subtle putridation, and sometimes some of these fistulae are penetrating.
E aquelas penetrantz so conogudas per aquo que es eyssit de aquelas per la egressio e per ventosetat; e alcunas vetz use le malaute de egressio, e fort leu es eyssit de aquelas verm.	And those that are penetrating are known by what comes out of them through egression and ventosity; and sometimes the patient uses the evacuation of egression, and very little comes out of those worms.
E so de aquelas fistulas alcunas veguadas en l’espazi penetrantz entro a la vesica, e entro al meat de la vergua; e so de aquelas penetrantz entro la junctura de la coyssa e entro al notz de la coeta.	And some of those fistulae occasionally penetrate into the bladder and into the urethra of the penis; and some of those penetrating into the junction of the pelvis and into the notch of the coccyx.
E aquo en que es conoguda fistula penetrant entro al cul e no-penetrant, es que tu metas le tieu dit endic en le cul, e entrometas tenta subtil de eram o de ferr en la fistula quan no y es turtuositat.	And the way to know if a penetrating fistula is not penetrating is that you put your finger into the anus and then insert a subtle probe of earthenware or iron into the fistula when there is no resistance.
Mays si en aquela es turtuositat, lahoras entromet en aquela tenta subtil de plom o de pels de caval entro que tu sentas la tenta o le pel en le tieu dit.	But if there is resistance in that, then insert into it a subtle probe of lead or horsehair until you feel the probe or hair in your finger.
E si no sentas aquela de tot ni no procezeys del trauc alcuna causa de egestio ni verm ni ventositat, ayssi cum havem dit, lahoras sapias que es no-penetrant, e lahoras coyta te a la curacio.	And if you do not feel it at all or there is no discharge of any kind, whether worms or wind, as we have said, then know that it is non-penetrating, and accordingly apply the cure.
E quan la fistula es penetrant entro a la vesica o entro al meat de la vergua, lahoras la significacio de lu es eyssiment de urina de aquela e prohibicio de lu ad aysso que·l loc am medicina sia consolidat.	And when the fistula is penetrating into the bladder or urethra of the penis, then the significance of it is that urine will come out of that and prohibition of it at this point so that the place with medicine may be consolidated.
Mays si es penetrant entro la junctura de la coyssa o entro al os e envencio de dolor en le circuit, lahoras senhal de lu es que la tenta perve entro aqui si en lu no es turtuositat entro al os, e envencio de dolor en le circuit de la partida; e que de lu yeys poyredura tostemps; e que no val en aquela medicacio, ni es consolidada am enguent.	But if it is penetrating into the junction of the pelvis or bone and causing pain in the circulation, then the sign of it is that the probe will go in here if there is no resistance to the bone, and causing pain in the circulation of the departure; and that from it always putridation appears; and that no remedy is valid in that, nor is it consolidated with a poultice.
E en totas aquelas fistulas penetrant no es curacio de tot, e la curacio de aquelas es trebalh e vanetat dels folyls metges sobre·l qual so fermatz.	And in all those penetrating fistulae there is no complete cure, and the cure of those is tedious and futile labor on the part of foolish doctors who are fixed.
Mays en aquela que no es penetrant e no antiqua, sanacio am ferr es sperada segon que yeu a tu recomtare, e aquo que ja yeu e proat.	But in that which is not penetrating and not old, healing with iron is expected according to what you have recommended, and what you have already proved.
E es que le malaute jagua entre las tuas mas sobre le sieu dos e eleva las cambas de lu entro sus, las coyssas sian enclinadas al ventre de lu, e aprop entromet tenta de plom, o de eram si es en la fistula turtuositat, entro que sapias le loc on perve la tenta.	And it is that the patient lies between two cushions over his back and elevates his legs up to them, so that the pelvis are inclined towards the belly of him, and accordingly insert a probe of lead or earthenware into the fistula if there is resistance, until you know the place where the probe will go in.
E si aquela sent le malaute entorn le cuol, lahora cove que tu entrometas le tieu dit endic en le cuol.	And if that makes the patient feel a sensation around the anus, then it is necessary that you put your finger into the anus.
E si sentas en le tieu dit la tenta ja per si meteyssa descuberta penetrar, otra aquo que sentas entre le tieu dit e aquela siphac o carn, lahoras sapias certanament que aquela es penetrant; e adonc no trebalhes en aquela, quar no es en aquela sanacio, ayssi cum havem dit.	And if you feel with your finger that the probe has already gone in and is penetrating, or if you feel between your finger and that siphac or flesh, then you will certainly know that it is penetrating; and accordingly do not trouble yourself with it, as we have said.
Mays empero diyssero alcus que es sana en alcus homes tart.	But yet some say that it cures in some people at times.
E de la medicacio per la qual es sperat juvament en lu es que tu ignes cauteri subtil segon le ample de la fistula, ayssi cum es precedit, e intrometas aquel ignit en la fistula entro que pervengua entorn le cuol; e aprop itera aquel doas o tres vetz entro que sapias que ja son adhustas totas aquelas carns ajustadas fistuladas que so semblantz a cana de pluma de ausel.	And of the medicine by which one hopes for improvement in that is that you apply a subtle cauterizing fire according to the size of the fistula, as has been previously said, and insert that ignited into the fistula until it reaches around the anus; and accordingly repeat that two or three times until you know that all those adjusted fleshy tissues that are similar to the quill of an eagle have become united.
E aprop cura aquela am calguas envolopadas en boder entro que en yescan totas aquelas carns que so adhustas, e aprop cura aquela am medicinas la carn engendrantz e consolidantz, e si es sanada, bo es; e sino, lahoras no es sana en degun temps per autra curacio.	And accordingly cure that with wrapped calkins in parchment until all those adjusted fleshy tissues are united, and accordingly cure that with medicines generating and consolidating flesh, and if it is healed, well it is; and otherwise, then it is not healed at any time by other cures.
E si la tenta intra, e no penetra entro·l tieu dit le qual es en le cul, e entre aquel e la tenta que es velament spes de carn o de ciphac, e vezes la fistula en aquo que siec la superficia de la codena, lahoras secca la codena del comensament de la fistula, e tu ve seccan am la tenta, e sia en la fistula entro que la seccio pervengua al loc en le qual perve la extremitat de la tenta, e per la tenta es liberat e catz.	And if the probe goes in and does not penetrate into the anus which is in the rectum, and between that and the probe which is a velament of flesh or nodule, and sometimes the fistula opens up on the surface of the codena, then dry out the codena from the beginning of the fistula, and you will see it drying with the probe, and be in the fistula until the drying reaches the location where the extremity of the probe goes in, and by the probe is liberated and freed.
E aprop mundifiqua aquelas carns fistuladas las quals so asembladas a canula de pena de ausel e no romangua de aquelas alcuna causa.	And accordingly, purify those fleshy tissues which are assembled like the quill of an eagle and do not remain for any reason.
Mays si flux de sanc vezes que vengua entre tu e la tua opperacio quan ensideysses aquelas carns, lahoras le milh que sia e del pus leugier instrument es cauterizar am foc o am medicina acuta, quar cauteri am foc ajusta bonas doas habitutz: so es adhustio de aquelas carns ajustadas, e abscizio del sanc exseccacio de las humiditatz.	But if the flow of blood comes and goes between you and your operation when you are purifying those fleshy tissues, then use the remedy that is easiest to apply with the least effort, which is cauterization with fire or sharp medicine, for cauterization with fire adjusts two good habits: so it adjusts the adjusted fleshy tissues, and abscizes the blood by excessive humidity.
E aprop cura aquela am calguas envolopadas en boder o en caus trissat entro que·l loc geta brac, e aprop lahoras cura la plagua am enguentz carn dura engendran e consolidan.	And accordingly cure that with wrapped calkins in parchment or in threefold cloth until the wound gets braised, and accordingly cure the wound with poultices of hard flesh that generate and consolidate.
E so medicinas en las quals so stipticitat e exseccio; quan lahoras es restaurada ja es sanada e no temes iteracio.	And such medicines in which there is astringency and excess; when that is restored it is healed and you do not fear relapse.
Mays si la fistula ja perve entro al preon del cul e es elonguada de lu superficia del cos, lahoras entromet le tieu dit en le cul e inquireys am aquel.	But if the fistula has already gone into the anus and is elongated from the surface of the body, then insert your finger into the anus and inquire about it.
E donc si centes la tenta e entre tu e ela es velament de ciphac o de carn, e es propda a la penetracio, lahora no es operacio en lu sino segon via di fiducia e de speransa.	And therefore if you feel the probe and it is between you and her a velament of nodule or flesh, and is inclined towards penetration, then there is no operation in that but according to the way of faith and hope.
La qual causa es aministrar en lu una de tres manieyras: o que cauterize aquela ayssi cum havem dit; o que secces aquela entro que consieguas la conquavitat de lu per que sia a tu possible entrometre las qualcas e la curacio propdana; e no procesiscas mot am seccio per so que no inscidas le lacert contenent le cuol, e que accidisque sobre le malaute eyssiment de la egistio ses voluntat; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que havem dit quar fort leu sira sanat; o que elongues aquel velament e mondes aquel pus que seccas aquel entro prop le cul, ayssi cum havem dit, o am tenta o am autre instrument de aguda extremitat, e aprop mondifique aquelas carns fistuladas las quals so en la seccio entro la on podes am percrustacio; e aprop esforsa te a far la restauracio de tota la plagua am seccio, e si le orrifici pus desus no es consolidat, e romangua la fistula uberta en la partida del cul, e sira pus leugier per le malaute.	Which cause is to be administered in that place by one of three ways: either to cauterize it as we have said; or to dry out that part until you achieve the conquest of it so that it becomes possible for you to insert some and the natural cure is achieved; and do not proceed with any drying out because you will not inscribe the lacert containing the anus, and it will occur over the patient's consent; and accordingly cure that with water as we have said, which will be quite healthy; or elongate that velament and dry out that part up to the prop of the anus, as we have said, or with a probe or another instrument of sharp extremity, and accordingly purify those fleshy tissues that are in the section until you can make an incision; and accordingly strive to restore all the wound with drying out, and if the opening above is not consolidated, and the fistula remains open on the side of the anus, and it will be easier for the patient.
E alscunas veguadas la fistula es finida segon aquesta manieyra: es quan tu entrometas la tenta en la fistula, e es en le latz del cul entorn la superficia del cos am la codena e en le marge del cul, lahoras pren tenta de perforada extremitat, que es ayssi cum agulha de preparantz les coers segon aquesta forma:	And in some cases the fistula is closed by this method: when you insert the probe into the fistula, and it is in the latz of the anus around the surface of the body with the codena and on the margin of the anus, then take hold of a perforated extremity, which is like an awl that prepares the skin according to this form:
e entromet en aquela fiel envolopat de v fiels o entorn aquels; e aprop entromet tenta am fiel en la fistula entro que consiegua la conquavitat de lu.	and insert it into that faithful wrapping of vein or around those; and accordingly insert the probe with faith in the fistula until you achieve the conquest of it.
Mays si es penetrant en le marge del cul prop dedintz, lahoras tu extratz le fiel de aquel trauc ayssi que tu intrometas le tieu dit en le cul; e extraguas la extremitat del fiel e ajustes las duas extremitatz essemps, e estrenh cascuna, e leyssa aquo per un dia o per dos, e quan mays inscideys le fiel en la carn, estrenh be aquel entro que aquelas carns sian inscididas las quals so entre doas extremitatz del fiel e que cajan.	But if it is penetrating into the margin of the anus proper to the inside, then you take out the vein from that hole as if you insert your finger into the anus; and pull out the extremity of the vein and adjust the two extremities together, and strengthen each one, and leave water for a day or two, and when more you insert the vein into the flesh, strengthen it until those fleshy tissues are inserted between the two extremities of the vein which fall.
E aprop cura la plagua entro que sia consolidada e sanada.	And accordingly cure the wound so that it is consolidated and healed.
Mays si le orrifici de la fistula no es penetrant, lahoras fay aquel penetrar, en qualque manieyre sia a tu preparat, sino que sia mot en le preon, quar no es a tu que fassas aquo per que no inscidas le lacert; e aprop fay am aquela entro que sia sanada.	But if the orifice of the fistula is not penetrating, then make it penetrate in any way you have prepared for it, but not so much that it reaches the anus, because it is not your business to do that; and accordingly make it healed with water as we have said.
La forma de spatum spinos am lo qual es fenduda la fistula: la curvitat del qual es mot aguda e l’autra partida es no-aguda, per so que no inscidas aquo que no es necessari, ayssi cum vezes.	The shape of the spatula with which the fistula is punctured: its curvature is very sharp on one side and not sharp at all on the other side, so that you do not insert what is not necessary, just like sometimes.
De sutura de emorroydas en las quals corra sanc en la inscizio de aquelas.	Of stitching of hemroids in which blood flows during the incision of those.
Emorroydas so segon dos manieyras, quar o so entre le cul semblantz aysi que es de carbos, o quays aquelas sian cum a gras de rasim.	Hemroids are according to two ways, for either they are between the anus resembling like those of charcoal, or those which are like a grass of rashes.
E de aquelas so petitas e grans, e que le sanc corr de aquelas tostemps e es una, e so motas, e so fora·l cul, e en las extremitatz de lu.	And those are small and large, and the blood flows from them always and is one, and many, and outside the anus, and in its extremities.
Mays empero aquelas que so foro le cul so segon las mes de pauca humiditat, de las quals corr aygua citrina o un petit de sanc am cos continuabla, e so segon la color del cos.	But those that are outside the anus are according to the months of little moisture, from which flows a yellowish water or a small amount of blood with continuous pus, and according to the color of the body.
E la curacio de aquela que es dedintz le cuol es que comandes al malaute que se assela e que se exprema entro que le cuol yesca e las emoroydas apparescan a tu.	And the cure for that which is outside the anus is to command the patient to settle down and to be expelled into the anus until the anus opens and the hemroids appear before you.
Adonc tu te coyte e suspen am uncis o que tenguas aquelas am la tua ungla, e aprop incideys aquelas deves las suas razitz.	Then you will cut and suspend with scissors or whatever you have those on your fingernail, and accordingly cut off the roots of those.
Mays si les uncis no so tengutz en aquelas per la humiditat de lor e mollificacio de aquelas, lahoras pren aquelas am drap aspre o am coto o am flassada de lana, e extratz aquelas am les tieus ditz, e aprop inscideys aquelas e polveriza sobre lor alcunas polveras caudas aprop la inscizio, per que sian ad aquelas en loc de cauteri; o cauteriza aquelas segon que es precedit en le capitol de cauterizar.	But if the scissors are not taken to those because of the humidity and softening of them, then take those with a rough cloth or with a piece of cotton or with a woolen rag, and pull out those with the aforementioned fingers, and accordingly cut off those and powder some powders on top of them nearby the incision, so that they are adapted to those in place of cauterization; or cauterize those as it is preceded in the chapter of cauterizing.
E aprop cura aquelas am l’autra curacio entro que sian sanadas.	And accordingly cure those with another cure until they are healed.
E si le cul no obezeys a egressio, lahoras cristerisa le malaute am cristeri en le qual sia mordicacio petita, e sia lavat am aquel aquo que es en le cuol e que obezesca a egressio leugierament quan le malaute s’esprem.	And if the anus does not obey evacuation, then cleanse the patient with a small amount of cistern in the cistern where there is slight biting, and wash him with that water that is in the anus and that will obey evacuation slightly when the patient is evacuated.
Mays si las emorroydas so defora le cul, lahoras la causa de lor es leugiera, e es que tu prenguas aquelas am la tua ungla, o que prenguas aquelas am unci, e inscidas aquelas, e aprop cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit entro que sian sanadas.	But if the hemroids are outside the anus, then the cause of them is slight, and it is that you take those with your fingernail or with scissors, and cut off those, and accordingly cure those with water as we have said until they are healed.
E aquel que avoreys inscizio, cove que aministres sutura de lor segon aquesta manieyra: pren fiel envolopat e entromet aquel en agulha e aprop extratz las emorroydas a las partidas dessus, e fay aquel penetrar am la agulha en la razit del autra part, e envolveys las doas extramitatz del fiel en la partida pus dejos de la agulha, e so latitudinalment; e estrenh la emorroyda am strectura fort, e aprop noza le fiel e extratz la agulha.	And whoever will have incision, should administer suture of theirs according to this method: take a faithful wrapping and insert that into the needle and accordingly pull out the hemroids at the upper parts, and make that penetrate with the needle in the root of the other part, and wrap the two extremities of the thread in the part most left behind of the needle, and so latitudinally; and strengthen the hemroid with a strong stitch, and accordingly remove the thread and extract the needle.
E fay aquo a totas, e layssa de aquelas una e no la cozes, per so que la superfluitat del sanc corra de aquela.	And do this with all of them, and leave one of those alone and do not cook it, so that the superfluity of blood flows from that.
E aprop pausa sobre le cul drap enfus en oli rozat o en cerot; e pausa aquel sobre·l cuol e comanda al malaute que·s repause.	And accordingly place a cloth soaked in rose oil or cerote on the anus, and place that on the anus and command the patient to rest.
E aprop layssa aquela entro que caja; e quan es casuda, cura aquelas am enguentz o am autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly leave that until it is hardened, and when it has hardened, cure those with poultices or with another cure until they are healed.
De curacio de fistulas.	The Cure of Fistulas.
Motas veguadas accideys per exseccacio de fenda o per costriccio de natura.	Many times it happens by excess of a wound or by constriction of nature.
E cum so antiquadas e no val en aquela medicina, lahoras cove que tu razas aquelas am la puncta de spatum o am la tua ungla entro que sian faytas humidas e sia hostada de aquelas la escorsa pus desus, la qual prohibeys aquelas de consolidacio; e aprop cura aquelas entro que sian consolidadas.	And since they are so old and not valid in that medicine, then you must scrape those with the point of a spatula or with your fingernail until they become moist and the scab above is prevented from forming; and accordingly cure those until they are consolidated.
Lahoras tu osta aquelas am razio pus vehement que la primieyra entro que mot sancno e sian excoriadas; e aprop cura aquelas entro que sian sanadas.	Then you must scrape those with reason more violent than the first time until there is no blood and they are exfoliated; and accordingly cure those until they are healed.
De curacio de almesamir, so es clau.	The Cure of Almesmir, this is the key.
Sapias que alamermar, so es clau, e no es si no notz redon segon la color del cors semblant a cap de claviel, e es fayt en tot le cors e majorment en las partidas dejos les pes e als ditz, e endeve per aquels dolor deves le anament.	Know that Almesmir is the key, and it is not so unless there are notes redone according to the color of the body resembling a head of clavicle, and it is made throughout the body and most in the parts left behind the weights and the dits, and thereby one must follow the pain through the love.
E adonc cove que sia inscidit aquo que es en le circuit del clau, e sia tengut am les forfexs o am unci, e sia eradicat de la sua razit; e aprop cura aquel.	And then it is necessary to cut off that which is in the circle of the key, and be held with forceps or scissors, and be eradicated from its root; and accordingly cure that.
E si vols, cauteriza le segont que es precedit en le sieu capitol.	And if you wish, cauterize it according to what is preceded in the chapter on cauterizing.
Mays de veruca es eminencia petita aspre fistulada redonda sobre la superficia del cos, e motas veguadas veno en las mas dels enfantz.	But of verruca is a small rough wart-like prominence that is fistulated and rounded on the surface of the body, and many times it appears in children's hands.
E curacio de lu es que estendas e inscidas aquela, o que estrenhas aquela am fiel o am pel entro que caja.	And the cure for that is to spread and cut off that, or to strengthen it with a thread or with a cloth until it hardens.
E si vols, cauteriza aquo, segon que havem dit, am foc o am medicina acuta.	And if you wish, cauterize it, as we have said, with fire or sharp medicine.
E ja so eradicadas enversas e no-enversas am le instrument le qual yeu diyre.	And already eradicated inwardly and outwardly with the instrument that you will say.
Mays formica es eminencia petita feutrada o fistulada grossa sobre la superficia del cos anant mot en le preon, e quan le freg atroba aquela es centit en lu semblant de mordificacio de formigua, e es fayta entorn le cos.	But a formic is a small prominence that is fatty or fistulated large on the surface of the body moving towards the anus, and when the heat finds it, it appears like a biting of an ant, and is made around the body.
E curacio de lu es que prenguas una canula de pena de auca o de pena de voltor, e sia fort, e pausa aquela sobre la formigua entro que la contengua le cercle de la canula de las partidas de lu; e aprop revolveys la tua ma am la canula entro que inscidas aquo que es en le circuit de la formigua, e pauses aquela en le preon de la carn, e que eradiques la formigua de la sua razit.	And the cure for it is that you take a quill of goose or of wolverine, and it be strong, and place it on the formic until it contains the circle of the quill around the parts of it; and accordingly revolve your hand with the quill until you cut off what is in the circuit of the formic, and place it in the anus of the flesh, and thereby eradicate the formic from its root.
E si vols, fay aquo am canula de eram o de ferr segon aquesta forma:	And if you wish, do this with a clay or iron quill according to this form:
Sia la partida desus de la canulha trahent a subtilitat, sorda (so es no-perforada), envolopada per so que sobre le dit la aprencio de lu sia ablaviada e la revolucio de aquela.	Be the upper part of the quill thin and subtle, not perforated, wrapped in such a way that on the said part of it is ablated and the rotation of it.
E si vols cauteriza la formiga segon que es denant dit en la cauterizacio de atheyl en le capitol de cauteri.	And if you wish, cauterize the ant according to what is said before in the chapter on cauterizing.
De forma dels instrumentz que so aministratz a dar cristeri.	The Form of the Instruments that are administered to give Cistern.
Alcunas veguadas es fayt cristeri de argent o de lato o de eram fondut o malleat; e alcunas veguadas es fayt de aquels instrumentz petit e gran segon aquels als quals so aministratz, quar aquel que es aministrat en la curacio dels petitz enfants sia petit; e de aquel dels quals los culs son freuls o doloyrozes, les cristeris de aquels sian petitz.	Sometimes cistern is made of silver or lead or clay melted or hammered; and sometimes it is made with small and large instruments according to those which are administered, for that which is administered in the cure of small children is small; and of those whose anus is rough or painful, their cisterns are small.
La forma de cristeri gran e pauc:	The Form of Cistern Great and Little.
Le cap de la canula de lu desus en le qual es liada la borsa sia ampla segon aquesta manieyra; e sia a lu distinacio la on la borsa es liada ayssi cum vezes.	The head of the quill above, in which the bag is tied, should be wide according to this method; and there should be a distinction at the place where the bag is tied just like sometimes.
E la extremitat de lu pus dejus, la qual es entromesa en le cul, sia sorda (so es no-uberta) mot leon, atrasent a subtilita; e en la un del latz de lu sian dos traucs, e en l’autre costat un trauc, e sia la amplesa del trauc segon la groseza dels rays e pus gros un petit.	And the extremity of it most below, which is inserted into the anus, should be blunt (so it is not open) very much like a lion, going back to subtlety; and on one side of it there are two holes, and on the other side one hole, and the width of the hole according to the thickness of the rays and slightly larger than small.
E sia la borsa en la qual sian pausadas las medicinas de vesica de bestia o de pel de ovelha, e la razit de lu sia un palm.	And the bag should be in which medicines from the bladder of an animal or from sheep's wool are placed, and the root of it should be a palm.
E sia perforada per motz traucs ayssi cum es revolvuda; e si l’espazi le qual es entre les traucs la grossetut del dit.	And it should be pierced with many holes just like it is rolled up; and if the space which is between the holes is as thick as said.
E aprop entromet en aquels traucs fiel fort de fiel cru le qual sia de detz fiels, o enviro aquels; e ajusta am aquel la borsa; e quan es pausada en lu la borsa, sia streyt en le cap del cristeri entre dos distingentz am fort costriccio, e aprop cristeriza am aquel quascun trauc: Mays la qualitat de cristerizar am aquel es que tu omples la borsa de la medicina, que sia escalfada segon la quantitat de la tolleransa del malaute; e guarda te que no sia trop cauda ni trop freja.	And accordingly insert into those holes a strong thread of raw thread which is of ten threads, or around those; and adjust the bag with that; and when it is placed in there the bag should be tight at the head of the cistern between two distinct parts with strong constriction, and accordingly cauterize each hole: But the quality of cauterizing is that you fill the bag with medicine, which should be warmed according to the quantity of the patient's tolerance; and beware that it is not too hot nor too cold.
E aprop le malaute sia resupinat sobre le sieu dos, e eleva las suas cambas en sus e pausa dejos lu un cuer sobre le qual ja so les homes o un lansol; e aprop unta la extramitat del cauteri am oli o am album de huou o am mucellage de fenugrec o de semblantz; e aprop entromet aquel en le cul am facilitat, e aprop le ministre prengua la borsa e exprema aquel am doas mas e essemps am vehemencia entro que sia evacuat en le budelh tot aquo que es en le cristeri; e aprop extra le cristeri e le malaute leva las suas cambas a la paret.	And accordingly the patient should be raised over his back, and lift his legs up high and place something flat underneath it on which men or a lansol rest; and accordingly anoint the extremity of the cauter with oil or album of wheat or mucilage of fenugreek or similar substances; and accordingly insert that into the anus with ease, and accordingly the minister should take the bag and expel that with two hands and sometimes with vehemence until it is evacuated in the bedpan all that is in the cistern; and accordingly remove the cistern and the patient will lift his legs to the wall.
E si la medicina forsa aquel a eyssiment, tengua le tant quant poyra; e si dorm am aquel per tota una nueyt, es mays derier en juvament.	And if the medicine forces him to sleep, let him sleep as long as he can; and if he sleeps with that all night, it is even later in judgment.
Mays si tu cristerizas aquel en las malautias de solucio de ventre e l’eyssiment de lu le coyta, lahoras tu itera le cauteri entro que sia sanat.	But if you cauterize that in diseases of stool evacuation and the patient's sleep is disturbed, then you must repeat the cauterization until he is cured.
E si en le cul so emorroydas o apostemas ledens, lahoras sia le cristeri mot subtil e leon, dels cristeris am les quals les enfantz so criterisatz.	And if in the anus there are hemroids or apoplastic lesions, then you should use a cistern that is very subtle and lion-like, from among those with which children are cisternized.
De curacio de las plaguas.	The Cure of Plagues.
Yeu ja e dit en la divisio de la curacio de las plaguas aquo que convenia al libre, e yeu dic assi la curacio de aquelas am ma e am medicinas segon le conpliment.	And so I have said in the division of the cure of plagues what is necessary for the free man, and I say thus the cure of those with me and with medicines according to the complement.
Donc dic que las plaguas son diversificadas segon aquo en que son faytas las plaguas e segon le loc sobre le qual cazo las plaquas.	Therefore I say that plagues are diversified according to what the plagues are made and according to the place on which the plagues are placed.
E las causas per que motas vetz son faytas las plaguas so ayssi cum getament de peyra, o inscisio d’espaza o de cotel, o percussio am lansa, o am fustz, o am sageta, o semblantz ad aquels de motas causas.	And the causes by which many times plagues are made are just like a blow of pepper, or incision of space or of cote, or percussion with lance, or with fist, or with arrow, or similar to those of many causes.
Mays las plaguas que so en les locz del cos so ayssi cum plagua la qual catz sobre le cap, o·l col, o·l pietz, o·l ventre, o·l fitge, e semblantz ad aquels dels membres.	But the plagues that are in the parts of the body are like a plague which lies on the head, or the neck, or the feet, or the belly, or the thigh, and similar to those of the limbs.
E yeu so recomtant la curacio de alcunas plaguas per que pauses aquela ratiocinacio e regla sobre las autras plaguas.	And I recommend the cure for some plagues by which you pause that reasoning and rule over other plagues.
E yeu comensare de las plaguas del cap simplas, quar la rememoracio de las compostas vindra al comensament del tertz capitol.	And I begin with the plagues of the head, simple ones, for the memory of the compound ones will come at the beginning of the fourth chapter.
Donc dic que quan accideys en le cap plagua simpla e no es fractura, lahoras considera: si es per getament de peyra o de semblant, e ja ha trinquada la codena tant solament e es gran plagla e temes sobre aquel malaute havinement de apostema caut, lahoras tu te coyta e fleubotoma la cephalica tantost, e no tardas aquo; e extrats ad aquel del sanc segon la quantitat de la vertut de lu si no mes alcuna causa prohibent de fleubotomia, majorment si·l sanc que es eyssit de la plagua es pauc.	Therefore I say that when a simple plague occurs in the head and it is not a fracture, then consider: if it is due to a blow of pepper or similar, and if the wound has already opened up just a little bit and it is a big plague and you fear that there may be an apostema forming, then you should take care of it and perform cephalic bleeding as soon as possible, and do not delay; and extract blood from it according to the quantity of its virtue, unless there are other causes prohibiting bleeding, especially if the blood that has flowed out of the plague is little.
E sia la flaubotomia del contrari de la partida plaguada; e guardase le malaute de replecio e de vi e de viandas grossas.	And perform the bleeding on the opposite side of the affected part; and beware that the patient does not get filled up with blood, nor eat nor drink strong foods.
Mays si de la minuicio prohibeys alcuna causa, lahoras sia aminorat de la vianda e no apropinque a carn ni a vi.	But if there is any prohibition from the minority, then it should be reduced in food and not approach meat nor wine.
E pausa sobre la plagua, si a lu accideys apostema caut, coto enfus en oli rozat solet o en vi en le qual es stipticat.	And place on the plague, if an apostema is forming cautiously, apply oil of roses or wine in which it is stipticated.
Mays si est segur de apostema caut, lahoras pausa sobre la plagua, si es recent am le sieu sanc e le ayre no ha mudat aquela la polvera la qual yeu recomtare aprop petit.	But if it is certain that an apostema is forming cautiously, then place on the plague, if it is fresh with its own blood and the air has not changed that powder which I recommended earlier in small amounts.
E si le ayre ja ha mudada aquela, lahoras pausa sobre alscus enguentz entro que sia sanada.	And if the air has already changed that, then place on it some poultice until it is healed.
Mays si la plagua es gran o es per inscizio d’espaza e de semblantz, e no so ajustadas las labias de lu per puvils, lahoras ajusta aquelas am sutura segon que yeu recomtare de la sutura de lor.	But if the plague is great or is due to incision of space and similar things, and the lips of it are not adjusted for pus, then adjust those with a suture according to how I recommend for the suturing of theirs.
Mays si la plagua ja es discuberta del os e pen, e no es retencio de lu sino un petit suspensori, lahoras inscideys aquela e aprop cura la plagua am medicinas e restaura la carn aprop en loc de codena, e comanda al malaute que sia pescut de viandas en las quals es groceza: caps e formen coyt e semblantz a lor, entro que sia compost.	But if the plague has already been discovered from the bone and pen, and there is no retention of it but only a small suspensor, then cut off that and accordingly cure the plague with medicines and restore the flesh in its proper place, and command the patient to eat foods in which there is grossness: caps and forms like theirs, until they are composed.
E si atrobas en la codena putrefaccio e no adhereys al os, lahoras tu inscideys tot aquo poyrit e geta aquo, e aprop cura aquo.	And if you find in the wound putrefaction and it does not adhere to the bone, then cut off all that putrid part and remove it, and accordingly cure what remains.
Mays si en aquestas plaguas es arteria o vena de la qual fluxs de sanc pot evenir, e no es abscindida per medicinas, lahoras tu inquier sobre la arteria, e si atrobas aquela no-inscidida, lahoras tu inscideys aquela am spatum, o lia aquela; e si necessitat te provoca que aquo que havem dit no comfereys, lahoras tu cauteriza entro que·l sanc sia abscidit.	But if in these wounds there is an artery or vein from which blood can flow and it is not abscessed by medicines, then you should inquire about the artery, and if you find that one which is not abscessed, then cut off that with a spatula or tie it; and if necessity demands that what we have said does not come to pass, then you should cauterize in order for the blood to be abscessed.
E si aquestas plaguas son simplas e petitas, lahoras la causa de lor es leugiere; enayssi que tu polverizas sobre aquelas aquesta polvera, quar consolidada aquela denant que l’ayre mude aquelas.	And if these wounds are simple and small, then the cause of them is slight; therefore you can powderize on those this powder, for it will consolidate that before the air changes those.
E la manieyra de la polvera es aquesta: recipe oli de enses partida una, de sanc de drago partida doas, de caus no-extincta partidas tres; sia tot mot trissat e crivellat, e de lu sia la plagua omplida, e sia constrengida per bona constriccio entro que be sobre aquela aderesca, e sia coagulada am le sanc.	And the method of the powder is this: take oil from a dragon's wound, one part, blood of a dragon, two parts, and non-extinguished charcoal, three parts; mix it all well and grind it finely, and fill the wound with it, and compress it with good constriction until it adheres well to that place, and coagulates with the blood.
E aprop strengeys aquela desus am pulvils e leyssa aquela, e no la deslias mentre esta ayssi que no es apostemada, quar no es eredicada de lu la medicina entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly strengthen that above with poultices and apply it, and do not remove it while it is like this, for the medicine has not yet been absorbed by it until it is healed.
E alcuna vetz fa aquo sola cautz, quan no es a tu en present enses e sanc de drago.	And sometimes make this alone, when you are not present with dragon's blood and dragon's wound.
E ja fa aquesta meteyssa operacio en las grans plaguas quan conveneys que sia pausada sobre aquelas e sian streytas, e so plaguas recentz am le lor sanc, las quals le ayre no ha alteradas.	And then do this same operation on large wounds when it is necessary to pause over those and compress them, and on fresh wounds with their own blood, which the air has not altered.
E si le ayre las ha alteradas, e majorment quan es en temps d’estiu, lahoras no es entencio a la posicio de aquesta polvera, mays adonc cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit, enayssi que tu pauses sobre aquelas alcus enguents degistius, o que pauses sobre aquelas pols de la farina del ordi am aygua e mel entro que getan poyredura; e aprop cura aquelas am l’autra curacio entro que sian sanadas.	And if the air has altered them, and especially when it is in the time of summer, then you should not think about the position of this powder, but rather cure those with what we have said, by applying poultices that are suitable for them, or by applying fine powder made from barley flour mixed with water and honey until a poultice forms; and accordingly cure those with another remedy until they are healed.
Mays si accideys am la plagua fractura en os, e es petita, lahoras tu extratz aquo am gesti.	But if it occurs in a fracture of the bone, and is small, then you should extract that with gauze.
E yeu diyre la cura de las fracturas del cap en aquo que es envenidor.	And I say the cure for fractures of the head in this way which follows.
De las plaguas del col.	Of the plagues of the neck.
Mays si la plagua accideys en le col, lahoras no es en lu differencia en medicacio, e entre la plagua del cap quan es simpla.	But if the plague occurs in the neck, then there is no difference in medication and between the plague of the head when it is simple.
Mays si ja le nervi del col es inscis o arteria, lahoras si es nervi, no es en lu engen sino que sia evitada curacio de lu am aquo que fa vehement stipticitat, ayssi cum ziniar e zegi que es vetriol e semblantz a lor quar nozo als nervis e contrazo aquel.	But if the nerves of the neck are cut or an artery is injured, then if it is a nerve, do not intervene with poultice, but rather avoid curing it with anything that causes vehement stiptication, just like vinegar and egg whites, which are like vitriol and similar to theirs, which hurt the nerves and contract that.
E no pauses sobre la plagua alcuna causa de tot freja, quar la sustancia dels nervis es freja e la continuacio de lu es am le cervel, le qual es le pus aut de totz les membres.	And do not apply anything to the wound that is too cold, for the substance of the nerves is cold and their continuation is in the brain, which is the highest part of all the members.
E si’ aquo am que es curat de medicinas leugieras, ayssi cum es caus lavada am aygua dousa, alcuna veguada enfusa en oli rozat o no-rozat, e thucia quan es lavada am aygua dousa e las autras peyras minarantz segon aquesta manieyra, e enguentz humitz.	And if the wound is cured with gentle medicines, just as it is washed with lukewarm water, some times infused in rose oil or not-rose oil, and thus when it is washed with lukewarm water and other parts are softened according to this manner, and poultices moist.
Mays si la plagua es gran, lahoras aministra sutura, o coarta las labias de lu, e aprop cura aquela am pulvils entro que sia sanada.	But if the wound is large, then administer a suture, or tie off the edges of it, and accordingly cure that with poultices until it is healed.
Mays si a la plagua es profunditat o accideys en lu a la pus bassa partida poyredura, lahoras perfora aquela en le loc mays depremegut.	But if the wound is deep or occurs in the lowest part of the poultice, then pierce that in the most suitable location.
Mays si en la plagua ja es inscisa arteria e es conseguit flux de sanc, lahoras separa o secca aquela, o lia aquela, o cauteriza aquela si necessitat te provoca ad aquo.	But if an artery has been cut in the wound and blood is flowing, then separate or dry it out, or tie it off, or cauterize it if necessity demands that too.
Mays si ja ha insciditz les spondils del golayro o tot, e so salvadas las venas del col, lahoras tu ajusta las labias de la codena am sutura sobre la cana del golayro e no toques aquel; abantz egala aquel e reduzeys aquel sobre la sua figura natural, e aprop strenh aquel am strectura decent, e leyssa aquela per alcus jorns; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz en les quals es stipticitat e excitacio entro que sia sanat.	But if the vertebrae of the neck have been cut or all, and the veins of the neck are saved, then you should adjust the edges of the wound with sutures over the canal of the neck and do not touch that; above equalize that and reduce it to its natural shape, and accordingly strengthen that with decent stricture, and leave it for a few days; and accordingly cure that with poultices in which there is stiptication and excitation until it is healed.
Mays si la plagua ja en le os a fayta enprecio, lahoras percuireys aquela, e lahoras si en lu ha fragmentz de hos, extratz totz aquels que podes de lor; e aquo que a tu no es apparelhat, leyssa aquo entro que la plagua se poyrisca, e sia separat e la egrecio de lu sia alleujada.	But if the wound has made an impression in the bone, then pierce it, and then if there are fragments of bone, extract all that you can from them; and what is not removable, leave that until the wound settles, and be separate and the excrescence from it be alleviated.
E si la plagua es recent lahoras polveriza sobre aquela polvera la qual t’e recomtada.	And if the wound is fresh, then powderize over it with the powder that I recommended.
Mays si en la plagua es fayta fistula, lahoras cura aquela am aquo del qual la rememoracio vindra aprop en le sieu capitol.	But if there is a fistula in the wound, then cure that with what will be remembered later in its own chapter.
De las plaguas del col o de semblantz quan fayta entre las spallas e es fayta am spaza o am cotel o am lansa o am semblantz.	Of the wounds of the neck or similar, when made between the vertebrae and is made with space or with a cote or with a lance or with similar things.
Si es percussio de lansa o de cotel, e vezes de lu la profunditat, lahoras considera mays si de la plagua yeys ventositat quan le malaute elena; lahoras sapias que la plagua es mortal.	If it is a blow from a lance or a cote and sometimes the depth of the wound, then consider more if there is ventilation in the wound when the patient breathes; know that the wound is mortal.
E si en lu no es profunditat e la plagua es recent am le sieu sanc, lahoras tu pauses en lu de la primieyra horo polvera, e no strenhas aquel per que no sia le sanc retengut en la profunditat de lu e que retorne al cor e que aucigua le malaute, mays pausa en lu enguent atractiu, e deslia aquela doas veguadas le dia.	And if there is no depth to the wound and it is recent with its own blood, then you should apply powder to it at the first hour, and not strengthen that so that the blood is not retained in the depth of it and returns to the heart and aches the patient, but rather pause on it an attractive poultice, and remove it twice a day.
E si l’enguent no es a tu present, lahoras tu pausa en le orrifici de la plagua coto viel per que sucque aquo que yeys de las humiditatz; e fay que le malaute dorma sobre la plagua per que corra aquo que es en lu ajustat.	And if the poultice is not present, then you should pause on the orifice of the wound with a cloth so that it sucks out what there is of the humidities; and make the patient sleep over the wound so that the water that is in it is adjusted.
Mays si ja de la plagua son passatz tres dias o mays e no accideys al malaute spasme ni tremor de cor mal ni strictura de ale, e vezes las autras dispozicios bonas de lu, lahoras sapias que plagua es salva; e adonc cura aquela am calguas e am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanada.	But if three days or more have passed since the wound and there is no spasm nor trembling of the heart nor constriction of the artery, and sometimes other good dispositions from it, then know that the wound is saved; and accordingly cure that with cauterization and another remedy until it is healed.
Mays si la sanacio de lu es excusada, e ja tot temps es uberta, lahoras sapias que ja es fayta fistula; cura donc aquela per le sieu capitol.	But if the healing of it is delayed, and all time has opened up, then know that a fistula has been formed; cure then that according to its own chapter.
E si la plagua es per inscisio de spaza o de cotel, e es simpla en la superficia del pietz o del dos, lahoras cura aquela am aquo que es precedit de sutura, si es gran, o am polvera, si es petita.	And if the wound is due to incision of space or cote, and is simple on the surface of the foot or hand, then cure that with what has preceded it by suture, if it is great, or with powder, if it is small.
Mays si ja ha fayta enprecio en le os, e so ja de lu inscizas pessas, lahoras tu torqua la plagua e coyta ad extrayre aquelas pessas, si so separadas.	But if it has made an impression in the bone, and there are fragments of bone, then pierce the wound and extract those fragments, if they are separated.
Mays si no so separadas, lahoras leyssa las entro que se poyresca la plagua, que la extraccio de lor es alleujada.	But if they are not separated, then leave them until the wound settles, so that the extraction of them is alleviated.
E de las autras plaguas accidentz en les autres membres le juvament en curacio es le juvament de aquo que havem dit.	And as for other wounds that occur in other limbs, the judgment in curing is the same as what we have said.
De las plaguas del ventre.	Of the wounds of the belly.
L’indisposicio la qual accideys en le ventre es o gran, o pauc, o migiera.	The indisposition which occurs in the belly is either great, or small, or middling.
De la gran alcunas veguadas yeys le budel o nervi del budel, per que es fayta intromissio de lor e la sutura de lor esser pus vehement e pus subtil.	Of the great, sometimes you find the bowels or nerves of the bowels, because an intrusion has been made and the suture of them is more violent and more subtle.
E disrupcio petita es fayta dificil per autra manieyra, e siec se que la reduccio de lor es pus dificil, si no te coytes de la intromissio de lor al sieu loc tantost, quar se ubre e es engrossat per que le intrament de lu es fayt difficil.	And a small disruption is made difficult by another manner, and you must know that the reduction of them is more difficult, if you do not take care to put their intrusion back into its place soon, for it opens up and becomes engorged so that the instrument of it is made difficult.
E donc la milhor disrupcio es migiera, quar en aquela no es dificil la reduccio del budel, ayssi cum es dificil en las doas specias denant ditas.	And therefore the best disruption is middling, because in that one there is no difficulty in reducing the bowels, just as it is difficult in the two species mentioned before.
E sapias que sutura del ventre es segon quatre manieyras, mays doas suturas son comunas que conveneysso en suturas de las autras plaguas del cors.	And know that the suture of the belly is according to four manners, but two sutures are common that are necessary in sutures of other wounds of the body.
E duas autras suturas proprias comunican a las autras plaguas, mays empero so mays proprias en la sutura del ventre.	And two other sutures proper communicate with the other wounds, but nevertheless are more proper in the suture of the belly.
E yeu recomti a tu quascuna am exposicio e declaracio.	And I recommend to you any exposition and declaration.
Donc dic que quan la plagua es petita e es eyssit alcuna causa del budel per aquela, e es fayt dificil a reduzir aquel, lahoras aquo es en una de doas manieyras: o per parvitat de la disrupcio ayssi cum havem dit, o quan al budel es venguda inflacio per la frigiditat de l’ayre.	Therefore I say that when the wound is small and some cause of the bowels has been made by it, and it is difficult to reduce it, then this is done in one of two manners: or by the smallness of the disruption as we have said, or when the bowels have become inflamed due to the coldness of the air.
E donc quan aquo es ayssi, lahora cove que tu scalfes aquel enayssi que tu submerges una sponga ho drap humit en aygua tebeza sola, o que coguas en aygua squinant, e cyperum, e spic, e embroques am aquela le budel entro que la imflacio sia resolvuda.	And therefore when this is so, it is necessary that you scrape that in such a way that you submerge a sponge or damp cloth in hot water alone, or that you soak it in water with squinant, and cypress, and spic, and wrap the bowels around that until the inflammation is resolved.
E alcunas veguadas fa aquo vi en le qual ha stipticitat, e es milhor que la aygua sola en resolucio de la imflacio.	And sometimes I find that this has a stiptic quality, and it is better than hot water alone in resolving the inflammation.
E donc cum tu vezes la imflacio esser resolvuda, lahoras tu humecta le budel am aygua en la qual es coyta altea e malvas, quar per aquo es alleujat le intrament de lu am pauca causa.	And therefore when you find that the inflammation is resolved, then you should moisten the bowels with water in which there are high and bitter roots, for by this the instrument of it with little cause.
Mays si es escusat le intrament de lu aprop aquesta curacio, lahoras scindeys la disrupcio un petit am strument am le qual so inscididas emorroydas.	But if the instrument of it is not suitable for this cure, then you should divide the disruption into small parts with an instrument which has been sharpened by cutting bloodless wounds.
E la curacio primieyra es milhor, quan es propriada que no es seccio, e no sia occupacio a seccar aprop necessitat e defaliment.	And the first cure is better when it is proper and not too dry, and there is no occupation in drying out too much necessity and deficiency.
Del instrument, sec se la forma de lu:	Of the instrument, see the shape of it:
La una partida de lu torta aguda, e l’autra partida no-acuta, e la extremitat subtil, e no sia am la subtilitat de spatum, abantz sia obtusa un pauc.	The one part of it is twisted sharp, and the other part not sharp, and the extremity subtle, and not so subtle as a spatula, but rather obtuse a little.
E donc cum la plagua es amplificada e yeys fora le budel, lahoras cove que la sua reduccio sia segon la forma de lu natural, en le sieu loc propri, si es possible sobre aquo, quar milhor es.	And therefore when the wound is enlarged and the bowels are outside, it is necessary that their reduction be according to its natural form, in its proper place, if possible above, for better.
Mays quan la disrupcio es ampla, e es en la partida pu bassa del ventre, lahoras cove que tu fassas jazer le malaute sobre le sieu dos, e pausa las suas cambas pus autas que·l sieu cap; e si es en la partida pus desus del ventre, lahoras tu pause le cap de lu e·l pietz pus autz que las partidas dejos.	But when the disruption is wide and is in the lower part of the belly, it is necessary that you make the patient lie on his back, and raise his hips higher than his head; and if it is in the upper part of the belly, then you should place the head of him and his feet higher than the remaining parts.
E semblantment si la disrupcio es en una de las doas partz del ventre, lahoras pausa la tua entencio e la tua consideracio tostemps en aysso per que la partida en la qual es la plagua sia pus auta que l’autra.	And similarly if the disruption is in one of the two parts of the belly, then pause your intention and consideration at that point for so long as the part in which the wound is located is higher than the other.
E ayssi cove que tu aministres aquo en las plaguas grans e en las plaguas migieras.	And similarly it is necessary that you administer this to great wounds and middling wounds.
E en las plaguas petitas, pausa aquo que es a tu preparat, e aprop fay que·l ministre sia entre las tuas mas pyatados, le qual tengua la disrupcio tota am la sua ma e ajusta las labias de lu, e aprop descuebre de aquela ad aquel que siec la sutura alcuna causa aprop autra.	And in small wounds, pause on what is prepared for you, and then make the minister to be between your most trusted servants, one who has the disruption all with his hand and adjusts the edges of it, and then uncover from that to that which knows some cause another.
E aquesta es la manieyra de sutura comuna: una que prenguas la agula, o comte de agula segon la cantitat de la amplitut de la plagua; e aprop layssa de la extremitat de la disrupcio del dit anular, e strenh la agula una, otre que tu no metas fiel en las doas extremitatz de la codena, am doas extremitatz del ciphac que es dejos la codena de las partidas dedintz, entro que fassas aquela penetrar de aquela partida; e tu ja has agreguadas doas extremitatz de la codena e doas extremitatz del ciphac, e so faytas quatre ordes.	And this is the common method of suturing: take a needle, or count the needles according to the quantity of the amplitude of the wound; and then leave from the extremity of the disruption of the ring finger, and strengthen the needle one, so that you do not put faith in the two ends of the cord, with the two ends of the ciphac that is left outside the cord, until it penetrates from that part; and you have already added two ends of the cord and two ends of the ciphac, and thus four orders are made.
E aprop strenh am fiel doble en le circuit de la agula, e alcunas veguadas de doas partz ensemps, e aprop agregua las doas labias e la plagua per agreguacio decent; e aprop layssa la grossitut del dit e fiqua una autra agulha en aquela, e aprop lia aquela am fiel ayssi cum fiest am la primieyra agulha; e no cesses far aquo si es necessitat am las agulhas entro que ajas complida tota la contriccio de la plagua.	And accordingly strengthen with double faith in the circuit of the needle, and sometimes from two parts together, and accordingly add the two edges and the wound by decent addition; and accordingly leave the thickness of the finger and put another needle in that place, and accordingly tie that with a thread as if it were a first needle; and do not cease to do this if it is necessary with the needles until you have completed all the constriction of the wound.
E sian las agulhas migieras entre groceza e subtilitat, quar las agulhas subtils mot leugierament insciden la carn; e las grossas so de dificil intrament en la codena, e donc per aquo cove que sian migieras en subtilitat e grosseza.	And the needles should be middling between coarseness and subtlety, because the fine needles barely cut into the flesh; and the coarse ones are of difficult instrument in the cord, and therefore it is necessary that they be middling in subtlety and coarseness.
E no cove que la agulha sia ficada en doas extremitatz de la codena propdana mot, per so que la carn no sia inscidida leugierament e que la plagua se huebra devant la sua consolidacio.	And it is not necessary that the needle be inserted in both ends of the cord at once, for fear that the flesh will be cut too little and the wound will become inflamed before its consolidation.
E no sian prolonguadas de sutura per que la plagua no sia prohibida de consolidacio.	And do not prolong the suturing so that the wound is prohibited from consolidation.
E aprop inscideys las extremitatz de las agulhas per so que no ledescan le malaute deves le sieu dormier; e pausaras sobre la sutura pulvils expanduts de tota partida, les quals tenguan las extremitatz de las agulhas; e layssa aquelas entro que sapias que la plagua ja es consolidada.	And accordingly insert the ends of the needles so that they do not disturb the patient's rest in his bed; and pause on the suturing with poultices spread out from all sides, which have the ends of the needles; and leave those until you know that the wound is already consolidated.
E aquestas specias de sutura am agulhas en cal manieyra es pus convenient en las plaguas petitas, quar habasta en la sutura de lor una agulha o doas o entorn aquelas.	And these species of suture with needles in this manner are more suitable for small wounds, because they suffice in the suture of them with one needle or two or around those.
Mays la segonda sutura es cominal: e es que tu aministres am sutura las quatre extremitatz, de la codena e doas extremitatz del ciphac, en una veguada, am agulha en la qual sia fiel envolopat engual en subtilitat e grosseza.	But the second suture is common: it is that you administer with suturing the four extremities, of the cord and two extremities of the ciphac, in one go, with a needle in which the thread is wrapped evenly in subtlety and coarseness.
E aprop quan am la agulha auras penetrat aquestas quatre extremitatz, reduzeys la agulha de aquela meteyssa partida de la qual comensest, per so que le fiel retrayt caja de la pus subirana partida a la plagua, per so que la sutura sia segon sutura de drap am la qual les draps so strengutz.	And accordingly, when you have the needle penetrate these four extremities, reduce the needle to that middle part from which it began, in order that the thread may be pulled back from the most elevated part of the wound to the wound itself, in order that the suture may be according to the suture of cloth with which the cloths are strengthened.
E pausa entre quascuna sutura la quantitat del gros del dit mendre.	And pause between each suture the quantity of the thickness of the little finger.
E aquesta sutura sabo les homes.	And this suture is known to men.
E am tal sutura yeu cozegui la plagua la qual era accidida a un home en le sieu ventre le qual era stat plaguat am un cotel, e era la disrrumpcio de la plagua major de un palm, e era eyssit dels budels entorn dos palms del budel del mieg loc e era la disrupcio en le mieg del membre; e adonc yeu reduzegui aquel depus que le budel havia stat foro la plagua per xxiiii horas.	And with this suture, I cured the wound which had occurred to a man in his belly, which was wounded with a cote, and the disruption of the wound was greater than one palm, and it was situated around two palms of the bowel from the middle location, and there was a disruption in the middle of the member; and then I reduced that from where the bowel had been perforated by the wound for 24 hours.
E la plagua fo consolidada en le spazi de xv dias o entorn, e curegui aquel e es sanat; e aprop aquo visquec per motz ans, e es conversat en las suas disposicios.	And the wound was consolidated in the space of 15 days or around, and I cured him and he is healed; and accordingly, he lived for many years and was converted to his former disposition.
E les autres metges havian jutgat que no fora sanat; e per miracle foc, quar yeu no curegui aquel am enguent, quar era en loc en le qual enguent no era atrobat ni deguna medicina, mays pausegui sobre la plagua coto viel dos veguadas lo dia e ablucio assiduo am aygua de mel entro que foc sanat.	And the other doctors had judged that he would not be healed; and by a miracle of God, for you did not cure him with poultice, because it was in a place where poultice was not found nor any medicine, but you paused over the wound with a cloth twice a day and ablution assiduous with water of honey until he was healed.
Mays yeu diyre dos specias de sutura proprias segon narracio de Paraula.	But I will tell two species of suture proper, according to the narration of Paraula.
E es que tu comenses am sutura de la codena, e entrometas agulha de la partida deforo a la partida dedintz.	And it is that you begin with the suture of the cord, and insert the needle from the outside part to the inside part.
E donc cum la agulha penetra en la codena e en aquel meteys lacertz segon rectetut e en longetut de tot le cos, e layssa la extremita del ciphac en le qual has entromesa la agulha; e fay penetrar en la autra extremitat la agulha de la partida dedintz a la partida deforo en l’autra extremitat del mihat.	And therefore, as the needle pierces into the cord and meets the lacertz according to rectitude and length of all the body, and leaves the end of the ciphac in which you inserted the needle; and make it penetrate on the other side through the inside part to the outside part in the other extremity of the mihat.
E don cum tu auras fayta aquela penetrar, lahoras tu fay aquela penetrar autra veguada en aquela meteyssa extremitat del mihat de la partida deforo a la partida dedintz; e leyssa la extramitat del ciphac que es en aquest latz, e fay penetrar la agulha en l’autra extremitat de la partida dedintz a la partida deforo.	And then, when you have made it penetrate once, you should make it penetrate again on the same side in that middle extremity of the mihat from the outside part to the inside part; and leave the end of the ciphac which is in this position, and make the needle penetrate into the other extremity of the inside part to the outside part.
E fay penetrar am aquela la tua penetracio am la qual fas aquela penetrar en le ciphac en la extremitat del mirat la qual es en la partida de lu entro que tot aquel penetre.	And make it penetrate with that penetration of yours, with which you make it penetrate into the ciphac in the extremity of the mirror, which is on the part of it, until all of that penetrates.
E aprop comensa de aquest meteys costat e cus aquel am la extremitat que es del ciphac en l’autra latz, e extratz la agulha de la codena la qual penetrec, e aprop redutz aquela en aquela codena e cos la extremitat del ciphac que es en l’autra costat am aquesta extramitat del mirat; e extratz aquela de la codena la qual es de part de lu.	And accordingly, begin on this side of the said cord and cut off that which is at the end of the ciphac in the other side, and pull out the needle from the cord which penetrated, and accordingly reduce it to that cord and tie the end of the ciphac which is on the other side with this extremity of the mirror; and pull out that part of the cord which is on the part of it.
E fay aquo una veguada e autra, e fay aquo una veguada aprop autre veguada entro que tu cozes tot aquo que es deforo segon aquel eysemple.	And do this once and another time, and do it again one more time, until you cut off all that is outside according to this example.
E la suma de aquesta manieyra de sutura es que tu cozes am sutura de pellicies am la qual cozo las pels, enayssi que tu cozes le ciphac una veguada de la part de la extremitat de la codena, e que leysses aquela autra veguada entro que la ajas complida.	And the sum of this manner of suture is that you cut off with a suture of skin, in which you cut off the skin, and so that you cut off the ciphac once on one side of the extremity of the cord, and then leave it there until you have completed it.
Mays la segonda specia de sutura propria la qual dieys eyssament Gualia , e aquest es de sermo de lu e per lu recomtat, es que tu cozas aquela segon semilitut am la qual alcus medicantz cozo aquela, enayssi que agreguan tota partida a la sua compar partida a lu convenient per natura; e aplican la extremitat de autre de lu e la extremitat del mirat al autra extremitat de lu, e aquo es fayt segon que yeu a tu recomti.	But the second species of suture proper, which you call Gualia, and this is according to the word of God and by his recommendation, is that you cut off according to semilitut with which some medics cut it off, in such a way that they add all parts to their corresponding part according to nature; and apply the extremity of one side of it and the extremity of the mirror to another extremity of it, and this is done according to what you recommend to yourself.
Cove que tu fiques la agulha en la extremitat del mirat a tu propdana de la partida deforo, e fassas aquela penetrar a la partida dedintz en aquel sol, e leysses dos extremitatz del ciphac; e aprop revolveys la agulha e fay aquela penetrar de foro a la dedintz en dos extremitatz del ciphac.	It is necessary that you put the needle in the extremity of the mirror at your own part from the outside, and make it penetrate to the inside in that same one, and leave two ends of the ciphac; and accordingly revolve the needle and make it penetrate from outside to inside in the two ends of the ciphac.
E aprop revolveys aquelas cascunas, e fay penetrar quascunas de la partida dededintz entro a la partida deforo en dos extremitatz del mirat autras que so en le latz contrari.	And accordingly, revolve those loops and make them penetrate from the inside to the outside in the two ends of the mirror, which are on the contrary side.
E aquesta manieyra de sutura es milhor de la sutura comuna leugiera, e es sutura de la qual precedic rememoracio.	And this manner of suture is better than the common light suture, and it is the suture which was previously remembered.
Aquest es le sermo de Gualia	This is the saying of Gualia.
E mays le diyssero alcus, sutura del ventre es rectificada am dos agulhas, so es que tu entrometas en aquestas a quascunas un fiel, e comensa am intromiccio de agulha de aquo que es deves tu, e fay aquela penetrar entro al autra latz segon sutura de aquels les quals cozo les cuers engualment.	And besides, some will say that the suture of the belly is rectified with two needles, so it is that you insert into these two one thread, and begin with the introduction of a needle from what belongs to you, and make it penetrate into the other side according to the suture of those who cut off the skins evenly.
E sapias que quan disrupcio es en le mieg loc del ventre, lahoras la sutura de lu es pus difficil que dels autres locs del ventre.	And you know that when disruption is in the middle location of the belly, then the suture of it is more difficult than in other locations of the belly.
Mays le juguament de medicacio de plagua es jutgament de las autras plaguas.	But the judgment of medicine for a wound is judgment of other wounds.
La qual causa es quar quan tu consieguas la plagua recent am le sieu sanc denant que l’ayre altera aquela, e reduses le budel e cozes aquela e aptas aquela decentment, lahoras pausa sobre aquela polvera encarnativa.	The reason is that when you succeed in the wound recently with the patient's blood before it has altered that, and reduce the belly and cut off that and adapt that decently, then pause over that flesh-powder.
E si le ayre ja ha alterada la plagua, lahoras pausa sobre aquela alcus enguentz les quals so a tu presens entro que fassan peyra dura e cajan les fiels, e sian consolidatz ciphac e mirat; e aprop cura aquela ayssi cum es la curacio de las autras plaguas entro que sia sanat.	And if the air has already altered the wound, then pause over that some poultices which are at your presence until they make a hard pressure and loosen the threads, and be consolidated ciphac and mirror; and accordingly cure it thus as is the cure of other wounds until it is healed.
Mays si a tu no so presens las medicinas, lahoras pausa sobre aquela tantost, pus que comensa a getar brac, coto viel, e permuta aquel dos veguadas le dia, ayssi cum a tu e ensenhat, entro que sia sanat, quar tu no indigeysses de autra medicacio en motas disposicios quan las plaguas so simplas.	But if you do not have the medicines at your presence, then pause over that for some time, since it begins to grow hard, and cut off, and exchange that twice a day, just as I teach you, until it is healed, because you will not need other medication in many situations when wounds are simple.
Mays si tu temes que la plagua comunique en lesio als membres principals, lahoras cove que tu submergas lana leon en oli de trempada qualiditat, o en oli rozat, e pausa aquela en le circuit dels locs que so entre les angonas e dejos las aysselas.
