But if you fear that the wound may communicate to lesions in the main members, then it is necessary that you soak linen in good quality oil of tempering or rose oil, and pause that in the circuit of the places which are between the angles and leave those as they are.
E si sent dolor o putrefaccio en les sieus budels, quar motas veguadas aquo s’endeve, lahoras cristeriza aquel am vi stiptic negre tebe, e majorment si la poyredura es pervenguda en le budel e es fayta exitura penetrant entro la conquavitat de lu.	And if you feel pain or putrefaction in your bowels, because many times this happens to be so, then it is necessary that you sterilize that with vinegar stiptic black water, and especially if the perforation has occurred in the bowel and has made an exit hole penetrating into the cavity of it.
E sapias que aquela que es del budel gros es de pus leugiera sanacio que aquela que es en les budels subtils.	And you know that what is from the large bowel is more easily healed than what is in the small bowels.
E es de dificil sanacio quar le budel le qual es apelat “gegunu” no recep sanacio de plagua que caja en lu de tot; e aquo es per la gran multitut de venas que so en lu e per la magnitut de lu que so en aquelas, e per subtilitat del cos de aquel, e per propinquitat de aquel a natura de nervis.	And it is of difficult healing because the bowel which is called "gegunu" does not receive healing from wound that enters into it completely; and this is because of the great multitude of veins that are in it and because of its magnitude, and because of the subtlety of the body of it, and because of its proximity to nature of nerves.
Mays si aquo que procezeys de la plagua es la tela, e conseguas aquela recent, redutz aquela segon la tua rectetut am la qual reduzes les budels engualment.	But if what proceeds from the wound is a thread, and you succeed in getting it recently, then reduce that according to your rectitude with which you reduce the bowels evenly.
Mays si es passat a lu spazi e ja es feyt vert o negre, lahoras que tu strenguas aquela am fiel sobre le loc que es denigrat de lu, per so que vengua fluxs de sanc, quar en la tela so venas e arterias.	But if it has passed into the space and is already made green or black, then you should strengthen that with thread on the location that is degraded from there, in order to bring back the flow of blood, because in the thread are veins and arteries.
E aprop inscideys aquo que es otra aquel liament, e pausa dos extremitatz del fiel pendentz de la partida dejos de la plagua foro lu, per que sobre tu sia alleujada la atraccio de lu deves le cazement de la tela e emissio del brac de la plagua.	And accordingly, insert there what is another binding, and pause the two ends of the thread pending from the left side of the wound, in order that above you may be alleviated the attraction of it from the cavity of the wound and emission of the flesh of the plague.
Rememoracio de las plaguas quan accideysso en le budel.	Remembrance of wounds when they occur in the bowel.
Quan accideys disrupcio en le budel e es petita, lahoras es possibla que sia resteurada en alcus homes, per aysso quar yeu vi aquel le qual era stat plaguat en le sieu ventre am percussio de lansa et era la plagua de la part dreyta del stomac, e la plagua era antiquada e fayta fistula, e eyssic de lu gestio e ventositat.	When a disruption occurs in the bowel and it is small, then it is possible that it can be restored in some men, because you saw that one who was wounded in his belly with a blow from a lance and had an old wound and made a fistula, and exuding pus and flatulence.
Adonc yeu pansegui la curacio de lu ja sia que no era confizat en la sanacio de lu, mays cessegui subtiliar aquel entro que foc sanat e le loc es consolidat.	Then you began to treat the wound as if it were not confined in its healing, but rather ceased to be subtle and allowed that to be healed and the location to be consolidated.
E yeu pus que vi le loc ja consolidat, timegui sobre le malaute que endevengues sobre lu accident de mal en le sieu ventre; e no endevenc alcu per aquo mal accident e romas en las suas milhos disposicios mangant e bevent, e aprop entrec en banh e es exercitat en sos ditz.	And then you saw that the location was already consolidated, and you waited for the patient who had been injured in his belly; and he did not take any medicine because of this bad accident and remained in his usual habits eating and drinking, and accordingly went to the bath and was exercised in his own strength.
E ja diysero alcus experimentados que quan endeve plagua en le budel, e es petita, lahoras cove que sia liada segon aquesta manieyra: e es que tu prenguas fromiguas de grans caps; e aprop ajusta las doas labias de la plagua e pausa una fromigua de aquelas que aja la boca uberta sobre las doas labias de la plagua; donc quan pren sobre aquelas e strenh la sua boca, abscindeys le cap de lu, quar adhereys e no es dissolvut.	And some experienced ones will say that when you encounter a wound in the bowel and it is small, then it is necessary to bind it according to this manner: and it is that you take fromies of large caps; and accordingly adjust the two lips of the wound and pause one fromie of those which has an open mouth over the two lips of the wound; therefore when you place it on top of them and strengthen its mouth, cut off the cap of it, because it adheres and is not dissolved.
E aprop pausa autra formigua prop la primieyra, e no cesses aquo a far am formiguas una aprop autra segon la quantitat de tota la plagua.	And accordingly, pause another fromie near the first one, and do not cease to make fromies one by one according to the quantity of the entire wound.
E aprop reduzeys aquela e cos la plagua; e romanguan aquels caps annexces en le budel entro que·l budel sia sanat; e no accideys al malaute degun nocument.	And accordingly, reduce that and close the wound; and those caps remain attached in the bowel until the bowel is healed; and do not cause any harm to the patient.
E ja es possible que·l budel sia liat am fiel subtil lo qual es fayt del budel de bestia annexs am lu, pus que es mes en agulha; e es que tu prenguas la extremitat de aquestz fiels de budel, e sia mot descarnat, e aprop lia la extremitat de lu am fiel de li, envolopat, e aprop entromet aquel fiel en agulhas e cos am aquel le budel, e areduzeys aquel en la disrupcio.	And already it is possible to bind the bowel with a subtle thread which is made from the bowel of an animal attached to it, because it is more in needle; and it is that you take the end of these threads from the bowel, and it is very bare, and accordingly tie the end of it to the thread of binding, wrapped, and accordingly insert that thread into the needles and close with it on the bowel, and reduce that in the disruption.
E aquesta manieyra de sutura am formiguas no es sino segon via de fiducia e d’esperansa.	And this manner of suture with fromies is nothing but according to the way of faith and hope.
Mays si la plagua es gran e ampla, majorment si es en un dels budels subtils, quar lahoras no es engen sino subtiliacio, e no es sanacio de lu de tot.	But if the wound is great and wide, especially if it is in one of the small bowels, because then it is not just a matter of suture, but rather subtlety, and there is no healing of it completely.
De curacio de zuchem e fistula.	On the cure of abscesses and fistulas.
Sapias que tota plagua e apostema quan se envilheseys e se Antiqua, e es fayt ulcus, e no es consolidat e geta braç tot temps e no es abscindit, lahoras, en qualque membre sia, universalment es nompnada fistula e nos la apelam aquela azukem.	Know that every wound and apostema when it becomes old and antiquated, and is made an ulcer, and is not consolidated and grows a hard crust all the time and is not cut off, then, regardless of what member it may be in, universally it is called fistula and we call it abscess.
E fistula segon veritat es nodacio feutrada, dura, blanqua am la qual no es dolor e a la qual es conquavitat ayssi cum es conquavitat de pena de ausel; e per aysso nompnat aquela alcus rizatz, id est pena.	And fistula according to truth is a nodular abscess, hard, white, and painless, with which there is no pain and it is as if the cavity of the abscess were the penalty of the owl; and for this reason they called that "rizatz", i.e. penalty.
E es en alcus homes humida, la qual geta brac; e fort leu la humiditat es abscidida en alcunas horas.	And it is in some men moist, which grows a crust; and the moisture is soon absorbed in a few hours.
E alcunas veguadas aquesta humiditat es mota, e es pauca, e es grossa, e es subtil.	And sometimes this moisture is more abundant, and it is little, and it is thick, and it is subtle.
E yeu ja he denant dit en la divisio, lahoras cum yeu diyssi las plaguas, que tot ulcus que no es sanat ni no es en lu nuda carn, no es aquo sino per una de ix causas: de las quals la una es o per pauquesa de sanc en le cos; o per malicia de lu; o quar entre lu e las labias es carn dura prohibent nativitat de carn; o quar es de mota legesa; o quar aquel ulcus en si meteys es poyrit e la materia que es a lu tramesa es de mala qualitat; o quar la medicina es enconvenient en la curacio de lu; o quan corrupcio catz en la regio, e es pestilencia; o per proprietat de regio ayssi cum endeve a Saragossa , en la qual es fayta difficil degestio de las malautias, e es tardada en aquela sanacio de apostema per natura; o quar en lu es os un, o motz osses.	And I already mentioned it in the division, when you said that all ulcers which are not healed or are not in bare flesh, there is only one of these causes: either because of a lack of blood in the body; or because of malice towards oneself; or because there is hard skin between it and the lips preventing the growth of new skin; or because it is too old; or because that ulcer within itself putsrefies and the material that is transmitted to it is of bad quality; or because the medicine is inconvenient in the healing of it; or when corruption breeds in the region, and it is pestilence; or due to the property of the region as is the case in Saragossa, where digestion of diseases is difficult and healing of apostemas is delayed by nature; or because there is one bone, or many bones.
Ja e mostrat totas aquelas causas, e·ls senhals de aquelas e la curacio de lor am medicinas en la divisio.	And now I have shown all those causes, and their signs, and the cure of them with medicines in the division.
E cove assi que yeu fassa a tu saber la curacio de fistula la qual es fayta per via de operacio am ma.	And it is necessary that you know how to treat fistulas which are made by way of operation with me.
E sapias que fistula accideys en totz les membres del cos; quar de aquelas son fistulas que perveno a las venas grantz e arterias, o als nervis, o al ciphac, o al budel, o a la vesica, o ad alcuna de las costas, o ad alcu dels spondils del dos, o ad alcuna de las juncturas compostas per composicio ayssi quo de la ma e del pe; e de aquelas so que dan a lu propinquitat del membre principal e de semblantz.	And know that fistulas occur in all the members of the body, because some are fistulas that penetrate into the great veins and arteries, or the nerves, or the ciphac, or the bowel, or the bladder, or to any of the ribs, or to some of the vertebrae of the back, or to any of the joints composed by composition as is the case with the hand and foot; and those are which give proximity to the main member and its likenesses.
E donc aquela de aquestas fistulas que es segon aquesta manieyra es de las malautias de dificil sanacio, e no recep curacio, e occupacio am aquela es trebalh e ignorancia.	And therefore, that one of these fistulas which is according to this manner is one of the difficult-to-heal diseases, and does not receive healing, and its occupation with it is toil and ignorance.
E si es de las fistulas alcuna la profunditat de la qual no perve ad aquestz locs que e dit, e esperas e confizas en la curacio de lu, e vols pervenir a cognicio de lu, lahoras pren tenta de eram o de ferr, e si la fistula va segon rectetut, e perquireys aquela am lu.	And if some of the fistulas have a depth that does not reach those places I mentioned, and you wait and hope for its healing, and wish to understand it, then take a try with iron or steel, and if the fistula follows the natural path, then explore it with the finger.
Mays si la fistula es tortuissitat, lahoras investigua aquela am tenta de plom subtil, quar plom am la levitat del sieu cors es alleujat e curvat deves la tortuositat.	But if the fistula is twisted, then investigate it with a subtle lead, because lead with the lightness of its own body is alleviated and curved in such a way that it follows the twisting.
E si la fistula es havent motz horrificis, no es a tu possible que signifiques sobre lu am tenta.	And if the fistula has many horrible appearances, it is not possible for you to signify on it with a probe.
Adonc cristeriza le orrifici per sos orrificis, quar la humiditat per la qual clisterizas aquela va deves las autras orrificis e corr de lor.	Then clean the orifice by its own orifices, because the moisture which you use to cleanse it flows through the other orifices and drains from them.
E aprop inquier exquisitament, segon qual manieyra a tu es possible que conoguas si aqui has os o nervi, e es la conquavitat de la fistula longinqua o propdana, o es una fistula a la qual so motz orrificis e esta sobre aquo tot am la suma de la tua fortaleza, am la tua enterroguacio, am la qual enterroguas le malaute, e la invencio de la dolor deves la tua compressio am la ma sobre le loc, e semblantz de las significacios e de las causas accidentz al apostema.	And accordingly, inquire exquisitely, according to the manner in which it is possible for you to know if there are bones or nerves here, and whether the fistula is distant or near, or if it is one of those many orifices that is situated above this entire sum of your strength, with your introspection, with which you reflect on the patient, and the invention of pain due to your compression with your hand on the location, and similar signs and causes of accidents affecting the apostema.
E cum tu auras stat sobre totas aquelas causas am stacio veraya, lahoras ve a la curacio segon confidencia: e es que tu consideras lahoras si es fistula apparent propinqua o en loc sal, longinqua de junctura, o de nervi, o de arteria, o de vena, o de un dels locs les quals yeu a tu e ditz.	And when you have stood on all those causes with steadfast true understanding, then go to the cure according to confidence: and it is that you consider now whether it is an apparent fistula near or in a salubrious location, distant from a joint, or nerve, or artery, or vein, or one of the places which I teach you and say.
Lahoras tu secca la fistula segon que denant es dit de la naracio de lu, e osta aquo que es en aquela filtracio e de carns corrumpudas, e aquo que es nascut en le orrifici de la carn, o de theil e de semblantz, e cura aquela entro que sia sanada.	And now you should cleanse the fistula according to what was said before about the narration of it, and stop at that which is in that filtration and of corrupted flesh, and that which is born from the orifice of the flesh, or from the bone and its likenesses, and cure that until it is healed.
Mays si la fistula es de longinqua profunditat, e es segon rectetut, lahoras cove que inscidas aquela en le preon atant quant a tu sira possible, e aprop mondifica aquela de totas las suas carns corrompudas; e aprop administra calguas envolopadas en medicinas acutas, e intromet aquelas entro a la conquavitat de la fistula, la qual has conprenduda am ferr.	But if the fistula is of long and deep depth, and follows its natural path, then you must insert it into the preon as far as possible for you, and accordingly, cleanse that from all its corrupted flesh; and accordingly, administer some wrapped in sharp medicines, and introduce those into the cavity of the fistula which you have understood with iron.
E fay aquo am aquela alcunas veguadas entro que la medicina acuta corroda tot aquo que es romas en la conquavitat de la fistula de la corrupcio.	And thus, with that, make it so some times until the sharp medicine has corroded all that remains in the cavity of the fistula from corruption.
E aprop restaura aquela am enguentz les quals engendran carn sana entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly, restore that with unguents which produce healthy flesh until it is healed.
Mays si no es sanada per aquo, lahoras tu cauteriza aquela segon que havem recomtat.	But if it is not healed by this, then you should cauterize it according to what we have recounted.
Mays si la causa de fistula es os e es deves tu certificat aquo, lahoras tu inquireys aquela e secca aquela segon que havem recomtat, si tu no prohibeys alcuna causa de vena o de nervi o de membre principal ayssi cum havem dit.	But if the cause of the fistula is bone and you are certain about it, then you should inquire into that and cleanse it according to what we have recounted, if you do not prohibit any cause of vein or nerve or main member as we have said.
Mays si le os es a tu descubert e es en lu alcuna corrupcio e negror, lahoras tu ratz aquel entro que la corrupcio sia hostada tota; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que lu encarne entro que sia sanat.	But if the bone is uncovered to you and it has some corruption and blackness, then you should remove that until all the corruption is removed; and accordingly, cure that with water which enters into it until it is healed.
E si no es sana e gieta brac ayssi cum fazia, lahoras sapias que tu no est pervengut a la eradicacio tota de la corrupcio; e adonc tu descuebre sobre lu segondanament e exquisitament fay la razio de lu e la mundificacio de lu am la deriera fortalasa tieua, e aprop restaura aquel.	And if it is not healed and grows crust like before, then you should know that you have not reached the total eradication of corruption; and therefore, you will uncover it again, carefully and exquisitely, make a reason for it and cleanse it with the last strength left in you, and accordingly restore it.
E donc si es sanat, bo es; e sino, lahoras sapias que aquela corrupcio es en la profunditat longinqua del cors, la qual no ha conseguida, e adonc a tu en aquel no es engen sino laysar aquela.	And therefore, if it is healed, good it is; and otherwise, you should know that this corruption is in the deep and distant part of the body, which has not been reached, and thus there is nothing for you to do but to leave it.
E si le os corromput es petit, o es a tu possible atirar aquel, lahora tu le atira am forceps subtils las quals conveno ad aquo.	And if the corrupted bone is small, or it is possible for you to attract it, then you should attract it with subtle forceps which are suitable for that.
E si so motz osses, lahoras exquisitament fay la extraccio de totz aquels, e de aquels no laysses denguna causa am la tua fortaleza.	And if there are many bones, then you should make the extraction of all those, and leave no cause for any reason with your strength.
Mays si a tu fa contrarietat alcuna causa de las humiditatz, e en lor inscizio no ha temor ni error, lahoras inscideys aquelas liaments o carns si so aqui, e deliura les osses.	But if you find any cause of the moistures which is contrary to your intention, and in its insight there is no fear or error, then you should insert those ligaments or flesh if they are here, and deliver the bones.
Mays si a tu no es preparacio de ostar les osses de la tua hora, lahoras pausa sobre la plagua aquo que poyresca la plagua aquela, e layssa aquela entro que aquo es al enviro de aquels osses de carns e de liamentz, e guarda la plagua que no sia consolidada, e sia constrengida la seccio la qual tu has inscidida en la tua operacio.	But if you are not prepared to remove the bones of your time, then pause over that wound which is causing the wound to fester, and leave it until that wound is in the environs of those bones of flesh and ligaments, and guard the wound so that it is not consolidated, and the section which you have inserted into your operation is constricted.
Habantz, si temes, pausa sobre lu coto submers en sopre trissat am oli, o coto submers en anguent egipciac, o en alcu dels enguentz vertz, quar quan poyriran aquelas liaments, e les osses son de lor seperatz la ablacio, e de aquels atraccio es alleujada.	They have it, if you fear, pause over the wound submerged in soap with oil, or wound submerged in Egyptian unguent, or in some of the green unguents, because when those ligaments putrefy, and the bones are separated from their ablation, and attraction is alleviated.
Mays si es un gran os ayssi cum le os de camba o de coyssa o semblantz ad aquels, e aquo que de lu es corromput es la facia de lu tant solament, lahoras ratz aquela am resio tant solament derriera entro que sia ostada aquela negror e corrupcio, e aprop restaura la plagua.	But if it is a great bone like the bone of the hip or the coccyx or similar to those, and that which is corrupted from it is only the surface of it, then you should remove that with scissors only as far back as necessary until that blackness and corruption is removed, and accordingly restore the wound.
Mays si aquo que de lu es corrumpyt es gran partida, e la corrupcio ja ha conseguida la medulla del os, lahoras es causa necessaria cerrar aquel e aquel tot inscidir entro al loc on es pervenguda la corrupcio, e lahoras cura aquel entro que sia consolidada.	But if that which is corrupted from it is a great part, and the corruption has already reached the marrow of the bone, then it is necessary to close it and insert all into the location where the corruption has spread, and then cure it until it is consolidated.
E yeu recomti a tu aquo que endevenc ad un home en la sua coyssa per que pausez aquela a eyssempli e adjutori sobre la tua operacio.	And I recommend to you that you approach one man in his own coccyx, so that you may pause over it and assist with your operation.
Foc un home jove per etat entorn xxx ans, al qual accideys dolor en la sua cueyssa, e de las partidas dedintz mauguda es sobre la materia dedintz le cors entro que la materia es pervenguda a la cueyssa, e es materia de apostema am gran apostema, e no foc a lu causa extrinseca.	A young man of about thirty years old, who feels pain in his coccyx, and the parts inside are swollen on the material inside the body until the material reaches the coccyx, and it is a matter of apostema with great apostema, and there is no external cause.
E adonc foc extendut le temps am aquela per la error dels metges entro que l’apostema es hubert, e acorrero de lu materias motas, e la sua curacio foc aprop pausada entro que la camba foc fistulada, e faytz son en lu motz orrificis les quals totz getavan poyredura e las humiditatz del cos.	And thus, the time was extended by the mistake of doctors until the apostema was hubert, and there was a flow of many materials from it, and its cure was accordingly paused until the hip was fistulated, and it made way for many orifices which all poured out putridity and the humors of the body.
E adonc le curec multitut de metges entorn dos ans, e no foc en aquels savia ma en la art, entro que yeu fu appelat.	And thus, many doctors were treating it for about two years, and they did not have knowledge in medicine, only in the art, until you were called.
E vi la camba de lu e las materias que corrian de lu aquels orrificis per gran cors; e ja le cos de aquel home era tot stabozit e la color de lu era citrina.	And I saw the hip of that man and the materials that were flowing from it through many orifices; and already the body of that man was totally stunted and his color was citrine.
E adonc yeu intromesi la tenta ad un de aquels orrificis e pervenguec la tenta al os.	And then I inserted a probe into one of those orifices and reached the bone.
E aprop yeu e perscrutat tostz les orrificis e trobegui aquels pervenir a lor de totas partidas de la camba.	And accordingly, I examined all the orifices and found those that reached their respective parts of the hip.
E adonc yeu me coytegui e inscidegui sobre un dels orrificis aquels entro que descrobegui una partida del os, e atrobegui aquel corromput, e ja era terros e corrumput e denigrat; e era ja corrumpuda una partida de la camba entro que havia penetrat entro a la mezola.	And then I cut and inserted myself into one of those orifices until I discovered a part of the bone, and I found it corrupted, and already it was rotten and corrupted and denigrated; and a part of the hip had already been corrupted to the extent that it had penetrated into the pelvis.
E adon yeu serregui aquo que a mi era discubert e preparat del os descubert.	And then I saw what was revealed and prepared for me from the discovered bone.
E yeu cujegui que no fos en le os sino aquela corrupcio la qual abscidigui e serregui, e yeu ja havia derraziguada.	And I saw that it was not in the bone, but rather that corruption which had consumed and destroyed, and I had already begun to desecrate.
E aprop pausegui la restauracio de la plagua am medicina consolidativas per lonc temps, e no es consolidada.	And accordingly, I paused the restoration of the wound with consolidative medicine for a long time, and it was not consolidated.
E aprop yeu iteregui e descubregui sobre le os segondament sobre le descubriment primier, e atrobegui continua corrupcio am le os.	And accordingly, I iterated and discovered again on the bone subsequently to the initial discovery, and found continued corruption in the bone.
E serregui aquo que a mi apares de aquela corrupcio, e aprop yeu fo perforsat fayre la curacio de lu e restauracio, e no es restaurat.	And I saw that what appeared to me from that corruption was not sufficient for the cure and restoration of it, and accordingly, I was forced to make the operation and restore it, but it was not restored.
E adonc yeu descubri sobre lu autra veguada e no cessegui inscidir le os petit a petit particuladament e perforsa la restauracio de lu, e no es restaurat entro que inscidigui entorn un palm de lu, e aquel extraxi am la medula sua, e aprop restauregui aquel am medicinas, e es consolidat leugierament e sanat.	And then I discovered again on the other side and did not cease to insert into the small bone little by little, particularly, and forced the restoration of it, but it was not restored until I inserted around a palm's width from it, and that extracted with its own marrow, and accordingly, I restored it with medicines, and it was consolidated slightly and healed.
E no es necessaria iteracio en la operacio de lu e seccio de lu sino per la disposicio de la freulesa de lu e per la paucitat de la tollerancia de lu e paor de lu de mort, quar a lu accidia en totas horas per superfluitat de evacuacio sincopi mala.	And there is no need for iteration in the operation of it and section of it, except by the disposition of the friar of it and by the paucity of tolerance of it and fear of death, because to it occurs at all hours due to superfluous evacuation syncopal bad.
E donc sanat es per sanacio entiera, e nada es en loc de os carn dura; e es fayta bona la disposicio de lu en le sieu cors e retornec la vertut de lu; e es conversat en las suas disposicios e no fec a lu contrarietat en ambulacio ni nocument en denguna causa.	And thus, the healing is by total healing, and nothing remains in place of bone hard flesh; and good disposition has been made for it within its own body, and the virtue of it returns; and it is converted into its own dispositions, and does not make contrariety in walking or harm to any cause.
Mays si es os eminent en loc del cors ja trauquat, lahoras cove que tu secces aquel segon aquesta manieyra: e es que tu prenguas liament e strenh aquel en la extremitat de aquel os eminent, e comanda ad alcu que extenda aquel en sus; e pausa aquel liament de lana pus gros del primier liament; e aprop lia aquel sobre la carn que es dejos le os, e exten la extramitat de lu per que atires la carn a las partidas dejos, e tu descuebras la carn sobre le loc le qual voles serrar per que la serra no leda la carn.	But if it is bone prominent in the body already traumatized, then you must cut that according to this manner: and it is that you take a ligament and stretch that at the end of that prominent bone, and command someone to extend it; and pause that ligament of coarse wool more than the first ligament; and accordingly, bind that over the flesh that remains on the bone, and extend the extremity of it so that you can draw the flesh to the parts left, and you uncover the flesh on the place which you want to cut off so that the cut does not harm the flesh.
E pausa fust o taula dejos le os decentment, quar quan tu fas aquo no es prohibida la serra que no secce la carn corrumpuda.	And pause the knife or table over the bone decently, for when you do this, it is not prohibited to cut off the corrupt flesh.
E cove que sia la serradura sobre le loc corrumput petit a petit, quar si es en la concavitat del os corrupcio e no appar en la sua apparicio al sentiment, e forssa a serratura de lu autra veguada.	And it is necessary that the cutting be done over the corrupt area little by little, because if there is corruption in the concavity of the bone and it does not appear in its appearance to the sense, and you are forced to cut off another part.
E si le os es corrumput e no-eminent, abantz es la una partida continuada am la autra, e la corrupcio es al mieg loc o en partida de lu, lahoras tu descuebre la carn de totas partz tota; e aprop pausa fust dejos, e aprop serra aquel de la primiera partida la on es la corrupcio entro que sia continuada la serratura del autra partida.	And if the bone is corrupted and not prominent, it is more likely that one part continues into another, and the corruption is in the middle or a part of it; then you will uncover all parts of the flesh entirely; and accordingly, pause your knife, and accordingly, cut off that from the first part where the corruption is until the cutting of the other part is continued.
E sia la serradura segon le loc de la corrupcio un petit, segon que havem dit.	And be the cutting according to the location of the corruption a little, as we have said.
E si la corrupcio es en la junctura, inscideys aquela junctura corrumpuda, e serra le os la on es continuat del autra part.	And if the corruption is at the joint, cut into that corrupted joint, and cut off the bone where it continues from the other part.
E si de la corrupcio es en la continuacio de doas juncturas, lahoras no es en lu razio sino engen.	And if the corruption is in the continuation of two joints, then it is not in reason but by nature.
E si la corrupcio es en le pecte de la ma o del pe, es mot dificil; empero cove que tu inquieras la corrupcio en qual manieyra appareys a tu, e que abradas aquela, e mondes aquela segon quascuna disposicio la qual es a tu possibla, e am cascum engen sia rectificat a tu, quan no fa a tu contrarietat vena o nervi.	And if the corruption is in the chest of the arm or leg, it is quite difficult; however, you must investigate the corruption in which manner it appears to you, and cut into that, and cleanse that according to any disposition that is possible for you, and with each case, rectify what is contrary to you, when it does not affect veins or nerves.
E sapias qual es inscididors e las serras a inscidir aquestz osses son motz segon le situament dels osses, e la preparacio de aquels, e la grosseza de aquels, e la subtilitat e la grandeza e la parvitat de aquels, e la duricia e la lor raritat; per que cove que tu prepares a tota specia de operacio estrument convenient ad aquela opperacio.	And you should know what instruments are used and the saws to cut into these bones are many according to the situation of the bones, and the preparation of those, and their thickness, subtlety, greatness, smallness, hardness, and rarity; therefore, it is necessary that you prepare for all kinds of operations and instruments suitable for that operation.
E sapias que aquela operacio significa a tu sobre la specia del strument del qual indigeysses; quan am tu es gran studi e lonc e conoyssensa de las manieyras de aquesta art, e testimoni de manieyras de malautias, quar lahoras ja tu las avias per tu meteys aquo que es convenient a lu dels sturmentz a tota malautia.	And you should know that this operation means to you about the kind of instrument which you need; when with you is great study and long and deep knowledge of the manners of this art, and witness to the mannerisms of diseases, for then you already have them for yourself, what is convenient to all instruments for every disease.
E yeu so a tu formant en la fi de aquest capitol le nombre dels instrumentz les quals pausaras cum eyssimples am les quals proceziras a la tua prohibicio la qual experimentaras sobre las autras.	And I shall present to you the list of instruments which will pause with you as simple ones, with which you will proceed to your prohibition which you will experience on others.
Forma de serra:	Forma of saw:
Forma de autra serra:	Form of another saw:
Forma de autra serra:	Form of another saw:
Forma de autra serra gran:	Form of another great saw:
Forma de ray:	Form of Ray:
Sia le cap de aquest ray segon la forma de cap de clau stellat, e les puntz de lu sian segon la forma dels puntz alstefegi.	So the head of this saw is like the head of a star-shaped key, and its points are shaped like those of an astelfigi.
E no conveneys sino que am aquel sian confricadatz les caps de las juncturas quan so corrumpudas, o es la boca gran ampla.	And it is not suitable to use this saw except when the heads of the joints are confricated (i.e., crushed or broken) and are corrupted, or if there is a large and wide mouth.
Forma de razori major dels autres:	Form of the largest razor among others:
Forma de razori menor:	Form of the smaller razor:
Forma de razori lat:	Form of the large razor:
Forma de serra autra decentment fayta: sia fayt arc de lu pus sobira e la acuitat de lu de ferr, e le membre de lu de boys punhal descentment fayt.	Form of another saw decently made:
Forma de lu:	Form of it:
Forma de razori en la qual ha concavitat:	Form of the razor with concavity:
Forma de razori autra subtil:	Form of another subtle razor:
Forma de autra razori de curvada extremitat:	Form of another curved-edge razor:
Forma de rasori petit semblant a tenta:	Form of a small razor resembling a probe:
Forma de incisori am le qual so inscidit les osses:	Form of an instrument used to cut bones:
Forma de inscisori autra minor:	Form of another smaller instrument used to cut:
Forma de un autra inscissori; aquest semblant a ray, e la extremitat de lu es cum serra, e es exhibit en motz locs en la razio dels osses:	Form of another instrument resembling a saw:
Forma de ray lo qual conveneys a rasio de aquel que es perforat dels osses:	Form of a saw that is suitable for cutting through bones:
E la extremitat de lu es triangulada e de aguda extremitat.	And the tip of it is triangular and has a sharp edge.
E es fayt de ferr de India , e semblantment cove que totas las causas que havem ditas de rasoris e de inscissoris e de serras.	And it is made of Indian iron, and similarly, it seems that all the causes we have discussed regarding razors, instruments, and saws are applicable to this instrument as well.
De inscizio extremitatz e de la serratura dels osses.	And it is used for cutting into extremities and cutting through bones.
Las extremitatz se poyresso o per causa intrinseca o per causa extrinseca, o cum tu auras medicat aquela corrupcio per curacio de aquelas medicinas e la curacio no comfereys, o vezes la corrupcio anar deves le membre la qual no percuteys denguna causa, lahoras cove que tu inscidas aquel membre entro aquo la hon acossec la corrupcio, per que le malaute evasesca per aquo de mort o de malicia que es major defeliment del membre.	The extremities can be affected either by an internal cause or an external cause, or as you will medicate that corruption with those medicines and the cure does not conform, sometimes the corruption goes to the member which is not struck by any cause. Then it is necessary for you to cut into that member until the harm caused by the corruption reaches a certain point, so that the sick person escapes from death or malice which is greater than the defect of the member.
E le senhal de aquel al qual accideys, es que·l membre es fayt negre entro que sia cujat que foc la ja comburit, o se poyreys aprop la negror entro que la poyredura aquela ane entro aquel membre que siec lu e que prengua tot le cors; e donc coyta te am inscizio de aquel.	And the sign of that to which it happens is when the member becomes black until it is cut and burned, or if you can bring the blackness closer so that the burning goes into that member that is like it and takes over the whole body; and thus you must take account of this.
E semblantment si es causa de la corrupcio percussio de alcunas causas venenosas ayssi cum de scorpio mari o de vupera o de rutela e de semblantz.	And similarly, if it is a cause of corruption due to the sting of certain venomous causes such as the scorpion of the sea or the viper or the ratel and similar ones.
E si la corrupcio o la percussio es en la extremitat del dit, lahoras tu inscideys le dit e no dones spazi a la corrupcio per que ane entro a la ma.	And if the corruption or sting is in the tip of the finger, then you must cut off the finger and not give space to the corruption so that it does not enter into the hand.
E semblantment si accedeys a la ma, lahoras tu inscideys aquela de la razit del focil, e no dones spazi a la corrupcio entro que prengua en le focil del bras.	And similarly, if it reaches the hand, then you must cut off that of the wrist, and not give space to the corruption so that it does not take hold in the armpit of the arm.
E si envezeys aquel, lahoras inscideys le bras entro al coyde en la junctura.	And if it reaches the arm, then you must cut off the arm at the shoulder joint.
E si passa otra la corrupcio e la vezes enviro le coyde, lahoras en aquel es la mort del malaute; e aministrar autra causa otra aquo en curacio es quantitat de vertut.	And if the corruption passes and spreads around the shoulder joint, then in that case it is the death of the patient; and to administer another cause other than this one in cure is a quantity of virtue.
E semblantment fay del pe quan corrupcio envezeys le dit del pe, lahoras tu inscideys aquel entro ad un dels nozes.	And similarly, when corruption reaches the toe of the foot, then you must cut off that at one of the joints.
E si pren en la pente del pe, lahoras tu inscideys tot le pe.	And if it takes hold at the ankle of the foot, then you must cut off the entire foot.
Mays si pueja entro al denol, lahoras tu inscideys la camba entro a la junctura del denol.	But if it penetrates into the leg, then you must cut off the thigh at the junction of the leg.
E si la corrupcio ja es pervenguda sobre le denol, lahoras en lu no es engen sino dimissio, e layssar le malaute a la mort.	And if corruption has already prevailed over the leg, then in that case there is no remedy, but only dismissal, and leaving the patient to death.
E la manieyra de inscidir le membre o de serrar lu es que tu strenhas le liament en la partida pus dejos la qual voles inscidir, e strenh autre liament sobre le loc; e extenda le ministre un liament a las partidas dejos, e extenda le ministra autra liament en sus; e tu separa la carn la qual es entre dos liamentz ain spatum lat entro que sia descuberta tota la carn; e aprop sia inscidit o serrat.	And the method of cutting off the limb or sawing it is that you strengthen one ligament at the part farthest from where you want to cut, and stretch another ligament over the location; and extend one minister's ligament to the parts behind, and extend the other minister's ligament on top; and you separate the flesh which is between two ligaments, leaving a gap about as wide as the thickness of a spatula, so that all the flesh is revealed; and then it is cut or sawed.
E cove que sia pausat drap de li de totas partidas per so que no toque le loc sa, e que vengua al malaute lesio ajustada e apostema caut.	And it is necessary that a cloth be placed over all the parts so that the location is not touched, and that the wound comes to the patient adjusted and cauterized.
Mays si accideys flux de sanc quan obras, lahoras tu cauteriza le loc coytadament, o pausa sus lu alcunas polveras restrenhentz le sanc; e aprop retorna a la tua medicacio entro que sia complida.	But if bleeding occurs during the operation, then you must cauterize the location calmly, or pause for a moment and use some binding powders to staunch the bleeding; and then return to your treatment until it is complete.
E aprop lia le membre plaguat am liament al u convenient, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And then apply a ligature to the wounded limb at a convenient point, and cure that until it is healed.
E yeu recomti a tu aquo que endevenc a un home en le sieu pe, aquest meteys accident le qual yeu e a tu recomtat, le qual es quar accidic a lu negror en le sieu pe am adustio que era asemblada a combustio de foc.	And I recommend to you that you attempt to heal a man whose toe is affected by this accident which we and you have recounted, which is when it becomes black in his foot with an inflammation that was assembled as if by the combustion of fire.
E aquela corrupcio accidic primierament en le sieu dit entro que tendec tot le pe.	And that corruption began first in his toe and spread throughout the foot.
E adonc aquel home preparec per si meteys pus que vic la curacio anar al membre am la vehemencia de lu que atrobec de dolor e de adustrio de lu, e el inscidic aquel pe entro a la junctura, e foc sanat.	And then that man prepared himself for the possibility that pus would come out and the cure would go to the member with the vehemence of his pain and inflammation of it, and he cut off that foot at the junction, and it became healthy.
Lonc temps accidic a lu aquela meteyssa corrupcio en le dit de la ma indic.	For a long time, that corruption had spread to the finger of his hand.
E adonc venc a mi, e so me perforsat repercutir aquela superfluitat am aquo que pausegui sobre la ma de las medicinas, aprop la mundificacio del cos de lu; e no es repercussa la superfluitat e comensec anar al autra dit entro que comensec en la ma.	And then it came to me, and thus I perceived the surplus of that corruption above which was suspended over his hand with regard to the medicines, so that the purging of his body began; and no longer was the surplus reflected back, but instead it began to move towards another finger in his hand.
E el apelec me a inscidir la ma de lu, e yeu no volgui far aquo sperant sobre la repercussio de aquela superfluitat, e mays que temegui deves la inscizio de la ma de lu mort, quar la vertut del malaute era sobre cazement.	And he asked me to cut off his hand, and I did not want to do that, hoping instead for the reflection of that surplus back onto itself, but rather fearing the amputation of his hand, since the patient's vital force was already at a low ebb.
E pus que el se desperec de mi, es retornat en la sua terra e pervenguec a mi que aquel home preparec e inscidic la sua ma tota, e es sanat.	And since he departed from me, he returned to his land and reported to me that the man had prepared and cut off his entire hand, and it was healed.
E no he adhuzida aquesta narracio sino per que sia adjutori sobre aquo que catz de aquesta malautia, e que sia significacio per la qual sia significada e segon la qual sia obrat.	And I have not narrated this story except to serve as an aid for those who seek to understand this disease, and to provide a signification by which it may be interpreted and acted upon.
De cura sinuum et qualitate clisterizationis cum medicinis.	The care of wounds and the quality of cleansing with medicines.
Quan accideys apostema en alcus membres carnozes e·l spazi de l’apostema es prolonguat entro que fa colleccio de sania, e aprop es romput e perforat, e es eyssida de lu la sania, e roman le loc vuoyt quays cum si era vayssel, e la codena que es desobre lu ayssi cum drap subtiliat, e no es pervengut a deriera corrupcio, e no inprimeys en le os o en nervi ni en liament, es apelat sinu, e no es nompnat fistula.	When an abscess occurs in some flesh and the space of the abscess is prolonged to form a collection of pus, and it is broken and perforated, and the pus is discharged from it, and the location remains open like a vessel, with a covering that is like thin cloth, and there is no further corruption, and it does not penetrate into bone or nerve or ligament, it is called a sinus, and it is not named fistula.
Mays empero si le spazi es prolonguat entro que la corrupcio enprema en alcun membre, lahoras es appelada fistula e no zukem.	But if the space is prolonged to the point where corruption enters into some member, then it is called a fistula and not a sinus.
E la cura de lu es que inscidas aquela codena tota ayssi cum es revolvut, e majorment quan es subtiliada e es fayta cum drap, e comfizas que no adhereys al loc per la sua corrupcio.	And the cure for this is that you cut out that covering entirely, as it is revolved, and especially when it is thinned out and made like cloth, and make sure that it does not stick to the location due to its corruption.
Mays si tu speras que la codena adheresca e que aquela corrupcio no aja conseguit per deriera consecucio, e en la codena ha spassitut de cara, lahoras tu cura aquel am clisteri.	But if you think that the covering will stick and that the corruption has not had its due consequence, and in the covering there has been a change of direction, then you cure that with poultice.
E es que consideras al sinu, e lahoras si es gran, e·l brac que yeys es de fetent odor, lahoras clisteriza aquel am medicament egipciac le qual es de oli e vi agre e ziniar recebent partidas enguals, e sian ajustadas en un vayssel, e sian coytas sobre le foc entro que’l medicament se fassa rog e pervengua a specitut de mel.	And so you consider the sinus, and then if it is large, and the arm that you have is of the kind that gives off an odor, then apply poultice to that with Egyptian medicine which is made from oil, vinegar, and zingiber receiving equal parts, and be adjusted in a vessel, and be poured over the fire until the medicine becomes rough and turns into a substance like honey.
E aprop tu pren de lu aquo que es necessari e dissolveys lu am aygua e mel; e clisteriza am aquel le sinu, e strenh le orrifici de lu, e layssa la medicina en lu per la quantitat de doas horas.	And then you take from it the water that is necessary and dissolve it with equal parts of water and honey; and apply poultice to that sinus, and strengthen the opening of it, and leave the medicine in it for the amount of two hours.
E aprop extratz aquela am sprecio; e fay aquo per tantz dias entro que sia mundificat le sinu e sia remauguda la pudor.	And then you extract that abscess; and make it so for as many days as is necessary until the sinus is cleansed and the stench is removed.
E alcunas veguadas es clisterizat am aygua de cendre, quan no es a tu prezent aquest medicament; e es que tu prenguas la cendra de vitz, e met sobre lu aygua; e aprop cola aquela e clisteriza aquel am ela entro que te confizes que·l sinu lahoras es ostat.	And sometimes it is applied with ash water, when this medicine is not present; and it is that you take the ash of vines, and put it on top of water; and then mix it together and apply poultice to that with it until you are convinced that the sinus is closed.
E si le malaute no ha tollerancia sobre le medicament egipciac ni l’aygua de la cendre, lahoras clisteriza aquel am aygua e mel e quays sia mesclat ziniar trissat, e clisteriza aquel am vi e mel mesclat, quar de proprietat de mel es que mondifique e lave, e le vi fa adherir le sinu, e majorment quan en le vi ha superfluitat de stipticitat e de siccitat.	And if the patient does not have tolerance for Egyptian medicine or ash water, then apply poultice to that with honey and water mixed with a small amount of zingiber shredded, and then apply poultice to that with vinegar and honey mixed, because the property of honey is that it purifies and cleanses, and vinegar makes the sinus adhere, and especially when in vinegar there is an excess of stiptic and drying properties.
E cum tu fas aquo alcunas veguadas e te comfizes que·l sinu ja es remaugut, lahoras clisteriza aquel am aquo que fa naysser la carn en lu.	And when you do this several times and are convinced that the sinus is now removed, then apply poultice to that with water that makes the skin appear in it.
E es que prenguas de enguent dyafinicon e dissolveys aquel am oli rozat e vi stiptic; o que clisterizas aquel am alcunas medicinas e enguentz autres que hajan las proprietatz les quals ja he yeu scritz en le tractat dels enguents.	And it is that you take from the divine dyafinicon and dissolve it with rose oil and stiptic vinegar; or that you apply poultice to that with several medicines and other substances that have properties such as those which I have already written in the treatise on medicines.
E si le orrifici del sinu es streyt en le qual no es recebuda la canula del clisteri, lahoras tu le amplifique aquel am ferr petit a petit, e pausa en lu calgua envolopada en enguent egipciac o en enguent basilicon entro que sia amplificat.	And if the opening of the sinus is narrow and cannot receive the canula of the poultice, then you amplify that with a small iron tool bit by bit, and pause in it wrapped in Egyptian or basilic cloth until it is amplified.
E semblantment si le orrifici es ample, lahoras tu agregua las labias de lu am sutura e layssa de lu quantitat en la qual intre le clisteri ses addicio.	And similarly, if the opening is wide, then you add the lips of it with a suture and leave it in such quantity that the poultice can be added to it.
E si le orrifici de lu del qual corr le brac es elevat a las partidas desus, lahoras secca aquel en le pus bas loc que es en lu per que le brac corra entro dejos, quar quan le brac es coartat en la preondeza de sinu la carn esser en lu engendrada.	And if the opening of that from which the arm flows is elevated to the parts above, then dry that in the lowest part of it so that the arm flows into it, because when the arm is constricted in the swelling of the sinus, the flesh will be generated in it.
E si no es a tu possible seccar le sinu entro al enviro del os pus bas segon que voles, lahoras te perforssa que prepares le membre am preparacio per la qual corr de lu le brac leugierament segon que es a tu apparelhat e que no sia en lu retengut alcuna causa del brac.	And if it is not possible to dry the sinus within the environs of the bone, then you should perforate the member with preparation for which the arm will flow slightly according to your apparel and that there be no reason in it for the arm to be retained.
E pren medicinas consolidativas que sian pausadas sobre le sinu convenientz ad aquo que vols exxten aquelas sobre drap de li.	And take consolidative medicines that are placed on the sinus in a way that you want to extend them onto cloth.
E le drap sia de tan gran quantitat cum fa la comunicacio de tot le sinu; e aprop inscidey am las forfexs en le dreyt del orrifici del sinu un trauc pus ample un pauc que l’orrifici del sinu; e aprop exten sobre autre drap de li dels enguentz leons segon la quantitat del trauc, e pausa le sobre aquel per posicio longinqua del orrifici del sinu per que sia aleujat le eyssiment del brac de lu e no ostes le drap gran sino aprop alcus dyas una veguada.	And the cloth should be of such great quantity that it makes communication with all the sinus; and then cut out the folds in the right side of the opening of the sinus, making a channel slightly wider than the opening of the sinus; and then extend over another cloth of linen the leon's enguents according to the quantity of the channel, and pause on that for a long position near the opening of the sinus so that it eases the exit of the arm from there and does not tear off the cloth too quickly.
Mays aquel que es sobre le orrifici del sinu, le qual remauguas en tota hora per so que yesca aquo que es ajust en lu del brac.	But that which is on the opening of the sinus, which remains in all its hour because it is adjusted to the arm.
E per que sapias si aquo que corr de lu del brac es mot o pauc, o es digest, o es no-digest.	And so that you can know if what comes out from the arm is much or little, or is digested, or is not digested.
E am aysso tu considera le loc de aquel sinu, si en lu sent le pacient dolor o no, e si es en lu apostema.	And at this point you consider the location of that sinus, if in it the patient feels pain or not, and if there is an abscess.
E cum la tua medicacio es prolonguada en la tal manieyra, e vesas la matiera que es gitada sobre le orrifici del sinu ja adhereys, o se apropria adherencia, lahoras le mayti tu le deslia o le tertz dia, e quan deslias la plagua, lahoras muda le drap per autre e renova le enguent.	And when your medication is prolonged in this way, and you see the matter that is dropped on the opening of the sinus already sticking or approaching adhesion, then dry it out with a cloth or a small tool on the third day, and when you remove the dressing, then change the cloth for another and renew the poultice.
Mays si del sinu aprop lon spazi yeys virus subtil, lahoras no te desperes de la adherencia de li, quar la sanacio de lu se apropria, quar so alcus homes en les quals tarda generacio de carn en las lors plaguas, e de aquels so en les quals es fayt le contrari de lu.	But if from the sinus there is too little space for a subtle virus to be present, then do not despair of its adhesion, because the healing of it is approaching, because some people in whom tardy generation of flesh occurs in their wounds, and others are in those in which the opposite occurs.
E si del sinu aprop motz dias es yssit brac indigest, lahoras sapias que·l sinu no adhereys; e si es tardada la adherencia del sinu e es la causa prolonguada, lahoras tu ajusta en exsiccacio de las medicinas, e si las medicinas so humidas en lor substancia e en la sua vertut, son seccas ayssi cum enguent dyafinicon, quan es en lu ajustada superfluitat de addicio de zegi.	And if from the sinus it takes many days for an undigested arm to be present, then you will know that the sinus does not adhere; and if the adhesion of the sinus is delayed and is the cause prolonged, then you adjust in exsiccation of medicines, and if the medicines are moist in their substance and virtue, they are dried out like enguent dyafinicon, when there is an excessive addition of zegi.
E le mays derier am le qual es curat, es que prenguas de enguent dyafinicon e sia dissout en oli rozat, e sia sobre lu vojat vi antic engual en la sua substancia, e aprop comfeys aquel am lu, e usa de aquel.	And the most later of all is that which is cured, that you take from dyafinicon and dissolve it in rose oil, and apply it to the wound with an old equal substance, and then confirm that on it, and use that.
E ja fa semblant en aquela accio, quan no y a brac, enguent dyafinicon, mel quan es coyt entro que sia engrossat, e usa de lu; o que prenguas mirra e aloen e enses, e trissa tot e polveriza sobre le mel quan es sus le foc, e aprop lineys aquo sobre drap e strenh aquel sobre le sinu; e lineys aquel am le mel le qual has cuoyt entro que es engrossat, e polveriza sobre drap e strenh aquel.	And it seems so in that action, when there is no brac, dyafinicon, and honey when it is mixed into being thickened, and use it; or that you take myrrh and aloen and onions, and grind everything together and powderize it over the honey when it is on the fire, and then line it up with water on cloth and stretch it over the sinus; and line it up with the honey which has been mixed into being thickened, and powderize it on cloth and stretch it.
E alcunas veguadas so administratz am lu aristologia longua e razitz de lili celesti (e es lili celesti) e farina de errs e centaurea, e usa de aquels simples o ajustatz, trissa aquels e cribela e polveriza sobre le mel le qual he recomtat; e husa de lu.	And some times it is administered at the aristological long and razed of celestial lily (and it is celestial lily) and farina of errors and centaurea, and use those simples or adjust them, grind them together and powderize them over the honey which has been recounted; and husk it.
E si es prolonguat le sinu, e no es sanat per aquesta curacio, lahoras sapias que la corrupcio es en le preon de lu, e ja fa enquisicio en les osses o en les autres membres durs o als liaments; lahoras tu le cura am curacio fistular, ayssi cum desus es dit.	And if the sinus is prolonged and does not heal with this treatment, then you will know that the corruption is in the preon of it, and already inquiry is made in the bones or in the other hard members or ligaments; then you cure it with fistular treatment, just as above is said.
De curacio de panarici et unguis attritae et incisione digiti additi et sectione.	Of the cure of panarici, and unguis attritae, and incision of finger added, and section.
Panarici es apostema le qual nays dejos la ungla del dit pous de la ma o del pe, e fort leu nays en les autres ditz, e cum es prolonguat e la sua curacio es mens prezada, o es apostemat de apostema caut, o es corrumput, e gieta brac entro que corrodeys la razitz de la ungla, e fort leu corromp aquela tota, e fort leu perve la sua corrupcio al os entro que es a lu odor fetent, e es fayta la extremitat del dit lada, e la color de lu es fayta fusca.	Panarici is an abscess that leaves behind the nail of the toe or finger, and spreads quickly to other fingers, and when it is prolonged and its cure is less valued, or it becomes apostematized with caution, or it becomes corrupted, and throws forth brackish water within which corrodes the root of the nail, and quickly corrupts that entirely, and quickly pervades its corruption to the bone, and makes a fetid odor, and causes the extremity of the finger to become gangrenous.
E donc quan tu auras aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no comfereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que tu inscidas am ferr tota la superfluitat que es romasa de la ungla e aprop cauteriza la plagla aprop aquo, quar cauteri mot es juvatiu en aysso.	And therefore when you have that which we have said in the division and do not confirm your cure, then it is necessary that you inscribe with iron all the superfluitat that remains of the nail and appropriate cauterize the wound with water, for cauterization is most helpful in this case.
Mays si le os es sa e la ungla es sana, e las addicios de la ungla vuoydas ja compremen las carns a las partidas dedintz, e comensan lu punger e ledeysso aquela, lahoras cove que tu pauses ray subtil dejos le angle de la ungla que pungeys la carn, e impelleys aquela sus e inscideys aquela carn am facilitat, e pausa sobre aquo que roman de la carn de las medicinas comburentz corrosivas entro que sia tot remaugut; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	But if the bone is sound and the nail is healthy, and the adductions of the nail are already compressing the flesh to the parts outside, and begin to prick and lead it away from that place, then you must pause a fine ray below the angle of the nail that pricks the flesh, and push it up and inscribe it into the flesh with ease, and pause over what remains of the flesh of the medicines combining corrosive substances until it is all removed; and then cure that with poultices until it is healed.
Mays si la corrupcio ja enprem en le os, lahoras cove que tu inscidas le os aquel e le extraguas, car nul temps no es sanat que sia en lu le os corrumput.	But if the corruption has already taken hold in the bone, then you must inscribe the bone and extract it, for no time is there healing that is corrupted in the bone.
E si vezes la corrozio e la corupcio anar en le dit, lahoras tu inscideys aquel en un dels nozes segons que es premesa la sua rememoracio, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if at times the corrosion and corruption go into the digit, then you must inscribe it in one of the joints according to the premonition of its reminiscence, and appropriate cure that until it is healed.
Mays si a la ungla endeve percussio o atricio, e endeve en aquela dolor vehement, lahoras cove que tu al comensament fleubotomes le malaute, e aprop secca la ungla am spatum agut am seccio transversa desus en jus, e guarda te que la seccio no pervengua entro a la carn que es dejos la ungla, quar tu faras accidir al malaute dolor vehement, e sira causa a nativitat de la carn ajustada superflua en le loc; e aprop cura aquel loc am aquo que ceda dolor.	But if the nail is inflamed with percussion or attrition, and inflames in that place with a vehement pain, then you must first fleubotomize the malady, and then secate the nail with a sharp spatula in a transverse section from top to bottom, and be careful not to allow the section to penetrate into the flesh that is left behind the nail, for you would make the malady cause a vehement pain, and thus cause unnecessary birth of superfluous flesh in that place; and then cure that place with what relieves pain.
Mays dit ajustat, le qual es nat en las mas de alcus homes, fort leu es carnos tot, e fort leu so en lu osses, o fort leu es en lu ungla.	But it is said that this adjustment is natural in many men, and for many is all flesh, or for many is in the bones, or for many is in the nail.
E alcus de lu son natz en la razit de la junctura, o es la nativitat de lu en alcus nozes dels ditz.	And some of them are born in the root of the joint, or is the birthplace of them in certain joints of the fingers.
Mays aquel que es nat en alcus nozes del dit no se mau, e aquest que es nat en las juncturas fort leu es maugut.	But that which is born in certain joints of the finger does not become mad, and that which is born in the junctures is very much maddened.
E de aquels que son natz carnoses, la seccio es leugiera, e es que tu inscidas aquel deves la sua razitz am spatum lat.	And from those who are born of flesh, the section is easy, and it is that you must inscribe the root with a sharp spatula.
Mays de aquel que es nat en la razitz de la junctura, la curacio es dificil; e donc guarda te de la abscizio de lu.	But from those who are born in the root of the joint, the cure is difficult; and therefore beware of the abscess of it.
Mays en aquel que es nat en dit deves les nozes, cove que tu inscidas al comensament la carn de lu am inscizio redonda entro al os, e aprop serra am una de aquelas serras convenientz ad aquo, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	But in that which is born of the digit, thou must first cut off the joints, and then inscribe with a round instrument into the bone, and afterwards saw with one of those saws suitable for this, and then cure that until it is healed.
Mays consolidacio la qual accideys als ditz entre lor motas veguadas o per nativitat del home que nays enayssi, o per consolidacio de plagua o per combustio de foc, o per semblantz, adonc cove que secces aquela consolidacio entro que les ditz retorno a la sua forma natural.	But the consolidation that occurs in the fingers between their joints or due to the nativity of the human being who is born with it, or due to the consolidation of a wound or due to combustion by fire, or for similar reasons, therefore you must cut away that consolidation until the fingers return to their natural form.
E aprop pausa entre lor draps de li enfuzes en oli rozat per que no sian consolidatz leugierament, e separa entre aquels, o pausa entre aquels una lamina de plom subtil entro que sia consolidat segon que cove.	And then pause between their folds with a little oil rose for not being consolidated lightly, and separate those, or pause between those one thin layer of lead so that it is consolidated according to what is needed.
E semblantment si accideys consolidacio en alcus ditz am la palma, lahoras tu secca aquela consolidacio segon que es preparada e conveneys a la figura del membre.	And similarly if consolidation occurs in some fingers at the palm, then you must cut away that consolidation according to what is prepared and conforms to the shape of the member.
De inscizio de vices, so son varicas.	Of the inscription of vice, there are several.
Vices so son varicas, e so venas envolutas grossas plenas de superfluitatz melencolicas las quals veno en motz dels membres del cors, e le major adveniment de lor en las cambas, e majorment en las cambas dels itinerantz e dels laborantz e dels portantz.	Vices are varicas, and so are veins enveloped in thick, full of superfluous melancholic fluids that come forth from the members of the body, and the most common occurrence of theirs is in the hips, and especially in the hips of travelers, laborers, and carriers.
Adonc cove que tu administres purguacio del cors de colera negra alcunas veguadas am expulcio fort, e aprop sangna le pacient de la vena basilica.	Therefore it is necessary that you administer purgation of the body with black cholera several times with strong expulsion, and then bleed the patient from the Basilic vein.
Mays la curacio de lor am ferr es segon dos manieyras: la una es que sia inscizas e sia atirat aquel sanc negre, e l’autra manieyra es que sia elevada la vena e sia extrayta tota.	But the cure of theirs with iron is according to two methods: one is that you inscribe and attract that black blood, and the other method is that you elevate the vein and extract all.
La seccio de lu es segon aquesta manieyra: embroca al comensament la camba am aygua cauda mot entro que le sanc gros sia resolvut, que es feculent de la camba, e aprop strenh la camba del malaute a la partida pus sobirana de la coyssa entro a la partida dejos del denol am una benda, e aprop secca la vena en un loc, o en dos, o en tres am seccio ampla, e aprop eleva le sanc negra am la tieua ma de la partida dejos de la camba entro en sus, e desus en jus, entro que del sanc sia yssida la quantitat que voles e que vezes habastar, e la qual tollera la vertut del malaute.	The section of this is according to this method: first, take the hip with cold water and make it moist until the thick blood is resolved, which is turbid from the hip, and then strengthen the hip of the patient at the highest point of the coccyx, and above that, above the denounment, with a bandage, and then cut off the vein in one place, or two, or three, with a wide section, and then raise the black blood by the tieua of the partition below the hip, from top to bottom, until the desired quantity of blood is removed, which takes away the virtue of the patient.
E aprop lia aquela, e comanda a lu que abstengua de las viandas colera negra engendrantz.	And then lie down, and command to him that he abstain from foods that generate black cholera.
E itera la curacio per fleubotomia quan las venas so umplidas e aquo notz al malaute.	And iterate the cure by phlebotomy when the veins are filled and this is noticed to the patient.
Mays la elevacio de lor es segon aquesta manieyra: tu que razas la camba del malaute, si en lu so motz pels, e aprop met le en banh e embroca la camba de lu am aygua cauda entro que s’enrogesesca e las venas sian exuberadas; o que sia exercitat per exercici fort, si banh no es a tu present, entro que·l membre sia scalfat.	But the elevation of theirs is according to this method: you who raise the hip of the patient, if it is covered with moss (mots pels), and then put it in a bath and wrap the hip with cold water until it becomes red and the veins are filled; or that he be exercised by strong exercise, even without bath, until the member is warm.
E aprop secsa la codena en le dreyt de la vena per seccio en le lonc o en le derier de lu deves le denol, o en le pus bas de lu deves lo talo.	And then cut the cord (codena) in the right side of the vein for a section in the long or end part of it, or in the lower part of it, you should make the hole (lo talo).
E aprop uobre la codena am uncis e excorja la vena de tota part entro que appara al sentiment, e es deves la appericio de lu que vezes aquela roga declinant a negror.	And then fill the cord (codena) with unguents and scrape off the vein from all parts until it appears to the sensation, and be aware of that which times that part often asks for darkness.
E donc cum evazeys e de la codena tu vezes aquela blanca quays sia corda.	And thus, as you take away (cum evazeys) the cord (codena), and the white substance that is cord-like (quays sia corda).
E aprop tu met dejos aquela le ray entro que sia elevada e sia gitada de la codena, e sospen aquela am onci orp leon.	And then you must put away that which is the way (le ray) so that it may be elevated and thrown away from the cord (codena), and suspend it with a hook (orp) like a lion.
E aprop secsa autra seccio aprop aquela seccio per tres ditz, e aprop excorja la codena de la partida desus de la vena entro que apparia.	And then you must make another section (seccio) near that section for three fingers (ditz), and then scrape off the cord (codena) from the upper part of the vein until it appears.
E aprop eleva aquela e inscideys aquela en deriera seccio deves le talo, e aprop extratz aquela e eleva aquela entro que sia yssida per la seccio segonda, e aprop extratz aquela de la seccio que es sobre aquela.	And then you must elevate that and inscribe it in the rear section of the talo (le talo), and then extract it and elevate it until it is emerged through the second section, and then extract it from the section above.
E fay aquo entro que extraguas aquela de la seccio que es pus sobirana o pus auta de totas las seccios, entro que tota es yssida; e lahoras inscideys aquela.	And then do this until you extract it from the highest or uppermost section of all the sections, until everything is emerged; and then inscribe it.
E si no obezeys a tu ad extrayre e elevar, lahoras intromet una agulha am fiel fort doble e ligua aquela e extratz la, o intromet dejos lu le ray e revolveys la tua ma a tota part entro qu’en sia getada.	And if it does not obey your order to extract and elevate, then insert a needle with a strong double thread and bind it (ligua aquela) and extract it, or insert below it the way and revolve your hand around the entire area until it is gone.
E guarda te que no sia inscidida; quar si es trencada, es fayt a tu dificil elevar aquela mot e es vengut sobre le malaute per aquela nocument.	And be careful that it is not torn (inscidida); for if it is broken, it will become difficult for you to elevate that part and it will come back upon the patient as a nuisance.
E cum aquela tota auras fora-gitada, lahoras pausa sobre le loc de la plagua lana submerssa en vi e oli rozat e oli no-rozat, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And when all that has been removed (tota) is fully gone, then pause over the place of the wound, submerged in wine and rose oil and non-rose oil, and cure it until it is healed.
E si la vit es contrayta havent tortuositat a la qual sia envolucio a las partidas, e no es segon rectitut segon que havem dit, lahoras cove que tu fendas sobre aquela a tota partida de tortuositat de lu e als locs de envolucio de lu, e aprop suspen aquela am uncis entro que eleves aquela tota.	And if the vein is contracted and twisted (tortuositat) without a normal curvature, and it is not straight according to what we have said, then you must cut across that part of tortuosity of yours and at the places where there is curvature, and then suspend it with unguents until you elevate it all.
E guarda te deves la tua seccio que no inscidas la vena e que no plagues aquela, quar dificil sira a tu elevar aquela; e serva la tua prudencia en aquela.	And beware that your incision (seccio) does not cut into the vein and does not injure it, for then it would be difficult for you to elevate it; and exercise caution in that.
Forma del inscident am le qual es seccada vit:	The shape of the incision that is made with the blood:
Forma de unci orp:	The shape of a hook-like instrument:
No es a lu accuitat ayssi cum als uncis ni es de aguda extremitat per so que no plague la vena; e es de grossa flexibilitat leon, quar si era subtil, inscidira la vena per la sua subtilitat; habantz es en lu superflua grosseza ayssi cum havem dit.	It is not like that of a hook or scissors, nor has it an acute extremity so as to injure the vein; but rather it has a thick and flexible lion-like shape, because if it were too subtle, it would cut into the vein due to its subtlety; and it has in excess a thickness similar to what we have said.
De extraccio venae cruris.	The extraction of the saphenous vein.
Aquesta vena es engendrada en las cambas en terras caudas ayssi cum al- Ategi en terra de Arabics e en las terras de India caudas e aridas de pauca teneritat e en las quals no nays erba ni aybre.	This vein is generated in the hips (cambas) in cold lands, as Al-Ategi said in the land of Arabs and in dry lands with little moisture and in those where there is no grass nor river.
E fort leu es engendrada en autres locs del cors otra las cambas.	And it is also generated in other parts of the body beyond the hips.
E la gestacio de lu es de putrefaccio que ve dejos la codena ayssi cum venen dedintz le cors serpentz e vermps e scarides e verms engendrantz entre la codena e la carn.	And its generation is from putrefaction that remains after the cord (codena) as well as venom poured out from the body of serpents, worms, and scorpions, and worms generated between the cord and the flesh.
E senhal de la suscepcio de l’adveniment de lu es de aquesta vena que accideys en la camba enflammacio vehement; e aprop le loc es vesicat; e aprop comensa la vena yssir del loc de aquela vesicacio quays sembla razit de planta.	And the sign of the susceptibility to the coming of it is when this vein in the hip becomes inflamed with great fervor; and at that place, vesicles form; and then the vein begins to emerge from that location where it appears as if a plant has taken root.
E adonc cum appar de lu la extremitat, lahoras cove que tu envolvas sobre aquela una pessa de plom del qual sia le pes de una drac. entro a ii drac., e noza aquela e layssa le plom suspendut de la camba.	And then, when the extremity appears from him, you must wrap around it a leaden cloth of which one ounce weighs two drams, and anoint it and let the lead hang from the hip.
E tantas veguadas cum yeys de lu alcuna causa a las partidas defora, envolveys aquo em plom e noza aquel.	And whenever you find some cause at the outer parts (partidas), wrap it in lead and bind it.
E si mot es prolonguat, lahoras tu inscideys una partida de lu e envolopa le romanent; e no inscidas aquela de razit entro que sia fora yssida, quar si inscideys aquela es contrayta e intra en la carn e fa accidir apostema e poyredura en le loc e ulceracio mala.	And if the part is prolonged (mot es prolonguat), you must incise one part of it and wrap up the remainder; and do not cut into that which has a root (de razit) until it is fully gone, for if you cut into it, it will be contracted and enter into the flesh and cause apostema and burning in that place and bad ulceration.
Per que cove que sia tractada suaument e sia extrayta petit a petit, entro que sia fora-gitada del derier de lu e no remangua de lu alcuna causa en le cors.	Therefore, it is necessary to treat it gently and extract it little by little, until it is fully removed from the body and there is no remaining cause in the body.
E de aquesta vena es yssit en alcus homes que es en la sua longitut de v palms e de detz e ja es pervengut a mi que yssic un de xx palms.	And from this vein, some men have been extracted who are in its length of 20 palms and I have already seen one who was 30 palms.
E si es inscidida en la hora de la sua medicacio, lahoras intromet lo ray en le trauc de lu e perfora aquela am lonc trauc am le cors, entro que sia evacuat tot aquo que es en la materia, e administra putrefaccio del loc per alcus dias am medicinas; e aprop cura aquela per la curacio de apostemas.	And if it is incised at the time of its medication (hora de la sua medicacio), then you must introduce the ray into the track of it and pierce that part with a long track through the body, until all that which is in the material is evacuated, and administer putrefaction of the place for some days with medicines; and then cure that part by the cure of apostemas.
E aquesta vena alcunas veguadas ha motz ramps, e majorment quan apar a la junctura del pe o en le pe, e veno a lu motz orrificis, e es yssit de quascu orrifici ram.	And this vein sometimes has many branches (motz ramps), and especially when it appears at the junction of the foot or in the foot, and comes out with many orifices (orrificis), and is issued from each orifice a branch.
E donc cura aquela ayssi cum havem dit en la divisio e am aquo que es desus dit.	And therefore, cure that part just like we have said in the division and also as has been said above.
De sectione super vermes generatos sub cute et dicitur aegritudo bovina.	On the removal of worms generated under the skin and it is called Bovine Ailment.
Aquesta malautia es nompnada en alcuna terra deves nos malautia bovina per so quar motas veguadas endeve als bious e es verm pauc un le qual es nat entre la codena e la carn, e va en tot le cos pujan e devalan, e es mostrat al sentiment deves le sieu anament de membre en membre entro que disromp la codena e yeys fora.	This illness is called in some lands the Bovine Ailment because many times it appears to be related to oxen and there is a worm that is born between the cord (codena) and the flesh, which goes throughout the body rising and falling, and is felt by the sensation of the own affection for limb to limb until it breaks the cord and comes out.
E la generacio de lu es per putrefaccio de alcunas humors ayssi cum accideysso verms e serpentz e lombrics e ascaridas en le ventre.	And the generation of this worm is due to putrefaction (putrefaccio) of certain humors, just like it happens with worms and serpents and lizards and scorpions in the womb.
E es temut per la malicia de lu, quar quan el va en le cors e es elevat al cap, e es pervengut al huel, lahoras fort leu uebre en lu e intra e destruzeys le huel, e aquo endeve motas veguadas.	And it is feared for the malice of this worm, because when it enters the body and rises to the head, and reaches the brain, then it is very strong in it and goes into it and destroys it, and that ends many times.
E donc quan tu voles curar aquel e extraire lu, lahoras no se fa si no deves la sieua ambulacio e apparacio de lu al sentiment, e adonc cove que tu strenhas aquo que es sobre lu e aquo que es dejos lu am liament e constriccio fort, e aprop secca sobre lu e extratz aquel.	And therefore, when you want to cure that and extract it, then do not proceed if you do not have the patient's consent and appearance of the wound (sentiment), and thus it is necessary to stretch what is above it and what is left of it with gentle constriction, and then bind over it and extract that.
E si es preondat en la carn e no le atrobes, lahoras tu pausa cauteri am foc sobre le loc entro que mora, e la major causa que es temuda es corrupcio de lu am la qual corrump le loc ayssi cum havem dit.
