And if it is buried in the flesh and you do not remove it, then you must pause the cauterizing iron with fire on the location until it dies, and the greatest fear that is feared is the corruption of the surrounding area which corrupts the location just as we have said.
May si tu vezes aquel esser pervengut al cap prop del huel, lahoras strenh sobre le sobrecil am fort strictura, e aprop secsa sobre lu, e extratz aquel; e cove que·l malaute use de mondificacio del sieu cors am medicinas evacuantz humors putridas malas, e guarda se de viandas generantz putrefaccio.	And if you find that the worm has reached the head near the brain, then strengthen the scalp with a strong stricture, and then bind over it, and extract it; and it is necessary for the patient to use the purification of their body with medicines evacuating bad humors, and beware of foods that generate putrefaction.
De sectione super aegritudinem nafir.	On the removal of worms from the skin (sectione super aegritudinem nafir).
Aquesta malautia es nompnada en nostra terra nafir, e es dolor la qual ve en alcus membres, e aprop es permudada de membre en membre.	This disease is called "nafir" in our land, and it is pain that comes to some members, and is spread from member to member.
E yeu ja e vista aquela segon que yeu te recomtare.	And you already know it, as I have recommended it to you.
Yeu fu apelat a una femna malauta ad una vila, e descubric le sieu bras e vi una imflacio petita en la vena funis del bras, e pus que fu romas per una hora, vi aquela imflacio anar ayssi cum va verm pujan ad aquest, mays pus leugierament que esser por, ayssi cum si fos argent viu quan corr de loc en loc.	I was called to a sick woman in a village, and I discovered her arm and saw a small swelling in the vein at the end of the arm, and after being there for an hour, I saw that swelling go away just like worms rise up to this place, but more slowly than it should be, as if it were live silver when it flows from place to place.
E adonc anet s’en la dolor de aquel loc e fiquet se en le muscle, e aprop aqui stec per una hora.	And then I went back to the pain in that place and fixed myself into the muscle, and there stayed for an hour.
E aprop correc en l’autre cors entro que pervenc al autre bras.	And then I corrected it in another direction until I reached the other arm.
E aprop recomtec a mi que revolvia se per tot le cors sieu segon que yeu vi; e fo trop meravelat de la permutacio de lu e de la velocitat de membre en membre.	And then I told myself that it was revolving itself around the entire body according to what you saw; and it was too marvelous the transformation of it and the speed from member to member.
E yeu ja havia vist denant aquo en les mieus huels segon aquela manieyra, empero yeu he vistz motz les quals atroban dolor esser permutada de membra a membre.	And I had already seen this before in my own flesh according to that manner; however, I have seen many others which also suffer from being transformed from member to member.
Mays no vi aquo am les huels ayssi cum en la femna.	But I did not see it in the same way with my own flesh as I saw it in the woman.
E yeu no cogiti esser aquo sino que es per aquo quar la femna era de viela, on so de secs cors e de venas descubertas, e en aquesta apparec al sentiment aquela ventositat permutada.	And I didn't think it was this way, but rather it is because the woman was old, with few seconds and veins uncovered, and in this appearance, that ventosity became perceptible.
E es necessari que no apparesca segon aquesta retro-curacio en aquels que son delicioses e am cors humitz de venas ameguadas.	And it is necessary that this condition does not appear according to this retrograde course in those who are delicacies and have humid hearts with veins hardened.
E cum tu voles la curacio de lu, e le pacient sent aquela dolor, lahoras no es a tu aparent al huel ayssi cum havem dit, lahoras tu strenh sobre aquel e dejos lu leugierament e secse sobre aquel entro que sia yssida aquela ventositat coartada, e cauterize le loc.	And when you want the cure of that, and the patient feels that pain, then it is not apparent to you what is happening at the top as we have said, but you must strengthen over that and leave it slightly open and dry over that until that ventosity is blocked, and cauterize the place.
Mays si tu no la vezes am los tieus huels, alhoras tu cura aquel am excussio del cors e am aquo que expelleys ventositatz, e carmina aquelas am pillulas fetidas e am pillulas de serapi e semblantz.	But if you do not treat it with the right pulse, then you must cure that with excitement of the chest and with what expels ventosity, and charm those with foul pills and with pills of serape and similar ones.
De extraccio de sagetas.	Of the removal of thorns.
Sagetas son diversificadas segon las specias, e segon les locs dels cors en les quals cazo, quar la lor diversitat es que de aquellas so que han grans puntas, e petitas, e concavas, e sordas, so es solidas; e de lor so que han tres angles, e de aquelas a las quals so que han lenguas; e de aquelas a las quals so astelas.	Thorns are diversified according to species, and according to the locations of the body where they grow, because their diversity is that some have great points, small ones, concave ones, dull ones, which are solid; and some have three angles, and those with tongues; and those with stars.
E aquela que es segon les membres e las pessas en las quals cazo es segon dos manieyras: quar les membres o so membres principals concaus, ayssi cum le cervel, le cor, e·l fitge, e le pulmo, e les ronhos, e les budels, e la vezica, e a lor semblantz; e donc quan catz en alcu de aquestz membres e aparo a tu senhals de mort, la qual causa yeu recomtare aprop, lahoras cove que tu evites extraccio de aquela sageta en aquels quar la mort siec aquel en le qual en las majors disposicios, e quan a tu no appareysso aquestz mals senhals, e la sageta no es amaguada en la profunditat del membre, lahoras tu extratz aquela e cura la plagua.	And that which is according to the members and the passions in which it grows is according to two manners: because the members or are principal members concave, like the brain, the heart, and the spine, and the lungs, and the kidneys, and the bladder, and the womb, and their likenesses; and therefore when it caters in one of these members and appears to you as a sign of death, which cause I will describe to you accurately, then it is necessary that you avoid extracting that thorn from those where death would be that member in its greatest disposition, and when it does not appear to you these evil signs, and the thorn is not hidden in the depth of the member, then you extract that one and cure the wound.
E dels senhals del servel es quan catz en lu sageta, e trespassa le os, e es yssit del cyphac le qual es sobre le cervel, quar accideys per lu soda vehement, e scotomia, e vertige, e rogor en les huels, e imflamacio e rogor de la lengua, e spasme e permixtio de entendament e vomi de colera, e fort leu es abscindida la paraula e es destruida la votz, e es yssit del loc de la plagua humiditat blanca semblant a pols, e yeys de lu semblant ad aquositat de la carn.	And among the signs of the servant is when it caters in the sageta, and trespasses the bone, and is situated above the cyphac which is on the brain, because accident occurs due to soda vehement, scotomia, vertigo, and roar in the ears, and inflammation and roar of the tongue, and spasm and mixture of understanding and vomiting of gall, and it is very much destroyed the word and is ruined the voice, and there is situated above the wound a humid white substance similar to powder, and there is an appearance of water like the flesh.
E donc si appareyso a tu aquestz senhals, lahoras tu abste de la curacio e de la extraccio de la sageta, si non es fora.	And therefore, if these signs appear to you, then it is necessary that you abstain from the cure and extraction of the thorn, unless it is outside.
Mays les senhals de la sageta quan catz en le cor, so que ela es prop de la mamila senestra, e sent am aquela quays sia ficada en causa dura, e no es causa vueda; e fort leu le movement de la sageta es semblant a movement del pols, e corr de la plagua sanc negra, e siec aquel fregiditat de las extremitatz, e suzor freja, e sincopi; e donc sapias que la mort descen ses tot dopte.	But the signs of the thorn when it caters in the heart are that it is near the left breast, and feels as if something has been placed there in a hard cause, and not a soft one; and very soon the movement of the thorn is like the movement of the pulse, and flows from the wound black blood, and there is a feeling of coldness in the extremities, and a shivering sensation, and fainting; and therefore know that death is descending upon you completely.
E les senhals quan la sageta ha plaglat le pulmo so eyssiment de sanc spumos de la plagua, e les vayssels que so prop del col so apostematz, e es mudada la color del malaute, e expira sperit gran aut, e demanda atraccio de ayre freg.	And the signs when the thorn has pierced the lung are that blood foam comes from the wound, and the vessels near the neck become inflamed, and the patient's complexion changes, and the spirit breathes heavily, and asks for fresh air.
E si catz la sageta en le velament le qual es en le pietz, e la dolor lahoras es prop de las costas petitas, e es fayt le ale gran am vehement dolor e am sospir, e no so maugutz totz les membres dels muscles.	And if the thorn pierces the membrane which is in the feet, and the pain is then near the small ribs, and it makes a great loud noise with violent pain and sighing, and none of the members of the muscles can be moved.
E si catz la sageta en le stomac, lahoras fort leu yeys de la plagua vianda alcuna indigesta.	And if the thorn pierces the stomach, then very soon there will be some undigested food coming out of the wound.
E si catz la sageta en le ventre, e es ficada en lu, yeys alcuna fenda de la plagua, o la tela, o budel le qual es disromput, e no es speransa en la curacio de lu extraccio de la sageta.	And if the thorn pierces the belly and is stuck there, then some gap or tear in the wound, or the membrane or bladder which is broken, and there is no hope for the cure of the extraction of the thorn.
E si la sageta catz en la vesica, e es yssida defora urina, e procesesca de lu alcuna causa a las partidas defora, e fort leu es dolor sobre le malaute, lahoras sapias que es mortal.	And if the thorn pierces the bladder and is voided outside as urine, and processes some cause to the parts outside, and very soon there is pain on the patient, then you should know that it is mortal.
Mays les autres membres ayssi cum es la cara, le col, e·l golayro, e las spallas e le adjutori, e les spondils del dos, e la furcula, e la coysa, e la camba e a lor semblantz dels membres, son salvatz segon las majors disposicios quan la sageta no atroba vena ni arteria e no es sageta venenosa.	But other members such as the face, neck, and groin, and the shoulders and assistants, and the vertebrae of the back, and the furcula, and the coccyx, and the hip and its likenesses to the members, are saved according to the greatest dispositions when the thorn does not touch a vein or artery and is not a venomous thorn.
E yeu recomtare aquo a tu que he vist del esser de aquestas sagetas, per que signifiques per aquo sobre la curacio tieua.	And I tell you this, that I have seen the being of these thorns, and for what it signifies for the cure of this illness.
La qual causa es, quar en un home cazec sageta en le lacrimal del huel de lu en la razitz del nas, e yeu extrayssi aquela a lu del autra partida, dejos le grays de l’aurelha de lu, e es sanat, e no accidic en le huel de lu nocument.	The cause is that when the thorn pierces in the lacrimal of the eye socket in the root of the nose, and I extract it from the other side, leaving the gray matter of the ear behind, and he recovers, and does not suffer any harm to the eye.
E extrayssi autra sageta a un Juzeu la qual cazec en lu en lo grays del sieu huel, dejos la palpebra pus dejos, e la sageta ja era occultada e no so conseguit de aquela sino una petita extremitat am la qual adhereys al sieu fust, e era gran sageta de las sagetas agudas dels Turcs , am ferr leon en la qual no havia aurelhas.	And I extracted another thorn from a Jew, which had pierced him in the gray matter of his eye socket, leaving behind the eyelid plus further, and the thorn was already hidden and not visible except for a small extremity with which it adhered to his fist, and it was a great thorn of the sharp thorns of the Turks, like a lion's claw without ears.
E senat es le Juzieu , e no accidic en le sieu huel mal accident.	And the Jew sat, and did not suffer any harm in his eye.
E extrayssi una autra sageta a un home Crestia la qual era cazuta en le golayro, e era sageta arabica, e es aquela a la qual so aurelhas; e adonc yeu inscidegui sobre aquela entre doas guidegi, e ja era submersa en le golayro de lu; e adonc yeu so subtiliat am aquela, e aprop extraxi aquela, e es sanat le Crestia .	And I extracted another thorn from a Christian man, which was lodged in the groin area, and it was an Arab thorn, and it had ears; and then I incised above that one between two guides, and it was already submerged in his groin; and then I carefully extracted it, and he is now healed, the Christian.
E extraxi autra sageta a un home la qual era cazuta en le sieu ventre, e cogitegui que moris per aquela; e donc, pus que foro passatz xxx dias e no es mudat sobre lu alcuna causa de las suas disposicios, inscidegui sobre la sageta e engenagui sobre aquela, e es sanat, e no accidic a lu accident mal.	And I extracted another thorn from a man, which was lodged in his stomach, and thought that he would die because of it; and therefore, since more than 30 days had passed and there was no change in his condition, I incised above the thorn and operated on it, and he is now healed, and not affected by the harm.
E vi mays un home en le qual cazec una sageta en le dos de lu, e consolidada es la plagua sobre lu, e pus que foc aprop set ans, yssic la sageta en la razitz de la coyssa.	And I saw a man in whom a thorn had pierced the spine of his back, and the wound was consolidated on him, and after almost seven years, the thorn came out at the root of the backbone.
E vi una femna a la qual cazec sageta en le sieu ventre, e la plagua es consolidada dedintz lu, e no es mudada en las suas disposicios en re, e la femna no atrobec nocument en alcunas de las suas opperacios naturals.	And I saw a woman in whom a thorn had pierced her stomach, and the wound was consolidated on the inside of her, and it had not changed in her condition for many years, and the woman did not experience any harm or difficulty with any of her natural operations.
E vi un autre home al qual cazec sageta en la sua cara e consolidada es la plagua e romas la sageta, no atrobant aqui mota dolor, e motz semblantz ad aquestz.	And I saw another man in whom a thorn had pierced his face and the wound was consolidated and the thorn remained, not causing any great pain or resembling those.
E extrayssi la sageta del home dels princeps del rey que era cazuda en le mieg loc del nas sieu e ja havia declinat a la partida dreyta un petit, e occultada era tota la sageta.	And I extracted the thorn from the king's nose, which was lodged in the middle of his nose and had already declined to the right side by a small amount, and the whole thorn was hidden.
E yeu fu appelat a la curacio de lu aprop le cazement de la sageta entro a tres dias.	And I was summoned for the treatment of him within three days after the thorn entered.
E adonc yeu atrobegui la plagua de la sageta mot streyta; e adonc yeu inquirigui aquela am tenta subtil, e no sentigui aquela; mays el la sentia puncio dejos la aurelha dreyta, e adonc speregui que aquela punccio era per la extremitat de la sageta.	And then I examined the wound of the thorn very carefully; and then I inquired about it with subtle attempts, and did not feel any pain; but he felt a pricking sensation behind his right earlobe, and then I suspected that this prick was from the extremity of the thorn.
E amplastregui le loc am emplaustre en le qual es vertut atrectiva e digestiva, confizant de mi que·l loc se apostemes per que appares a mi le loc de la sageta, per que secces sobre aquela.	And I applied the ointment to the place where it is virtuous for attracting and digestion, believing that the place is inflamed because of the thorn's presence, and that it needs to be cleansed over that area.
E no accidic en le loc accident significant que la sageta hagues conseguit aquel loc; e yeu continuegui am le emplaustre sobre lu per motz dias e no accidic accident; e consolidada es la plagua entretant, e romas le malaute de la extreccio de lu per spazi de motz dias entro que un jorn sentic la sageta dintz le sieu nas e recontec aquo a mi.	And there was no significant accident in the place where the thorn had managed to reach that location; and I continued to apply the ointment on him for many days, and there was no accident; and the wound consolidated in the meantime, and the patient's malady from the exit of his nose remained for several days until one day he felt the thorn inside his nose and recognized it again.
E adonc yeu pausegui sobre la plagua medicina acuta corrosiva per motz dias entro que foc ubert, e am la tenta yeu assagegui aquel, e atrobegui la extremitat de la sageta subtil, la qual adhereys al fust.	And then I applied to the wound acute corrosive medicine for many days until it was fully open, and with the attempt, I carefully extracted that extremity of the thorn which adhered to his fist.
E aprop yeu ajustegui en la apersio de la plagua per aquela medicina acuta entro que apparec a mi visiblament la extremitat de la sageta, e passec a mi temps am aquo per le spazi de temps entro quatre meses.	And then I adjusted in the appearance of the wound with that acute medicine until it became visible to me as the extremity of the thorn, and passed on to something else with this space of time within four months.
E aprop pus que la plagua foc amplificada, e foc a mi possible entrometre las forfexs en lu, e remaure aquela, e no obezic ad eyssiment, lahoras yeu no cessegui subtiliar e ingeniar sobre aquela am manieyras de engen, entro que comensegui un dia sobre aquela am manieyras de engens pendre lu am forceps descentment faytas, segon que vindra la forma de aquelas en la fi del capitol, entro que extraxi aquela; e aprop restauregui aquela plagua.	And then as the wound became amplified, and I had the possibility to enter it with forceps, and remain there, and not obey any orders, but rather, I continued to subtilize and engineer on that spot using the methods of engineering, until one day on that spot using the methods of engineers, taking him with descending forceps, according to the shape of those in the end of the capital, within which I extracted it; and then restored that wound.
E alcus metges jutgavan que la cartillage del nas no es restaurada, e yeu restauregui aquela e la plagua es consolidada, e sanat es le malaute per sanetat entiera, e no noguec en lu en deguna causa.	And some doctors judged that the cartilage of the nose was not restored, and I restored it and the wound is consolidated, and the patient is healed by whole health, and there is no damage to him in any cause.
E yeu recomti a tu la qualitat de extraccio de alcunas sagetas per que pauses aquo regla e significacio sobre aquo que no he dit, quar las partidas de aquesta art e las difinicios de aquela no so conprehendudas am narracio ni no comprehen aquelas le libre.	And I recommend to you the quality of extraction of some thorns because it is necessary that you pause here and consider the rule and significance of what has been said, for the parts of this art and the definitions of that are not comprehended by narration or free speech.
E le artifexs savi compara am pauc sobre mot; e am aquo que es present sobre aquo que es absent; e atroba operacio novela e instrument novel deves le descendement de las causas extranhas del art quan accideysso.	And the artisans know well how to compare a little with much, and on what is present with what is absent; and they find new operation and new instruments that are necessary for the descent of external causes from art when accidents occur.
E donc yeu dic que sagetas no son fora-gitadas dels membres en les quals son ficadas sino segon dos manieyras: o per atraccio del loc en le qual intrec; o per le contrari de la autra partida.	And therefore, I say that thorns are not expelled from the members in which they are stuck, except according to two ways: or by attraction of the place where they entered; or by contrary motion of the other part.
E aquela que es gitada per le loc don es intrada, o es sageta procedent en loc carnos, e es atirada e fora-gitada.	And that which is expelled by the place where it entered, or is a thorn proceeding from a fleshly location, and is attracted and expelled.
E si no obezeys a eyssiment de la hora en la qual catz, lahoras cove que tu la laysses per alcus dias entro que poyresca la carn que es al enviro de lu, e sia alleujada l‘atraccio de lu e la sua egressio.	And if it does not obey the sign of the hour in which it was caught, then you should leave it for some days until the flesh around it becomes putrid, and the attraction to it and its exit are alleviated.
E semblantment si es ficada en os e no obezeys a tu a eyssiment, lahoras layssa aquela per alcus dias e itera aquela am atraccio e mocio en quascun dia, e ja es fora-gitada.	And similarly, if it is stuck in bone and does not obey your sign, then leave it for some days and iterate the attraction and motion every day, and it will be expelled.
E si no obezeys a tu eyssiment aprop alcus dias, lahoras cove que tu perforas en le circuit de la sageta en aquel os de tota partida am taravel subtil entro que·l loc sia amplificat de la sageta, e aprop extratz aquela.	And if it does not obey your sign after some days, then you should pierce the circuit of the thorn in that bone on all sides with a subtle tool until the location is amplified by the thorn, and then extract it.
E si la sageta es ficada en le os del cap e ja ha procezit en un dels ventres del cervel, e apparo en le malaute alcus de aquels accidentz les quals yeu e ditz, lahoras abste de la extraccio de la sageta e layssa aquela entro que·l sieu esser sia equat aprop alcus dias; quar si la sageta perve al ciphac, lahoras la mort no es a lu prolonguada.	And if the thorn is stuck in the bone of the skull and has already proceeded into one of the ventricles of the brain, and appears to be causing some kind of malady or illness due to those accidents which I have described, then refrain from attempting to extract the thorn and leave it alone for a few days until its essence becomes equalized. For if the thorn penetrates too deeply, then death is not prolonged.
E si la sageta no es ficada sino en le cors del os tant solament e no passa entro al ciphac, e roman le malaute per alcus dias, e no accideys a lu denguna causa de aquels accidentz, lahoras tu engenia en la atraccio de la sageta e en la atraccio de lu.	And if the thorn is not stuck but only in the marrow of the bone and does not pass into the brain, and the malady remains for a few days, and there is no cause to fear any of those accidents, then you should endeavor to attract the thorn and its attraction.
Mays si es mot ficada e no obezeys a tu a extraccio, lahoras tu aministra taravels en le circuit de la sageta ayssi cum havem recomtat, e aprop cura le loc entro que sia sanat.	And if it is very stuck and does not obey your attempts at extraction, then you should administer subtle instruments (taravels) in the circuit of the thorn as we have recommended, and properly care for the location until it is healed.
Mays si la sageta ja es amaguada en le loc del cors, e es amaguada del sentiment, lahoras tu inquireys aquela am tenta, e si tu sentas aquela, lahoras atira aquela am alcus sturmentz les quals so convenientz a la atraccio de lu.	And if the thorn is already hidden in the location of the flesh, and is hidden from feeling, then you should inquire into it with gentle attempt, and if you feel it, then attract it with some suitable instruments that are fitting for its attraction.
E si no podes sobre lu per la constriccio de la plagua e per la longitut del preon, e aqui no es os ni nervi ni vena, lahoras tu fen sobre la plagua entro que sia amplificada e que sia possible extrayre la sageta.	And if you cannot get to it on that side due to the constriction of the wound and the length of the preone, and here there is no bone or nerve or vein, then you should feel over the wound until it is amplified and it becomes possible to extract the thorn.
E si so a lu aurelhas am las quals sia tenguda, lahoras tu deliura la carn en la qual es ficada de tota partida am tot le engen que poyras far; e ingenia sobre aquo, si no podes sobre la evasio de la carn en la fractura de las aurelhas e en torssio de aquelas entro que obezesca.	And if you have the means to obtain them at a suitable price, then you should deliver the flesh in which it is stuck on all sides with all the skill that you can muster; and invent something over this, if you cannot obtain the evasion of the flesh in the fracture of the ears and in torsion of those until it complies.
E quan tu administras la extraccio de la sageta en quascun loc on sia, lahoras tu usa am torcio de la tua ma am forceps a totas partidas entro que fassa aquela obezir; e subtilia am deriera subtilitat que la sageta no sia trencada e que sia fayta a tu dificil atraccio de lu e de aquela extraccio.	And when you administer the extraction of the thorn in every location where it is, then you should use with twisting of your hand and forceps on all sides until it complies; and subtlety with subtle delicacy that the thorn is not broken and that it is made to fit your difficult attraction to it and its extraction.
E si no podes sobre aquela de la tua hora, lahoras tu layssa per alcus dias entro que se poyrescan las partidas que so en le circuit de lu, e aprop itera aquela quar lahoras es alleujada.	And if you cannot do anything about that of your hour, then you should leave for some days until the parts that are in the circle of it become settled, and then iterate again when it is alleviated.
Mays si a tu fa contrarietat flux de sanc, lahoras tu administra aquo que havem dit de curacio en le sieu capitol.	But if there is contrary flow of blood to you, then you should administer the water that we have said in our chapter on cure.
E guarda la tua vertut de inscizio de vena o de nervi, o de corda, e aministra engen en tota manieyra a tu possibla de la evasio de la sageta; e fay aquo am facilitat e tranquillitat e tarditat e fermetat ayssi cum yeu e a tu recomtat.	And take care of your virtue of inscizio of vein or nerve or cord, and administer skill in every manner possible to the evasion of the thorn; and do this with facility and tranquility and slowness and firmness as you have recommended.
E donc que fassas contrayre la sageta per so que·l malaute sia segon la figura segon la qual foc deves le cazement de la sageta en lu, quar es mays juvatiu.	And therefore, that you may counteract the thorn in such a way that the malady is according to the figure according to which you are forced to cauterize the thorn in it, because it is more justifiable.
Mays si aquo no es a tu possible, lahoras tu aministra aquo que es a tu possible per las figuras.	But if this is not possible for you, then you should administer what is possible to you according to the figures.
Mays las sagetas que son fora-gitadas per le contrari del autra partida, o que ja de lu procezeys alcuna partida a las partidas de fora, o fa gilbositat la extramitat de la sageta per sentiment de la partida pus desus de la codena propdana e vezes aquela eminent; adonc tu secsa sobre aquela; e sia la seccio segon la quantitat en la qual prenguan las forceps; e aprop atira aquela, quar ela es fayta leugiera a eyssiment.	But the thorns that are expelled by the contrary of the other part, or which already have proceeded some part to the parts outside, or make softness (gillibositat) at the extremity of the thorn due to the sensation of the part above the codena propdana and sometimes elevated; then you should see over it; and be the section according to the quantity in which the forceps take hold; and properly attract it, because it is made light for a sign.
Mays si es retenguda en le os, lahoras tu tortz lama segon contrarietat entro que la sageta enprema en le os, e amplifique a si meteys, e aprop extratz aquela.	But if it is retained in the bone, then you should twist the thread (lama) according to contrary motion until the thorn (sageta) presses into the bone, and amplify as far as possible, and properly extract that.
E sino, layssa aquela per alcus dias, e aprop itera aquela entro qu’en yesca.	And if not, then leave that for some days, and properly iterate that until it is consumed.
E si le fust de la sageta es en aquela, lahoras tu impelleys aquela am lu.	And if the root of the thorn is in that place, then you should push it into place.
Mays si le fust es cazut e voles aministrar inpulsio, lahoras tu intromet e aquela, si es sorda, sturment concau per so que intre la concavitat de lu en la coa de la sageta e aprop impelleys aquela am lu.	But if the root is cut and you must administer impulse, then you should introduce it into that place, even if it is deaf, using a hidden instrument so that it enters the concavity of it in the tail of the thorn and properly push it into place.
Mays si la sageta es concava, lahoras tu impelleys aquela am sturment fort intrant en aquela, quar la sageta es alleujada per aquela.	But if the thorn is concave, then you should push it into place with a strong instrument entering into that, because the thorn is alleviated by that.
E si la sageta es entoxiguada, lahoras cove que tu concaves tota la carn en la qual es le vere, si es a tu possible aquo, e aprop cura aquela am aquo que si conveneys.	But if the thorn is embedded, then you should cover all the flesh where it is located, if that is possible to you, and properly care for it with what is necessary.
E si la sageta catz en le pietz, o en le ventre, o en la vesica, o en le costat, e es propinqua per so que tu tocas aquela am la tenta, e es a tu possible secsar sobre aquela, lahoras secsa sobre aquela e guarda te de inscizio de vena o de nervi, e extratz aquela, e aprop cos la plagua si indigeys, e cura aquela entro que sia sanada.	And if the thorn (sageta) is stuck in the foot, or in the belly, or in the bladder, or in the ribcage, and it is close enough that you can touch it with your hand, and it is possible to see over it, then look over it and take care not to damage any veins or nerves, and extract it, and properly cover the wound if necessary, and cure it until it is healed.
Forma de forceps am las quals so atiradas las sagetas:	Forma of forceps by which are attracted thorns:
Sian las extremitatz de lor cum a bec de ausel que son faytas cum serra quan prendon sobre la sageta per so que no la layssen.	The extremities (ends) of which are like the beak of an owl, and are made as if they were a saw when they take hold on the thorn so that it does not let go.
E de aquelas son faytas motas specias, grans, paucas e migieras, segon la quantitat de la grandeza de la sageta e de la sieua pauqueza, e de la amplitud de la plagua, e de la constriccio de lu.	And there are many species, great, few, and mid-sized, according to the quantity of greatness of the thorn and its smallness, and the width of the wound, and the constriction of it.
Forma de impellent concau de aquesta extremitat conquava ayssi cum pena de ausel per so que sia alleujat le intrament de la sageta en lu, e impulcio de aquela sorda:	The shape of the hidden impulse of this extremity is like the beak of an owl, so that it may be alleviated the instrument of the thorn in it, and the silent push:
Forma de impellent de sorda extremitat:	The shape of the silent impulse:
ayssi cum ray per so que sia alleujat le intrament de lu en la sageta concava e es impellida am aquel.	As if a ray of light that is alleviated the instrument of it in the concave thorn and is pushed into it.
De fleubotomia de las venas.	Of phlebotomy on the veins:
Las venas de fleubotomia de las quals corr costuma de fleubotomar so .xxx., de las quals so en le cap .xvi., so es doas venas pulsatils las quals so aprop las aurelhas, dic alhasisain; doas herbas que so en les dos templars apparentz; e doas venas que so en dos lacrimals de dos huels que son appeladas aspicientz; e la vena preparada en le mieg loc del front, e la vena que es en la extremitat del nas; e doas guidegi que so al col; e doas venas que so en la labia desus; e doas venas que so en la labia dejos; e — aquestas so las venas que so appeladas algelic —; e so doas venas que so dejos la lengua.	The veins of phlebotomy, which are accustomed to being cut by phlebotomy... of which there are 16 on the head... which are two pulsating veins that are near the ears, as they say; two herbs that are in the two temples apparent; and two veins that are in the two lacrimals of the two eyes which are called aspicientz; and the vein prepared in the middle of the forehead, and the vein that is at the extremity of the nose; and two guides that are to the throat; and two veins that are in the upper lip; and two veins that are in the lower lip; and – these are the veins that are called algelic –; and there are two veins below the tongue.
Mays las venas que so fleubotomadas en les brasses so .v.; quar de aquelas es una cephalica, e es deves le latz silvestre; e le poble appela “la vena del cap”, e sorda, e es vena migiera, e es composta de un ram de la basilica, e de autre ram de la cephalica; e nomna aquela le poble “vena de tot le cors”, e basilica es vena la qual es pausada en le latz domestic, e es nomnada “citillar”, e nompnan aquela les vulguars “vena del ventre”; e funis del bras, e es pausada sobre le focil, e es aquela en la qual es fleubotomat, e es aquela que appar sobre le poutz per apparicio manifesta; e salvatella, e es la vena que es entre lo dit auricular e·l pus petit dit, e so en lu dos ramps.	But there are 5 veins that are cut in the arms... because one of those is a cephalic vein, and it is located in the wild arm; and the people call it "the vein of the head", silent, and it is a mid-sized vein, and it is composed of one branch of the basilica, and another branch of the cephalic; and they name that the people "the vein of all the body", and the basilica is a vein that is located in the domestic arm, and it is called "citillar", and common people call it "vein of the belly"; and the arm veins, and it is located on the forearm, and it is the one where phlebotomy is done, and it is the one that appears on the shoulder for manifest appearance; and salvatella, and it is the vein that is between the said auricular and the smallest said, and there are two branches in it.
E en le pe e la camba so tres venas; la una de aquelas es que es dejos la curvatura del denolh del latz silvestre; e la segonda es sophena, e·l loc de lu es dejos la camba del latz domestic; e la vena sciatica, e·l loc de lu es dejos la camba del latz silvestre; e en la camba son autras venas semblantz ad aquelas.	And in the foot and thigh there are three veins; one of which is that which is located below the curvature of the tibia of the wild arm; and the second is saphena, and its location is below the thigh of the domestic arm; and the sciatic vein, and its location is below the thigh of the wild arm; and in the thigh there are other veins similar to those.
Le juvament de las venas que so aprop las aurelhas es a cataris antics e emigranea e sahafati e ulceracios del cap malas antiquas.	The flow of the veins that are near the ears is for catarrhs, antiques and migraines, saharitis and ulcerous sores on the head, old evils.
E la qualitat de sagnar aquelas es segon que yeu recomti a tu: es que sia ras le cap del malaute, e sia freguat le cap del malaute en le occipiti en le loc de amdoas las venas am drap ample am bona fricacio; aprop strenha le malaute le sieu col am una benda entro que apparan las doas e les locs de lor so aprop las aurelhas en dos locs depremegutz del cap; e quereys aquela am le tieu dit, e si tu sentes le pols de aquelas am le dit tieu, aqui senha am tenta.	And the quality of bleeding those is according to what you recommend to yourself: that it should be clean the head of the patient, and that the head of the patient should be massaged on the occiput in the location where both veins meet with a wide cloth and good friction; bring the patient's neck tight with a bandage until the two veins appear at their locations near the ears in two spots under the cap; and then ask yourself if you feel the pulse of those with your own said, and if you do not sense it with your own said, here I will not try.
Aprop tu pren la lancea cutellar, e es aquela que es inscident, e aprop tu intromet aquel dejos la vena en la codena entro que·l fleubotomi vengua al os.	Take the lancet-cutting instrument, and it is that which is inserted, and take it into that location below the vein in the cord until the phlebotomy comes to the bone.
E aprop eleva la tua ma am la vena e la codena a las partidas desus e inscideys la vena am inscizio inscident.	And then lift your hand and take hold of the vein and cord at the parted parts above and cut into the vein with a cutting instrument.
E sia la longitut de la inscizio la quantitat de dos ditz ajustatz o entorn de aquo; e fay yssir del sanc atant quant voles.	And make the length of the incision two digits or around that, and let blood flow out as much as you want.
E aprop strenh am pulvils e layssa aquela entro que sia sanada.	And then take out the blood and leave it to be healed.
E ja e precedit en le comensament del libre la inscizio de aquelas e de lor la cauterizacio.	And now and previously in the beginning of this book, I have described the incision of those and their cauterization.
Mays de las doas venas arterias que so als templars le juvament de la fleubotomia es a emigranea antiqua e sode malvada e obtalmia assidua e cors de superfluitatz acutas effusas als huels.	But of the two arteries that are on the temples, the flow of bloodletting is for ancient and bad migraines, frequent obtalmia, and a body with acute effusions in the eyes.
E la qualitat de fleubotomar aquelas es segon que yeu recomti a tu: constrengua le malaute le sieu col mot entro que apparan las doas venas al sentiment per appericio manifesta e sia demonstrat le pols de lor dejos le tieu dit; e lahoras tu senha am tenta.	And the quality of bloodletting those is according to what you recommend to yourself: constrain the patient's neck tightly until the two veins appear by sensation and are demonstrated manifestly, and let your pulse be felt below the said tie; and then try again if it doesn't work.
E aprop tu eleva la codena desobre la vena a las partidas desus am le tieu dit indic, e intromet le fleubotomi inscident dejos, e eleva la vena en sus; e inscidey aquela ayssi cum has fayt en las doas venas autras; e fay correr del sanc segon la quantitat de la tua necessitat.	And then lift the cord above the vein at the parted parts above, indicated by your pulse, and insert the bloodletting instrument below, and lift the vein up; and cut into it just like you have done with the other two veins; and let the blood flow according to the quantity of your necessity.
E aprop deslia la coartacio del malaute, e pausa le tieu dit sobre la vena per una hora, e aprop pausa sobre aquela coto e pulvils e strenh aquela desus am fort constriccio, e layssa aquela entro que sia sanada.	And then release the constriction of the patient, and pause your pulse on the vein for an hour, and then pause on that spot and pulp and strengthen that part above with strong constriction, and leave it to be healed.
E ja es precedida la rememoracio de lor, e de aquelas la inscizio, e la atraccio en le comensament del libre.	And now it is preceded by the remembrance of theirs, and of those, and their incision, and attraction in the beginning of this book.
E donc le juvament de fleubotomia de la vena del front es aprop la fleubotomia de la cephalica a las malautias antiquas de la cara e a emigranea e rogor e ulceracios fetidas.	And thus the flow of bloodletting from the vein of the forehead is suitable for the bloodletting of the cephalic vein in old diseases of the face and ancient migraines, and rages, and foul ulcers.
E la qualitat de la fleubotomia de lu es segon que yeu recomti a tu; so es que·l malaute strenha le sieu col am una benda entro que apparesca la vena; e aprop pren le insturment le qual es nompnat fossori del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And the quality of the bloodletting there is according to what you recommend to yourself; so it is that the patient tightens their neck with a bandage until the vein appears; and then take the instrument which is named fossor, of which this is its form:
Pausa la puncta eminent la qual es al cap del fossori sobre aquela vena e percuteys sobre lu am penche o am autre causa en la manieyra de lu, e layssa lo sanc correr segon la quantitat la qual voles; e aprop deslia la perforacio del malaute e strenh aquela entro que sia sanada.	Pause the point that is at the tip of the fossor above that vein and strike on it with a gentle or another cause in the manner of it, and let the blood flow according to the quantity that you want; and then release the perforation of the patient and strengthen it until it is healed.
E alcunas veguadas es uberta am fleubotomi lat, empero no cove que·l fleubotomi sia de acuta extremitat ayssi cum les autres fleubotomis, abantz sia de lada extremitat, e fleubotoma aquela segon le tranvers, quar le os es propda e fort leu trencaria en lu le fleubotomi quan es subtil.	And sometimes it is opened with bloodletting late, but it does not need that the bloodletting be of acute extremity just like the other bloodlettings, but rather ahead of the lateral extremity, and bloodlet there according to the traverse, because the bone is propitious and strong enough to break through the bloodletting when it is subtle.
Mays le juvament de las duas venas que so als lacrimals de dos huels per scabia del huels per rogor e sebol en les huels, e a las malautias de la cara.	But the flow of the two veins that are on the lacrimals of two eyes for the scabs of the eyes due to rage and sebum in the eyes, and to the diseases of the face.
E la qualitat de la fleubotomia es que·l malaute strenha le col sieu am una benda, e aprop fleubotoma aquelas, e tu sias stant sobre le cap de lu.	And the quality of the bloodletting is that the patient tightens their neck with a bandage, and then you stand on top of it.
E sia fayta la fleubotomia segon le transvers a longitut un pauc am fleubotomi pauc, quar en le loc no es carn; e si le fleubotomi es subtil, fort leu la extremitat de lu es trencada.	And so the bloodletting is done according to the traverse at a length of a little bit with some bloodletting, because in that location there is no flesh; and if the bloodletting is subtle, then the extremity of it is broken.

Mays le fleubotomi de la vena del nas es conferent a febre acuta e a soda vehement, e a las malautias de la cara e emigranea e rogor que accideys en la cara, e majorment quan es antiqua.	But the bloodletting of the nasal vein is related to acute fever and strong thirst, and to diseases of the face and ancient migraines and rages that occur on the face, and most especially when it is old.

E la qualitat de la fleubotomia de aquelas es que el malaute strenha dejos quascuna en le sieu col am liament; e estia le artifexs sobre le cap del malaute, e le malaute sia sezent sobre una sezela.	And the quality of bloodletting from those is that the patient tightens each one in their neck with a bandage; and the artist sits on top of the patient's head, and the patient is seated on a stool.
E aprop fleubotoma la vena al lonc am fleubotomi ample petit a petit; e aprop extratz de sanc segon temprada quantitat o segon aquo que vezes de necessitat que es ad aquo; e aprop fay semblant del autra vena.	And then let blood flow from the vein at length with an ample and small bloodletting, little by little; and then extract blood according to the quantity of time or according to what is needed, as it is required; and then make it similar to the other vein.
E aprop deslia le liament e strenh las doas venas am strictura migiera per so que·l malaute no sia prefocat, e laysa entro al mati quar la plagua es sanada.	And then release the bandage and strengthen the two veins with a gentle pressure to ensure that the patient is not suffocated, and leave it until morning when the wound is healed.
E le juvament de la fleubotomia de las venas algerich, comfereys a petitas apostemas e pustulas de la boca e corrupcio de las gengivas e malas ulceracios e fissuras, e a malas ulceracios que so en le nas e en le circuit de lu.	And the flow of bloodletting from the Algerian veins, causes small abscesses and pustules in the mouth and corruption of the gums and bad ulcers and fissures, and to bad ulcers that are on the nose and in the surrounding area.
E la qualitat de la fleubotomia de aquelas es que fases cezer le malaute denant tu, e strenh le col de lu am una benda, e aprop revolveys las labias de lu e reguarda a doas venas de las quals la una es de la dextra de la labia e la segonda de la senestra; e la demonstracio de quascuna es per la negror de quascuna de amdos, e aquo mays es quar en le circuit de aquelas so venas menudas negras; e adonc inscideys cascuna per inscizio inscident.	And the quality of bloodletting from those is that it makes the patient sit before you, and tighten their neck with a bandage, and then turn up the lips and look at two veins, one on the right side of the lip and the other on the left; and the demonstration of each is by the darkness of each of both, and this more so because in the circuit of those small black veins; and therefore incise each for incision incident.
Mays si dubitacio es dejos tu, e no sabes qual es de aquelas, lahoras tu enten a inscisio de la major de aquelas, e de la pus manifesta de aquelas.	But if there is doubt left in you, and you do not know which one is the greatest of these, then you must understand to incise the most prominent one of those, and the most evident one.
E fay le semblant de las doas venas que so en las labias desus.	And make the appearance of the two veins that are on the lips above.
Mays costuma corr mays a inscidir las doas venas que so en la labia dejos.	But it is more common to cut into the two veins that are on the lip below.
Mays de doas venas que so dejos la lengua le juvament es aprop la fleubotomia de la cephalica a prefocacios que so en le guolayro, a la malautia de la uvula, e a malautias de la boca.	But the flow from the two veins below the tongue is suitable for bloodletting of the cephalic vein in cases of obstruction that are in the goiter, to the disease of the uvula, and to diseases of the mouth.
E la qualitat de fleubotomar aquelas es que segue le malaute entre las tuas mas denant le solel, e eleva la lengua de lu, e reguarda dejos la lengua, de la un latz de lu vena e del autre latz vena, e la color de quascuna es declinant a negror.	And the quality of bloodletting from those is that it follows the patient between your arms in front of the sun, and raises the tongue of him, and looks down at the tongue, from one side of the vein to the other side of the vein, and the color of each is declining to blackness.
E adonc fleubotoma quascuna; e guarda te que no ultimes la tua ma en fleubotoman aquelas, quar dejos aquelas so arterias.	And then bleed each one (fleubotoma quascuna); and be careful that you don't finish your hand in bleeding those veins, because below those are arteries.
E las tuas venas que so fleubotomadas en le coyde so en las quals corr costuma en totz les homes, e la fleubotomia de lor es fayta segon dos manieyras, o pongen am le fleubotomi mirtilat o olivar a subtilitat declinant; o secsar am fleubotomi cutellar, e apelha si alnessil, e aquesta es la forma de lu:	And your veins that are bloodletted in the cold are those in which bleeding is customary for all men, and the bloodletting of theirs is done according to two methods, either by placing the bloodletting instrument on the vein with a subtle inclination or on an olive branch; or cutting it off with a cutlery instrument and calling it "silence", and this is the form that is used:
E aquest alnessil es que conveneys a seccio e de aquels so specias latz e subtils segon la amplitut de las venas e segon la strictura de aquelas.	And this silence is that which corresponds to the section and of those species, fine and subtle, according to the amplitude of the veins and according to the constriction of those.
Forma de fleubotomi mirti:	Forma de fleubotomi mirti:
sia le latz de lu ayssi cum vezes, e conveneys a obrir las venas concavas plenas procedentz apparentz grossas, e ad aquelas que conteno sanc gros torbat.	So be it that the width of him is as much as times, and it corresponds to open the concave veins full of blood proceeding from apparent great thickness, and to those that contain thick blood.
E aquesta es la forma de fleubotomi olivar:	And this is the form of olive branch bloodletting:
E aquest fleubotomi es de menor latitut e de pus subtil extremitat, e conveneys a fleubotomia de venas subtils que conteno sanc subtil citri.	And this bloodletting is of lesser latitude and more subtle extremity, and it corresponds to bloodletting of fine veins that contain subtle citrine blood.
Mays le juvament de la fleubotomia de la vena basilica la qual es una de tres venas: quar extratz le sanc de las malautias que so dejos le guolayro e·l col, e de aquo que siec le pietz e·l ventre.	But the flow of bloodletting from the basilic vein, which is one of three veins, for extracting the blood of diseases that are below the goiter and throat, and from this it clears the feet and belly.
E conveneys al fleubotomador, quan fleubotomia aquela, que guarde be aquela e sia sobre-temor en aquela, quar dejos lu ha arteria, e si erra e ajusta en la punctura del fleubotomi, inscidira aquela arteria e accidira fluxs de sanc, per so que cove que no fleubotomes aquela am fleubotomi pungent, abantz sia sectant cum alnessil.	And it is fitting for the bloodletting practitioner, when bloodletting that, to be careful with that and to have a preoccupation with that, because beneath him there is an artery, and if he erred and adjusted in the puncture of the bloodletting, he would incise that artery and cause bleeding, which is why it is necessary not to bloodlet that with the sharp instrument, but rather to cut with silence.
E si no appar la basilica per apparicio manifesta, lahoras cove que tu laysses aquela e que tu mudes a la autre, o que cerques alcun ram sieu; o que fleubotomes en loc de lu finis del bras, quar aquela es manifesta; e secsa aquela am fleubotomi alnessil ayssi cum havem dit.	And if the basilic vein does not appear in a manifest manner, then you must leave it and move to another or seek out some branch of it; or bloodlet at the end of the arm, where it is manifest; and cut it with the bloodletting instrument as we have said.
Mays si tu voles la fleubotomia de lu meteyssa, lahoras cove denant la strictura del bras que toques le loc entro que conogues le loc dels pols, e aprop senha sobre lu am tencha; e aprop lia le bras e secsa la vena am seccio concava am fleubotomi alnessil ayssi cum havem dit; e guarda te que caja la percussio per alcu spazi del loc de la arteria.	But if you want to do the bloodletting of him, then it is necessary before the constriction of the arm that touches the location inside where you know the location of the hands, and place a sign on him with a notch; and tie the arm and cut the vein with a concave sectioning instrument as we have said; and be careful not to hit the percussion for some space from the location of the artery.
E quan tu vezes, cum strenhes le liament, imflacio en le loc que has senhat am tencha, lahoras aquela inflacio es inflacio de la arteria, e donc squiva aquela.	And when you tie, with the ligature, inflation in the location that you have marked with a notch, then that inflation is an inflation of the artery, and therefore avoid it.
E si vezes le sanc fluir en la fleubotomia ayssi cum aurina de enfant, e·l sanc es subtil rog, lahoras sapias que es del sanc de la arteria; e lahoras tu coyta e pausa le tieu dit sobre aquel per lonc spazi; e aprop osta le tieu dit, e si lo sanc es abscindit, quar motas veguadas es abscindit, lahoras tu strenh le bras e layssa aquel.	And if the blood flows in the bloodletting as if it were the milk of a child, and the blood is very subtle and red, then you know that it is from the artery; and when you see and pause your statement about that for a long time; and appropriately open your statement, and if the blood has been cut off, because many veins are cut off, then you tighten the arm and leave that.
E guardes le malaute de la moccio de lu, e sia sobre-temor de lu e no maugua aquel per alcus dias entro que sia sanat.	And beware of the patient's excrement and be over-concerned with him and do not worry about it for a few days until he is healed.
Mays si le sanc no es abscindit, e vezes que deves tu no es present medicina ad aquo, lahoras tu inscideys la arteria, si appar a tu; quar la extremitat de lu es contrayta, e es abscindit le sanc; o que prenguas scorsa de fistic, e fen aquela, e pren la una maytat e strenh aquela sobre le loc de la vena am strictura descent am liament e am pulvils entro al autra dia.	But if the blood is not cut off and you are not present with medicine to that, then you must incise the artery, if it appears to you; for the extremity of him is contracted, and the blood is cut off; or take a scissor-like device made from fists, and open it up, and take one half and tighten it on the location of the vein with constriction and ligament and powder inside another day.
E lahoras si le sanc es abscindit, bo es; e sino, lahoras cura aquel am aquo del qual es precedit a la rememoracio del loc de las polveras abscindentz flux de sanc.	And if the blood is cut off, it is good; and otherwise, then cure that with what preceded it to the memory of the location where the powder-filled vessels have been cut off.
E la abscizio del sanc de lu es dificil en motas disposicios per le loc petit de la plagua e la possibilitat del liament del bras.	And the cutting off of the blood from him is difficult in many situations due to the small location of the wound and the possibility of binding the arm.
Mays de la vena fusca la fleubotomia es juvament que extratz lo sanc de la partida subirana del cap e a la partida dejos del cors; per aquo quar es composta de ram de la basilica e de ram de cephalica, ayssi cum havem dit.	But from the jugular vein (de la vena fusca) bloodletting is a flow that extracts blood from the upper part of the head and the lower part of the chest; therefore, because it is composed of branches of the basilic and cephalic veins, as we have said.
E cove al fleubotomant aquela que sia sobre-temor en la fleubotomia de lu, quar dejos aquela es un nervi; e adonc si ajusta en la punctura del fleubotomi e atroba le nervi, accidira a lu stupor, e es difficil la sanacio de lu, e fort leu no es sanat de tot, E aquest nervi motas veguadas apar al sentiment; e si es ocultat ad alcus homes e es subtil e no es monstrat, lahoras cove que tu pauses le fleubotomi am le qual tu fleubotomas am seccio de alnessil, e evita le nervi am la tua fortalesa.	And it is necessary for the bloodletting practitioner to be over-concerned with that which lies beneath the skin, for beneath it there is a nerve; and accordingly, if he adjusts in the puncture of the bloodletting and finds the nerve, he will cause stupor in him, and it is difficult for him to recover, and even if he is not entirely healed, And this nerve often appears with sensation; and if it is hidden from some men and is subtle and does not show itself, then it is necessary for you to pause the bloodletting with the instrument of sharpness, and avoid the nerve with your strength.
E si la vena es entre dos nervis, lahoras tu fen la vena en la longitut.	And if the vein is between two nerves, then you must cut the vein in its length.
