And the quality of bloodletting from there is that the patient inserts their foot into cold water and makes a pressure on it until the veins appear; and then applies pressure over the junction of the foot and the ankle bone; and the location of the vein appears to be deviated from the usual path, and from there it ramifies in the face of the foot with many branches.
E donc fleubotoma le pus ample ram o dejos la camba deves le talo deves la agreguacio de lu, quar es milhor e pus sal.	And therefore bloodletting should be done on the most prominent branch below the hip bone, since it is better and safer.
E si fleubotomas aquela en la facia del pe, lahoras tu te guarda dels nervis que so dejos aquela sobre la facia del pe, e pausa la tua fleubotomia am la qual tu fleubotomas per le travers, quays cum si tu la volias inscidir.	And if you are bloodletting in the face of the foot, then you should beware of the nerves that are below it on the face of the foot, and pause your bloodletting with which you are bleeding through the transverse incision, as if you were going to cut into it.
E sia le fleubotomi vosil.	And thus the bloodletting is useless.
Mays si es prohibit le issiment del sanc; lahoras tu itera le pe de lu en l’aygua cauda e layssa correr le sanc en aquela entro que sia evacuat.	But if it is prohibited to let the blood flow; then you should insert the foot of that into cold water and let the blood run into it until it is evacuated.
E si le fleubotomador erra en la primieyra veguada, lahoras itera am le fleubotomi en sus un pauc, quar le loc es sal; e no temes de lu malician, mays que te guardes dels nervis ayssi cum havem dit.	And if the bloodletting practitioner is wrong in the first attempt, then you should repeat the bloodletting procedure a little, because the location is too difficult; and do not fear for evil, but beware of the nerves just as we have said.
E semblantment fay de la sophena del autre pe engualment.	And similarly, make the same incision on the other foot.
E de la vena sciatica, le loc ayssi cum havem dit es deves le talo dejos la cavilha de la partida silvestra.	And for the sciatic vein, the location is just as we have said, namely below the hip bone at the level of the gluteal fold.
E le juvament de la fleubotomia de lu es a dolo de anca quan es per sanc caut.	And the recommendation of bloodletting from there is for the hip when it is necessary to stop bleeding.
E la qualitat de la fleubotomia de lu es que·l malaute intre en banh, e festine e strenha la cueyssa de lu del latz de la ancha entro desus le talo desus quatre ditz an una benda longua subtil, quar no appar sino per aquo.	And the quality of bloodletting from there is that the patient should enter into a bath, and hasten and strengthen the skin of the limb from the lateral side to the medial side above the ankle bone, and then make a thin bandage around it, so that nothing appears except through that.
E donc quan appar, lahoras tu fleubotoma aquela segon cascun engen que es a tu possible e segon le tranvers, e es milhor; o inscidas aquela per inscizio o secces aquela per seccio, quar le loc de lu es sal.	And therefore, when it appears, then you should bloodlet that vein according to each individual's ability and according to the transverse direction, and it is better; or make an incision on that side or separate that part by sectioning it, since the location is difficult.
E ela es en motz homes mot ameguada; e si atrobas aquela, e no appar al sentiment de tot, lahoras fleubotoma alcun ram de lu, e es aquel que appar en le dos del pe enves le dit auricular e le anular.	And it is in a few men who are moderately affected; and if you find that one, and there is no appearance of the feeling of all, then bloodlet on some branch of it, and that is the one that appears on the two sides of the foot below the auricular and anular bones.
E guarda te dels nervis, e fay correr del sanc la quantitat que voles.	And beware of the nerves, and let the blood run as much as you like.
E aprop deslia la strictura e pausa sobre le loc de la fleubotomia coto e strenh le loc, quar leugierament es sanat.	And approach closely the stricture and pause over the location of the bloodletting, cutting and strengthening the location, so that it becomes slightly healthy.
De ventozacio e de las qualitatz de uzar de aquelas.	Of ventilation and the qualities of using those.
Ventozas so de corns, o de eram, o de veyre.	Ventozas are from corns, or from ears, or from veins.
E ventozacio es fayta segon doas manieyras: la una de lor es am scarificacio e extracio de sanc, e l’autra es ventozacio ses scarificacio.	And ventilation is done according to two methods: one of them is through scarification and extraction of blood, and the other is without scarification.
E aquesta ventozacio que es ses scarificacio es segon doas manieyras, quar o es am foc o ses foc.	And this ventilation without scarification is done according to two methods, because it can be with fire or without fire.
E a las ventozas que so administradas am scarificacio e extraccio de sanc son xiiii locs del cors, dels quals la un en lo qual so pausadas ventozas es alnocrati, e es la deriera partida del cap; e le mieg loc d’el de doas partz del col ensemp; e ventozas del mento dejos la mandibula pus dejos de la boca; e ventozas de doas spatulas; e ventozas de alohoster, e es sobre la fi de la coeta; e ventozas de dos focils, e so de dos brasses; e ventozas de doas cavilhas; e ventozas de doas cuoyssas.	And the ventozas that are administered with scarification and extraction of blood are 14 locations on the body, among which one place where ventozas are paused is the alnocrati, which is the rear part of the head; and the middle location between the two parts of the neck; and ventozas below the mandible plus below the mouth; and ventozas with two spatulas; and ventozas with alohoster, which is above the end of the coccyx; and ventozas with two fociels, which are on two brasses; and ventozas with two cavilhas; and ventozas with two cuoyssas.
E ventozacio no extratz le sanc sino de las venas menudas sparssas en la carn, e per aquo no catz la vertut per aquelas, ayssi cum es cazement per fleubotomia; ni no cove que ventozacio sia fayta am foc o ses foc en alcuna malautia fayta per replecio entro que le cors tot sia evacuat.	And ventilation does not extract the blood, but rather releases it from small veins scattered throughout the flesh, and therefore it does not cure the disease through those means, just as is done by bloodletting; nor does it matter whether ventilation is done with fire or without fire in any illness caused by repletion, until the entire body is evacuated.
Mays si necessitat provoca a ventozacio per malautia o per continua, aministrem aquela en tota hora al comensament del mes e en la fi de lu, e en le mieg loc de lu e en qualque temps sia.	But if necessity demands it, provoke ventilation for illness or continued administration, administer that in the beginning of the month and at the end of it, and in the middle of it, and at any time.
La qual causa es quar dels homes es en les quals es sanc multiplicat entro que indigeys de extraccio de lu per ventozacio e atroba en le sieu cap graveza e soda; e de aquels es que atroba replecio e rogor en la sua cara e en le sieu cap, e en le sieu col; e de aquels es que atroba pruziment en la sua cara e en le sieu front e tenebrositat e hebetut en les sieus huels; e de aquels que gieta le loc de la sua ventozacio; e de aquels es que le lor ris es multiplicat; e de aquels es que atroba gustament de sanc en la sua boca, o que la lengua es apostemada e escup sanc; e de aquels es que lor dormir es multiplicat, e de aquels que vetz sanc en lo dormir rogor e antics e plaguas e autras causas a lor semblantz.	The cause is that in some men the blood is multiplied within them to such an extent that they become desperate for extraction through ventilation and find themselves with great heaviness and sickness in their head; and those who find repletion and rigor in their face and head, and in their neck; and those who find pruritus in their face and forehead, and tenebrosity and obtuseness in their eyes; and those who lose the place of their ventilation; and those whose laughter is multiplied; and those who find a taste of blood in their mouth, or that their tongue becomes apostemated and spits up blood; and those whose sleep is multiplied, and those who see blood in their dreams, with great pain and ancient and other causes to their likeness.
E donc quan vezes en alcuna causa de aquelas, e propriament si es en le tertz o miga del mes, lahoras comandam ventozacio esser fayta pus que so passadas del dia dos o tres horas.	And therefore, when it happens in some of those causes, and specifically if it is in the third or middle of the month, then command ventilation to be performed more than two or three hours after sunrise.
E juvament de ventozacio de la nuca es que quan aquela confereys a gravitat en le cap e ad aquo que es efondit als huels; mays cove que aquo sia aprop evacuacio de tot le cors.	And the recommendation for ventilation of the neck is that when it confers gravity in the head and goes down to the eyes; but it is necessary that this be accompanied by evacuation of the entire body.
E aquesta ventoza es en le loc de fleubotomia de la cephalica.	And this ventozas is in the location of bloodletting of the cephalic.
E no es legut que use de lu aquel que es de frega complecio, o en le qual es catarr, quar dona ad aquel gran nocument.	And it is not allowed that one uses this method on someone who has a complexion of phlegm or in whom is catarrh, for it gives them great harm.
E per aquo no cove que uso de aquela les vielhs, e en les caps dels quals so malautias frejas.	And therefore, one should not use this method on the elderly, and in those whose heads are afflicted with cold diseases.
Mays ad aquel que sobre aquela es continuant sobre lu es fayta oblivio; e per aquo cove que tu comandes al ventozador que depause la sua ma un petit am la ventosa a las partidas dejos, temen de la generacio de oblivio.	But to those who are continuing on that [path] is made forgetfulness; and therefore it is necessary that you command the ventozador to pause his hand a little before the ventosa at the partitions, in order to fear the generation of forgetfulness.
Mays ventozacio de alkehel es en loc de fleubotomia de la vena fusca e de la basilica: e per aquo confereys a asma, e a la constriccio de ale e a la scissura del sturment de ale, e a tos, e a replecio.	But the ventozacio of alkohel is in the location of bloodletting of the vena fusca and basilica: and therefore confers on asthma, constriction of the lungs, rupture of the lung's membrane, and to the coughing, and repletion.
E cove que sia enpellida la ventoza alkehel un petit, quar si es pausada dejos, engendra debilitat en le cors e en le stomac.	And it is necessary that the alkohel ventozas be a little filled, because if it is paused too long, it will generate weakness in the body and stomach.
E la ventozacio de alhagdahan confereys a las dolors accident en le cap e a obtalmia, e emigranea, e prefocacio, e a dolors en las razitz de las dentz; e es en loc de fleubotomia de la basiliqua.	And the ventozacio of alhagdahan confers on accidental pains in the head and obtalmia, emigration, preoccupation, and pains in the roots of the teeth; and it is located in the location of bloodletting of the basilica.
E cove que comandes al ventozador que no prema la sua ma am scarificacio per que no inscida la arteria e accida fluxs de sanc.	And it is necessary that you command the bloodletter to not press his hand with scarification so that he does not cut the artery and cause flows of blood.
E ventozacio dejos le mento comfereys a alcola en la boca, e a corrupcio de la gingiva, e a semblantz a lor de las malautias que so en la boca, e stan en loc de fleubotomia de aliheric que so en las doas labias.	And ventozacio on the mento confers on alcola in the mouth, and corruption of the gingiva, and likenesses to their own diseases that are in the mouth; and it is located in the location of bloodletting of aliheric that is on both lips.
Mays la ventozacio que es fayta sobre las doas spatulas confereys a caphatan, le qual es fayt per replecio de caliditat.	But the ventozacio that is done on the two spatulas confers on caphatan, which is made by repletion of warmth.
E la ventosacio de las doas partidas dedintz dels focils confereys juvament de la fleubotomia de tres venas, so es de la basilica, fusca e cephalica, quar aquela atratz le sanc de totas aquelas venas pus manudas que so en la carn, e aquelas venas menudas de las autras venas pus grossas entro que pervengua la atraccio a las tres venas.	And the ventozacio of the two parts behind the foci confers on justly the bloodletting of three veins, that is, the basilica, fusca, and cephalica, because that draws out the blood from all those small veins that are in the flesh, and those small veins that are attached to the other larger veins until it reaches the attraction to the three veins.
E comanda al ventozador que trop no procezesca en scarificacio, quar le loc es denudat de carn, e dejos lu so nervis e arterias.	And command the bloodletter not to proceed too quickly with scarification, because the location is stripped of flesh and leaves him only nerves and arteries.
E es una ventoza am la qual es ventozat sobre alshosses e confereys a las emorroydas del cul e a las ulceracios pus dejos.	And it is a ventozas on which it is ventozated over alshosses and confers on the hemorrhoids of the anus and on ulcers that are later.
E cove que comandes al ventozador que sia gran ventoza, e que sia de eram, quar le loc indigeys de fort seccio; e fort leu so traucadas ventozas subtils e sia scarificat am scarificacio.	And it is necessary that you command the bloodletter to make a great ventozas, and one of earth, because the location requires strong section; and let there be gentle and subtle ventozas, and let it be scarified with scarification.
Mays ventozas de las cambas minueysso per minuicio manifesta, quar atiran le sanc de tot le cors, e comfereysso a dolors antiquas dels ronhos e de la mayre, e de la vesica; e provocan las mestruas, e comfereysso a bothor e ademil; e stan en loc de fleubotomia de doas sophenas, e alahorcoben, e de doas cavilhas.	But the ventozas of the cambas are manifested through minuicio, because they attract the blood from all over the body, and confer on old pains in the kidneys and bladder, and provoke menstruation, and confer on bothor and ademil; and they stand in the location of bloodletting of two sophenas, and alahorcoben, and two cavilhas.
Enpero mot debelitan tot le cors e fan accidir sincopi en motz homes.	However, they are so debilitating that they make accidents of syncope occur in many men.
E de las ventozas alahorcoben le juvament es propda al juvament a las ventozas de doas cambas.	And the ventozas alahorcoben have a justness that is proportional to the justness of the ventozas of two cambas.
E la qualitat de la posicio de las ventozas es que pauses la ventoza al comensament vueda e sucguas per succio temprada, e no prolongues la posicio de las ventozas, mays pausa aquelas leugierament, e reman aquelas coytadament, e que las humors venguan al loc per adveniment engual.	And the quality of the position of the ventozas is that it pauses the ventoza at the beginning, and sucks up by early succussion, and does not prolong the position of the ventozas, but pauses those slightly, and remains those quietly, and let the humors come to the place by natural arrival.
E no cesses iterar aquo e continuar entro que veja le loc ja enrojezir e inflar e que appara la rogor del sanc.	And do not cease until you see the location already redden and swell, and the rigor of the blood appears.
E lahoras tu scarifiqua e itera la succio pauc a pauc, e aprop considera en la dispozicio dels cors.	And after that, scarify and iterate the suction little by little, and carefully consider the disposition of the body.
Quar aquel home que es de tendra carn de rars pors, cove que tu le scarifiques una veguada e no pus, per que le loc no sia ulcerat.	Because that person who has tender flesh and few pores, you should only scarify it once and not again, so that the location is not ulcerated.
E comanda al ventozador que amplifique la scarificacio e pronde un pauc, e atempre la succio am facilitat.	And command the bloodletter to amplify the scarification and proceed a little, and then apply the suction with ease.
E si en le sanc es grossitut, lahoras cove que scarifiques doas veguadas, quar en la primieyra veguada es uberta la via de subtiliacio al sanc e a la aquositat de lu.	And if the blood is thickened, then afterwards you should scarify twice, because in the first scarification, the way of subtlety to the blood and to its satiation is opened up.
Mays en la segunda a la perscrutacio aquisida de la extraccio del sanc gros.	But in the second [scarification], you should proceed with the acquired scrutiny and extraction of the thickened blood.
E si le sanc es mot feculent, lahoras sia fayta scarificacio la tersa veguada per que consiegua le derier.	And if the blood is very foul, then a third scarification should be done so that the final result is achieved.
E derierament, quan volem extrayre le sanc pauc a pauc o un petit, abasta a nos una scarificacio.	And finally, when we want to extract the blood little by little or in small quantities, it is enough for us with one scarification.
E si volem extraccio de mot sanc, scarificam am mota scarificacio; e si nos conoyssem que·l sanc es gros, lahoras cove que scarifiquem per scarificacio preonda.	And if we want to extract a lot of blood, we should scarify with many scarifications; and if we know that the blood is thick, then afterwards you should scarify again.
E le terme de scarificacio en la qual es la profunditat de la codena tant solament.	And the term of scarification is the depth of the incision, not just.
E si aquel del qual la codena es grossa, dura, fusca, e les sieus pors so streytz, cove que les locs de las ventosas sian untatz lenitius, apertius resolutius; si es en temps d’estiu, ayssi cum es oli de aloen o oli de violat, o oli de amellas dossas, o oli de cemensa de coja; e si es en temps ivern, lahoras oli narci, o oli de liri, o oli de camamilla, o de sanc, e ad aquels semblantz.	And if the scar is thick, hard, dark, and its pores are narrow, it is necessary that the sites of the ventosas be anointed with lenitive, apertive, and resolutive ointments; if it is in the summer, thus it should be done as with olive oil or violet oil or almond oil or sesame oil; and if it is in the winter, afterwards you should use winter ointments such as narcissus oil or lily oil or chamomile oil or blood oil and those similar to them.
E si la superfluitat es grossa, freja, lahoras le oli sia amaranti, o oli de balsamita, o oli de aloen, o oli aneti, e a lor semblantz.	And if the superfluity is great, then afterwards you should use oil that is amaranthine, or oil of balsamita, or olive oil, or anise oil and those similar to them.
Mays si le ventozador es de amples pors de tendra carn, lahoras cove que sia prohibit de oli, e cove que ad aquest les locs de ventozas de lor aprop la ventozacio sian lavatz am ayguaros o am aygua freja de solatrum, o am aygua de coja, o am aygua de bordolaguas, e semblantz ad aquelas.	But if the bloodletter is of large pores and tender flesh, then afterwards it is necessary to prohibit oil, and it is necessary that those sites of ventozas where the ventozacio is closest be washed with cold water or icy water from a saltpeter or with water of coja, or with water of bordolaguas, and similar to those.
E aquel del qual le sanc es de mota humiditat, lava las suas ventozas am vi agre, o am aygua de mirt e sumac e semblant ad aquels.	And that one whose blood is of great humidity, washes his ventozas with vinegar or with water of myrtle and sumac, and similar to those.
E de aquel del qual las superfluitatz son grossas, lava las suas ventozas am vi antic, o am aygua de sansuc, que es majorana, o de decoccio de anet, o de camamilla, e a lor semblantz.	And that one whose superfluities are great, washes his ventozas with antiseptic vinegar or with water of sansuc (which is majorana), or with the decoction of anise, or chamomile, and similar to those.
E cove que la ventozacio sia guardada denant de banh; habantz cove que sia aministrada aprop issiment del banh per una hora o per doas, e cove que dorma aprop la ventozacio.	And it is necessary that the ventozation be done before dawn; having to administer it about an hour or two before dawn, and it is necessary that he sleep near the ventozation.
Quid est quo oportet ut regatur ventosandus aus phlebotomatus ante ventosationem.	What is it that should be regulated so that the windpipe may be opened and the blood let out before the bleeding?
Cove que consideras al comensament: lahoras si le ventozador o aquel que·s deu fleubotomar es coleric e ventz sobre lu sanc agut e imflamacio, lahoras cove que prengua causas infrigidantz, ayssi cum milgranas acetosas, e endivia an vi agre e laytuguas, e secanabin, e julep, e a lor semblantz.	And thus consider at the beginning: afterwards, if the bloodletter or one who is to be fleubotomized is choleric and vents upon him with sharp blood and inflammation, then it is necessary that he take cooling causes, such as milgranas acetosas, endivia in vinegar and lettuce, and secanabin, and julep, and similar to those.
E pausa a lor viandas ayssi cum poletz, e carns de auzels serbiges, e viandas conditas am agras, e a lu semblantz.	And pause from their foods as well as pulse, and meat of hens serving, and foods cooked with herbs, and similar to those.
E de aquel del qual la compleccio es freja, cove que prengua en beure eyssarop almiva, o eyssarop de alsecanabin de semensas, e sumac, e vi mot odorant migier entre viel et noel; e que a lu sia comendat que use de paucitat de beure e de mangar, e pausa las viandas de lu poletz e canabir e pissers e petitz auzels e colombat.	And of that one whose complexion is fresh, it is necessary that he take in drink essence of almiva or essence of alsecanabin of sesame seeds, and sumac, and very fragrant myrrh between veal and Christmas; and that it be commended to him that he uses moderation in drinking and eating, and pause the foods of his pulse and canabir and pigeons and small hens and doves.
E cove que en lo dia de ventozacio e de fleubotomia le beure sia major que la vianda.	And it is necessary that on the day of ventozation and fleubotomia, drink be more abundant than food.
E cove que sia donat en beure en alcunas horas ad alcus homes tyriaca alpharac, o medicamentz de musc, so es muscada, o alcelita denant la ventozacio o denant fleubotomia o aprop, per so que·ls membres principals sian confortatz e que·l sanc sia subtiliat; e no cove que prenguan aquela scalfatz.	And it is necessary that it be given in drink to certain people at some hours tyriaca alpharac, or medicines of musc, as it is muscadada, or alcelita before ventozation or before fleubotomia or nearby, so that the main members may be comforted and the blood be subtilized; and it is not necessary that they take those scaldings.
Mays las ventozas que so ses scarificacio sian ventozas que so pausadas sus le fetge, e sobre la melsa e podagra, e sobre le umbelic, en les locs dels jonolhs, e la pixida del ancha, quar aquestz membres no suffertan scarificacio sobre si.	But the ventozas that are to be done by scarification should be ventozas that are paused on the liver, and over the gallbladder and podagra, and over the navel, in the places of the joints, and at the tip of the large intestine, because these members do not tolerate scarification upon themselves.
E no es querit per aquelas sino atraccio de sanc de membre, ayssi cum pausam ventosa sobre mamilha en malautia de flux de sanc del sanc de las nars; e usam de aquela per que sia dissolvuda ventositat freja inviscade del membre, ayssi cum pausam sobre le ventre e l’umbelic; quar aquela rarifique le membre e scalfa lu e ramau la dolor quar resolveys ventositat.	And it is not sought for those [places] but attraction of blood from the member, just as pause a ventosa on the nipple in illness of flux of blood from the nose; and they use that to dissolve ventosity fresh viscous from the member, just as pause over the belly and navel; because that rarefies the member and scalds it and relieves the pain which resolves ventosity.
E ja es pausada sobre les ronhos quan accideys en lor opilacio o poyra, quar per vertut de atraccio fort leu huobre opilacio e erradica le poyra de son loc.	And it is paused over the tonsils when they are obstructed or swollen, because by virtue of attraction it forcefully opens up obstruction and eradicates swelling from its place.
E semblantment fa quan es pausada sobre le fetge e la melsa deves ventositat en aquels enclausa.	And similarly it is done when it is paused over the liver and gallbladder to dissolve ventosity in those who are enclosed.
E aquestas ventozas so administradas vuedas amb succio tant solament; e alcunas veguadas so administradas am foc.	And these ventozas are administered with suction alone, and sometimes with fire.
E alcunas veguadas so administradas plenas de aygua tebeza en las malautias de la melsa.	And sometimes they are administered full of hot water in illnesses of the gallbladder.
E aquo es per que la ventoza sia umplida e sia pus gran, so es aygua cauda sola o aygua en la qual sian cuytas herbas ad aquo convenientz.	And that is why the ventoza should be filled and be made greater, either with hot water or with water in which certain herbs are steeped to suitable proportions.
Forma de ventoza aministrada am foc: sia la amplitud del orrifici de dos ditz, segon que nos la havem formada; e la quantitat del preon sia la maytat de un palm; e sia en lo latz de lu, en le loc que es en le circuit, la maytat de lu, le trauc sia petit segon la quantitat que intre en lu una agulha.	The form of ventoza administered with fire: the diameter of the orifice should be two digits, according to how we have formed it; and the quantity of the preon should be half a palm; and it should be in the left side, at the location where it is in the circuit, half of that, the hole being small according to the amount that enters through an agulha.
Sia fayta de eram rog o citri, de grosses marges, leon, enguals e terses per so que no leda le membre deves la sua posicio sobre lu.	It should be made of earthenware or citrine, with large margins, lion, equal, and terse, in order that it may not lead the member to deviate from its position on it.
E sia al mieg de lu vergua transversa de eram o de ferr, on es pausada candela am lo foc.	And it should have in the middle a cross-shaped handle of earthenware or iron, where a candle is placed with fire.
E ja sia aquesta ventoza gran major de aquela la qual havem recomtat; e la pauca mendre de aquela segon las malautias e la etat de aquel que usa de aquela.	And this ventoza is much larger than the one we have described before; and the small size of that one, according to the diseases and condition of the person who uses it.
E las ventosas dels efantz e extenuatz so autres que las ventozas dels joves e de grosses corssas.	And the ventosas of the old and exhausted are different from those of the young and strong.

And the quality of placing this ventoza with fire on the member is that it extends the ember with good fuel decently before a small candle made of wax, and places it on the middle of the cross-shaped handle in the middle location of the ventoza, so that the fire is lit around the part left over, so that the patient's body is not burned.

Another method for making a stronger emplaustra!

The importance of careful examination and treatment!

The description of three types of drill bits!

The importance of using the right instruments!

De restauracio de la mandibula quan es trincada.	The restoration of the jawbone!

Capitol .v.	The fifth chapter!
De restauracio de la furcula quan es trinquada.	The treatment of a broken sternum!
Motas veguadas es trencada la furcula de la partida denant deves le muscle, e aquela fractura es fayta en una de tres manieyras.	The classification of sternum fractures!
Quar o es trencada, o seperada, o es seperada en doas partz otra que no accidan satagias; e es leugier a la restauracio de lu; o es ayssi que accideysso en lu satagias, e es dificil a restauracio de lu; o es ayssi que la fractura es am plagua.	The classification of sternum fractures into three categories!
E la operacio en aquela, quan la fractura es ses plagua, es que tu fassas esser present dos ministres, per so que la un tengua le adjutori e siegua la furcula trencada, e l’autre extenda le col ves aquela partida.	The surgical procedure for treating a sternum fracture with a wound!

The use of splints and bandages to immobilize the sternum!

The importance of proper sleeping position and elevation for bone healing!

De restauracio de fractura del bras.	The final chapter: "De restauracio de fractura del bras"!
Bras es compost de dos osses les quals so appelatz dos focils; dels quals la un es petit, e es aquel que siec le dit pous, e l’autre es gran e es aquel le qual es pausat dejos le petit dit, de la partida pus dejus.	The anatomy of the arm!

The treatment plan for a compound fracture of the arm!

The text is concluding with a message of reverence and respect for the Creator!
Ayssi fineysso las paraulas de Albucasim perfieytament de las quals Dieus ne sia benezeyt.	The final sentence!
Amen.	Amen indeed!
